# notes:                
40001001	Dore igitabo cy’amasekuruza ya Yezu Kristu , umwana wa Dawudi , mwene Abrahamu .
40001002	Abrahamu yabyaye Izaki , Izaki abyara Yakobo , Yakobo abyara Yuda n’abavandimwe be ,
40001003	Yuda abyara Faresi na Zara , kuri Tamara , Faresi abyara Esiromi , Esiromi abyara Aramu .
40001004	Aramu abyara Aminadabu , Aminadabu abyara Nahasoni , Nahasoni abyara Salimoni .
40001005	Salimoni abyara Bowozi , kuri Rahabu , Bowozi abyara Yobedi , kuri Ruta , Yobedi abyara Yese ,
40001006	Yese abyara umwami Dawudi . Dawudi abyara Salomoni , ku mugore wa Uriya ,
40001007	Salomoni abyara Robowamu , Robowamu abyara Abiya , Abiya abyara Asa ,
40001008	Asa abyara Yozafati , Yozafati abyara Yoramu , Yoramu abyara Oziyasi ,
40001009	Oziyasi abyara Yowatamu , Yowatamu abyara Akazi , Akazi abyara Ezekiyasi ,
40001010	Ezekiyasi abyara Manase , Manase abyara Amoni , Amoni abyara Yoziyasi ,
40001011	Yoziyasi abyara Yekoniyasi na barumuna be , igihe bajyanwa bunyago i Babiloni .
40001012	Ijyanwabunyago ry’i Babiloni rirangiye Yekoniyasi abyara Salatiyeli , Salatiyeli abyara Zorobabeli ,
40001013	Zorobabeli abyara Abiyudi , Abiyudi abyara Eliyakimu , Eliyakimu abyara Azori ,
40001014	Azori abyara Sadoki , Sadoki abyara Akimu , Akimu abyara Eliyudi ,
40001015	Eliyudi abyara Eleyazari , Eleyazari abyara Matani , Matani abyara Yakobo ,
40001016	Yakobo abyara Yozefu , umugabo wa Mariya ari we wabyaye Yezu witwa Kristu .
40001017	Ibisekuruza byose hamwe rero ni ibi : kuva kuri Abrahamu kugeza kuri Dawudi , ni ibisekuruza cumi na bine ; kuva kuri Dawudi kugera ku ijyanwabunyago ry’i Babiloni , ni ibisekuruza cumi na bine ; kuva ku ijyanwabunyago ry’i Babiloni kugera kuri Kristu , ni ibisekuruza cumi na bine .
40001018	Dore uko Yezu Kristu yavutse . Nyina Mariya yari yarasabwe na Yozefu ; mu gihe batarabana , aza gusama inda ku bubasha bwa Roho Mutagatifu .
40001019	Yozefu , umugabo we , wari intungane kandi utashakaga kumuteza urubwa , yigira inama yo kumusezerera rwihishwa .
40001020	Igihe yari akibizirikana , Umumalayika wa Nyagasani amubonekera mu nzozi , aramubwira ati « Yozefu , mwana wa Dawudi , witinya kuzana umugeni wawe Mariya , kuko yasamye ku bubasha bwa Roho Mutagatifu .
40001021	Azabyara umwana uzamwite Yezu , kuko ari we uzakiza umuryango we ibyaha byawo . »
40001022	Ibyo byose ariko byabereye kugira ngo huzuzwe ibyo Nyagasani yavugishije umuhanuzi ati
40001023	« Dore Umukobwa w’isugi agiye gusama inda , maze azabyare umuhungu , nuko bazamwite Emanuweli » , ari byo kuvuga ngo « Imana turi kumwe . »
40001024	Yozefu akangutse abigenza uko Umumalayika wa Nyagasani yamutegetse nuko azana umugeni we .
40001025	Ariko ntiyamwegera kugeza igihe Mariya abyariye umwana w’umuhungu nuko amwita Yezu .
40002001	Yezu amaze kuvukira i Betelehemu ya Yudeya ku ngoma y’umwami Herodi , abanyabwenge baturutse iburasirazuba baza i Yeruzalemu ,
40002002	babaza bati « Umwami w’Abayahudi uherutse kuvuka ari hehe ? Twabonye inyenyeri ye mu burasirazuba , none tuje kumuramya . »
40002003	Umwami Herodi abyumvise , akuka umutima , we na Yeruzalemu yose .
40002004	Akoranya abatware bose b’abaherezabitambo n’abigishamategeko b’umuryango , abasiganuza aho Kristu yagombaga kuzavukira .
40002005	Baramusubiza bati « Ni i Betelehemu ya Yudeya ; kuko ari byo umuhanuzi yanditse ati
40002006	’ Nawe , Betelehemu , umusozi wo muri Yudeya , si wowe giseswa mu migi yaho yose ; kuko ari wowe uzaturukaho umutware uzaragira umuryango wanjye , Israheli ’ . »
40002007	Nuko Herodi atumiza ba banyabwenge rwihishwa , abasiganuza igihe inyenyeri yabonekeye ,
40002008	abohereza i Betelehemu , ababwira ati « Nimugende mubaririze iby’uwo mwana ; maze nimumubona , muzabimenyeshe kugira ngo nanjye njye kumuramya . »
40002009	Bamaze kumva amagambo y’umwami , baragenda . Nuko ya nyenyeri bari baboneye mu burasirazuba ibajya imbere irinda igera hejuru y’aho umwana yari ari , irahahagarara .
40002010	Ngo babone inyenyeri barishima cyane .
40002011	Binjiye mu nzu babona umwana , na nyina Mariya ; nuko barapfukama baramuramya . Hanyuma bapfundura impago zabo , bamutura zahabu , ububani n’imibavu .
40002012	Cyakora baburirwa mu nzozi kudasubira kwa Herodi , banyura indi nzira basubira mu gihugu cyabo .
40002013	Bamaze kugenda , Umumalayika wa Nyagasani abonekera Yozefu mu nzozi , aramubwira ati « Byuka , ujyane umwana na nyina , uhungire mu Misiri ; maze ugumeyo kugeza igihe nzakubwirira , kuko Herodi agiye guhigahiga umwana ngo amwice . »
40002014	Yozefu arabyuka , ajyana umwana na nyina iryo joro , maze ahungira mu Misiri .
40002015	Nuko abayo kugeza igihe Herodi apfiriye . Ibyo byabereye kugira ngo huzuzwe ibyo Nyagasani yavugishije umuhanuzi ati « Nahamagaye umwana wanjye wari mu Misiri . »
40002016	Nuko Herodi abonye ko abanyabwenge bamubeshye , ararakara cyane , maze yohereza abica abana bose bo kuri Betelehemu n’abo ku mirenge yose iyikikije , bamaze imyaka ibiri n’abatarayigezaho , akurikije igihe yari yasobanuriwe n’abanyabwenge .
40002017	Nuko huzuzwa ibyo umuhanuzi Yeremiya yavuze ati
40002018	« Kuri Rama bumvise ijwi riboroga riganya cyane : ni Rasheli uririra abana be , kandi yanze guhozwa kuko batakiriho . »
40002019	Herodi amaze gupfa , Umumalayika wa Nyagasani abonekera Yozefu mu nzozi akiri mu Misiri ;
40002020	aramubwira ati « Haguruka , ujyane umwana na nyina , usubire mu gihugu cya Israheli ; kuko abashakaga kwica umwana bapfuye » .
40002021	Yozefu arabyuka , ajyana umwana na nyina , asubira mu gihugu cya Israheli .
40002022	Ariko yumvise ko Arikelawusi yazunguye se Herodi mu Yudeya , atinya kujyayo . Nk’uko rero yabisobanuriwe mu nzozi , agana mu karere ka Galileya ,
40002023	ajya gutura ku musozi witwa Nazareti . Bityo huzuzwa ibyavuzwe n’abahanuzi , ngo « Azitwa Umunyanazareti » .
40003001	Muri iyo minsi , Yohani Batisita atangira kwigishiriza mu butayu bwa Yudeya ,
40003002	avuga ati « Nimwisubireho , kuko Ingoma y’ijuru yegereje ! »
40003003	Uwo ni we wavuzwe n’umuhanuzi Izayi , ati « Ni ijwi ry’uvugira mu butayu aranguruye ati ’ Nimutegure inzira ya Nyagasani , muringanize aho azanyura ! ’ »
40003004	Yohani uwo yambaraga umwambaro uboheshejwe ubwoya bw’ingamiya , agakenyeza umukoba ; ibyo kurya bye byari isanane n’ubuki bw’ubuhura .
40003005	Nuko abaturage b’i Yeruzalemu , n’abo muri Yudeya yose , n’abo mu ntara yose ya Yorudani bakamusanga ,
40003006	bakabatirizwa na we mu ruzi rwa Yorudani , babanje kwiyemeza ibyaha byabo mu ruhame .
40003007	Abonye Abafarizayi n’Abasaduseyi benshi baje kubatizwa , arababwira ati « Mwa nyoko z’impiri mwe , ni nde wababwirije guhunga uburakari bwegereje ?
40003008	Noneho nimugaragaze imigenzereze ikwiranye n’ukwisubiraho nyako !
40003009	Kandi ntimwitwaze ngo ’ Abrahamu ni we mubyeyi wacu ! ’ Ndanabiberuriye , ndetse aya mabuye muruzi , Imana ishobora kuyabyutsamo abana ba Abrahamu .
40003010	Dore intorezo irambitse ku mizi y’ibiti ; none igiti cyose kitera imbuto nziza kigiye gutemwa maze gicanwe .
40003011	Jyewe ndababatirisha amazi kugira ngo mwisubireho , ariko Uje ankurikiye andusha ububasha , ndetse sinkwiriye no kumukuramo inkweto ; We azababatirisha Roho Mutagatifu n’umuriro .
40003012	Afite urutaro mu ntoki , kandi agiye gukubura imbuga ye : hanyuma azahunika ingano ze mu kigega , naho imishishi ayitwikishe umuriro utazima . »
40003013	Nuko Yezu ava mu Galileya ajya kuri Yorudani , asanga Yohani kugira ngo abatizwe na we .
40003014	Yohani ashaka kumuhakanira ati « Ni jye ukeneye kubatizwa nawe , none uransanze ! »
40003015	Ariko Yezu aramusubiza ati « Emera ubikore , tubone kuzuza dutyo icyo Imana ishaka . » Nuko aramwemerera .
40003016	Yezu amaze kubatizwa , ako kanya ava mu mazi . Ubwo ijuru rirakinguka : abona Roho w’Imana amanuka nk’inuma , amuhagarara hejuru .
40003017	Ubwo ijwi rituruka mu ijuru rivuga riti « Uyu ni Umwana wanjye nkunda cyane unyizihira . »
40004001	Hanyuma Yezu ajyanwa na Roho Mutagatifu mu butayu kugira ngo ashukwe na Sekibi .
40004002	Asiba kurya iminsi mirongo ine n’amajoro mirongo ine , hanyuma arasonza .
40004003	Nuko Umushukanyi aramwegera , aramubwira ati « Niba uri Umwana w’Imana , tegeka aya mabuye ahinduke imigati . »
40004004	Yezu aramusubiza ati « Haranditswe ngo ’ Umuntu ntatungwa n’umugati gusa , ahubwo atungwa n’ijambo ryose rivuye mu kanwa k’Imana . ’ »
40004005	Nuko Umushukanyi amujyana mu murwa mutagatifu , amuhagarika ku gasongero k’Ingoro ,
40004006	maze aramubwira ati « Niba uri Umwana w’Imana , ijugunye hasi ; kuko handitswe ngo ’ Izategeka abamalayika bayo kuzagusama , kugira ngo udasitara ku ibuye . ’ »
40004007	Yezu aramusubiza ati « Biranditswe kandi ngo ’ Ntuzagerageze Nyagasani , Imana yawe . ’ »
40004008	Umushukanyi yongera kumujyana ku musozi muremure , amwereka ingoma zose z’isi n’ubukire bwazo ,
40004009	nuko aramubwira ati « Ibyo byose nzabikugabira , numfukamira ukandamya . »
40004010	Yezu aramusubiza ati « Igirayo , Sekibi , kuko handitswe ngo ’ Uzaramye Nyagasani , Imana yawe , abe ari We uzakorera wenyine . ’ »
40004011	Umushukanyi amusiga aho . Ubwo abamalayika baramwegera , baramuhereza .
40004012	Yezu yumvise ko Yohani yatanzwe , yigira mu Galileya ,
40004013	yimuka i Nazareti , ajya kuba i Kafarinawumu ku nkuka y’inyanja , mu rugabano rwa Zabuloni na Nefutali ,
40004014	kugira ngo huzuzwe ibyo umuhanuzi Izayi yavuze ati
40004015	« Gihugu cya Zabuloni , nawe gihugu cya Nefutali , nzira igana inyanja , hakurya ya Yorudani , Galileya y’abanyamahanga !
40004016	Imbaga yari yigungiye mu mwijima yabonye urumuri rutangaje ; n’abari batuye mu gihugu gicuze umwijima w’urupfu , urumuri rwabarasiyeho . »
40004017	Guhera ubwo Yezu atangira kwigisha , agira ati « Nimwisubireho , kuko Ingoma y’ijuru yegereje ! »
40004018	Nuko igihe yagendaga ku nkombe y’inyanja ya Galileya , abona abavandimwe babiri , Simoni bita Petero na Andereya murumuna we ; bariho baroha inshundura mu nyanja , kuko bari abarobyi .
40004019	Arababwira ati « Nimunkurikire , nzabagira abarobyi b’abantu . »
40004020	Ako kanya basiga aho inshundura zabo , baramukurikira .
40004021	Yigiye imbere , abona abandi bavandimwe babiri , Yakobo mwene Zebedeyi , na murumuna we Yohani , bari mu bwato hamwe na se Zebedeyi ; bariho basana inshundura zabo . Nuko arabahamagara .
40004022	Ako kanya basiga aho ubwato na se , baramukurikira .
40004023	Nuko Yezu azenguruka Galileya yose , yigishiriza mu masengero yabo , atangaza Inkuru Nziza y’Ingoma , akiza icyitwa indwara n’ubumuga cyose muri rubanda .
40004024	Ubugiraneza bwe bumenyekana muri Siriya yose , bakajya bamuzanira imbabare zose zifite indwara n’ibyago by’amoko yose : abahanzweho , abanyagicuri , ibimuga , nuko akabakiza .
40004025	Maze abantu benshi bavuye muri Galileya no muri Dekapoli , iYeruzalemu no muri Yudeya , no hakurya ya Yorudani , bamuhombokaho .
40005001	Yezu abonye icyo kivunge cy’abantu aterera umusozi . Aricara , abigishwa be baramwegera .
40005002	Nuko araterura arigisha ati
40005003	« Hahirwa abakene ku mutima , kuko Ingoma y’ijuru ari iyabo .
40005004	Hahirwa abiyoroshya , kuko bazatunga isi ho umurage .
40005005	Hahirwa abababaye , kuko bazahozwa .
40005006	Hahirwa abasonzeye ubutungane bakabugirira inyota , kuko bazahozwa .
40005007	Hahirwa abagira impuhwe , kuko bazazigirirwa .
40005008	Hahirwa abakeye ku mutima , kuko bazabona Imana .
40005009	Hahirwa abatera amahoro , kuko bazitwa abana b’Imana .
40005010	Hahirwa abatotezwa bazira ubutungane , kuko Ingoma y’ijuru ari iyabo .
40005011	Murahirwa nibabatuka , bakabatoteza , bakanababeshyera ku buryo bwose , ari jye babahora .
40005012	Nimwishime munezerwe , kuko ingororano yanyu izaba nyinshi mu ijuru ! Ni uko batoteje abahanuzi bababanjirije .
40005013	Muri umunyu w’isi . Ariko se umunyu wakayutse , bawusubirishamo iki uburyohe ? Nta kandi kamaro kawo kereka kujugunywa hanze , ugakandagirwa n’abantu .
40005014	Muri urumuri rw’isi . Ikigo cyubatse mu mpinga y’umusozi nticyihishira .
40005015	Kandi nta we ucana itara ngo aryubikeho icyibo , ahubwo arishyira ku gitereko cyaryo aho rimurikira abari mu nzu bose .
40005016	Urumuri rwanyu niruboneshereze rutyo abantu kugira ngo barebe ibyiza mukora , bakurizeho gusingiza So uri mu ijuru .
40005017	Ntimukeke ko naje kuvanaho Amategeko cyangwa Abahanuzi ; sinaje gukuraho , ahubwo naje kunonosora .
40005018	Koko rero , ndababwira ukuri : kugera igihe ijuru n’isi bizashirira , nta kanyuguti , nta n’akadomo kazava mu Mategeko ibyo byose bitarangiye .
40005019	Nuko rero , uzarenga kuri rimwe muri ayo mategeko yoroheje , kandi akigisha n’abandi kugenza batyo , azitwa igiseswa mu Ngoma y’ijuru . Naho uzajya ayakurikiza akayatoza abandi , azitwa umuntu ukomeye mu Ngoma y’ijuru .
40005020	Reka kandi mbabwire : niba ubutungane bwanyu budasumba ubw’abigishamategeko n’abafarizayi , nta bwo muzinjira mu Ngoma y’ijuru .
40005021	Mwumvise ko abakurambere babwiwe ngo ’ Ntuzice ’ , kandi nihagira uwica , azabibarizwa mu rubanza .
40005022	Jyewe mbabwiye ko umuntu wese urakariye mugenzi we , azabibarizwa mu rukiko ; naho nabwira mugenzi we ’ Gicucu ! ’ azabibarizwa mu Nama Nkuru ; namubwira ati ’ Uri umusazi ! ’ , azishyurira mu nyenga y’umuriro .
40005023	Nuko rero nujyana ituro ryawe imbere y’urutambiro , ukahibukira ko mugenzi wawe mufitanye akantu ,
40005024	rekera ituro ryawe imbere y’urutambiro , ubanze ujye kwigorora na mugenzi wawe ; hanyuma ugaruke ubone guhereza ituro ryawe .
40005025	Jya ugira ubwira bwo kwiyunga n’uwo mwangana , igihe mukiri kumwe mu nzira kugira ngo ataguteza umucamanza , umucamanza akagushyikiriza umupolisi , ubwo ukaba uroshywe mu buroko .
40005026	Mbikubwize ukuri : nta bwo uzavamo utishyuye byose , kugeza ku giceri cya nyuma .
40005027	Mwumvise ko byavuzwe ngo ’ Ntuzasambane ’ ,
40005028	jyeweho , mbabwiye ko ureba umugore akamwifuza , mu mutima we aba yamusambanyije .
40005029	Ijisho ryawe ry’iburyo nirikubera impamvu yo gukora icyaha , rinogore urijugunye kure yawe : ikigufitiye akamaro ni ukubura rumwe mu ngingo zawe , aho kubona umubiri wose utawe mu nyenga y’umuriro .
40005030	Niba ikiganza cy’iburyo kigutera gukora icyaha , gice ukijugunye kure yawe : ikiruta ni uko wabura rumwe mu ngingo zawe , aho kubona umubiri wawe wose ugiye mu nyenga y’umuriro .
40005031	Kandi byaravuzwe ngo ’ Usenze umugore we agomba kumuha urwandiko rwo kumusenda ’ .
40005032	Naho jye mbabwiye ko umuntu wese usenda umugore we — usibye iyo babanaga bitemewe — aba amuteye gusambana ; n’ucyura umugore wasenzwe , aba asambanye .
40005033	Mwumvise kandi ko abakurambere babwiwe ngo ’ Ntuzarahire ibinyoma ahubwo uzahigura Nyagasani ibyo wamusezeranije mu ndahiro ’ .
40005034	Jyeweho mbabwiye kutarahira na gato : ari ukurahira ijuru , kuko ari inteko y’Imana ;
40005035	ari ukurahira isi , kuko ari umusego w’ibirenge byayo ; ari na Yeruzalemu , kuko ari Umurwa w’Umwami mukuru .
40005036	Ntukarahize n’umutwe wawe , kuko udashobora guhindura n’umwe mu misatsi yawe umweru cyangwa igikara .
40005037	Mujye muvuga muti ’ Yego ’ , niba ari yego , cyangwa ’ Oya ’ , niba ari oya ; ibigeretsweho bindi biba biturutse kuri Sekibi .
40005038	Mwumvise ko byavuzwe ngo ’ Ijisho rihorerwe ijisho , iryinyo rihorerwe irindi ’ .
40005039	Jyeweho mbabwiye kudashyamirana n’umugiranabi ; ahubwo nihagira ugukubita urushyi mu musaya w’iburyo , mutegeze n’uwundi .
40005040	Nihagira ushaka kukuburanya ngo agutware ikanzu yawe , mwegurire n’igishura cyawe .
40005041	Nihagira uguhatira gutera intambwe igihumbi , muterane ibihumbi bibiri .
40005042	Ugusabye , umuhe ; n’ushatse ko umuguriza , ntukamwihunze .
40005043	Mwumvise ko byavuzwe ngo ’ Uzakunde mugenzi wawe , wange umwanzi wawe . ’
40005044	Jyeweho ndababwira ngo ’ Nimukunde ababanga , musabire ababatoteza ’ .
40005045	Bityo muzabe abana ba So uri mu ijuru , We uvusha izuba rye ku babi no ku beza , kandi akavubira imvura abatunganye n’abadatunganye .
40005046	Nimwikundira gusa ababakunda , muzahemberwa iki ? Ese abasoresha bo , si ko babigenza ?
40005047	Maze se nimuramutsa gusa abo muva inda imwe , muzaba murushije iki abandi ? Ese abatazi Imana bo , si ko babigenza ?
40005048	Mwebweho rero , muzabe intungane nk’uko So wo mu ijuru ari intungane .
40006001	Murajye mwirinda kugira neza mu maso y’abantu mugira ngo babarebe ; mwaba mwivukije ingororano kwa So mu ijuru .
40006002	Igihe rero utanga imfashanyo , ntukavugishe ihembe imbere yawe , nk’uko indyarya zibigira mu masengero no mu mayira , kugira ngo baratwe n’abantu . Ndababwira ukuri : baba bashyikiriye ingororano yabo .
40006003	Naho wowe , nutanga imfashanyo , ikiganza cyawe cy’ibumoso ntikikamenye icyo icy’iburyo gikora ,
40006004	bityo imfashanyo yawe ijye igirirwa mu ibanga ; maze So umenya ibyihishe , azabikwiture .
40006005	Igihe musenga , ntimukagenze nk ’ indyarya zikunda gusenga zihagaze mu masengero no mu mayirabiri , ngo zibonwe n’abantu . Ndababwira ukuri : baba bashyikiriye ingororano yabo .
40006006	Naho wowe , nushaka gusenga , ujye winjira mu nzu yawe , ukinge , maze usenge So uri aho atagaragara ; maze So umenya ibyihishe , azabikwiture .
40006007	Igihe musenga , ntimugasukiranye amagambo nk’abatazi Imana , bibwira ko amagambo menshi ari yo atuma bumvwa neza .
40006008	Ntimukagenze nka bo ; kuko So azi neza icyo mukeneye , na mbere y’uko mukimusaba .
40006009	Mwebwe rero mujye musenga , mugira muti : Dawe uri mu ijuru , izina ryawe ryubahwe ,
40006010	Ubwami bwawe nibuze , icyo ushaka gikorwe mu nsi nk’uko gikorwa mu ijuru .
40006011	Ifunguro ridutunga uriduhe none .
40006012	Utubabarire ibicumuro byacu , nk’uko natwe tubabarira abaducumuyeho .
40006013	Ntudutererane mu bitwoshya , ahubwo udukize ikibi .
40006014	Koko , nimubabarira abantu amakosa yabo , So wo mu ijuru na We azabababarira ayanyu .
40006015	Naho nimutababarira abantu , na So ntazabababarira amakosa yanyu .
40006016	Igihe musiba kurya , ntimukijime mu maso nk’uko indyarya zibigira : zikambya agahanga kugira ngo babone ko zisiba . Ndababwira ukuri : ziba zashyikiriye ingororano yazo .
40006017	Wowe rero nusiba kurya , ujye wisiga mu mutwe , wiyuhagire mu maso ,
40006018	kugira ngo utamenyesha abantu ko usiba , ahubwo bimenywe na So uri aho atagaragara ; maze So umenya ibyihishe , azabikwiture .
40006019	Ntimugashakire ubukungu hano mu nsi , aho udusimba n’imungu byonona , aho abajura baca ibyuho bakiba .
40006020	Ahubwo mwizigamire ubukungu mu ijuru , aho udusimba n’imungu bitonona , aho abajura badaca ibyuho ngo bibe .
40006021	Kuko , aho ubukungu bwawe buri , ni ho n’umutima wawe uzaba uri .
40006022	Itara ry’umubiri ni ijisho . Niba rero ijisho ryawe ridafite inenge , umubiri wawe wose uzamurikirwa .
40006023	Naho niba ijisho ryawe ari ribi , umubiri wawe wose uzaba mu mwijima . Noneho se , niba urumuri rukurimo ruhindutse umwijima , uwo mwijima uzangana iki !
40006024	Nta wushobora gukorera ba shebuja babiri : azanga umwe akunde undi , cyangwa azibanda kuri umwe , asuzugure undi . Ntimushobora gukorera Imana na Bintu .
40006025	Ni cyo gituma mbabwira nti ’ Mwihagarikwa imitima n’uko muzamera , ari ku bibatunga cyangwa ku byo muzambika umubiri wanyu . ’ Ubugingo se ntiburuta ibyo kurya ? Umubiri se wo nturuta umwambaro ?
40006026	Nimurebe inyoni zo mu kirere : ntizibiba , ntizisarura , ntizihunika mu bigega , nyamara So wo mu ijuru arazigaburira ! Mwebwe se , ntimuzitambukije agaciro ?
40006027	Ni nde muri mwe , n’aho yahagarika umutima ate , washobora kugira icyo yongera ku bugingo bwe ?
40006028	Imyambaro yo yabahagarikira iki umutima ? Nimwitegereze indabo zo mu gasozi uko zikura : ntiziruha , ntiziboha .
40006029	Nyamara rero ndababwira ko na Salomoni mu bukire bwe bwose atigeze yambara nka rumwe muri zo .
40006030	Niba Imana yambika ityo icyatsi cyo mu murima kiriho none , ejo kikazatabwa mu muriro , mwe ntizabarengerezaho , mwa bemera gato mwe ?
40006031	Mwibunza rero imitima muvuga ngo ’ Tuzarya iki ? Tuzanywa iki ? Tuzambara iki ?
40006032	Ni ibyo byose abanyamahanga bahihibikanira . So wo mu ijuru azi ko ibyo byose mubikeneye .

40006034	Mwiterwa impagarara n’iby’ejo : umunsi w’ejo uzazana impagarara zawo . Umuruho wa buri munsi urahagije .
40007001	Mwica urubanza namwe mutazarucirwa ,

40007004	Ubwo se wabwira ute mugenzi wawe uti ’ Reka ngutokore akatsi kakuri mu jisho ’ kandi utareba umugogo uri mu ryawe ?
40007005	Wa ndyarya we , banza ukure umugogo uri mu jisho ryawe , hanyuma uzabone neza , ushobore gutokora akatsi ko mu jisho rya mugenzi wawe .
40007006	Ikintu gitagatifu ntimukakigabize imbwa , amasaro yanyu ntimukayajugunye imbere y’ingurube : hato zitayaribata hanyuma zikabahindukirana zikabashiha .
40007007	Musabe , muzahabwa ; mushakashake , muzaronka ; mukomange , muzakingurirwa .
40007008	Kuko usaba wese ahabwa ; ushakashatse akaronka , n’ukomanze agakingurirwa .

40007010	Cyangwa se , yamusaba ifi , akamuhereza inzoka ?
40007011	Niba rero , mwebwe n’ububi bwanyu , muzi guha abana banyu ibintu byiza , So uri mu ijuru azarushaho ate guha ibyiza abamusabye ?
40007012	Ibyo mwifuza ko abandi babagirira byose , namwe muzajye mubibagirira : ngayo Amategeko n’Abahanuzi .
40007013	Nimwinjirire mu muryango ufunganye , kuko umuryango wagutse n’inzira y’igihogere ari byo bijyana mu cyorezo , kandi abahanyura ni benshi .
40007014	Mbega ukuntu umuryango ugana mu bugingo ufunganye , n’inzira ijyayo ikaba impatanwa , maze bikabonwa na bake !
40007015	Muritondere abahanurabinyoma babasanga , inyuma basa n’intama , naho imbere ari ibirura by’ibihubuzi .
40007016	Muzabamenyera ku mbuto bera . Hari usoroma imizabibu ku mahwa ? Cyangwa se imitini ku mikeri ?
40007017	Burya igiti cyose cyiza cyera imbuto nziza , naho igiti kibi kikera imbuto mbi .
40007018	Igiti cyiza ntigishobora kwera imbuto mbi , n’igiti kibi ntigishobora kwera imbuto nziza .
40007019	Igiti cyose kitera imbuto nziza baragitema , bakakijugunya mu muriro .
40007020	Nuko rero , muzabamenyera ku mbuto bera .

40007023	Ubwo nzaba bwira nti ’ Sinigeze mbamenya ; nimwigireyo , mwa nkozi z’ibibi mwe ! ’
40007024	Nuko rero , umuntu wese wumva ayo magambo maze kuvuga , kandi akayakurikiza , ameze nk’umuntu w’umunyabwenge wubatse inzu ye ku rutare .

40010001	Amaze guhamagara abigishwa be cumi na babiri , abaha ububasha bwo kuganza roho mbi no kuzirukana , n’ubwo gukiza icyitwa indwara n’icyitwa ubumuga cyose .

40011004	Yezu arabasubiza ati « Nimugende mutekerereze Yohani ibyo mwumva n’ibyo mubona :
40011005	impumyi zirabona , abacumbagira baragenda , ababembe barakira , ibipfamatwi birumva , abapfuye barazuka , n’abakene barigishwa Inkuru Nziza .
40011006	Hahirwa utazagushwa n’ibyo nkora ! »
40011007	Izo ntumwa zitirimutse , Yezu abwira rubanda ibya Yohani , ati « Mwagiye kureba iki mu butayu ? Urubingo se ruhubanganywa n’umuyaga ?
40011008	Mwagiye kureba iki ? Umuntu se wambaye imyenda y’agatangaza ? . . . Abambaye iy’agatangaza se ko batuye mu ngoro z’abami !
40011009	Nk’ubwo se , mwagiye kureba iki ? Umuhanuzi se ? Koko rero ndabibabwiye , ndetse atambutse umuhanuzi .
40011010	Ni we banditseho ngo ’ Dore nohereje intumwa yanjye imbere yawe , kugira ngo izagutegurire inzira . ’ »
40011011	Ndababwira ukuri : mu bana babyawe n’abagore , ntihigeze kuboneka uruta Yohani Batisita ; nyamara umuto mu Ngoma y’ijuru , aramuruta .
40011012	Guhera igihe cya Yohani Batisita kugeza ubu , Ingoma y’ijuru iraharanirwa , ab’ibyihare ni bo bayikukana .
40011013	Ni uko Abahanuzi bose kimwe n’Amategeko bavuze kugeza kuri Yohani .
40011014	Kandi niba mushaka kunyemera , ni we Eliya wagombaga kuza .
40011015	Ufite amatwi yo kumva niyumve !
40011016	Mbese ab’iki gihe nabagereranya na bande ? Bameze nk’abana bicaye ku bibuga , bagahamagara abandi ,
40011017	bati ’ Twavugije umwironge , maze ntimwabyina ! Duteye indirimbo z’amaganya , ntimwarira ! ’
40011018	Koko rero Yohani yaje atarya , atanywa , bati ’ Yahanzweho ! ’
40011019	Naho Umwana w’umuntu aje arya kandi anywa , bati ’ Ni igisambo , ni umusinzi , ni incuti y’abasoresha n’abanyabyaha ! ’ Nyamara ubuhanga bw’Imana bwagaragajwe n’ibikorwa byayo . »
40011020	Nuko atangira gutonganya imigi yabonye ibitangaza bye byinshi , ikarenga ntiyihane , avuga ati
40011021	« Iyimbire , Korazini ! Iyimbire , Betsayida ! Kuko ibitangaza byabakorewemo , iyo bikorerwa muri Tiri no muri Sidoni , baba barisubiyeho kuva kera , bakambara ibigunira bakisiga ivu .
40011022	Ni cyo gituma mbibabwiye : ku munsi w’urubanza muzahanwa kurusha Tiri na Sidoni .
40011023	Naho wowe , Kafarinawumu , ubona ko uzakuzwa kugera mu bicu ? Uzarohwa mu kuzimu . Kuko ibitangaza byagukorewemo , iyo bikorerwa muri Sodoma , iba ikiriho n’ubu .
40011024	Ni cyo gituma ku munsi w’urubanza uzahanwa kurusha igihugu cya Sodoma . »
40011025	Icyo gihe Yezu yungamo ati « Dawe , Mutegetsi w’ijuru n’isi , ngushimiye ko ibyo wabihishe abanyabwenge n’abahanga , ukabihishurira abaciye bugufi .
40011026	Koko , Dawe , ni ko wabyishakiye .
40011027	Byose nabyeguriwe na Data , kandi nta we uzi Mwana keretse Data , nta n’uzi Data , keretse Mwana n’uwo Mwana ashatse kumuhishurira .

40011030	Koko rero umutwaro wanjye uroroshye , n’ibyo mbakorera ntibiremereye . »
40012001	Icyo gihe , ku munsi w’isabato , Yezu anyura mu mirima yeze . Abigishwa be bakaba bashonje , bamamfuza ingano , barazirya .
40012002	Abafarizayi babibonye baramubwira bati « Dore re , abigishwa bawe barakora ibyabujijwe ku isabato ! »
40012003	Ariko we arababwira ati « Ntimwasomye uko Dawudi yabigenjeje , igihe yari ashonje , we n’abo bari kumwe ?
40012004	Uko yinjiye mu Ngoro y’Imana , n’uko bariye imigati y’umumuriko batashoboraga kurya , kuko yari igenewe abaherezabitambo bonyine ?
40012005	Cyangwa se ntimwasomye mu Mategeko uko abaherezabitambo bakorera mu Ngoro y’Imana ku munsi w’isabato bahora bica ikiruhuko cyayo , ntibibabere icyaha ?
40012006	Nyamara rero ndabibabwiye : hano hari igitambutse iyo Ngoro .
40012007	Iyo musobanukirwa n’iri jambo ngo ’ Icyo nshaka ni impuhwe , si igitambo ’ , ntimuba mwarahamije icyaha abaziranenge .
40012008	Koko , Umwana w’umuntu ni Umugenga w’isabato . »
40012009	Avuye aho , ajya mu isengero ryabo .
40012010	Maze ubwo hakaba umuntu ufite ikiganza cyumiranye . Nuko baramubaza bati « Ese biremewe gukiza umuntu ku munsi w’isabato ? » , bagira ngo babone icyo bamurega .
40012011	We rero arabasubiza ati « Ni nde muri mwe wagira intama imwe , yagwa mu mwobo ku munsi w’isabato , ntajye kuyikuramo ?

40012013	Hanyuma abwira uwo muntu ati « Rambura ikiganza cyawe . » Arakirambura , nuko kimera neza , kiba kizima nk’ikindi .
40012014	Ni bwo Abafarizayi basohotse , bajya inama yo gushaka uko bamwicisha .
40012015	Yezu abimenye , ava aho hantu . Abantu benshi baramukurikira , nuko arabakiza bose ,
40012016	kandi arabihanangiriza ngo boye kumwamamaza .
40012017	Bityo huzuzwa ibyavuzwe n’umuhanuzi Izayi , ngo
40012018	« Dore Umugaragu wanjye nitoreye , Inkoramutima yanjye natonesheje rwose . Nzamushyiraho Roho wanjye , na we azamenyeshe abanyamahanga ukuri .

40012021	abanyamahanga bazizera Izina rye . »
40012022	Nuko Yezu bamuzanira umuntu wahanzweho na roho mbi , akaba impumyi n’ikiragi ; aramukiza , nuko ikiragi kiravuga kandi kirareba .
40012023	Rubanda rwose baratangara , baravuga bati « Aho uriya ntiyaba Mwene Dawudi ? »
40012024	Abafarizayi babyumvise , baravuga bati « Belizebuli , umutware wa roho mbi , ni we yirukanisha roho mbi . »
40012025	Yezu amenye ibyo batekereza , arababwira ati « Ingoma yabyaye amahari irarimbuka : nta mugi , nta rugo byasubiranamo ngo bikomere .
40012026	Niba Sekibi yirukana Sekibi , ubwo ni we wirwanya . Ingoma ye izakomera ite ?
40012027	Niba kandi ari Belizebuli nirukanisha roho mbi , abana banyu bazirukanisha nde ? Ni bo rero bazababera abacamanza .
40012028	Ariko niba ari Roho w’Imana nirukanisha roho mbi , ni uko Ingoma y’Imana yabagezemo .
40012029	Cyangwa se , umuntu ashobora ate kwinjira mu nzu y’umunyamaboko no gusahura ibintu bye atabanje kumuboha ? Ni bwo yabona kumusahurira inzu .
40012030	Utari kumwe nanjye arandwanya , n’utarunda hamwe nanjye aranyanyagiza .
40012031	Ni cyo gituma mbabwira nti : Icyaha cyose n’ubutukamana bwose bizababarirwa , ariko gutuka Roho Mutagatifu ntibizababarirwa .
40012032	Kandi nihagira uvuga Umwana w’umuntu nabi , azagirirwa imbabazi ; ariko navuga nabi Roho Mutagatifu , ntazagirirwa imbabazi , ari muri iki gihe , ari no mu kizaza .
40012033	Niba mufite igiti cyiza , n’imbuto zacyo zizaba nziza ; nyamara nimugira igiti kibi , n’imbuto zacyo zizaba mbi : kuko igiti kirangwa n’imbuto zacyo .
40012034	Mwa nyoko mbi z’impiri mwe , mwashobora mute kuvuga amagambo meza kandi muri babi ? N’ubundi akuzuye umutima gasesekara ku munwa !
40012035	Umunyamico myiza avana mu mutima we ibyiza bibitsemo ; n’umunyamico mibi akavana mu mutima we ibibi byawusabitse .
40012036	Ndabibabwira : ku munsi w’urubanza , abantu bazabazwa ijambo ryose ritagira aho rishingiye bazaba baravuze .
40012037	Kuko amagambo yawe ari yo azatuma uba intungane , cyangwa se agatuma ucibwa . »
40012038	Nuko bamwe mu bigishamategeko no mu Bafarizayi baraterura , bati « Mwigisha , turifuza kubona ukora igitangaza . »
40012039	Arabasubiza ati « Iyi nyoko mbi kandi y’abahemu irashaka ikimenyetso ! Nta kindi kimenyetso izahabwa , atari icy’umuhanuzi Yonasi .
40012040	Nk’uko Yonasi yamaze mu nda y’igifi iminsi itatu n’amajoro atatu , ni na ko Umwana w’umuntu azamara mu nda y’isi iminsi itatu n’amajoro atatu .
40012041	Ku munsi w’urubanza , Abanyaninivi bazahagurukira ab’iyi ngoma , maze babatsinde , kuko bo bumvise inyigisho za Yonasi maze bakisubiraho , kandi hano hari uruta Yonasi !
40012042	Umwamikazi w’igihugu cy’epfo azahagurukira ab’iyi ngoma kuri uwo munsi w’urubanza , maze abatsinde , kuko yaturutse iyo gihera aje kumva ubuhanga bwa Salomoni , kandi hano hari uruta Salomoni !
40012043	Iyo roho mbi ivuye mu muntu , ibungera ahantu h’agasi , ishaka uburuhukiro maze ikabubura .
40012044	Nuko ikibwira iti ’ Nsubiye mu nzu yanjye navuyemo . ’ Yahagera igasanga idatuwe , ikubuye , iteguye .
40012045	Nuko ikagenda ikazana roho mbi zindi ndwi ziyitambukije ubugome , zikaza zikahatura . Nuko imimerere ya nyuma y’uwo muntu ikarushaho kuba umwaku . Nguko uko bizamerera iki gisekuru kibi . »
40012046	Akibwira rubanda , nyina n’abavandimwe be baba bari hanze , bashaka kugira icyo bamubwira . (
40012047	Nuko umuntu aramubwira ati « Dore nyoko n’abavandimwe bawe bahagaze hanze , barashaka ko muvugana . » )

40012049	Nuko arambura ukuboko yerekeje ku bigishwa be , ati « Dore mama n’abavandimwe banjye !
40012050	Kuko ukora icyo Data wo mu ijuru ashaka wese , ni we muvandimwe wanjye , na mushiki wanjye , na mama . »
40013001	Uwo munsi Yezu ava imuhira , maze yicara ku nkombe y’inyanja .
40013002	Abantu benshi bamuteranira iruhande , bituma ajya kwicara mu bwato , naho rubanda rwose ruhagaze ku nkombe .
40013003	Ababwirira byinshi mu migani , ati « Umubibyi yavuye iwe ajya kubiba .
40013004	Nuko igihe abiba , imbuto zimwe zigwa iruhande rw’inzira , inyoni ziraza zirazirya .

40013006	izuba rivuye zirashya , ziruma , kuko zitari zifite imizi .
40013007	Izindi zigwa mu mahwa , amahwa arakura , nuko arazipfukirana .
40013008	Izindi zigwa mu gitaka cyiza , nuko zera imbuto , imwe ijana , indi mirongo itandatu , indi mirongo itatu .
40013009	Ufite amatwi , niyumve ! »
40013010	Abigishwa baramwegera , baramubaza bati « Igituma ubabwira mu migani ni iki ? »

40013016	Mwebweho , amaso yanyu arahirwa kuko abona , n’amatwi yanyu arahirwa kuko yumva .
40013017	Ndababwira ukuri : abahanuzi benshi n’intungane nyinshi bifuje kubona ibyo muruzi ntibabibona , kumva ibyo mwumva ntibabyumva !
40013018	Mwebweho rero , nimwumve icyo umugani w’umubibyi uvuga .
40013019	Umuntu wese wumva ijambo ry’Imana , ariko ntaryiteho , ameze nk’imbuto yabibwe iruhande rw’inzira : Sekibi araza akamukuramo icyari cyabibwe mu mutima we .
40013020	Imbuto yabibwe mu rubuye , isobanura umuntu wumva ijambo , ako kanya akaryakirana ibyishimo ,
40013021	nyamara ntirimucengeremo ngo rimushingemo imizi kubera ko ahora ahindagurika ; iyo hadutse amagorwa cyangwa ibitotezo bitewe n’iryo jambo , agwa ako kanya .
40013022	Naho imbuto ibibwe mu mahwa , yo isobanura umuntu wumva neza ijambo , ariko imihihibikano y’isi n’ibishuko by’ubukungu bigapfukirana iryo jambo , rigapfa ubusa .
40013023	Hanyuma imbuto ibibwe mu gitaka cyiza , isobanura uwumva ijambo akaryitaho : uwo arera akabyara imbuto , umwe ijana , undi mirongo itandatu , undi mirongo itatu . »
40013024	Abacira undi mugani ati « Ingoma y’ijuru imeze nk’umuntu wabibye imbuto nziza mu murima we .
40013025	Ariko igihe abantu basinziriye , umwanzi we araza , abiba urumamfu hagati y’ingano , nuko arigendera .
40013026	Ingano ziramera , zimaze kugengarara , ubwo urumamfu na rwo ruragaragara .
40013027	Abagaragu basanga nyir’umurima , baramubaza bati ’ Shobuja , ntiwari warabibye imbuto nziza mu murima wawe ? Ni iki gituma harimo n’urumamfu ? ’
40013028	Arabasubiza ati ’ Ni umwanzi wabigize ! ’ Abagaragu barongera bati ’ Urashaka ko tujya kururandura ? ’
40013029	Ati ’ Oya , muri uko gutoranya urumamfu , mutavaho murandura n’ingano .
40013030	Nimureke bikure byombi kugeza mu isarura ; igihe cy’isarura nzabwira abasaruzi , nti ’ Nimubanze mutoranye urumamfu muruhambiremo imiba , muyijugunye mu muriro ; naho ingano muzihunike mu kigega cyanjye . ’ »
40013031	Abacira undi mugani ati « Ingoma y’ijuru imeze nk’imbuto ya sinapisi , umuntu yateye mu murima we .
40013032	Ni yo ntoya mu mbuto zose , ariko iyo imaze gukura , isumba imyaka yose yo mu murima , ndetse ikaba igiti , ku buryo inyoni zo mu kirere ziza kwarika mu mashami yacyo . »
40013033	Abacira undi mugani ati « Ingoma y’ijuru imeze nk’umusemburo umugore yavanze n’incuro eshatu z’ifu , kugeza igihe byose bitutumbye . »
40013034	Ibyo byose Yezu yabibwiraga rubanda mu migani , nta cyo yababwiraga atababwiriye mu migani ;
40013035	bityo huzuzwa ibyo umuhanuzi yavuze ati « Umunwa wanjye uzavuga mu migani , nzamamaza ibyahishwe kuva isi ikiremwa . »
40013036	Hanyuma asiga aho rubanda , ajya imuhira . Nuko abigishwa be baramwegera , baramubaza bati « Dusobanurire umugani w’urumamfu rwo mu murima . »
40013037	Arabasubiza ati « Ubiba imbuto nziza ni Umwana w’umuntu ;
40013038	umurima ni isi ; imbuto nziza ni abana b’Ingoma ; urumamfu ni abana ba Nyakibi ;
40013039	umwanzi warubibye ni Sekibi ; isarura ni iherezo ry’isi ; abasaruzi ni abamalayika .
40013040	Nk’uko rero batoranya urumamfu , bakarujugunya mu muriro , ni ko bizagenda mu iherezo ry’isi .
40013041	Umwana w’umuntu azohereza abamalayika be , bavangure mu Ngoma ye abateye abandi kugwa mu cyaha bose , n’inkozi z’ibibi zose ,
40013042	maze babarohe mu nyenga y’umuriro , aho bazaririra kandi bagahekenya amenyo .
40013043	Ubwo intungane zizabengerana nk’izuba mu Ngoma ya Se . Ufite amatwi , niyumve !
40013044	Ingoma y’ijuru imeze nk’ikintu cy’agaciro gakomeye gihishe mu murima ; umuntu iyo akiguyeho , yongera kugihisha , akagenda yishimye , agatanga ibyo atunze byose , akagura uwo murima .
40013045	Byongeye kandi Ingoma y’ijuru imeze nk’umucuruzi washakashakaga amasaro meza .
40013046	Yabona isaro rimwe ry’agaciro kanini , akagenda , akagurisha ibyo atunze byose , maze akarigura .
40013047	Byongeye kandi Ingoma y’ijuru imeze nk’urushundura banaze mu nyanja , maze rugafata amafi y’amoko yose .
40013048	Iyo rwuzuye , barukururira ku nkombe , hanyuma bakicara , bakarobanurira mu bitebo afite akamaro , naho adafite akamaro bakayajugunya .
40013049	Ni ko bizamera mu iherezo ry’isi : abamalayika bazaza batandukanye intungane n’abagome .
40013050	Maze bo babarohe mu nyenga y’umuriro ; aho bazaririra kandi bagahekenya amenyo .
40013051	Ibyo byose mwabyumvise ? » Bati « Yee . »
40013052	Arongera ati « Ni cyo gituma umwigishamategeko wese , wigishijwe iby’Ingoma y’ijuru , asa na nyir’urugo ukura mu bushyinguro bwe ibishya n’ibishaje . »
40013053	Yezu arangije iyo migani , ava aho .
40013054	Nuko ajya mu karere k’iwabo , ahigishiriza abantu mu isengero ryabo , bituma batangara bavuga bati « Ubu buhanga n’ubu bubasha bwinshi abikomora he ?

40013056	Bashiki be bose ntiduturanye ? None se biriya byose abikomora he ? »

40014001	Icyo gihe Herodi , umutware w’intara ya Galileya , yumva iby’ubwamamare bwa Yezu .
40014002	Nuko abwira ibyegera bye , ati « Uriya muntu ni Yohani Batisita , ni we wazutse mu bapfuye ! Ni cyo gituma afite ububasha bwo gukora ibitangaza . »
40014003	Koko Herodi yari yarafashe Yohani , aramuboha aranamufungisha , abitewe na Herodiya , umugore w’umuvandimwe we Filipo .
40014004	Kuko Yohani yamubwiraga , ati « Ntibyemewe ko umutunga . »
40014005	Herodi asigara ashaka kumwica , ariko agatinya rubanda rwabonaga ko Yohani ari umuhanuzi .
40014006	Ku munsi wo kwibuka ivuka rya Herodi , umukobwa wa Herodiya abyinira mu ruhame , Herodi aranyurwa .
40014007	Ni bwo arahiriye kumuha icyo ari bumusabe cyose .
40014008	Nuko uwo mukobwa amaze kugirwa inama na nyina , aravuga ati « Ngaho mpera aha ngaha ku mbehe , umutwe wa Yohani Batisita . »
40014009	Umwami ni ko kubabara , ariko kubera indahiro yagiriye imbere y’abatumirwa be , ategeka ko bawumuha .
40014010	Yohereza ujya gucira Yohani umutwe mu nzu y’imbohe .
40014011	Umutwe bawuzana ku mbehe , bawuha wa mukobwa , awushyira nyina .
40014012	Nuko abigishwa ba Yohani baraza batwara umurambo we , barawuhamba . Hanyuma bajya kubimenyesha Yezu .
40014013	Yezu amaze kubyumva , ajya mu bwato , agana ahantu h’ubutayu hitaruye ; rubanda rubimenye ruva mu migi , rumukurikira ku maguru .
40014014	Amaze kwambuka , abona abantu benshi , abagirira impuhwe ; akiza ibimuga byabo .
40014015	Bugorobye , abigishwa be baramwegera , bati « Aha hantu ntihatuwe , kandi umunsi uciye ikibu ; none sezerera aba bantu bajye mu ngo kwigurira ibyo barya . »
40014016	Ariko Yezu we arababwira ati « Bikwirirwa bajyayo ; nimubahe ibyo kurya mwebwe ubwanyu . »
40014017	Baramusubiza bati « Dufite hano imigati itanu n’amafi abiri gusa . »
40014018	Arababwira ati « Nimubinzanire hano . »
40014019	Amaze gutegeka ko bicaza abantu mu byatsi , afata ya migati itanu na ya mafi abiri , areba ku ijuru , ashimira Imana ; hanyuma amanyura ya migati ayiha abigishwa be , na bo bayiha rubanda .
40014020	Bose bararya barahaga . Nuko barundarundira hamwe ibisigaye , byuzura inkangara cumi n’ebyiri !
40014021	Nyamara abariye bari ibihumbi bitanu , batabariyemo abagore n’abana .
40014022	Nuko Yezu aherako ategeka abigishwa be kujya mu bwato no kumutanga hakurya , igihe agisezerera rubanda .
40014023	Amaze kubasezerera , azamuka umusozi kugira ngo asengere ahiherereye . Umugoroba ukuba ari wenyine .
40014024	Naho ubwato bwari bugeze kure y’inkombe , buhungabanywa n’imivumba , kuko umuyaga wabuturukaga imbere .
40014025	Nuko bujya gucya , aza abasanga agenda hejuru y’inyanja .
40014026	Abigishwa babonye agenda hejuru y’inyanja , bakuka umutima , bati « Ni Baringa ! » Bashya ubwoba , ni ko kuvuza induru .

41002015	Igihe Yezu yari ku meza iwe , hamwe n’abigishwa be , haza abasoresha benshi n’abanyabyaha gusangira na bo , kuko bamukurikiraga ari benshi .

41002017	Yezu ngo abyumve , arabasubiza ati « Abazima si bo bakeneye umuvuzi , ahubwo ni abarwayi ; sinazanywe n’intungane , ahubwo nazanywe no guhamagara abanyabyaha . »

41002019	Yezu arabasubiza ati « Birakwiye se ko abakwe basiba kurya , umukwe akiri kumwe na bo ? Igihe cyose bakiri kumwe n’umukwe ntibakwiye gusiba kurya .
41002020	Ariko hari igihe umukwe azabavanwamo , ubwo rero bazasiba kurya kuri uwo munsi .
41002021	Nta we utera igitambaro gishya ku mwenda ushaje , kuko abigenje atyo , igishya cyakurura igishaje maze umwenda ukarushaho gucika .

41002023	Umunsi umwe , ku isabato , Yezu anyura mu mirima y’ingano , abigishwa be batangira kugenda bazimamfuza .
41002024	Abafarizayi ni ko kumubwira bati « Dore re ! Kuki bakora ibibujijwe ku isabato ? »
41002025	Arabasubiza ati « Ntimwasomye uko Dawudi yabigenjeje , igihe ashonje akabura uko agira , we n’abo bari kumwe ?
41002026	N’uko yinjiye mu Ngoro y’Imana mu gihe cy’Abiyatari umuherezabitambo mukuru , akarya imigati y’umumuriko atashoboraga kurya , kuko yari igenewe abaherezabitambo bonyine , kandi akayihaho n’abari kumwe na we ? »

41002028	Ni cyo gituma Umwana w’umuntu agenga ndetse n’isabato ! »
41003001	Nuko yongera kwinjira mu isengero , maze ahasanga umuntu wari ufite ikiganza cyumiranye .
41003002	Ubwo bagenzuraga Yezu ngo berebe ko amukiza ku munsi w’isabato , bagira ngo babone icyo bamurega .
41003003	Nuko abwira uwo muntu wari ufite ikiganza cyumiranye , ati « Haguruka , uze hano hagati ! »
41003004	Maze arababwira ati « Ni iki cyemewe ku munsi w’isabato , ari ukugira neza , cyangwa ari ukugira nabi ? Ari ugukiza umuntu , cyangwa se kumwica ? » Nyamara bo baraceceka .
41003005	Nuko abararanganyamo amaso arakaye , ashavujwe n’imitima yabo yanangiye . Ni ko kubwira uwo muntu ati « Rambura ikiganza cyawe . » Nuko arakirambura , kirakira .
41003006	Abafarizayi basohotse , baherako bajya inama n’Abaherodiyani yo gushaka uko bamwicisha .
41003007	Yezu yigira ku nyanja hamwe n’abigishwa be . Abantu benshi baramukurikira , baturutse muri Galileya . N’abandi benshi baturutse mu Yudeya ,
41003008	n’i Yeruzalemu , no muri Idumeya , no hakurya ya Yorudani , no mu karere ka Tiri na Sidoni , baza bamugana , bumvise ibyo yakoraga .
41003009	Nuko abwira abigishwa be ngo bamuteganyirize ubwato , agira ngo ikivunge cy’abantu kitaza kumubyiganaho .
41003010	Koko rero yari yarakijije benshi , bigatuma abarwayi bose bamwirohaho bagira ngo bamukoreho .
41003011	Abahanzweho na roho mbi na bo , iyo bamubonaga , barambararaga imbere ye , bagatera hejuru bati « Uri Umwana w’Imana ! »
41003012	We ariko akabihanangiriza cyane , ababuza guhishura uwo ari we .
41003013	Hanyuma Yezu azamuka umusozi , maze ahamagara abo yishakiye ubwe , baramusanga .
41003014	Abashyiraho ari cumi na babiri , kugira ngo babane na we , kandi ngo abatume kwamamaza Inkuru Nziza ,
41003015	abaha n’ububasha bwo kwirukana roho mbi .
41003016	Abo ni Simoni , ari we yahimbye izina rya Petero ;
41003017	na Yakobo mwene Zebedeyi , na Yohani umuvandimwe we , ari bo yahimbye irya ’ Bowanerigesi ’ , bikavuga bene inkuba ;

41003019	na Yuda Isikariyoti , wa wundi wamugambaniye .
41003020	Bageze imuhira , abantu benshi bongera guterana , bituma badashobora kugira icyo barya .
41003021	Nuko bene wabo wa Yezu babyumvise , baza kuhamuvana ; kuko bavugaga ngo « Yasaze ! »
41003022	N’abigishamategeko bari bavuye i Yeruzalemu baravugaga ngo « Yahanzweho na Belizebuli ! » kandi ngo « Umutware wa roho mbi ni we yirukanisha roho mbi ! »
41003023	Nuko abakoranyiriza iruhande rwe , ababwirira mu migani ati « Sekibi yabasha ate kwiyirukana ?
41003024	Ingoma yibyayemo amahari ntishobora gukomera .
41003025	N’umuryango wabyaye amahari , na wo ntushobora gukomera .
41003026	Niba rero Sekibi yirwanya akicamo ibice , ntaba agikomeye , ake kaba kashobotse !
41003027	Kandi nta muntu ushobora kwinjira mu nzu y’umunyamaboko ngo asahure ibintu bye , atabanje kuboha uwo munyamaboko , hanyuma ngo abone uko asahura inzu ye .
41003028	Ndababwira ukuri , abana b’abantu bazakizwa ibyaha byose bakoze , ndetse n’ibitutsi batutse Imana .
41003029	Nyamara uzaba yaratutse Roho Mutagatifu , nta bwo azagirirwa imbabazi bibaho ; ahubwo azashinjwa igicumuro cye iteka . »
41003030	Yezu yababwiye ibyo , abitewe n’uko bavugaga ngo « Yahanzweho na roho mbi . »
41003031	Nyina wa Yezu n’abavandimwe be baraza , bahagarara hanze , bamutumaho ngo aze babonane .
41003032	Abantu benshi bakaba bicaye bamukikije . Baramubwira bati « Dore nyoko n’abavandimwe bawe bari hanze baragushaka . »
41003033	Arabasubiza ati « Mama ni nde , n’abavandimwe banjye ni bande ? »

41003035	Umuntu wese ukora icyo Imana ishaka , ni we muvandimwe wanjye , ni we mushiki wanjye , kandi ni we mama . »
41004001	Arongera atangira kwigishiriza ku nkombe y’inyanja . Abantu benshi cyane bamuteranira iruhande , bituma ajya kwicara mu bwato , mu nyanja , naho abantu bose bari imusozi ku nkombe y’inyanja .
41004002	Yabigishaga byinshi avugira mu migani , maze mu nyigisho ze akababwira ati
41004003	« Nimutege amatwi ! Umubibyi yavuye iwe ajya kubiba .

41004006	izuba rivuye zirashya , ziruma kuko zitari zifite imizi .

41004008	Naho izindi zose zigwa mu gitaka cyiza , zo zirakura ziragara , zera imbuto , imwe ikera mirongo itatu , indi mirongo itandatu , indi ijana . »
41004009	Nuko Yezu aravuga ati « Ufite amatwi yo kumva , niyumve ! »
41004010	Igihe bari basigaye bonyine , ba cumi na babiri n’abandi bari kumwe na we , bamusiganuza iby’imigani .
41004011	Arababwira ati « Mwebweho mwahawe kumenya amabanga y’Ingoma y’Imana , naho bariya bo hanze , byose bibabera urujijo ,
41004012	’ ku buryo bitegereza ariko ntibabone , bakumva ariko ntibasobanukirwe , kugira ngo badahinduka bagakizwa . ’
41004013	Nuko yungamo ati « Nta bwo mwumva uwo mugani ! Ubwo se iyindi migani yose , muzayumva mute ? »
41004014	Umubibyi , ni Ijambo ry’Imana abiba .
41004015	Hari rero abari iruhande rw’inzira aho iryo Jambo ribibwa . Bamara kuryumva , ako kanya Sekibi akaza , akabakuramo iryo jambo ryababibwemo .

41004017	ariko ntirishore imizi muri bo , bakarimarana igihe gito ; hatera amagorwa cyangwa batotezwa bahorwa iryo Jambo , bagahita bagwa .

41004019	ariko imihihibikano y’isi , n’ibishuko by’ubukungu , n’ibindi byifuzo bibi bibatwara umutima , bigapfukirana iryo Jambo , ntiryere imbuto na busa .
41004020	Naho abakirira imbuto nko mu gitaka cyiza , ni abumva Ijambo bakaryakira , bakera imbuto , umwe mirongo itatu , undi mirongo itandatu , undi ijana . »
41004021	Yezu arababaza ati « Harya bazanira itara kugira ngo baryubikeho icyibo cyangwa ngo barishyire mu nsi y’urutara ? Si ukugira ngo rishyirwe ku gitereko cyaryo ?
41004022	Koko rero , nta cyahishwe kitazahishurwa , nta n’ibanga rizahera ritamenyekanye ! »
41004023	Ufite amatwi yo kumva , niyumve ! » .
41004024	Arongera aravuga ati « Mwitondere ibyo mwumva . Igipimisho muzageresha , ni cyo namwe muzagererwamo , ndetse muzarengerezwaho .

41004026	Na none aravuga ati « Iby’Ingoma y’Imana byagereranywa n’umuntu watera imbuto mu gitaka .

41004032	ariko yamara kubibwa , igakura ikaruta ibindi bihingwa byose , ikagira amashami manini , bigatuma inyoni zo mu kirere ziza kwarika mu gicucu cyayo . »
41004033	Nguko uko yabigishaga Ijambo ry’Imana , abacira imigani myinshi , iringaniye n’ibyo bashoboraga kumva .

41005004	Kenshi yari yaraboheshejwe n’ingoyi n’iminyururu , maze agaca iminyururu agacagagura n’ingoyi , kandi nta washoboraga kumufata ngo amuherane .

41005013	Arabizemerera . Nuko roho mbi ziva muri uwo muntu , zinjira mu ngurube , maze uwo mukumbi wose ukonkoboka mu manga n’umuriri mwinshi , wiroha mu nyanja ; uko zari nk’ibihumbi bibiri , ziroha mu nyanja .
41005014	Nuko abashumba bazo barahunga , bajya kubimenyesha abari mu mugi n’abari mu cyaro na bo baza kureba ibyabaye .
41005015	Basanga Yezu , babona na wa muntu wigeze guhangwaho na Gitero , ya roho mbi , yicaye , yambaye , kandi noneho yagaruye ubwenge . Nuko bashya ubwoba .

41006012	Nuko baragenda , batangaza ko abantu bagomba kugarukira Imana .

41006020	kubera ko Herodi yatinyaga Yohani bigatuma amurengera , abitewe n’uko yari azi ko ari umuntu w’intabera kandi w’intungane . Iyo yabaga yamwumvise yabunzaga imitima cyane , nyamara yakundaga kumwumva .
41006021	Nuko haza kuba umunsi mukuru , ubwo Herodi yari yahimbaje isabukuru y’ivuka rye , maze atumira abatware be , n’abakuru b’ingabo ze hamwe n’abanyacyubahiro bo mu Galileya .
41006022	Umukobwa wa Herodiya araza arabyina , ashimisha Herodi n’abatumirwa be . Nuko umwami abwira umukobwa ati « Nsaba icyo ushaka cyose , ndakiguha . »
41006023	Aramurahira ati « Icyo unsaba cyose ndakiguha , kabone n’iyo cyaba icya kabiri cy’igihugu cyanjye . »
41006024	Umukobwa arasohoka abaza nyina ati « Nsabe iki ? » Undi aramusubiza ati « Saba umutwe wa Yohani Batisita . »
41006025	Umukobwa agaruka bwangu asanga umwami , amusaba avuga ati « Ndashaka ko umpa nonaha umutwe wa Yohani Batisita ku mbehe . »
41006026	Umwami biramushavuza cyane , ariko kubera indahiro ye n’abo yari yatumiye , yanga kwivuguruza .
41006027	Ako kanya umwami yohereza umwe mu ngabo ze , amutegeka kuzana umutwe wa Yohani . Uwo mugabo aragenda , amucira umutwe mu buroko .
41006028	Nuko azana umutwe ku mbehe , maze awuha uwo mukobwa , umukobwa na we awuha nyina .
41006029	Abigishwa ba Yohani babyumvise , baraza bajyana umurambo we , baramuhamba .
41006030	Intumwa zihindukiye , ziteranira iruhande rwa Yezu maze zimumenyesha ibyo zari zakoze byose n’ibyo zari zigishije byose .
41006031	Nuko arazibwira ati « Nimuze ahitaruye , hadatuwe , maze muruhuke gatoya . » Koko rero abazaga n’abagendaga bari benshi , bigatuma batabona n’umwanya wo kurya .
41006032	Nuko bajya mu bwato bambukira ahantu hadatuwe bagira ngo biherere .
41006033	Abenshi mu bababonye bagenda barabamenya , nuko baza ku maguru baturuka mu migi yose bahirukira , ndetse barahabatanga .
41006034	Yezu amaze kwambuka abona iyo mbaga nyamwinshi y’abantu , abagirira impuhwe , kuko bari bameze nk’intama zitagira umushumba , atangira kubigisha byinshi .
41006035	Umunsi uciye ikibu , abigishwa be ni bwo bamwegereye , maze baramubwira bati « Aha hantu ntihatuwe , kandi umunsi uciye ikibu ;
41006036	none sezerera aba bantu bajye mu ngo no mu nsisiro za hafi kwigurira ibyo barya . »
41006037	Arabasubiza ati « Nimubahe ibyo kurya mwebwe ubwanyu . » Baramubwira bati « Urashaka ko tujya kugura imigati y’amadenari magana abiri , ngo tubahe barye ? »
41006038	Arabasubiza ati « Mufite imigati ingahe ? Nimujye kureba . » Babimenye baravuga bati « Dufite itanu , n’amafi abiri . »
41006039	Nuko abategeka kwicaza bose mu bwatsi butoshye , mu dutsiko udutsiko .
41006040	Bicara ari inteko z’abantu ijana n’iz’abantu mirongo itanu .
41006041	Amaze gufata ya migati itanu na ya mafi abiri , areba hejuru , ashimira Imana . Hanyuma amanyura ya migati , ayiha abigishwa be kugira ngo babagaburire . Na ya mafi abiri ayabagabanya bose .
41006042	Bose bararya barahaga .
41006043	Nuko bakoranya ibisate by’imigati byasigaye n’iby’amafi , buzuza inkangara cumi n’ebyiri .
41006044	Nyamara abari bariye bari abagabo bageze ku bihumbi bitanu .
41006045	Nuko ako kanya ategeka abigishwa be kujya mu bwato no kumutanga hakurya , hafi ya Betsayida , we asigara asezerera abantu .
41006046	Amaze kubasezerera azamuka umusozi , ajya gusenga .
41006047	Umugoroba ukubye , ubwato buba bugeze mu nyanja hagati , we akiri imusozi wenyine .
41006048	Abona abigishwa be bananijwe no kugashya , kubera umuyaga wahuhaga ubarwanya . Nuko bujya gucya , aza abasanga agenda hejuru y’inyanja , ndetse ashaka no kubacaho .
41006049	Babonye agenda hejuru y’inyanja , bakeka ko ari baringa bavuza induru .
41006050	Bose bari bamubonye , bagira ubwoba . Yezu ni ko kubavugisha ati « Nimuhumure ni jye , mwigira ubwoba . »
41006051	Nuko abasanga mu bwato , maze umuyaga urahosha . Barushaho gutangara ,
41006052	kuko batari bumvise iby’imigati ; imitima yabo yari ikinangiye .
41006053	Bamaze kwambuka , bagera i Genezareti , maze bashyikira ku nkombe .
41006054	Bakiva mu bwato , abantu baramumenya ,
41006055	nuko bazenguruka ako karere kose , maze batangira kumuzanira abarwayi mu ngobyi , aho bumvaga yageze hose .
41006056	N’aho Yezu yinjiraga hose , ari mu nsisiro , mu migi no mu midugudu , bashyiraga abarwayi ku kibuga , maze bakamusaba ngo abareke bakore ku ncunda z’umwambaro we . Nuko abamukozeho bose bagakira .
41007001	Abafarizayi na bamwe mu bigishamategeko bari baturutse i Yeruzalemu , bateranira iruhande rwa Yezu .
41007002	Babona bamwe mu bigishwa be barisha intoki zanduye , ari byo kuvuga zidakarabye .
41007003	Koko rero , Abafarizayi n’Abayahudi bose ntibarya batabanje gukaraba ibiganza kugeza ku nkokora , bakurikije akamenyero k’abakurambere ,
41007004	n’iyo bavuye mu materaniro , ntibarya batabanje kwitera amazi . Hariho kandi n’indi migenzo myinshi bakurikiza by’akarande , nko koza ibikombe , ibibindi , n’amasahani . . .
41007005	Nuko rero , Abafarizayi n’abigishamategeko baramubaza bati « Ni iki gituma abigishwa bawe badakurikiza umuco w’abakurambere , bakarisha intoki zanduye ? »
41007006	Arabasubiza ati « Izayi yabahanuye neza , mwa ndyarya mwe ! Nk’uko byanditswe ngo ’ Uyu muryango unyubahisha akarimi gusa , naho imitima yabo indi kure .
41007007	Icyubahiro bampa ni amanjwe : inyigisho bigisha ni amategeko y’abantu gusa . ’
41007008	Murenga ku itegeko ry’Imana , mukibanda ku muco w’abantu . »
41007009	Maze arababwira ati « Murubahuka mugakuraho itegeko ry’Imana mwitwaza gukurikiza umucokarande wanyu .
41007010	Dore Musa yaravuze ati ’ Jya wubaha so na nyoko ’ , kandi ati ’ Uzatuka se cyangwa nyina , azacirwa urwo gupfa . ’
41007011	Naho mwe mukavuga ngo ’ Umuntu wese ubwira se cyangwa nyina ati : Ibintu najyaga kuzagufashisha ni « Korbani » , ari byo kuvuga ituro ry’Imana ,
41007012	mumwemerera kutagira icyo afashisha se cyangwa nyina ;
41007013	bityo mukavuguruza ijambo ry’Imana mwitwaza umucokarande . Kandi mukora n’ibindi byinshi bisa n’ibyo . »
41007014	Yongera guhamagara rubanda , arababwira ati « Nimutege amatwi mwese , kandi munyumve neza !
41007015	Nta kintu kijya mu muntu giturutse inyuma kimuhumanya , ahubwo ikivuye mu muntu ni cyo kimuhumanya .
41007016	Ufite amatwi yo kumva niyumve ! »
41007017	Amaze kwinjira mu nzu yitaruye rubanda , abigishwa be bamusobanuza uwo mugani .
41007018	Arabasubiza ati « Namwe mubuze ubwenge bigeze aho ? Ntimwumva se ko nta kintu na kimwe cyinjira mu muntu giturutse inyuma gishobora kumuhumanya ,
41007019	kuko kitinjira mu mutima we , ahubwo kijya mu nda , kigasohoka kijya gutabwa mu rwobo . » Bityo yemeza ko ibiribwa byose bidahumanya .
41007020	Arongera ati « Ikivuye mu muntu ni cyo kimuhumanya .
41007021	Kuko mu mutima w’abantu ariho haturuka imigambi mibi : ubusambanyi , ubujura , ubwicanyi ,
41007022	ubuhabara , umururumba , ubugome , uburyarya , ingeso mbi , ishyari , gutukana , ubwirasi , n’amafuti .
41007023	Ibyo bintu byose bibi biva mu mutima , ni byo bihumanya umuntu . »
41007024	Ahagurutse aho , Yezu ajya mu gihugu cya Tiri . Nuko yinjira mu nzu , adashaka ko hagira ubimenya , ariko ntiyashobora kuhaguma bitamenyekanye .
41007025	Ako kanya , umugore wari ufite umwana w’umukobwa wahanzweho na roho mbi yumvise bamuvuga , araza amupfukama imbere .
41007026	Uwo mugore yari umunyamahanga , kavukire k’i Fenisiya ho muri Siriya , nuko amusaba kwirukana iyo roho mbi yari mu mukobwa we .
41007027	Yezu aramubwira ati « Reka abana babanze bahage , kuko bidakwiye gufata umugati w’abana ngo bawujugunyire ibibwana . »
41007028	Umugore aramusubiza ati « Ni koko , Nyagasani ! Ariko n’ibibwana birya utuvungukira abana bataye mu nsi y’ameza . »
41007029	Aramubwira rero ati « Ngiriye iryo jambo uvuze , ngaho genda , roho mbi ivuye mu mukobwa wawe . »
41007030	Uwo mugore arataha , asanga umwana arambaraye ku buriri , koko roho mbi yamuvuyemo .
41007031	Yezu ava mu gihugu cya Tiri yambukiranya igihugu cya Sidoni , agaruka ku nyanja ya Galileya , yerekeje kuri Dekapoli .
41007032	Nuko bamuzanira igipfamatwi kidedemanga , baramwinginga ngo amuramburireho ibiganza .
41007033	Amuvana muri rubanda , amujyana ahitaruye , ashyira intoki ze mu matwi ye , nuko acira amacandwe ayamukoza ku rurimi .
41007034	Hanyuma yubura amaso ayerekeje ku ijuru , asuhuza umutima ati « Efata » , bikavuga ngo « Zibuka . »
41007035	Ako kanya , amatwi ye arazibuka , n’ururimi rwe ruragobodoka , maze atangira kuvuga neza .
41007036	Maze Yezu abihanangiriza kutagira uwo babibwira , nyamara uko abihanangiriza , akaba ari ko barushaho kubyamamaza .
41007037	Bagatangara cyane bakavuga bati « Byose yabikoze neza ; atuma ibipfamatwi byumva n’ibiragi bivuga . »
41008001	Muri iyo minsi , hongera kuza imbaga y’abantu badafite ibyo kurya . Yezu ahamagara abigishwa be arababwira ati
41008002	« Iyi mbaga nyifitiye impuhwe , kuko hashize iminsi itatu bankurikiye , kandi bakaba badafite ibyo kurya .
41008003	Nimbasezerera batariye , baragwa mu nzira , kandi muri bo harimo abaturutse kure . »
41008004	Abigishwa be baramusubiza bati « Imigati ihagije aba bantu bangana batya umuntu yayikura he muri ubu butayu ? »
41008005	Arababaza ati « Mufite imigati ingahe ? » Bati « Irindwi . »
41008006	Nuko ategeka rubanda kwicara hasi , maze afata ya migati irindwi , ashimira Imana , arayimanyura , maze ayiha abigishwa be ngo bayibahereze .
41008007	Bayihereza imbaga . Bari bafite n’udufi dukeya ; Yezu ashimira Imana , abategeka kutubahereza na two .
41008008	Nuko bararya barahaga . Hanyuma bakoranya ibisate byasigaye , byuzura inkangara ndwi !
41008009	Ubwo kandi bari nk’ibihumbi bine . Nuko Yezu arabasezerera .
41008010	Aherako ajya mu bwato hamwe n’abigishwa be , agana mu karere ka Dalimanuta .
41008011	Abafarizayi baraza , maze batangira kumwiyenzaho bamusaba ikimenyetso giturutse mu ijuru , byo kumwinja .
41008012	Nuko asuhuza umutima , ati « Kuki abantu b’iki gihe bashaka ikimenyetso ? Ndababwira ukuri , nta kimenyetso abantu b’ubu bateze kubona . »
41008013	Nuko abasiga aho , arongera ajya mu bwato agana ku yindi nkombe y’inyanja .
41008014	Abigishwa bari bibagiwe kujyana imigati , maze bakagira umugati umwe gusa mu bwato .
41008015	Nuko Yezu arabihanangiriza ati « Murabe maso , kandi mwirinde umusemburo w’Abafarizayi n’umusemburo wa Herodi . »
41008016	Bo rero batangira kujya impaka ngo nta migati bafite .
41008017	Yezu abimenye , arababwira ati « Kuki mujya impaka ngo nta migati mufite ? Ntimurumva kandi ntimurasobanukirwa ? Mbese umutima wanyu uracyanangiye ?
41008018	Mufite amaso ntimubone , mukagira n’amatwi ntimwumve ? Kandi ntimwibuka ,
41008019	igihe manyuriye imigati itanu abantu ibihumbi bitanu , mwahakuye inkangara zingahe zuzuye ibisate ? » Baramusubiza bati « Ni cumi n’ebyiri . »
41008020	Arongera ati « N’igihe manyuriye imigati irindwi abantu ibihumbi bine , mwahakuye inkangara zingahe zuzuye ibisate ? » Baramusubiza bati « Ni indwi . »
41008021	Nuko arababwira ati « Na n’ubu ntimurasobanukirwa ? »
41008022	Ngo bagere i Betsayida , abantu bamuzanira impumyi , bamwingingira ko ayikoraho .
41008023	Afata impumyi ukuboko , ayikura mu rusisiro , ayisiga amacandwe ku maso , ayiramburiraho n’ibiganza , maze arayibaza ati « Hari icyo ubona ? »
41008024	Impumyi irambura amaso , iramusubiza iti « Ndabona abantu , barasa n’ibiti , ariko baragenda . »
41008025	Yezu arongera ashyira ibiganza ku maso ye , undi atangira kubona bigaragara , arakira , abona neza ibintu byose uko biri .
41008026	Nuko Yezu amwohereza iwe , amubwira ati « Ntiwinjire no mu rusisiro . »
41008027	Yezu ajyana n’abigishwa be , agana mu nsisiro za Kayizareya ya Filipo . Bakiri mu nzira , abaza abigishwa be ati « Abantu bavuga ko ndi nde ? »
41008028	Baramusubiza bati « Ngo uri Yohani Batisita , abandi ngo uri Eliya ; naho abandi ngo uri umwe mu bahanuzi . »
41008029	Ati « Mwebwe se , muvuga ko ndi nde ? » Petero aramusubiza ati « Uri Kristu . »
41008030	Nuko Yezu arabihanangiriza ngo ntibagire uwo babibwira .
41008031	Nuko atangira kubigisha ko Umwana w’umuntu agomba kuzababara cyane , agacibwa n’abakuru b’imiryango , n’abaherezabitambo bakuru , n’abigishamategeko , akicwa , ariko akazazuka nyuma y’iminsi itatu .
41008032	Ibyo yabibabwiye akomeje . Nuko Petero aramwihugikana , atangira kumutonganya .
41008033	We ariko arahindukira , maze areba abigishwa be , acyaha Petero , amubwira , ati « Hoshi , mva iruhande , Sekibi ! Kuko ibitekerezo byawe bitavuye ku Mana , ahubwo ku bantu ! »
41008034	Nuko ahamagara rubanda hamwe n’abigishwa be , arababwira ati « Niba hari ushaka kunkurikira , yiyibagirwe ubwe , aheke umusaraba we , maze ankurikire !
41008035	Kuko uzashaka gukiza ubugingo bwe azabubura , naho uzahara ubugingo bwe kubera jyewe n’Inkuru Nziza , azabukiza .
41008036	Umuntu watunga iby’isi yose , ariko akabura ubugingo bwe , byaba bimumariye iki ?
41008037	Cyangwa se umuntu yagurana iki ubugingo bwe ?
41008038	Koko rero , umuntu uzanyihakana agahinyura n’amagambo yanjye imbere ya bariya bantu b’abasambanyi kandi b’abanyabyaha , Umwana w’umuntu na we azamwihakana igihe azazira mu ikuzo rya Se , ashagawe n’abamalayika batagatifu . »
41009001	Nuko yungamo ati « Ndababwira ukuri : mu bari hano , harimo abatazapfa batabonye Ingoma y’Imana ije mu bubasha . »
41009002	Hashize iminsi itandatu , Yezu ajyana na Petero , na Yakobo , na Yohani ukwabo mu mpinga y’umusozi muremure . Nuko yihindura ukundi mu maso yabo .
41009003	Imyambaro ye irererana , irabengerana bitambutse kure uburyo umumeshi wo ku isi yashobora kuyeza .
41009004	Ubwo Eliya arababonekera hamwe na Musa , baganira na Yezu .
41009005	Petero ni ko guterura abwira Yezu ati « Mwigisha , kwibera hano nta ko bisa ; reka tuhace ibiraro bitatu , kimwe cyawe , ikindi cya Musa , n’ikindi cya Eliya . »
41009006	Yari yabuze icyo avuga , kuko bari bahiye ubwoba .
41009007	Nuko igicu kirabatwikira , maze muri icyo gicu haturukamo ijwi riti « Uyu ni umwana wanjye nkunda cyane , nimumwumve ! »
41009008	Ako kanya , barebye hirya no hino , ntibagira undi wundi bongera kubona , uretse Yezu wenyine wari kumwe na bo .
41009009	Mu gihe bamanukaga umusozi , Yezu abategeka kutazagira uwo batekerereza ibyo bari bamaze kubona , kugera igihe Umwana w’umuntu azaba amaze kuzuka mu bapfuye .
41009010	Bakomeza kuzirikana iryo jambo , ariko banabazanya bati « Kuzuka mu bapfuye bivuga iki ? »
41009011	Abigishwa babaza Yezu bati « Ni kuki abigishamategeko bavuga ko Eliya ari we ugomba kubanza kuza ? »
41009012	Arabasubiza ati « Koko Eliya azabanza aze atunganye byose . Nyamara se kuki byanditswe ngo Umwana w’umuntu azababazwa ku buryo bwinshi kandi asuzugurwe ?
41009013	Reka rero mbibabwire : Eliya yaraje , kandi bamugiriye uko bishakiye , nk’uko Ibyanditswe bimuvuga . »
41009014	Igihe rero bazaga basanga abigishwa be , babona ikivunge cy’abantu kibakikije n’abigishamategeko bajyaga impaka na bo .
41009015	Rubanda rwose bakimurabukwa , barahomboka , maze biruka bajya kumusuhuza .
41009016	Arababaza ati « Icyo mujyaho impaka na bo ni iki ? »
41009017	Umwe muri rubanda aramusubiza ati « Mwigisha , nakuzaniye umwana wanjye wahanzweho na roho mbi y’ikiragi .
41009018	Iyo imweguye , imutura hasi , maze akazana urufuro , agahekenya amenyo , kandi akagagara . Nasabye abigishwa bawe kuyirukana , ntibabishobora . »
41009019	Arababwira ati « Yemwe bantu b’iki gihe mutemera ! Nzabana namwe kugeza ryari ? Nzabiyumanganya mpereze hehe ? Nimunzanire uwo mwana . »
41009020	Baramumuzanira . Roho mbi ikibona Yezu , icugusa umwana cyane , yikubita hasi , arigaragura azana urufuro .
41009021	Yezu abaza se ati « Hashize igihe kingana iki agirwa atya ? » Se aramusubiza ati « Kuva mu bwana bwe .
41009022	Incuro nyinshi yamuroshye mu muriro no mu mazi kugira ngo imwice ; ariko niba hari icyo ushobora , tubabarire udutabare ! »
41009023	Yezu aramubwira ati « Ngo niba hari icyo ushobora . . . ? Erega byose bishobokera uwemera ! »
41009024	Ako kanya se w’umwana arangurura ijwi ati « Ndemera ! Ariko komeza ukwemera kwanjye guke ! »
41009025	Yezu abonye abantu baza banigana , akabukira roho mbi avuga ati « Wowe roho mbi , umubuza kuvuga no kumva , ndagutegetse : va muri uwo mwana , kandi ntukamugarukemo ukundi . »
41009026	Roho mbi ivuza induru , icugusa umwana cyane , imusohokamo . Nuko uwo mwana amera nk’uwapfuye , ndetse bituma abantu benshi bavuga ngo « Yapfuye ! »
41009027	Naho Yezu amaze kumufata ukuboko , aramuhagurutsa , umwana arahagarara .
41009028	Yezu yinjiye mu nzu , abigishwa be bamubariza ahiherereye bati « Kuki twebwe tutashoboye kuyirukana ? »
41009029	Arabasubiza ati « Buriya bwoko bwa roho mbi , nta kindi gishobora kubwirukana , usibye isengesho . »
41009030	Bavuye aho ngaho , bambukiranya Galileya , ariko Yezu ntiyashakaga ko babimenya .
41009031	Yigishaga abigishwa be , ababwira ati « Umwana w’umuntu agiye gushyirwa mu maboko y’abantu , bakazamwica , ariko yamara gupfa , akazazuka ku munsi wa gatatu . »
41009032	Iryo jambo ariko ntibaryumva , batinya no kumubaza .
41009033	Nuko bagera i Kafarinawumu . Bari mu nzu , Yezu arababaza ati « Mu nzira mwajyaga impaka z’iki ? »
41009034	Baraceceka , kuko mu nzira bari bagiye impaka zo kumenya umukuru muri bo .
41009035	Amaze kwicara , ahamagara ba Cumi na babiri , arababwira ati « Ushaka kuba uwa mbere , azigire uwa nyuma muri bose , abe n’umugaragu wa bose . »
41009036	Nuko afata umwana , amuhagarika hagati yabo , aramuhobera , arababwira ati
41009037	« Umuntu wese wakira umwana nk’uyu nguyu , ari jye abigirira , ni jye aba yakiriye . Kandi unyakira wese , si jyewe aba yakiriye , ahubwo aba yakiriye Uwantumye . »
41009038	Yohani aramubwira ati « Mwigisha , twabonye umuntu wirukana roho mbi mu izina ryawe kandi atadukurikira ; turabimubuza kuko atadukurikira . »
41009039	Yezu ati « Mwibimubuza , kuko nta muntu ushobora gukora igitangaza mu izina ryanjye , maze ngo ahindukire amvuge nabi .
41009040	Utaturwanya wese ari kumwe natwe .
41009041	Umuntu wese uzabaha ikirahuri cy’amazi yo kunywa abitewe n’uko muri aba Kristu , ndababwira ukuri , ntazabura igihembo cye .
41009042	Ariko nihagira ugusha mu cyaha umwe muri aba bato bemera , ikimukwiye ni uko bamuhambira ku ijosi urusyo rusheshwa n’indogobe , bakamuroha mu nyanja .
41009043	Niba ikiganza cyawe kigutera gukora icyaha , ugice , kuko ikiruta ari ukwinjirana akanimfu mu bugingo ,
41009044	aho kujyana ibiganza byawe byombi mu nyenga y’umuriro utazima .
41009045	Niba ikirenge cyawe kigutera gukora icyaha , ugice , kuko ikiruta ari ukwinjira mu bugingo ucumbagira ,
41009046	aho kurohwa mu nyenga ufite ibirenge byawe byombi .
41009047	Niba ijisho ryawe rigutera gukora icyaha , rinoboremo ; kuko ikiruta ari uko wakwinjirana rimwe mu Ngoma y’Imana , aho kwinjirana yombi mu nyenga ,
41009048	aho urunyo rudapfa , n’umuriro ntuzime .
41009049	Ahubwo buri wese ajye asukurwa n’umunyu n’umuriro .
41009050	Umunyu ufite akamaro ; ariko iyo ukayutse ; mwawusubiza mute uburyohe bwawo ? Nimwigiremo umunyu kandi mubane mu mahoro . »
41010001	Nuko Yezu ava aho ngaho , ajya mu ntara ya Yudeya yo hakurya ya Yorudani . Abantu benshi bongera gukoranira iruhande rwe , nuko abigisha uko bisanzwe .
41010002	Abafarizayi baramwegera , maze bamubaza niba umugabo afite uruhushya rwo gusenda umugore we , ariko bamwinja .
41010003	Arababwira ati « Musa yabategetse iki ? »
41010004	Baramusubiza bati « Musa yemereye umugabo kwandika icyemezo cyo gusenda umugore , akabona kumusezerera . »
41010005	Yezu arababwira ati « Icyamuteye kwandika iryo tegeko , ni uko umutima wanyu unangiye .
41010006	Naho mu ntangiriro y’isi , ’ Imana yaremye umugabo n’umugore ;
41010007	ni yo mpamvu umugabo azasiga se na nyina , akifatanya n’umugore we ,
41010008	maze bombi bakaba umubiri umwe . ’ Bityo ntibaba bakiri babiri , ahubwo baba ari umubiri umwe .
41010009	Nuko rero ntihakagire umuntu utandukanya icyo Imana yafatanyije . »
41010010	Basubiye imuhira , abigishwa bongera kumusobanuza ibyerekeye iyo ngingo .
41010011	Arababwira ati « Koko umugabo usenda umugore we akazana undi aba asambana ;
41010012	umugore na we utandukana n’umugabo we agacyurwa n’undi , aba asambana . »
41010013	Nuko bamuzanira abana bato ngo abakoreho , maze abigishwa barabakabukira .
41010014	Yezu abibonye ararakara , maze arababwira ati « Nimureke abana bansange , mwibabuza , kuko Ingoma y’Imana ari iy’abameze nka bo .
41010015	Ndababwira ukuri : umuntu wese utazakira Ingoma y’Imana nk’umwana , ntazayinjiramo bibaho . »
41010016	Nuko arabahobera , abasabira umugisha abashyizeho ibiganza .
41010017	Yezu agihaguruka aho , umuntu aza yiruka amupfukama imbere , aramubaza ati « Mwigisha mwiza , nkore iki kugira ngo nzabone ubugingo bw’iteka ho umurage ? »
41010018	Yezu aramubwira ati « Kuki unyita mwiza ? Nta mwiza ubaho , keretse Imana yonyine .
41010019	Uzi amategeko : ntuzice , ntuzasambane , ntuzibe , ntuzahamye ibinyoma , ntuzagirire abandi nabi , urajye wubaha so na nyoko . »
41010020	Uwo muntu aramusubiza ati « Mwigisha , ibyo byose nabikurikije kuva mu buto bwanjye . »
41010021	Yezu aramwitegereza yumva amukunze ; aramubwira ati « Ubuze ikintu kimwe gusa : genda ugurishe ibyo utunze , ubihe abakene , uzagira ubukire mu ijuru , hanyuma uze unkurikire . »
41010022	We ariko abyumvise arasuherwa , agenda ababaye , kuko yari atunze ibintu byinshi .
41010023	Nuko Yezu araranganya amaso , abwira abigishwa be ati « Mbega ukuntu kuzinjira mu Ngoma y’Imana biruhije ku bakungu ! »
41010024	Abigishwa batangazwa n’ayo magambo ; Yezu ariko abibasubiriramo ati « Bana banjye , mbega ukuntu biruhije kwinjira mu Ngoma y’Imana .
41010025	Byoroheye ingamiya guca mu mwenge w’urushinge , kurusha uko byoroheye umukungu kwinjira mu Ngoma y’Imana ! »
41010026	Abigishwa barushaho gutangara , barabazanya bati « Ubwo se ni nde ushobora kurokoka ? »
41010027	Yezu arabitegereza , maze arababwira ati « Ku bantu ntibishoboka , ariko ku Mana birashoboka , kuko nta kinanira Imana . »
41010028	Nuko Petero araterura , aramubwira ati « Dore twebwe twasize byose turagukurikira . »
41010029	Yezu arasubiza ati « Ndababwira ukuri , nta we uzaba yarasize urugo , cyangwa abavandimwe be , cyangwa bashiki be , cyangwa nyina , cyangwa se , cyangwa abana , cyangwa isambu ye , ari jye abigirira n’Inkuru Nziza ,
41010030	ngo abure kwiturwa karijana muri iki gihe , ari amazu , ari abavandimwe , ari na bashiki be , na ba nyina , n’abana n’amasambu , ariko n’ibitotezo bitabuze , kandi no mu gihe kizaza , akaziturwa ubugingo bw’iteka .
41010031	Benshi mu ba mbere bazaba aba nyuma , n’aba nyuma babe aba mbere . »
41010032	Ubwo bari mu nzira bazamuka bajya i Yeruzalemu , Yezu abarangaje imbere . Bari bahagaritse umutima , n’abari babakurikiye bari bafite ubwoba . Yongera kwihererana ba Cumi na babiri iruhande rwe , ababwira ibigiye kumubaho ati
41010033	« Dore tuzamutse tujya i Yeruzalemu , kandi Umwana w’umuntu agiye kugabizwa abatware b’abaherezabitambo n’abigishamategeko ; bazamucira urubanza rwo gupfa , maze bamugabize abanyamahanga .
41010034	Bazamushinyagurira , bamuvunderezeho amacandwe , bamukubite , bamwice , ariko nyuma y’iminsi itatu azuke . »
41010035	Nuko Yakobo na Yohani , bene Zebedeyi , begera Yezu , baramubwira bati « Mwigisha , turashaka ko udukorera icyo tugiye kugusaba . »
41010036	Arababaza ati « Murashaka ko mbakorera iki ? »
41010037	Baramusubiza bati « Uraduhe kuzicarana nawe , umwe iburyo , undi ibumoso mu ikuzo ryawe . »
41010038	Yezu arababwira ati « Ntimuzi icyo musaba . Mushobora se kunywera ku nkongoro nzanyweraho , cyangwa se guhabwa batisimu nzahabwa ? »
41010039	Baramusubiza bati « Turabishobora ! » Yezu arababwira ati « Koko inkongoro nzanyweraho muzayinywesha , na batisimu nzahabwa muzayihabwa ;
41010040	naho ibyo kwicara iburyo bwanjye cyangwa ibumoso bwanjye , si jye ubitanga ; bizahabwa ababigenewe . »
41010041	Abandi uko ari icumi babyumvise , batangira kurakarira Yakobo na Yohani .
41010042	Yezu arabahamagara , arababwira ati « Muzi ko abahawe kugenga amahanga , bayagenga uko bashatse , kandi ko abatware bayo bayategekesha agahato .
41010043	Kuri mwebwe rero si ko bimeze . Ahubwo ushaka kuba mukuru muri mwe , ajye yigira umugaragu wanyu ,
41010044	maze ushaka kuba uwa mbere , yihindure umucakara wa bose .
41010045	Dore n’Umwana w’umuntu ntiyazanywe no gukorerwa , ahubwo yazanywe no gukorera abandi , no gutanga ubugingo bwe ngo bube incungu ya benshi . »
41010046	Nuko bagera i Yeriko . Igihe agisohoka muri Yeriko , ari kumwe n’abigishwa be n’imbaga y’abantu benshi , umuntu w’impumyi witwaga Baritimeyo , mwene Timeyo , akaba yari yicaye iruhande rw’inzira asabiriza .
41010047	Yumvise ko ari Yezu w’i Nazareti , atera hejuru ati « Yezu , Mwana wa Dawudi , mbabarira ! »
41010048	Benshi baramucyaha ngo aceceke , ariko we arushaho gusakuza ati « Mwana wa Dawudi , mbabarira ! »
41010049	Yezu arahagarara , aravuga ati « Nimumuhamagare . » Bahamagara iyo mpumyi , barayibwira bati « Humura , haguruka , dore araguhamagaye . »
41010050	Ajugunya igishura cye , ahaguruka bwangu , asanga Yezu .
41010051	Yezu aramubaza ati « Urashaka ko ngukorera iki ? » Impumyi iramusubiza iti « Mwigisha , mpa kubona ! »
41010052	Yezu aramubwira ati « Genda , ukwemera kwawe kuragukijije . » Ako kanya arahumuka , maze akurikira Yezu .
41011001	Bagiye kugera i Yeruzalemu , ahagana i Betifage n’i Betaniya , hafi y’umusozi w’Imizeti , Yezu yohereza babiri mu bigishwa be ,
41011002	arababwira ati « Nimujye mu ngo ziri imbere yanyu ; mukihagera murabona icyana cy’indogobe kiziritse , kitigeze kigira uwo giheka , mukiziture , maze mukinzanire .
41011003	Nihagira ubabwira ati ’ Ibyo mukora ni ibiki ? ’ musubize muti ’ Umwigisha aragikeneye , kandi aracyohereza vuba . ’ »
41011004	Baragenda , basanga icyana cy’indogobe kiziritse ku irembo iruhande rw’inzira , barakizitura .
41011005	Bamwe mu bari aho ngaho barababwira bati « Ibyo mukora ni ibiki ? Kuki muzitura iyo ndogobe ? »
41011006	Bo babasubiza uko Yezu yari yababwiye , nuko barabihorera .
41011007	Icyana cy’indogobe bakizanira Yezu , bagisasaho ibishura byabo , acyicaraho .
41011008	Nuko abantu benshi basasa ibishura byabo mu nzira ; abandi basasa amashami bari batemye mu mirima .
41011009	Abamugendaga imbere n’abari bamukurikiye barangurura ijwi bati « Hozana ! Hasingizwe Uje mu izina rya Nyagasani !
41011010	Hasingizwe Ingoma y’umubyeyi wacu Dawudi itugezeho ! Hozana , Imana nihabwe impundu mu ijuru ! »
41011011	Nuko Yezu agera i Yeruzalemu , yinjira mu Ngoro y’Imana . Amaze kwitegereza byose hirya no hino , umugoroba ukubye , arasohoka , ajyana na ba Cumi na babiri i Betaniya .
41011012	Bukeye , bahagurutse i Betaniya , Yezu aza gusonza .
41011013	Akiri kure , arabukwa igiti cy’umutini gifite amababi , ajya kureba ko hari imbuto yakibonaho , acyegereye , asanga ni ibibabi bisa , kuko kitari igihe cyacyo cyo kwera .
41011014	Abwira icyo giti ati « Ntihakagire umuntu urya imbuto zawe ukundi ! » Ubwo abigishwa be baramwumvaga .
41011015	Baragenda , bagera i Yeruzalemu . Yezu yinjira mu Ngoro y’Imana , atangira kwirukana abacuruzi n’abaguzi bari mu Ngoro ; ahirika ameza y’abavunjaga amafaranga , n’intebe z’abacuruzaga inuma ,
41011016	kandi abuza abikoreraga imitwaro kwahuranya ikibuga cy’Ingoro .
41011017	Nuko abigisha ababwira ati « Mbese ntihanditswe ngo : Inzu yanjye izitwa inzu yo gusengerwamo n’amahanga yose , naho mwebwe mwayigize ubuvumo bw’abambuzi ! »
41011018	Abatware b’abaherezabitambo n’abigishamategeko ngo babimenye , bashaka ukuntu bamwicisha , ariko bakamutinya , kuko rubanda rwatangariraga inyigisho ze .
41011019	Bugorobye , Yezu n’abigishwa be bava mu mugi .
41011020	Mu gitondo bahita , babona wa mutini wumye kugeza mu mizi .
41011021	Petero yibuka ibyabaye , maze abwira Yezu ati « Mwigisha , cya giti wavumye , dore cyumye cyose ! »
41011022	Yezu aramusubiza ati « Nimwemere Imana !
41011023	Ndababwira nkomeje ko uwizera Imana ashobora kubwira uriya musozi ati ’ Shyiguka aho wirohe mu nyanja ’ , niyizera adashidikanya ko ibyo avuze biba , bizaba .
41011024	Ni cyo gituma mbabwira nti ’ Icyo musabye cyose musenga , mwizere ko mugihawe , kandi muzagihabwa . ’
41011025	Kandi igihe muhagaze musenga , mujye mubabarira uwo mwaba mufitanye akantu , kugira ngo namwe So wo mu ijuru abababarire ibicumuro byanyu .
41011026	Naho nimutababarira abandi , na So wo mu ijuru ntazabababarira ibicumuro byanyu . »
41011027	Barongera bagaruka i Yeruzalemu . Ubwo Yezu yagendagendaga mu Ngoro y’Imana , abaherezabitambo bakuru , abigishamategeko n’abakuru b’imiryango baramwegera ,
41011028	baramubwira bati « Ibyo ubikoresha bubasha ki ? Ni nde waguhaye ubwo bubasha ? »

41011030	Batisimu ya Yohani yaturutse mu ijuru cyangwa ku bantu ? Nimunsubize ! »
41011031	Naho bo baribwira bati « Nituvuga ko yaturutse mu ijuru , aratubwira ati ’ Mwabujijwe n’iki kumwemera ? ’
41011032	Nituramuka tuvuze ko yaturutse ku bantu , bizatugendekera bite ? » Koko rero batinyaga rubanda , kuko bose bahamyaga ko Yohani ari umuhanuzi nyawe .

41012001	Nuko Yezu atangira kubabwira mu migani , avuga ati « Umuntu yateye imizabibu mu murima we , ayikikizaho uruzitiro , acukuramo urwengero , yubakamo n’umunara w’abararirizi , awatira abahinzi , maze yigira mu rugendo .
41012002	Igihe cy’isarura kigeze , yohereza umugaragu kuri ba bahinzi , ngo bamumuhere ku mbuto z’imizabibu .
41012003	Ariko bo basumira uwo mugaragu , baramuhondagura , bamwohereza amara masa .
41012004	Arongera abatumaho undi mugaragu , uwo na we bamurema uruguma mu mutwe , baramutukagura .
41012005	Nuko yoherezayo undi , we baramwica . Nyuma yohereza n’abandi benshi , bamwe barabakubita , abandi barabica . Ibuye ryajugunywe n’abubatsi , ni ryo ryabaye insanganyarukuta .
41012006	Hari hasigaye umwana we yakundaga , nyuma aba ari we abatumaho , yibwira ati ’ Umwana wanjye we nta cyo bazamutwara . ’
41012007	Ariko abahinzi bamubonye , barabwirana bati ’ Dore uzamuzungura ; nimuze tumwice , maze tuzazungure ibye . ’
41012008	Nuko baramufata baramwica , bamujugunya inyuma y’umurima w’imizabibu .
41012009	Mbese mubona nyir’imizabibu azakora iki ? Azaza , arimbure abo bahinzi , maze imizabibu ayishinge abandi .
41012010	Ntimwasomye se mu Byanditswe ngo Ibuye ryajugunywe n’abubatsi , ni ryo ryabaye insanganyarukuta .
41012011	Ngicyo icyo Nyagasani yakoze , kikaba kibaye igitangaza mu maso yacu . ’ »
41012012	Bashaka uko bafata Yezu , ariko batinya rubanda . Bari bumvise neza ko ari bo yavugaga muri uwo mugani . Nuko bamusiga aho , barigendera .
41012013	Hanyuma bamwoherereza bamwe mu Bafarizayi no mu Baherodiyani , kugira ngo bamufatire ku byo avuga .
41012014	Baraza baramubwira bati « Mwigisha , tuzi ko uvuga ukuri nta cyo wikanga , kuko udatinya amaso y’abantu , ahubwo wigisha inzira y’Imana mu kuri . Ese gutanga umusoro wa Kayizari biremewe , cyangwa se ntibyemewe ? Tujye tuwutanga cyangwa se twoye kuwutanga ? »
41012015	Ariko Yezu kuko yari azi uburyarya bwabo , arababwira ati « Kuki muntega iyo mitego ? Nimunzanire igiceri ndebe ! »
41012016	Barakimuzanira . Yezu arababaza ati « Iri shusho n’iri zina biriho ni ibya nde ? » Barasubiza bati « Ni ibya Kayizari . »
41012017	Yezu ni ko kubabwira ati « Ibya Kayizari mubisubize Kayizari , n’iby’Imana mubisubize Imana ! » Ngo avuge atyo , baramutangarira cyane .
41012018	Nuko Abasaduseyi baza bamugana , ba bandi bavuga ko kuzuka bitabaho . Baramubaza bati
41012019	« Mwigisha , dore Musa yatwandikiye iri tegeko ngo ’ Umuntu napfa asize umugore batabyaranye , umuvandimwe we agomba gucyura uwo mugore , kugira ngo acikure nyakwigendera . ’
41012020	Habayeho rero abavandimwe barindwi , uwa mbere ashaka umugore maze apfa batabyaranye .
41012021	Uwa kabiri acyura wa mupfakazi , na we apfa batabyaranye . N’uwa gatatu bigenda gutyo .
41012022	Bose uko ari barindwi bapfa badasize imbuto . Amaherezo wa mugore na we arapfa .
41012023	Igihe cy’izuka , nibamara kuzuka , mbese uwo mugore azaba uwa nde muri bo , ko bose uko ari barindwi bazaba baramutunze ? »
41012024	Yezu arabasubiza ati « Aho ntimwayobejwe no kutamenya Ibyanditswe , mukirengagiza n’ububasha bw’Imana ?
41012025	Erega igihe abapfuye bazazuka , nta we uzagira umugore , nta n’uzagira umugabo , ahubwo bazamera nk’abamalayika bo mu ijuru .
41012026	Naho ku byerekeye ko abapfuye bazazuka , nta bwo mwasomye mu gitabo cya Musa , uko Imana yamubwiriye muri cya gihuru kigurumana , iti ’ Ndi Imana ya Abrahamu , Imana ya Izaki , n’Imana ya Yakobo ? ’ »

41012028	Umwe mu bigishamategeko wari wumvise bajya impaka , abonye ko Yezu abashubije neza , aramwegera aramubaza ati « Itegeko riruta ayandi ni irihe ? »
41012029	Yezu aramusubiza ati « Irya mbere ni iri ngiri : Tega amatwi Israheli , Nyagasani Imana yacu ni We Nyagasani umwe rukumbi :
41012030	Urajye ukunda Nyagasani Imana yawe n’umutima wawe wose , n’amagara yawe yose , n’ubwenge bwawe bwose , n’imbaraga zawe zose .
