41012033	Kandi kuyikunda n’umutima wawe wose , n’ubwenge bwawe bwose , n’imbaraga zawe zose , ugakunda mugenzi wawe nk’uko wikunda , ibyo biruta ibitambo n’amaturo byose . »
41012034	Yezu yumvise ko amushubije neza , aramubwira ati « Nta bwo uri kure y’Ingoma y’Imana . » Nuko ntihagira utinyuka kongera kugira icyo amubaza .
41012035	Igihe Yezu yigishirizaga mu Ngoro y’Imana , araterura ati « Ni iki gituma abigishamategeko bavuga ko Kristu ari Mwene Dawudi ?
41012036	Kandi Dawudi ubwe yaravuze ati ‘ Nyagasani yabwiye Umutegetsi wanjye ati ’ Icara iburyo bwanjye , kugeza igihe abanzi bawe mbahindura imisego y’ibirenge byawe ’ .
41012037	Uwo Dawudi yita Umutegetsi , yaba umwana we ate ? » Abantu benshi bamwumvanaga umunerezo .
41012038	Mu nyigisho ze Yezu akavuga ati « Murajye mwirinda abigishamategeko , bakunda gutembera bambaye amakanzu maremare , no kuramukirizwa mu materaniro .
41012039	Bakunda kandi guhabwa intebe z’icyubahiro mu masengero n’imyanya y’imbere aho batumiwe .
41012040	Icyabo ni ukurya ingo z’abapfakazi , maze bakiha kuvuga amasengesho y’urudaca . Abo bazacirwa urubanza rukaze kurusha abandi . »
41012041	Yezu yari yicaye mu Ngoro y’Imana , ahateganye n’ububiko ba shyiragamo amaturo , yitegereza uko rubanda batura . Abakungu benshi bashyiragamo byinshi .
41012042	Maze haza umupfakazi w’umukene , ashyiramo uduceri tubiri .
41012043	Yezu ahamagara abigishwa be , arababwira ati « Ndababwira ukuri : Uriya mupfakazi w’umukene yarushije abandi bose gutura .
41012044	Kuko bariya bose bashyizemo ku by’ikirenga , naho we yashyizemo ibyari bimutunze byose . »
41013001	Yezu asohotse mu Ngoro , umwe mu bigishwa be aramubwira ati « Mwigisha , irebere nawe : mbega amabuye manini ! Mbega amazu meza ! »
41013002	Yezu aramubwira ati « Ntureba ariya mazu ukuntu asa ? Nkubwiye ko nta buye rizasigara rigeretse ku rindi , yose azasenyuka . »
41013003	Nuko igihe yari yicaye ku musozi w’Imizeti , ahateganye n’Ingoro , Petero na Yakobo na Yohani na Andereya bamubaza biherereye bati
41013004	« Tubwire igihe ibyo bizabera , n’ikimenyetso kizereka abantu ko ibyo byose bigiye gushira . »
41013005	Yezu ni ko guterura ati « Muramenye ntihazagire ubayobya ,
41013006	kuko hazaza benshi biyitirira izina ryanjye , bavuga bati ’ Ni jye Kristu ’ , maze bayobye abantu benshi .
41013007	Nimwumva bavuga intambara cyangwa impuha zayo , ntimuzakuke umutima . Ibyo bigomba kuba , ariko ntibizaba ari byo herezo .
41013008	Igihugu kizahagurukira ikindi , ingoma ishyamirane n’indi , kandi hamwe hazaba imitingito y’isi , ahandi hatere inzara . Bizamera nk’intangiriro y’ububabare bw’umugore wenda kubyara .
41013009	Namwe ubwanyu , muramenye ! Bazabagabiza inkiko , mukubitirwe mu masengero . Bazabahagarika imbere y’abami n’abandi bategetsi , ari jye babaziza , bityo muzambere abagabo imbere yabo .
41013010	Icyakora , Inkuru Nziza izabanza yogezwe mu mahanga yose .
41013011	Maze igihe bazaba babajyanye kubatanga , ntimuzabunze imitima mwibaza icyo muzavuga . Muzavuge ikibajemo muri uwo mwanya , kuko atari mwe muzaba muvuga , ahubwo azaba ari Roho Mutagatifu ubavugiramo .
41013012	Umuvandimwe azicisha umuvandimwe we , umubyeyi yicishe umwana we , abana na bo bazahinduka ababyeyi babicishe .
41013013	Kandi muzangwa n’abantu bose , muzira izina ryanjye ; ariko uzakomera kugeza ku ndunduro , uwo nguwo azarokorwa .
41013014	Nimubona ’ ishyano ry’icyorezo ’ riri aho ritagomba kuba — usoma abyumve neza ! — icyo gihe abazaba bari muri Yudeya bazahungire mu misozi ;
41013015	uzaba ari hejuru y’inzu , ntazamanuke ku nzu ye ngo yinjiremo , maze agire icyo avanamo ;
41013016	kandi uzaba ari mu murima ntazahindukire ngo ajye gushaka igishura cye imuhira .
41013017	Hagowe abazaba batwite n’abazaba bonsa muri iyo minsi !
41013018	Nimusabe kugira ngo ibyo byose bitazaba ari mu itumba .
41013019	Kuko muri iyo minsi hazaba amakuba atigeze abaho , kuva mu ntangiriro Imana irema isi kugeza ubu ngubu , kandi nta n’ubwo azongera kubaho .

41013025	inyenyeri zizahanuka ku ijuru , maze ibikomeye byo mu ijuru bihungabane .
41013026	Ni bwo bazabona Umwana w’umuntu aje mu bicu , afite ububasha bukomeye n’ikuzo ryinshi .
41013027	Ubwo rero azohereza abamalayika mu mpande enye z’isi , aho isi iherera kugeza ku mpera y’ijuru , maze akoranye intore ze .
41013028	Nimugereranye muhereye ku giti cy’umutini maze mwumve : iyo amashami yacyo amaze gutoha akameraho amababi , mumenyeraho ko igihe cy’imbuto cyegereje .

41013030	Ndababwira ukuri , iki gisekuru ntikizahita ibyo byose bitabaye .
41013031	Ijuru n’isi bizashira , ariko amagambo yanjye nta bwo azashira .
41013032	Nyamara uwo munsi cyangwa iyo saha , nta we ubizi , habe n’abamalayika bo mu ijuru , habe ndetse na Mwana ; bizwi n’Imana Data wenyine .
41013033	Mwitonde , mube maso , kuko mutazi igihe bizabera .
41013034	Bizaba bimeze nk’umuntu wagiye mu rugendo , agashinga abagaragu be urugo rwe , akagenera buri wese umurimo we , naho umunyarugi akamutegeka kuba maso .
41013035	Murabe maso rero kuko mutazi igihe nyir’urugo azazira , ari ku mugoroba , ari mu gicuku , ari mu nkoko , cyangwa mu gitondo ,
41013036	kugira ngo atazaza abatunguye , agasanga musinziriye .
41013037	Ibyo mbabwiye , mbibwiye n’abandi bose : Murabe maso ! »
41014001	Hari hasigaye iminsi ibiri ngo Pasika ibe , n’umunsi mukuru w’imigati idasembuye . Nuko abatware b’abaherezabitambo n’abigishamategeko bashaka gufata Yezu ku mayeri ngo bamwice .

41014010	Nuko Yuda Isikariyoti , umwe muri ba Cumi na babiri , asanga abatware b’abaherezabitambo bakuru , agira ngo azamubagabize .

41016019	Nuko Nyagasani Yezu amaze kubabwira atyo , ajyanwa mu ijuru , maze yicara iburyo bw’Imana .

42001002	mbese nk’uko twabigejejweho n’ababyiboneye kuva mu ntangiriro , ari na bo bari bashinzwe kwamamaza ijambo ry’Imana ,
42001003	nanjye , maze kubaririza neza uko byagenze kuva bigitangira , niyemeje , nyakubahwa Tewofili , kukwandikira ayo mateka nyakurikiranyije ,
42001004	ngo umenye nyakuri ukuntu inyigisho washyikirijwe zihamye .
42001005	Ku ngoma ya Herodi , umwami wa Yudeya , hari umuherezabitambo wo mu cyiciro cya Abiya , akitwa Zakariya , n’umugore we akaba uwo mu muryango wa Aroni , akitwa Elizabeti .
42001006	Bombi bari intungane imbere y’Imana , bagakurikiza badatezuka amategeko n’amabwiriza yose ya Nyagasani .
42001007	Ariko nta mwana bari bafite , kuko Elizabeti yari ingumba ; byongeye bombi bari bageze mu zabukuru .
42001008	Igihe rero Zakariya yariho akora imihango y’ubuherezabitambo imbere y’Imana , mu mwanya ugenewe icyiciro cye ,
42001009	nk’uko abaherezabitambo babigenzaga , ubufindo buramufata ngo ajye gutwika ububani mu Ngoro ya Nyagasani .
42001010	Rubanda rwose rwasengeraga hanze igihe cyo gutwika ububani .
42001011	Nuko Umumalayika wa Nyagasani amubonekera ahagaze iburyo bw’urutambiro rw’ububani .
42001012	Zakariya amubonye arikanga , ubwoba buramutaha .
42001013	Ariko Malayika aramubwira ati « Wigira ubwoba , Zakariya , kuko isengesho ryawe ryashimwe : umugore wawe Elizabeti azakubyarira umuhungu , maze ukazamwita Yohani .
42001014	Azagutera ibyishimo n’umunezero , kandi benshi bazashimishwa n’ivuka rye ,
42001015	kuko azaba umuntu ukomeye mu maso ya Nyagasani . Ntazanywa divayi n’icyitwa inzoga cyose , kandi azuzura Roho Mutagatifu akiri mu nda ya nyina .
42001016	Azagarura abana benshi ba Israheli kuri Nyagasani , Imana yabo ,
42001017	kandi azagenda imbere y’Imana arangwa n’umutima n’ubushobozi nka Eliya , agira ngo yunge ababyeyi n’abana babo , no kugira ngo ab’ibigande abagire intungane , maze ategurire atyo Nyagasani umuryango umutunganiye . »
42001018	Nuko Zakariya abwira Malayika , ati « Nzabibwirwa n’iki , ko ndi umusaza , n’umugore wanjye akaba ageze mu zabukuru ? »
42001019	Malayika aramusubiza ati « Ndi Gaburiyeli uhora imbere y’Imana ; natumwe kukubwira no kukugezaho iyo nkuru nziza .
42001020	Nyamara guhera ubu ngubu ugiye kuba ikiragi ; ntuzongera kuvuga kugeza ku munsi ibyo bizaberaho , kuko utemeye ibyo nakubwiye bizagaragara igihe cyabyo kigeze . »
42001021	Ubwo rubanda rwari rutegereje Zakariya , rutangazwa n’uko yatinze mu Ngoro .
42001022	Aho asohokeye , ntiyari agishobora kuvuga , maze bamenya ko yabonekerewe mu Ngoro . Nuko aba uwo kubacira amarenga , akomeza kuba ikiragi .
42001023	Iminsi y’imihango y’ubuherezabitambo irangiye arataha .
42001024	Hashize iminsi , umugore we Elizabeti arasama , amara amezi atanu atajya ahagaragara , avuga ati
42001025	« Dore ibyo Nyagasani yangiriye , yarangobotse ankiza icyankozaga isoni mu bantu . »
42001026	Hahise amezi atandatu , Malayika Gaburiyeli atumwa n’Imana , mu mugi wo mu Galileya witwa Nazareti ,
42001027	ku mukobwa w’isugi wari warasabwe n’umusore witwa Yozefu , wo mu muryango wa Dawudi ; uwo mukobwa yitwaga Mariya .
42001028	Malayika aza iwabo , aramubwira ati « Ndakuramutsa , mutoni w’Imana ; Nyagasani ari kumwe nawe . »
42001029	Yumvise ayo magambo , arikanga , yibaza icyo iyo ndamutso ivuga .
42001030	Malayika aramubwira ati « Wigira ubwoba , Mariya , kuko wagize ubutoni ku Mana .
42001031	Dore ugiye gusama inda , ukazabyara umuhungu , maze ukazamwita izina rya Yezu .
42001032	Azaba umuntu ukomeye , kandi bazamwita Mwene Nyir’ijuru . Nyagasani Imana azamwegurira ingoma ya se Dawudi ;
42001033	azategeka umuryango wa Yakobo ubuziraherezo , ingoma ye ntizashira . »
42001034	Nuko Mariya abwira Malayika , ati « Ibyo bizashoboka bite , kandi nta mugabo mfite ? »
42001035	Malayika aramusubiza ati « Roho Mutagatifu azakumanukiraho , maze ububasha bwa Nyir’ijuru bukubundikire mu gicucu cye , ndetse ugiye kuvuka azaba intungane , kandi azitwa Umwana w’Imana .
42001036	Dore Elizabeti mwene wanyu , na we yasamiye mu zabukuru ; uku kwezi ni ukwa gatandatu , kandi ubundi yitwaga ingumba ,
42001037	koko nta kinanira Imana . »
42001038	Mariya aravuga ati « Ndi umuja wa Nyagasani ; byose bimbeho nk’uko ubivuze . » Nuko Malayika amusiga aho aragenda .
42001039	Muri iyo minsi , Mariya yarahagurutse agenda yihuta , ajya mu misozi miremire , mu mugi wa Yuda ,
42001040	agera kwa Zakariya , aramutsa Elizabeti .
42001041	Nuko Elizabeti yumvise indamutso ya Mariya , umwana atwite yisimbiza mu nda , maze Elizabeti yuzura Roho Mutagatifu .
42001042	Arangurura ijwi ati « Wahebuje abagore bose umugisha , n’Umwana utwite arasingizwa .
42001043	Mbikesha iki kugira ngo nyina w’Umutegetsi wanjye angenderere ?

42001045	Urahirwa , wowe wemeye ko ibyo watumweho na Nyagasani bizaba . »
42001046	Nuko Mariya na we aravuga ati
42001047	« Umutima wanjye urasingiza Nyagasani , kandi uhimbajwe n’Imana Umukiza wanjye .
42001048	Kuko yibutse umuja we utavugwaga ; rwose , kuva ubu amasekuruza yose azanyita umuhire .
42001049	Ushoborabyose yankoreye ibitangaza , Izina rye ni ritagatifu .
42001050	Impuhwe ze zisesekarizwa abamutinya , bo mu bihe byose .
42001051	Yagaragaje ububasha bw’amaboko ye , atatanya abantu birata ;
42001052	yahanantuye abakomeye abakura ku ntebe zabo , maze akuza ab’intamenyekana ;
42001053	abashonje yabagwirije ibintu , abakungu abasezerera amara masa ;
42001054	yagobotse Israheli umugaragu we , bityo yibuka impuhwe ze ,
42001055	nk’uko yari yarabibwiye abakurambere bacu , abigirira Abrahamu n’urubyaro rwe iteka . »
42001056	Mariya yamaranye na Elizabeti nk’amezi atatu , abona gutaha .
42001057	Nuko Elizabeti ageze igihe cyo kubyara , abyara umwana w’umuhungu .
42001058	Abaturanyi na bene wabo , bumvise ko Nyagasani yamugiriye ubuntu , bafatanya na we kwishima .
42001059	Ku munsi wa munani , baza kugenya umwana , bashaka kumwita Zakariya nka se .
42001060	Ariko nyina aravuga ati « Oya , aritwa Yohani . »
42001061	Baramubwira bati « Nta muntu wo mu muryango wanyu wigeze kwitwa iryo zina ! »
42001062	Nuko babaza se mu marenga uko yifuza kwita umwana .
42001063	Zakariya yaka akabaho , maze yandikaho aya magambo : « Izina rye ni Yohani . » Bose baratangara .
42001064	Ako kanya umunwa we urabumbuka , n’ururimi rwe ruragobodoka , maze atangira kuvuga , asingiza Imana .
42001065	Nuko ubwoba butaha abaturanyi babo bose , n’abo mu misozi yo mu Yudeya , bakwiza hose ibyabaye .
42001066	Ababyumvaga bose bakomezaga kubizirikana mu mitima , bibaza bati « Uyu mwana azamera ate , ko ububasha bwa Nyagasani buri kumwe na we ? »
42001067	Nuko se Zakariya yuzura Roho Mutagatifu , ahanura avuga ati
42001068	« Nihasingizwe Nyagasani , Imana ya Israheli , kuko yasuye umuryango we kandi akawukiza .
42001069	Yatugoboreye ububasha budukiza mu nzu ya Dawudi umugaragu we ,
42001070	nk’uko abahanuzi be batagatifu bari barabitumenyesheje kuva kera
42001071	ko azadukiza abanzi bacu , akatugobotora mu nzara z’abatwanga bose .

42001073	ya ndahiro yarahiye Abrahamu umubyeyi wacu ,
42001074	avuga ko namara kutugobotora mu maboko y’abanzi bacu , azaduha kumukorera nta cyo twikanga ,
42001075	turangwa n’ubuyoboke hamwe n’ubutungane , iminsi yose y’ukubaho kwacu .
42001076	Nawe rero wa kana we , uzitwa umuhanuzi w’Umusumbabyose , kuko uzabanziriza Nyagasani ngo umutegurire amayira ,
42001077	ukamenyesha umuryango we umukiro , bazakesha kubabarirwa ibyaha byabo .

42001079	akabonekera abari batuye mu mwijima no mu gicucu cy’urupfu , kugira ngo atuyobore mu nzira y’amahoro . »
42001080	Umwana uko yakuraga , ni na ko yungukaga ubwenge . Nuko yibera ahantu h’ubutayu kugeza igihe yigaragaje imbere ya Israheli .
42002001	Muri iyo minsi , Kayizari Ogusito yaciye iteka ryo kubarura abantu bo mu bihugu byose yategekaga .
42002002	Iryo barura rya mbere ryabaye igihe Kwirini yari umutware wa Siriya .
42002003	Bose bajyaga kwiyandikisha , buri muntu mu mugi we .
42002004	Yozefu na we ava mu mugi wa Nazareti ho mu Galileya , ajya mu mugi wa Dawudi witwaga Betelehemu yo mu Yudeya , kuko yari uwo mu muryango wa Dawudi ,
42002005	agira ngo abarwe , we n’umugore we Mariya wari utwite .
42002006	Nuko bagezeyo , umunsi wo kubyara uragera .
42002007	Abyara umuhungu we w’imfura , amworosa utwenda , amuryamisha mu kavure , kuko nta wundi mwanya ukwiye bari babonye aho bacumbika .
42002008	Muri ako karere hari abashumba barariraga amatungo yabo ku gasozi .
42002009	Nuko Umumalayika wa Nyagasani abahagarara iruhande , ikuzo rya Nyagasani ribasesekazaho urumuri , maze bashya ubwoba .
42002010	Malayika arababwira ati « Mwigira ubwoba , kuko mbazaniye inkuru ikomeye cyane , izashimisha umuryango wose .
42002011	None , mu mugi wa Dawudi , mwavukishije Umukiza ari we Kristu Nyagasani .
42002012	Dore ikimenyetso kimubabwira : murasanga uruhinja rworoshe utwenda , ruryamye mu kavure . »
42002013	Nuko ako kanya , inteko y’ingabo zo mu ijuru yifatanya na wa Mumalayika , basingiza Imana bavuga bati
42002014	« Imana nikuzwe mu bushorishori bw’ijuru , kandi mu nsi abo ikunda bahorane amahoro . »
42002015	Abamalayika babasiga aho , basubira mu ijuru . Nuko abashumba bajya inama bati « Nimucyo tujye i Betelehemu , turebe ibyabaye Nyagasani atumenyesheje . »
42002016	Nuko bagenda bihuta , basanga Mariya na Yozefu , n’uruhinja ruryamye mu kavure .
42002017	Bamaze kureba bamenyesha hose ibyo bari babwiwe kuri uwo Mwana .
42002018	Maze ababumvaga bose , batangazwa n’ibyo abashumba bavugaga .
42002019	Mariya we yashyinguraga mu mutima we ibyabaye byose , akabizirikana .
42002020	Nuko abashumba bataha bakuza Imana kandi bayisingiza , babitewe n’ibyo bari babonye kandi bumvise bihuje n’uko bari babibwiwe .
42002021	Hashize iminsi munani , igihe cyo kugenya Umwana kiragera ; bamwita izina rya Yezu , Malayika yari yamwise atarasamwa .

42002023	nk’uko byanditse mu itegeko rya Nyagasani , ngo « Umuhungu wese w’imfura azaba intore y’umwihariko wa Nyagasani . »
42002024	Bari bajyanywe kandi no gutura igitambo cy’intungura ebyiri cyangwa inuma ebyiri bakurikije itegeko rya Nyagasani .
42002025	Icyo gihe , i Yeruzalemu hari umuntu witwaga Simewoni ; yari intungane kandi yubaha Imana . Yari ategereje ihumure rya Israheli , kandi Roho Mutagatifu yari amurimo .
42002026	Byongeye Roho Mutagatifu yari yaramuhishuriye ko atazapfa atabonye Kristu wa Nyagasani .
42002027	Nuko Simewoni aza mu Ngoro y'Imana abibwirijwe na Roho Mutagatifu . Igihe Ababyeyi b’Umwana Yezu bamuzanye ngo bamurangirizeho ibyategetswe ,
42002028	na we amwakira mu biganza bye , ashimira Imana avuga ati
42002029	« Nyagasani , noneho sezerera umugaragu wawe mu mahoro nk’uko wabivuze ;
42002030	kuko amaso yanjye yabonye agakiza kawe ,
42002031	wageneye imiryango yose .
42002032	Ni we rumuri ruboneshereza amahanga , akaba n’ikuzo ry’umuryango wawe Israheli ! »
42002033	Se na nyina batangazwaga n’ibyo bamuvugagaho .
42002034	Nuko Simewoni arabashima , maze abwira Mariya , nyina wa Yezu , ati « Dore uyu nguyu yashyiriweho kubera benshi muri Israheli impamvu yo korama cyangwa gukira , azaba n’ikimenyetso bazagiriraho impaka .
42002035	Nawe kandi inkota izakwahuranya umutima . Bityo ibitekerezo biri mu mitima ya benshi bigaragare . »
42002036	Hakaba n’umuhanuzikazi Ana , umukobwa wa Fanuweli wo mu muryango wa Azeri ; yari ageze mu zabukuru . Nyuma y’ubusugi bwe , yamaranye n’umugabo we imyaka irindwi ,
42002037	hanyuma aba umupfakazi kugeza mu kigero cy’imyaka mirongo inani n’ine . Ntiyavaga mu Ngoro , agakorera Imana umunsi n’ijoro , asiba kurya kandi asenga .
42002038	Nuko uwo mwanya na we arahagoboka , atangira gusingiza Imana , no gutekerereza iby’uwo mwana abari bategereje ugukira kwa Yeruzalemu .
42002039	Bamaze gutunganya ibyategetswe na Nyagasani , basubira mu Galileya mu mugi wabo wa Nazareti .
42002040	Nuko umwana arakura , arakomera , abyirukana ubwenge , yuzuye ubwitonzi , afite n’ubutoni ku Mana .
42002041	Uko umwaka utashye ababyeyi be bajyaga i Yeruzalemu guhimbaza umunsi mukuru wa Pasika .
42002042	Nuko umwana amaze imyaka cumi n’ibiri , bajyanayo uko babimenyereye ku munsi mukuru .
42002043	Iminsi mikuru irangiye barataha , umwana Yezu asigara i Yeruzalemu ababyeyi be batabizi .
42002044	Bagenda urugendo rw’umunsi wose , bakeka ko ari mu bo bagendanaga . Hanyuma bamushakira muri bene wabo no mu bamenyi .
42002045	Bamubuze , basubira i Yeruzalemu bamushaka .
42002046	Hashize iminsi itatu bamusanga mu Ngoro y'Imana , yicaye hagati y’abigisha , abateze amatwi kandi abasiganuza .
42002047	Abamwumvaga bose batangariraga ubwenge bwe n’amagambo yabasubizaga .
42002048	Ababyeyi be bamubonye barumirwa , maze nyina aramubwira ati « Mwana wanjye , watugenje ute ? Jye na so twagushakanye umutima uhagaze . »
42002049	Arabasubiza ati « Mwanshakiraga iki ? Muyobewe ko ngomba kuba mu Nzu ya Data ? »

42003001	Nuko mu mwaka wa cumi n’itanu w’ingoma ya Tiberi Kayizari , igihe Ponsiyo Pilato yatwaraga Yudeya , Herodi na we atwara Galileya , murumuna we Filipo atwara igihugu cya Itureya n’icya Tirakoniti , na Lizaniya atwara Abileni ,

42003009	Dore intorezo irambitse ku mizi y’ibiti ; noneho igiti cyose kitera imbuto nziza kigiye gutemwa maze gicanwe . »

42003015	Kuko rubanda rwari rutegereje , kandi bose bibaza mu mutima wabo niba Yohani atari we Kristu ,

42003017	Afite urutaro mu ntoki , kandi agiye gukubura imbuga ye : hanyuma azahunika ingano mu kigega cye , naho imishishi ayitwikishe umuriro utazima . »
42003018	Nguko uko Yohani yahuguraga rubanda mu nyigisho nyinshi , abagezaho Inkuru Nziza .

42004001	Yezu ava ku nkombe ya Yorudani yuzuye Roho Mutagatifu , maze ajyanwa na Roho Mutagatifu mu butayu .
42004002	Ahamara iminsi mirongo ine ashukwa na Sekibi ; ntiyagira icyo arya muri iyo minsi , maze ishize arasonza .
42004003	Nuko Sekibi aramubwira ati « Niba uri Umwana w’Imana , tegeka iri buye rihinduke umugati . »

42004006	aramubwira ati « Nzaguha gutegeka biriya bihugu byose , nguhe n’ubukire bwabyo , kuko nabihawe kandi nkabigabira uwo nshatse .
42004007	Wowe rero nundamya , biriya byose biraba ibyawe . »
42004008	Yezu aramusubiza ati « Haranditswe ngo ’ Uzaramya Nyagasani Imana yawe , abe ari we uzasenga wenyine . ’ »

42004019	kandi namamaze umwaka w’impuhwe za Nyagasani . »
42004020	Yezu abumba igitabo , agisubiza umuhereza , maze aricara ; mu isengero bose bari bamuhanze amaso .

42004024	Yungamo ati « Ndababwira ukuri : nta muhanuzi ushimwa iwabo .

42004028	Abari mu isengero bumvise ayo magambo , bose barabisha ,

42004030	Nyamara we abanyura hagati arigendera .

42004032	Batangariraga inyigisho ze , kuko yavugaga nk’umuntu ufite ububasha .
42004033	Ubwo nyine , mu isengero ryabo hakaba umuntu wahanzweho na roho mbi , nuko itera hejuru cyane iti

42004036	Bose ubwoba burabataha , baravugana bati « Mbega ijambo rikomeye ! Dore arategekesha roho mbi ubushobozi n’ububasha zikamenengana ! »
42004037	Nuko Yezu aba ikirangirire muri ako karere kose .
42004038	Yezu ava mu isengero , ajya mu rugo rwa Simoni . Ubwo rero nyirabukwe wa Simoni yari yahinduwe ahinda umuriro mwinshi , baramumwingingira ngo arebe uko amugira .
42004039	Amwunama hejuru , ategeka umuriro kumuvamo , maze koko urazima . Ako kanya arabyuka , arabazimanira .
42004040	Izuba rimaze kurenga , abari bafite abarwayi bafashwe n’indwara z’amoko yose , barabamuzanira ; we abaramburiraho ibiganza , arabakiza .

42004042	Ngo bucye , arasohoka ajya ahantu hiherereye . Abantu baramushaka , baramwinginga ngo yoye kubasiga .

42005001	Umunsi umwe , abantu benshi bamuniganagaho bashaka kumva ijambo ry’Imana ; naho we akaba ahagaze ku nkombe y’ikiyaga cya Genezareti .

42005003	Ajya mu bwato bumwe bwari ubwa Simoni , amusaba kubutsura gato . Nuko aricara , maze yigisha abantu ari mu bwato .

42005005	Simoni aramusubiza ati « Mwigisha , twagotse ijoro ryose , ntitwagira icyo dufata , ariko ubwo ubivuze , ngiye kuroha inshundura . »
42005006	Baraziroha , maze bafata amafi menshi cyane , inshundura zabo zenda gucika .

42005018	Nuko haza abantu bari bahetse ikirema , bashaka kucyinjiza ngo bagishyire imbere ye .

42005020	Abonye ukwemera kwabo , Yezu aravuga ati « Wa muntu we , ibyaha byawe urabikijijwe . »
42005021	Abigishamategeko n’Abafarizayi batangira kwibaza bati « Uyu utuka Imana ni muntu ki ? Ni nde ushobora gukiza ibyaha atari Imana yonyine ? »
42005022	Yezu amenye ibitekerezo byabo , arababwira ati « Ni iki gituma mutekereza mutyo mu mitima yanyu ?
42005023	Icyoroshye ni ikihe : ari ukuvuga ngo ’ Ibyaha byawe urabikijijwe ’ , cyangwa kuvuga ngo ’ Haguruka ugende ’ ?
42005024	Nyamara kugira ngo mumenye ko Umwana w’umuntu afite ububasha bwo gukiza ibyaha mu nsi . . . » , abwira ikirema ati « Ndabikubwiye : haguruka , ufate ingobyi yawe witahire ! »
42005025	Ako kanya , ahaguruka bamureba , ajyana ingobyi yari aryamyemo , ataha asingiza Imana .
42005026	Nuko bose barumirwa , basingiza Imana , kandi barakangarana , bakavuga bati « Uyu munsi twabonye ibintu bitangaje ! »

42005036	Yungamo abacira uyu mugani ati « Nta we utabura ikiremo ku gishura gishya ngo agitere ku gishura gishaje . Agenje atyo , yaba yangije igishura gishya , kandi icyo kiremo kivuyeho , nticyaba gikwiranye n’icyo gishura gishaje !
42005037	Nta n’ushyira divayi nshya mu masaho ashaje , kuko divayi nshya yasandaza amasaho , divayi ikameneka , kandi amasaho akaba apfuye ubusa .

42006001	Nuko ku munsi umwe w’isabato , Yezu anyura mu mirima yeze , abigishwa be bamamfuza amahundo y’ingano , bayavungira mu ntoki , barazirya .

42006005	Nuko yungamo ati « Umwana w’umuntu ni we mugenga w’isabato . »

42006009	Nuko Yezu arababwira ati « Reka mbabaze : icyemewe ku munsi w’isabato ni ikihe ? Ari ukugira neza , cyangwa ari ukugira nabi ? Ari ugukiza umuntu , cyangwa se kumwica ? »

42006011	Ariko bo barabisha , basigara bashaka uko bagenza Yezu .
42006012	Muri iyo minsi , Yezu ajya ku musozi gusenga , ijoro arikesha asenga Imana .
42006013	Bukeye , ahamagara abigishwa be , abatoramo cumi na babiri , abita intumwa .
42006014	Ni bo b’aba : Simoni yise Petero , na Andereya murumuna we , na Yakobo , na Yohani , na Filipo , na Baritolomayo ,
42006015	na Matayo , na Tomasi , na Yakobo mwene Alufeyi , na Simoni bitaga Murwanashyaka ,

42006018	Bari baje kumwumva no gukizwa indwara bari barwaye . N’abababazwaga na roho mbi , bagakira .
42006019	Kandi rubanda rwose rwaharaniraga kumukoraho , kuko ububasha bwamuvagamo bwabakizaga bose .
42006020	Nuko Yezu yerekeza amaso ku bigishwa be , maze aravuga ati « Murahirwa mwe abakene , kuko Ingoma y’Imana ari iyanyu .
42006021	Murahirwa mwe mushonje ubu , kuko muzahazwa . Murahirwa mwe murira ubu , kuko muzaseka .
42006022	Murahirwa igihe cyose abantu babanga , bakabaca , bakabatuka , bakabahindura ruvumwa , babaziza Umwana w’umuntu .
42006023	Icyo gihe muzishime kandi munezerwe , kuko ingororano yanyu ari nyinshi mu ijuru . Nguko uko ababyeyi babo bagenzerezaga abahanuzi .
42006024	Ariko muragowe mwe bakungu , kuko mwashyikiriye imaragahinda yanyu .
42006025	Muragowe mwe mwijuse ubu , kuko muzasonza . Muragowe mwe museka ubu , kuko muzarira , mukaganya .
42006026	Muragowe igihe cyose abantu babavuga neza , kuko ari uko ababyeyi babo bagenzerezaga abahanuzi b’ibinyoma .
42006027	Ahubwo , mwe munyumva , reka mbabwire : nimujye mukunda abanzi banyu , mugirire neza ababanga ;
42006028	mwifurize ineza ababavuma , musabire abababeshyera .
42006029	Nihagira ugukubita ku itama , umutege n’irindi . Nihagira ukwambura igishura cyawe , ntumwime n’ikanzu yawe .
42006030	Ugusabye wese , ujye umuha , n’ukwambuye icyawe ntukakimwake .
42006031	Kandi uko mushaka ko abandi babagirira , abe ari ko namwe mubagirira .
42006032	Niba mwikundiye ababakunda gusa , mwabishimirwa mute , ko n’abanyabyaha bakunda ababakunda ?
42006033	Bisubiye kandi , niba mugirira neza ababagirira neza namwe , mwabishimirwa mute , ko n’abanyabyaha babigenza batyo ?
42006034	Kandi nimuguriza gusa abo mwizeye ko bazabishyura , mwabishimirwa mute ? Abanyabyaha bo ntibaguriza abandi banyabyaha , bizeye ko na bo bazabagenzereza batyo !
42006035	Ahubwo nimujye mukunda abanzi banyu , mugire neza , kandi mutange inguzanyo mutizeye inyiturano . Ubwo rero ingororano yanyu izaba nyinshi , kandi muzaba mubaye abana ba Nyir’ijuru , kuko agirira neza indashima n’abagiranabi .
42006036	Nimube abanyampuhwe , nk’uko So ari Umunyampuhwe .
42006037	Ntimugashinje abandi , namwe mutazashinjwa ; ntimugacire abandi urubanza , namwe mutazarucirwa ; nimubabarire abandi , namwe muzababarirwe .
42006038	Mujye mutanga , namwe muzahabwa : icyibo gishimishije , gitsindagiye , gicugushije , gisheshekaje , ni cyo bazabuzuriza , kuko igipimisho mugeresha , ari cyo muzasubirizwamo . »
42006039	Abacira n’umugani , ati « Harya impumyi ishobora ite kurandata indi mpumyi ? Aho zombi ntizagwa mu mwobo ?
42006040	Nta mwigishwa usumba umwigisha we ; ahubwo umwigishwa wese ushyitse azamera nk’umwigisha we .

42006042	Washobora ute kubwira uwo muva inda imwe uti ’ Muvandimwe , reka ngutokore akatsi kakuri mu jisho ’ , kandi ubwawe utareba umugogo uri mu jisho ryawe ? Wa ndyarya we , banza ukure umugogo mu jisho ryawe , hanyuma uzabona neza , ushobore gutokora akatsi kari mu jisho ry’uwo muva inda imwe .
42006043	Nta giti cyiza cyera imbuto mbi , nta n’igiti kibi cyera imbuto nziza .

42006045	Umunyamico myiza avana mu mutima we ibyiza bibitsemo , n’umunyamico mibi avana mu mutima we ibibi byawusabitse ; kuko akuzuye umutima gasesekara ku munwa .
42006046	Ni iki gituma mumpamagara ngo ’ Mwigisha ! Mwigisha ! ’ kandi mudakora ibyo mbabwira ?
42006047	Umuntu wese ungana , akumva amagambo yanjye , kandi akayakurikiza , reka mbereke uwo namugereranya .
42006048	Ameze nk’umuntu wubatse inzu , agacukura akageza ku rutare , akarugerekaho amabuye y’ishingiro . Umwuzure uteye , umuvu wiroha kuri iyo nzu , ariko ntiyanyeganyega , kuko yari yubatse neza .
42006049	Naho rero uwumva amagambo yanjye ntayakurikize , ameze nk’umuntu wubatse inzu ku butaka , ashinga imiganda yayo ahadakomeye . Umuvu uyiroshyeho , iherako itemba , maze aho yari iri hahinduka itongo . »
42007001	Yezu amaze kubwira rubanda ayo magambo yose , arahaguruka , ajya i Kafarinawumu .

42007020	Abo bantu basanga Yezu , baramubwira bati « Yohani Batisita yakudutumyeho ngo : Mbese ni wowe Wawundi ugomba kuza , cyangwa se dutegereze undi ? »
42007021	Ubwo Yezu akaba arakiza abarwayi benshi , n’abamugaye , n’abahanzweho na roho mbi , agahumura n’impumyi nyinshi .
42007022	Nuko arabasubiza ati « Nimugende mubwire Yohani ibyo mwabonye n’ibyo mwumvise : dore impumyi zirahumuka , abacumbagira baragenda , ababembe barahumanurwa , ibipfamatwi birumva , abapfuye barazuka , n’abakene barabwirwa Inkuru Nziza .
42007023	Kandi hahirwa utazatsitara ku mpamvu yanjye . »
42007024	Intumwa za Yohani zimaze kugenda , Yezu atangira kubaza rubanda ibyerekeye Yohani , ati « Mwagiye kureba iki mu butayu ? Urubingo ruhungabanywa n’umuyaga ?
42007025	Ariko se mwagiye kureba iki ? Umuntu wambaye imyenda y’agatangaza ? Dore , abambaye ibishashagira bakiberaho mu mudamararo , batuye mu ngoro z’abami .
42007026	Nk’ubwo se , mwagiye kureba iki ? Umuhanuzi se ? Koko rero ndabibabwiye , ndetse atambutse umuhanuzi .
42007027	Ni we banditseho ngo ’ Dore nohereje intumwa yanjye imbere yawe , kugira ngo izagutegurire inzira . ’
42007028	Mbabwiye kandi ko mu babyawe n’umugore , nta we uruta Yohani ; nyamara umuto mu Ngoma y’Imana aramuruta .
42007029	Nuko rubanda rwose rwamwumvaga , ndetse n’abasoresha , bakuza Imana bayigarukira , banahabwa batisimu ya Yohani ;
42007030	Abafarizayi n’abigishamategeko , bo bahinyura icyo Imana yabashakagaho , banga kubatizwa na we . »
42007031	Yezu yungamo ati « Mbese abantu b’iki gihe nabagereranya na nde ? Bameze nka nde ? Bameze nk’abana bicaye ku kibuga ,
42007032	bamwe babwira abandi bati ’ Twavugije umwirongi maze ntimwabyina ! Duteye indirimbo z’amaganya , ntimwarira ! ’
42007033	Koko rero Yohani Batisita yaje atarya umugati , kandi atanywa divayi , muravuga muti ’ Yahanzweho ! ’
42007034	Naho Umwana w’umuntu aza arya kandi anywa , muravuga muti ’ Ni igisambo , ni umusinzi , ni incuti y’abasoresha n’abanyabyaha ! ’
42007035	Nyamara ubuhanga bugaragazwa n’ibikorwa byabwo . »
42007036	Nuko umwe mu Bafarizayi , atumira Yezu ngo basangire ; yinjira iwe , ajya ku meza .
42007037	Maze haza umugore wari ihabara mu mugi . Yari yamenye ko Yezu ari ku meza , mu nzu y’uwo Mufarizayi , aza afite urweso rurimo umubavu .
42007038	Nuko aturuka inyuma ya Yezu , yunama ku birenge bye arira . Amarira atonyangira ku birenge bya Yezu , abihanaguza imisatsi ye , agumya kubisoma , anabisiga umubavu .
42007039	Umufarizayi wari wamutumiye , ngo abibone , aribwira ati « Uyu muntu , iyo aba umuhanuzi koko , aba yamenye uyu mugore umukora uwo ari we , n’icyo ari cyo : ko ari umunyabyaha . »
42007040	Yezu araterura , aramubwira ati « Simoni , mfite icyo nkubwira . » Undi aravuga ati « Mbwira , Mwigisha . »
42007041	Yezu ati « Umuntu yari afite abantu babiri bamurimo umwenda ; umwe yari amurimo amadenari magana atanu , undi mirongo itanu .
42007042	Babuze icyo bishyura , abarekera uwo mwenda . Muri abo bombi , ni uwuhe uzarusha undi kumukunda ? »
42007043	Simoni arasubiza ati « Ndasanga ari uwarekewe umwenda munini . » Yezu aramubwira ati « Ushubije neza . »
42007044	Nuko ahindukirira wa mugore , abwira Simoni ati « Urabona uyu mugore ? Ninjiye mu nzu yawe , ntiwansuka amazi ku birenge ; naho we , yuhagije ibirenge byanjye amarira ye , maze abihanaguza imisatsi ye .
42007045	Ntiwampobeye unsoma ; naho we , kuva aho yinjiriye mu nzu , ntiyahwemye kunsoma ibirenge .
42007046	Ntiwansize amavuta ahumura mu mutwe ; naho we , yansize umubavu ku birenge .
42007047	Ni cyo gitumye nkubwira nti : ibyaha bye byose uko bingana arabibabariwe , kubera urukundo rwe rwinshi . Naho ubabariwe bike , akunda buke . »
42007048	Nuko Yezu abwira uwo mugore ati « Ibyaha byawe birakijijwe . »
42007049	Abari kumwe na we ku meza batangira kwibaza bati « Uyu ni muntu ki ugeza n’aho gukiza ibyaha ? »
42007050	Nuko Yezu abwira wa mugore ati « Ukwemera kwawe kuragukijije ; genda amahoro . »
42008001	Nuko Yezu ashyira nzira , azenguruka imigi n’insisiro , yamamaza Inkuru Nziza y’Ingoma y’Imana . Ba Cumi na babiri bari kumwe na we .
42008002	Hari kandi n’abagore bamwe bari bakijijwe roho mbi n’izindi ndwara ; barimo Mariya bise Madalena , wari wameneshejwemo roho mbi ndwi ;
42008003	hari na Yohana muka Shuza , umunyabintu wa Herodi , na Suzana n’abandi benshi babafashishaga ibintu bari bafite .
42008004	Nuko abantu benshi bamaze guterana , baturutse mu migi yose bamusanga , Yezu ababwiza uyu mugani ati
42008005	« Umubibyi yavuye iwe ajya kubiba imbuto ye . Igihe abiba , imbuto zimwe zigwa iruhande rw’inzira ; barazikandagira , n’inyoni zo mu kirere zirazirya zose .
42008006	Izindi zigwa mu mabuye ; zimaze kumera ziruma , kuko zabuze amazi .
42008007	N’izindi zigwa mu mahwa ; amahwa arakura , arazipfukirana .
42008008	Izindi zigwa mu butaka bwiza ; ziramera , zera imbuto karijana . » Amaze kuvuga atyo , atera hejuru , ati « Ufite amatwi yo kumva , niyumve ! »
42008009	Abigishwa be bamubaza icyo uwo mugani ushaka kuvuga .
42008010	Arabasubiza ati « Mwebweho mwahawe kumenya amabanga y’Ingoma y’Imana ; naho abandi bakabwirwa mu migani , ’ kugira ngo barebe boye kubona , bumve boye gusobanukirwa . ’
42008011	Dore rero icyo uwo mugani uvuga : imbuto ibibwa ni ijambo ry’Imana .
42008012	Abameze nk’imbuto zaguye iruhande rw’inzira ni abumva iryo jambo , hanyuma Sekibi akaza , akarikura mu mutima wabo , agira ngo batemera , bagakira .
42008013	Abameze nk’imbuto zaguye mu mabuye , ni abumva iryo jambo bakaryakirana ibyishimo , nyamara ntiribacengeremo ngo ribashingemo imizi . Ni abemera by’akanya gato ; ibishuko byaza , bagahita bacika intege .
42008014	Abameze nk’imbuto zaguye mu mahwa , ni abumva ijambo , ariko imihihibikano n’ubukungu n’amaraha y’isi bikabapfukirana , bikababuza kwera imbuto .
42008015	Abameze nk’imbuto zaguye mu butaka bwiza , ni abumva ijambo , bakaryakirana umutima ukeye kandi mwiza , maze bakera imbuto nziza babikesha ubudacogora bwabo .
42008016	Nta muntu ucana itara ngo arishyire mu nsi y’ikibindi , cyangwa mu nsi y’urutara , ahubwo arishyira ku gitereko , agira ngo rimurikire abinjira bose .
42008017	Koko rero , nta cyahishwe kitazahishurwa , nta n’ibanga rizahera ritamenyekanye .
42008018	Mwitondere rero uburyo mwumva aya magambo . Kuko ufite byinshi , ari we uzongererwa ; naho udafite , n’icyo yibwiraga ko afite bazakimwaka . »
42008019	Nuko nyina wa Yezu n’abavandimwe be baza bamusanga , ariko babura uko bamugeraho kubera abantu benshi bari bamukikije .
42008020	Babimenyesha Yezu bati « Nyoko n’abavandimwe bawe bari hanze barifuza ko mubonana . »
42008021	Arabasubiza ati « Mama n’abavandimwe banjye , ni abumva ijambo ry’Imana , bakarikurikiza . »
42008022	Umunsi umwe , Yezu ajya mu bwato ari kumwe n’abigishwa be . Arababwira ati « Twambuke ikiyaga , dufate hakurya . » Nuko bagana amazi magari .
42008023	Mu gihe bambuka , Yezu arasinzira . Nuko haza umuhengeri , ubwato buravoma , benda kurohama .
42008024	Baramwegera baramukangura , bavuga bati « Mwigisha , Mwigisha , turashize ! » Nuko arakanguka , akangara umuyaga n’umuvumba w’amazi . Birahosha haza ituze .
42008025	Arababwira ati « Ukwemera kwanyu kuri he ? » Bagira ubwoba , baratangara , bakabazanya bati « Uyu ni muntu ki , ugeza aho gutegeka imiyaga n’imivumba bikamwumvira ! »
42008026	Bakukira mu gihugu cy’Abanyageraza giteganye n’icya Galileya .
42008027	Yezu ageze imusozi , asanganirwa n’umuntu uturutse mu mugi , wahanzweho na roho mbi . Yari amaze igihe kirekire atikoza imyambaro , nta n’inzu yabagamo , ahubwo yiberaga mu marimbi .
42008028	Abonye Yezu , amwikubita imbere , maze atera hejuru cyane , ati « Uranshakaho iki , Yezu mwana w’Imana Isumbabyose ? Ndakwinginze , winyica urubozo . »
42008029	Roho mbi yavuze ibyo kubera ko Yezu yari yatangiye kuyitegeka ngo ive muri uwo muntu . Koko rero , roho mbi yamuhangagaho kenshi ; bakamubohesha iminyururu amaboko n’amaguru bagira ngo adacika , ariko akarenga agaca ingoyi , maze roho mbi ikamujyana kwangara ku gahinga .
42008030	Yezu aramubaza ati « Izina ryawe ni irihe ? » Aramusubiza ati « Nitwa Gitero . » Kumusubiza atyo yabitewe n’uko roho mbi nyinshi zari zaramwaritsemo .
42008031	Nuko zimwingingira kutazitegeka gusubira mu nyenga .
42008032	Ubwo aho ngaho hakaba umukumbi w’ingurube zarishaga kuri uwo musozi . Roho mbi zinginga Yezu ngo azireke zigire muri izo ngurube , arazemerera .
42008033	Nuko roho mbi ziva muri uwo muntu , zijya mu ngurube , maze uwo mukumbi ukonkoboka mu manga n’umuriri mwinshi , wiroha mu kiyaga , urarohama .
42008034	Abashumba babibonye barahunga , bajya kubimenyesha abari mu mugi n’abari mu cyaro .
42008035	Abantu b’aho barahurura , baza kureba ibyabaye . Bageze iruhande rwa Yezu , basanga wa muntu roho mbi zari zavuyemo yicaye imbere ye , yambaye , kandi yagaruye ubwenge . Nuko bagira ubwoba .
42008036	Abari babibonye , babatekerereza ukuntu uwo muntu wari wahanzweho na roho mbi yakize .
42008037	Nuko abaturage bose bo mu gihugu cy’Abanyageraza basaba Yezu ngo abavire aho , kuko bari bafite ubwoba bwinshi . Yezu yurira ubwato aragenda .
42008038	Nuko uwo muntu roho mbi zari zavuyemo , aramusaba ngo bibanire . We rero amusezerera , amubwira ati
42008039	« Ahubwo taha , maze utekerereze abandi ubuntu Imana yakugiriye . » Uwo muntu aragenda , atangaza mu mugi wose ibyo Yezu yari yamugiriye .
42008040	Yezu agarutse , abantu baramwakira , kuko bose bari bamutegereje .
42008041	Nuko haza umuntu witwa Yayiro , akaba umutware w’isengero . Apfukamira Yezu , aramwinginga ngo aze iwe ,
42008042	kuko umukobwa we wari ufite nk’imyaka cumi n’ibiri yendaga gupfa . Mu gihe aganayo , rubanda bamubyiganaho .
42008043	Ubwo rero hakaba umugore wari umaze imyaka cumi n’ibiri ava amaraso , ntihagira n’umwe ushobora kumukiza .
42008044	Amuturuka inyuma , akora ku ncunda z’igishura cye ; ako kanya amaraso arakira .
42008045	Nuko Yezu arabaza ati « Ni nde unkozeho ? » Bose barahakana . Petero aramusubiza ati « Mwigisha , ni aba bantu bagukikije , bakubyiga ! »
42008046	Yezu asubiramo ati « Hari umuntu unkozeho , kuko numvise ububasha bumvamo . »
42008047	Umugore abonye ko yamenyekanye , aza ahinda umushyitsi , maze apfukama imbere ya Yezu , avugira mu ruhame icyatumye amukoraho , n’uko yahereyeko akira ako kanya .
42008048	We rero aramubwira ati « Mwana wanjye , ukwemera kwawe kuragukijije , genda amahoro . »
42008049	Mu gihe akivuga ibyo , haza umuntu uvuye kwa wa mutware w’isengero , aramubwira ati « Umukobwa wawe amaze guca ; reka kurushya Umwigisha . »
42008050	Yezu abyumvise abwira Yayiro ati « Witinya ! Upfa kwemera gusa , arakira . »
42008051	Ageze mu rugo , ntiyatuma hari uwinjirana na we mu nzu , kereka Petero na Yakobo na Yohani , hamwe na se na nyina b’umwana .
42008052	Bose baramuririraga , kandi bashavujwe na we . Yezu aravuga ati « Mwirira : umukobwa ntiyapfuye , ahubwo arasinziriye . »
42008053	Baramuseka , kuko bari bazi neza ko umwana yapfuye .
42008054	Naho we amufata ukuboko , aramuhamagara ati « Mwana , kanguka . »
42008055	Umukobwa agarura akuka , ako kanya arahaguruka . Nuko Yezu ategeka ko bamugaburira .
42008056	Ababyeyi be baratangara cyane , ariko ababuza kugira uwo babwira ibimaze kuba .
42009001	Nuko Yezu akoranya ba Cumi na babiri , abaha gutegeka no kwirukana roho mbi zose , abaha n’ububasha bwo gukiza indwara .
42009002	Abatuma kwamamaza Ingoma y’Imana no gukiza abarwayi .
42009003	Arababwira ati « Ntimugire icyo mujyana mu rugendo , yaba inkoni , waba umufuka , waba umugati , byaba n’ibiceri » , ababwira no kutajyana amakanzu abiri .
42009004	Arongera ati « Urugo muzinjiramo rwose , muzarugumemo kugeza igihe muhaviriye .
42009005	Naho abatazabakira , nimujya kuva mu mugi wabo , muzakungute umukungugu wo ku birenge byanyu , bibe ikimenyetso cy’uko bahemutse . »
42009006	Nuko baragenda bazenguruka insisiro , bamamaza Inkuru Nziza , kandi bakiza abarwayi hose .
42009007	Icyo gihe Herodi , umutware w’intara ya Galileya , yumva ibyabaye byose , biramushobera , kuko bamwe bavugaga bati « Ni Yohani wazutse mu bapfuye » ;
42009008	abandi ngo « Ni Eliya wagarutse » ; naho abandi ngo « Ni umwe mu bahanuzi ba kera wazutse . »
42009009	Ariko Herodi akavuga ati « Yohani , jyewe namucishije umutwe ; none se uwo muntu numva bavugaho ibyo yaba nde ? » Asigara ashaka uko yamubona .
42009010	Intumwa zihindukiye , zitekerereza Yezu ibyo zakoze byose . Nuko ajyana na zo , ajya ahantu hiherereye , ahagana ku mugi wa Betsayida .
42009011	Ariko abantu benshi baza kuhamenya , baramukurikira . Yezu abakira neza , ababwira iby’Ingoma y’Imana , kandi akiza abari babikeneye .
42009012	Umunsi uciye ikibu , ba Cumi na babiri baramwegera , baramubwira bati « Sezerera aba bantu , bajye mu nsisiro no mu ngo ziri hafi aha , bashake icumbi n’icyo barya , kuko aha turi ari ku butayu . »
42009013	Maze arababwira ati « Mwebwe ubwanyu nimubahe ibyo kurya . » Baramusubiza bati « Nta kindi dufite kitari imigati itanu n’amafi abiri gusa ; keretse ahari twebwe ubwacu twajya kubagurira icyo barya . . . »
42009014	Koko hari abagabo bageze nko ku bihumbi bitanu . Yezu abwira abigishwa be ati « Nimubicaze mu dutsiko tw’abantu nka mirongo itanu mirongo itanu . »
42009015	Babigenza batyo , barabicaza bose .
42009016	Nuko afata ya migati itanu na ya mafi abiri , areba ku ijuru , abivugiraho amagambo y’umugisha , hanyuma arabimanyura , abiha abigishwa be kugira ngo babihereze abantu bari aho .
42009017	Bararya , bose barahaga ; barundarundira hamwe ibisigaye , byuzura inkangara cumi n’ebyiri .
42009018	Umunsi umwe Yezu yasengeraga ahiherereye ari kumwe n’abigishwa be , maze arababaza ati « Rubanda bavuga ko ndi nde ? »
42009019	Barasubiza bati « Bamwe bavuga ko uri Yohani Batisita , abandi ngo uri Eliya , naho abandi ngo uri umwe mu bahanuzi ba kera wazutse . »
42009020	Yongera kubabaza ati « Mwebwe se , muvuga ko ndi nde ? » Petero aramusubiza ati « Uri Kristu w’Imana . »
42009021	Nyamara we abihanangiriza kutagira uwo babibwira .
42009022	Yungamo avuga ko Umwana w’umuntu agomba kuzababara cyane , agacibwa n’abakuru b’umuryango , n’abatware b’abaherezabitambo , n’abigishamategeko , akicwa , kandi akazazuka ku munsi wa gatatu .
42009023	Nuko akabwira bose , ati « Niba hari ushaka kunkurikira , yiyibagirwe ubwe , aheke umusaraba we , maze ankurikire !
42009024	Kuko uzashaka gukiza ubugingo bwe , azabubura ; naho uzahara ubugingo bwe ari jye agirira , azabukiza .
42009025	Umuntu watunga iby’isi yose , ariko akabura ubugingo bwe , cyangwa akabwangiza , byaba bimumariye iki ?
42009026	Koko rero , umuntu uzanyihakana , agahakana n’amagambo yanjye , uwo nguwo Umwana w’umuntu na we azamwihakana , igihe azazira mu ikuzo rye , n’irya Se , n’iry’Abamalayika batagatifu .
42009027	Ndababwira ukuri : mu bari hano , harimo abatazapfa batabonye Ingoma y’Imana . »
42009028	Nuko hashize nk’iminsi munani Yezu amaze kuvuga ayo magambo , ajyana na Petero , na Yohani , na Yakobo , aterera umusozi ajya gusenga .
42009029	Mu gihe yasengaga , mu maso he hahinduka ukundi , n’imyambaro ye irakirana nk’umurabyo .
42009030	Nuko haza abagabo babiri baganira na we , ari bo Musa na Eliya .
42009031	Bababonekera babengerana ikuzo , bavugana na we iby’urupfu rwe , yari agiye gupfira i Yeruzalemu .
42009032	Icyo gihe Petero na bagenzi be bari batwawe n’ibitotsi . Ngo bakanguke , babona ikuzo rya Yezu na ba bagabo babiri bari kumwe .
42009033	Bagiye kugenda , Petero abwira Yezu ati « Mwigisha , kwibera hano nta ko bisa . Reka tuhace ibiraro bitatu , kimwe cyawe , ikindi cya Musa , n’ikindi cya Eliya . » Icyakora ntiyari azi icyo avuga .
42009034	Akivuga ibyo , igihu kiraza kirabatwikira ; kibarenzeho bashya ubwoba .
42009035	Nuko ijwi rituruka muri cya gihu rivuga riti « Uyu ni Umwana wanjye nihitiyemo ; mujye mumwumvira ! »
42009036	Ijwi ngo rimare kuvuga , babona Yezu ari wenyine . Nuko muri iyo minsi baryumaho , ntibagira uwo babwira ibyo bari babonye .
42009037	Bukeye bwaho , igihe bamanuka umusozi , abantu benshi baza kumusanganira .
42009038	Maze umuntu wo muri iyo mbaga atera hejuru ati « Mwigisha , ndabigusabye : dore uyu mwana wanjye mufite ari ikinege .
42009039	Hari ubwo roho mbi imwegura , agacura imiborogo , ikamuhotagura , akazana urufuro ; kandi ikamuvamo byaruhanije , igasiga ari intere .
42009040	Ninginze abigishwa bawe ngo bayirukane , ariko ntibabishoboye . »
42009041	Yezu arasubiza ati « Bantu b’iki gihe batemera kandi b’inkozi z’ibibi , nzabana namwe kugeza ryari ? Nzabiyumanganya mpereze he ? Cyo zana umwana wawe hano . »
42009042	Igihe umwana ariho yegera Yezu , roho mbi imutura hasi , iramuhotagura . Nuko Yezu akangara roho mbi , akiza umwana , amusubiza se .
42009043	Bose batangarira ububasha bw’Imana . Mu gihe bose bagitangarira ibyo Yezu yakoraga byose , abwira abigishwa be ati
42009044	« Mwebweho mutege amatwi , mwumve ibyo ngiye kubabwira : dore Umwana w’umuntu agiye kugabizwa abantu . »
42009045	Ariko ntibumva iryo jambo , ribabera urujijo , ntibasobanukirwa kandi batinya kumusobanuza .
42009046	Ubundi , baza kujya impaka , bibaza uwaba mukuru muri bo .
42009047	Yezu amenya ibyo batekereza , maze arembuza umwana muto , amushyira iruhande rwe .
42009048	Arababwira ati « Umuntu wese wakira uyu mwana ari jye abigirira , ni jye aba yakiriye . Kandi uzanyakira wese , azaba yakiriye Uwantumye . Koko rero umuto muri mwe , ni we mukuru . »
42009049	Ni bwo Yohani amubwiye ati « Mwigisha , twabonye umuntu wirukana roho mbi mu izina ryawe ; turabimubuza kuko atagukurikira hamwe natwe . »
42009050	Yezu aramusubiza ati « Ntimukagire uwo mubibuza , kuko utabatambamira , burya aba ari kumwe namwe . »
42009051	Igihe cya Yezu cyo kuvanwa ku isi cyari cyegereje , nuko yiyemeza adashidikanya kujya i Yeruzalemu .
42009052	Yohereza integuza ngo zimubanzirize imbere . Baragenda binjira mu rusisiro rw’Abanyasamariya kumuteguriza .
42009053	Ariko ab’aho banga kumwakira , kuko yajyaga i Yeruzalemu .
42009054	Babiri mu bigishwa be , Yakobo na Yohani , babibonye baravuga bati « Nyagasani , urashaka se ko dutegeka umuriro , ukamanuka mu ijuru , ukabatsemba ? »
42009055	We rero arahindukira , arabatonganya cyane .
42009056	Nuko baboneza bajya mu rundi rusisiro .
42009057	Igihe bari mu nzira bagenda , umuntu umwe aramubwira ati « Nzagukurikira aho uzajya hose . »
42009058	Yezu aramusubiza ati « Imihari igira amasenga , n’inyoni zo mu kirere zikagira ibyari ; naho Umwana w’umuntu we , ntagira aho arambika umutwe . »
42009059	Yezu abwira undi ati « Nkurikira . » We aramusubiza ati « Reka mbanze njye guhamba data . »
42009060	Yezu aramubwira ati « Reka abapfu bahambe abapfu babo ; naho wowe , genda ujye kwamamaza Ingoma y’Imana . »
42009061	Undi na we ati « Mwigisha , nzagukurikira , ariko reka mbanze njye gusezera ku bo mu rugo . »
42009062	Yezu aramusubiza ati « Umuntu wese watangiye guhinga agasubiza amaso inyuma , uwo ntakwiye gukorera Ingoma y’Imana . »
42010001	Nyuma y’ibyo Nyagasani ahitamo n’abandi mirongo irindwi na babiri , maze abohereza imbere ye babiri babiri , mu migi yose n’ahandi hose yajyaga kunyura .

42010017	Ba bigishwa uko bari mirongo irindwi na babiri , bagaruka bishimye cyane , bavuga bati « Mwigisha , na roho mbi ziratwumvira kubera izina ryawe . »

42011011	Mbese ni nde mubyeyi muri mwe , umwana we yasaba umugati , akamuhereza ibuye ? Cyangwa se yamusaba ifi , aho kuyimuha , akamuhereza inzoka ?

42012001	Nuko abantu bageze ku bihumbi n’ibihumbi barakorana ndetse barabyigana . Yezu abanza kubwira abigishwa be ati « Mwirinde umusemburo w’Abafarizayi ! » ashaka kuvuga uburyarya bwabo .

42012046	amaherezo shebuja azaza umunsi atamwitezeho , no ku isaha atazi , maze amwirukane nabi , amuherereze mu nteko y’abahemu .
42012047	Uwo mugaragu rero wari uzi icyo shebuja ashaka , ntacyiteho ngo agikore uko yari yamutegetse , azakubitwa nyinshi ;
42012048	naho utazi icyo shebuja ashaka , agakora ibidakwiye , we azakubitwa nkeya . Uzaba yarahawe byinshi , azabazwa byinshi ; n’uwo bazaba barashinze byinshi , azabazwa ibiruta iby’abandi . »
42012049	Yezu yungamo ati « Nazanywe no gukongeza umuriro ku isi , mbega ukuntu nifuza ko wagurumana !

42012051	Aho ntimwibwira ko nazanywe no gutera amahoro ku isi ? Oya , ndabibabwiye , ahubwo naje kubateranya .
42012052	Koko , kuva ubu , urugo rw’abantu batanu ruzicamo ibice , batatu barwanye babiri , babiri na bo barwanye batatu .
42012053	Bazashyamirana , umugabo n’umuhungu we , umuhungu na se , umugore n’umukobwa we , umukobwa na nyina , nyirabukwe n’umukazana we , umukazana na nyirabukwe . »

43001001	Mu ntangiriro ya byose Jambo yariho , kandi Jambo yabanaga n’Imana , kandi Jambo akaba Imana .

43007008	Mwe nimugende , mujye mu munsi mukuru ; jye sinjya muri uwo munsi mukuru , kuko igihe cyanjye kitaruzuzwa . »
43007009	Amaze kubabwira atyo , yihamira mu Galileya .
43007010	Abavandimwe be bamaze kugenda bajya mu munsi mukuru , na we ajyayo , atari ku mugaragaro ahubwo nka rwihishwa .
43007011	Abayahudi bamushakiraga mu munsi mukuru , babaririza bati « Mbese wa wundi ari hehe ? »
43007012	Rubanda bahwihwisaga byinshi bimwerekeyeho , bamwe bati « Ni umuntu mwiza » , abandi bati « Oya , ahubwo arayobya rubanda . »
43007013	Nta muntu watinyukaga kuvuga ibimwerekeyeho yeruye , kuko batinyaga Abayahudi .
43007014	Umunsi mukuru ugeze hagati , Yezu ajya mu Ngoro y'Imana , arigisha .
43007015	Abayahudi baratangara , baravuga bati « Uyu ashobora ate kumenya Ibyanditswe , atarigeze yiga ? »
43007016	Yezu arabasubiza ati « Inyigisho mvuga , si izanjye , ahubwo ni iz’Uwantumye .
43007017	Ukereye gukora icyo Imana ishaka , amenyeraho ko inyigisho mvuga ari iz’Imana , cyangwa se ko ari izo nihimbira ubwanjye .
43007018	Uvuga ibye bwite , aba ashaka kwihesha ikuzo , naho ushaka ikuzo ry’Uwamutumye , uwo ni umunyakuri , kandi nta kinyoma kimurangwaho .
43007019	Mbese nta mategeko Musa yabahaye ? Nyamara nta n’umwe muri mwe uyakurikiza .
43007020	Kuki mushaka kunyica ? » Rubanda baramusubiza bati « Aho ntuhanzweho na roho mbi ? Ni nde ushaka kukwica ? »
43007021	Yezu arabasubiza ati « Nakoze igikorwa kimwe , mwese muratangara .
43007022	Musa yabahaye umuhango wo kugenya kandi utamuturutseho , ahubwo yarawukuye kuri ba sogokuruza , maze mukagenya umuntu ku isabato .
43007023	Niba umuntu agenywa ku munsi w’isabato , ntibyice itegeko rya Musa , mutewe n’iki kundakarira kuko nakijije umuntu ku munsi w’isabato ?
43007024	Ntimugace urubanza mukurikije ibigaragara , ahubwo mujye muruca mukurikije ubutabera . »
43007025	Bamwe mu batuye i Yeruzalemu baravuga bati « Uriya si wa wundi bahigaga bashaka kumwica ?
43007026	Nyamara dore aravugira mu ruhame , nta cyo bavuga . Aho abategetsi bacu ntibamenye by’ukuri ko ari we Kristu ?
43007027	Ariko uyu tuzi aho akomoka , naho Kristu naza , nta we uzamenya aho aturuka . »
43007028	Yezu yigishiriza mu Ngoro y'Imana aranguruye ijwi , ati « Ni koko muranzi kandi muzi n’aho nkomoka ! Icyakora sinaje ku bwanjye ; Uwantumye ni We Munyakuri , Uwo mwe ntimumuzi .
43007029	Jye ndamuzi , kuko ari We nkomokaho , kandi akaba ari We wantumye . »
43007030	Ni bwo bashatse kumufata , ariko ntihagira n’umwe umukozaho n’urutoki , kuko igihe cye cyari kitaragera .
43007031	Icyakora benshi muri rubanda baramwemera , baravuga bati « Kristu naza , aho azakora ibimenyetso biruta ibyo uyu akora ? »
43007032	Abafarizayi bumvise ko rubanda rukomeza guhwihwisa ibyo byose , bo n’abatware b’abaherezabitambo bohereza abagaragu babo ngo bamufate .
43007033	Yezu aravuga ati « Ndacyari kumwe namwe igihe gito , nyuma ngasanga Uwantumye .
43007034	Muzanshaka mumbure , kandi ntimuteze kugera aho nzaba ndi . »
43007035	Abayahudi batangira kubazanya bati « Agiye kuzajya he , tutazamusanga ? Azabe agiye gusanga Abayahudi batataniye mu banyamahanga , maze akigisha abanyamahanga ?
43007036	Aya magambo avuze arashaka kuvuga iki , ngo ’ Muzanshaka mumbure , kandi ntimuteze kugera aho nzaba ndi ’ ? »
43007037	Ku munsi usoza iminsi mikuru , ari na wo uyirusha ibirori , Yezu arahagarara , arangurura ijwi ati « Ufite inyota nansange anywe .
43007038	Unyemera , nk’uko byanditswe , imigezi y’amazi atanga ubugingo izamuvubukamo . »
43007039	Ibyo yabivuze abyerekeje kuri Roho uzahabwa abamwemera . Kugeza icyo gihe , Roho yari ataratangwa , kuko Yezu yari atarahabwa ikuzo rye .
43007040	Benshi muri rubanda bumvise ayo magambo , bati « Uyu ni we wa Muhanuzi koko . »
43007041	Abandi bati « Ni Kristu . » Abandi na bo bati « Kristu azaturuke se mu Galileya ?
43007042	Ibyanditswe ntibivuga ko Kristu ari uwo mu nkomoko ya Dawudi , ko azaturuka ku musozi wa Betelehemu , aho Dawudi yavukiye ? »
43007043	Ibyo bituma rubanda bicamo ibice kubera we .
43007044	Bamwe muri bo bashakaga kumufata , ariko ntihagira umukozaho n’urutoki .
43007045	Nuko abagaragu baragaruka basanga abatware b’abaherezabitambo n’Abafarizayi ; barababaza bati « Ko mutamuzanye ni iki ? »
43007046	Abagaragu barabasubiza bati « Nta muntu wigeze avuga nk’uwo muntu . »
43007047	Abafarizayi bati « Ese namwe mwashukitse ?
43007048	Hari n’umwe mu Bategetsi cyangwa se mu Bafarizayi wamwemeye ?
43007049	Si rubanda ruriya rutazi amategeko ? Ni ibivume . »
43007050	Umwe muri bo , Nikodemu , wigeze gusanga Yezu mbere , arababwira ati
43007051	« Harya amategeko yacu apfa gucira umuntu urubanza , batabanje kumwumva ngo bamenye icyo yakoze ? »
43007052	Baramusubiza bati « Mbese nawe uri Umunyagalileya ? Uzashishoze , uzasanga ari nta muhanuzi uvuka mu Galileya ! »
43007053	Nuko bose barikubura barataha , umwe iwe , undi iwe .
43008001	Naho Yezu yigira ku musozi w’Imizeti .
43008002	Bugicya , agaruka mu Ngoro y'Imana , rubanda rwose baza bamugana , maze aricara arabigisha .
43008003	Ni bwo abigishamategeko n’Abafarizayi bamuzaniye umugore wari wafashwe asambana , bamuhagarika hagati .
43008004	Babwira Yezu bati « Mwigisha , uyu mugore bamufashe asambana .
43008005	Mu Mategeko , Musa yadutegetse kwicisha amabuye abagore nk’aba . Wowe se ubivugaho iki ? »
43008006	Ibyo babivugiraga kumwinja , bagira ngo babone ibyo bamurega . Ariko Yezu ariyunamira atangira kwandikisha urutoki ku butaka .
43008007	Bakomeje kumubaza , arunamuka arababwira ati « Muri mwe udafite icyaha , ngaho namubanze ibuye . »
43008008	Yongera kunama , akomeza kwandika ku butaka .
43008009	Bumvise avuze atyo , batangira kugenda umwe umwe , bahereye ku basaza .
43008010	Nuko Yezu asigara aho wenyine na wa mugore agihagaze aho hagati .
43008011	Yezu yunamutse aramubaza ati « Mugore , ba bandi bari he ? Nta n’umwe waguciriye urubanza ? » Umugore arasubiza ati « Nta n’umwe , Mwigisha . » Yezu aramubwira ati « Nanjye rero singuciriye urubanza ; genda ariko uherukire aho gucumura ukundi . »
43008012	Nuko Yezu yongera kubabwira ati « Ndi urumuri rw’isi , unkurikira ntazagenda mu mwijima , ahubwo azatunga urumuri rw’ubugingo . »
43008013	Abafarizayi baramubwira bati « Ubwo ari wowe ubwawe uhamya ibikwerekeyeho , ibyo uhamya si iby’ukuri ! »
43008014	Yezu arabasubiza ati « N’ubwo ari jye uhamya ibinyerekeyeho , ibyo mpamya ni ukuri , kuko nzi aho nturuka n’aho ngana , naho mwe ntimuzi aho nturuka n’aho ngana .
43008015	Mwe muca urubanza mukurikije umubiri , jye nta we ncira urubanza .
43008016	N’iyo nciye urubanza , ruba ari urw’ukuri , kuko mba ntari jyenyine , ahubwo mba ndi kumwe na Data wantumye .
43008017	Ni na ko byanditse mu Mategeko yanyu ngo ’ Icyo abagabo babiri bemeje , kiba ari icy’ukuri . ’
43008018	Koko ni jye uhamya ibinyerekeyeho , ariko na Data wantumye na we arabyemeza . »
43008019	Baramubwira bati « So aba hehe ? » Yezu arabasubiza ati « Ari jye ari na Data , nta we muzi ; iyaba mwari munzi , mwamenye na Data . »
43008020	Ayo magambo Yezu yayavugiye iruhande rw’ububiko , aho yigishirizaga mu Ngoro y'Imana . Ntihagira umufata , kuko igihe cye cyari kitaragera .
43008021	Yezu yongera kubabwira ati « Ndagiye kandi muzanshaka , ariko muzapfana icyaha cyanyu . Aho ngiye ntimushobora kuhajya . »
43008022	Abayahudi baravuga bati « Aho ntagiye kwiyahura , ubwo avuze ngo ’ Aho ngiye ntimushobora kuhajya ’ ? »
43008023	Yezu arababwira ati « Mwe muri abo hasi , jye nkaba uwo hejuru ; mwe muri abo kuri iyi si , jye sindi uwo kuri iyi si .
43008024	Nababwiye ko muzapfana ibyaha byanyu . Muramutse mutemeye ko ndi uriho , muzapfana ibyaha byanyu . »
43008025	Nuko baramubaza bati « Uri nde ? » Yezu arabasubiza ati « Ndi uwo nababwiye ngitangira .
43008026	Mfite byinshi mbavugaho n’urubanza nabacira . Ariko Uwantumye ni umunyakuri , kandi ibyo namwumvanye ni byo mbwira isi . »
43008027	Ntibamenya ko yababwiraga Se .
43008028	Yezu yungamo ati « Nimumara kwerereza Umwana w’umuntu , icyo gihe muzamenya ko ndi uriho , kandi ko ari nta cyo nkora ku bwanjye , ahubwo mvuga nk’uko Data yambwirije .
43008029	Uwantumye turahorana , ntiyansize jyenyine , kuko mpora nkora ibimunyura . »
43008030	Amaze kuvuga atyo , benshi baramwemera .
43008031	Nuko Yezu abwira Abayahudi bari bamwemeye , ati « Nimukomera ku ijambo ryanjye muzaba mubaye abigishwa banjye by’ukuri .
43008032	Kandi muzamenya ukuri , maze ukuri kubahe kwigenga . »
43008033	Baramusubiza bati « Turi abo mu nkomoko ya Abrahamu , nta wigeze atwigarurira . Watubwira ute ngo muzigenga ? »
43008034	Yezu arabasubiza ati « Ndababwira ukuri koko : umuntu wese ukora icyaha aba ari umugaragu w’icyaha .
43008035	Burya umugaragu ntahora iteka mu nzu , ahubwo umwana ni we uyihoramo .
43008036	Mwana nabakura ku bugaragu , icyo gihe muzaba mubaye abigenga koko .
43008037	Nzi ko mukomoka kuri Abrahamu , ariko murashaka kunyica , kuko ijambo ryanjye mutarizirikana .
43008038	Jye mvuga ibyo nabonye kwa Data , namwe mukora ibyo mwumvanye so . »
43008039	Baramusubiza bati « Umubyeyi wacu ni Abrahamu . » Yezu na we arababwira ati « Niba muri abana ba Abrahamu , nimukore ibyo Abrahamu yakoze .
43008040	Ubu rero murashaka kunyica , jye ubabwira ukuri numvanye Imana . Ibyo Abrahamu ntiyabikoze .
43008041	Mwe murakora ibyo so akora . » Baramubwira bati « Nta bwo turi ibibyarirano . Dufite Data umwe , ni Imana . »
43008042	Yezu arababwira ati « Iyaba Imana yari so mwankunze , kuko nkomoka ku Mana , nkaba naraje . Sinaje ku bwanjye , ni We wantumye .
43008043	Kuki mudasobanukirwa n’ibyo mvuga ? Ni uko mudashobora kwakira ijambo ryanjye .
43008044	Ubabyara koko ni Sekibi , none murashaka gukora ibyo so yifuza . Kuva mu ntangiriro yamye ari umwicanyi , kandi ntiyigeze aba mu kuri , kuko atigeze atunga ukuri . Igihe avuga ibinyoma , aba avuga ibiri ibye , kuko yamye ari umubeshyi , ndetse akaba na Sekinyoma .
43008045	None jye navuga ukuri , mukanga kwemera .
43008046	Muri mwe , ni nde wampamya icyaha ? Niba rero mvuga ukuri , mubuzwa n’iki kunyemera ?
43008047	Umuntu w’Imana yumva amagambo y’Imana . Ngaho mwamenya igituma mutumva , ni uko mutari ab’Imana . »
43008048	Abayahudi baramusubiza bati « Si ngaha twavuga ukuri , ko uri Umunyasamariya kandi ko wahanzweho na Sekibi ? »
43008049	Yezu arasubiza ati « Simpanzweho na Sekibi , ahubwo nubaha Data , naho mwe ntimunyubahe .
43008050	Jye simparanira ikuzo ryanjye , hari Undi uriharanira agaca n’urubanza .
43008051	Ndababwira ukuri koko : ukomera ku magambo yanjye , ntateze gupfa bibaho . »
43008052	Abayahudi baramubwira bati « Ngaha twamenya ko wahanzweho na Sekibi ! Abrahamu yarapfuye , n’abahanuzi barapfa . None wowe uravuga ngo ’ Ukomera ku magambo yanjye , ntazakorwaho n’urupfu bibaho . ’
43008053	Uzabe se uruta umubyeyi wacu Abrahamu wapfuye ? N’abahanuzi na bo barapfuye ! None ubwawe , wibwira ko uri iki ? »
43008054	Yezu arabasubiza ati « Niba ubwanjye niha ikuzo , ikuzo ryanjye ryaba ari ubusa . Data ni we umpa ikuzo , ari na we muvuga ngo ni Imana yacu .
43008055	Nyamara ntimumuzi , ariko jye ndamuzi ; ndamutse mvuze ko ntamuzi , naba ndi umubeshyi nkamwe . Ni koko ndamuzi kandi ngakomera ku ijambo rye .
43008056	Umubyeyi wanyu Abrahamu yahimbajwe no kubona umunsi wanjye , yarawubonye maze aranezerwa . »
43008057	Abayahudi baramubwira bati « Uba utaragira imyaka mirongo itanu , none ngo wabonye Abrahamu ! »
43008058	Yezu arababwira ati « Ndababwira ukuri koko : Abrahamu atarabaho nari ndiho . »
43008059	Ni bwo bafashe amabuye yo kumutera ; Yezu arihisha , nuko ava mu rugo rw'Ingoro y'Imana .
43009001	Yihitira abona umuntu wavutse ari impumyi .
43009002	Maze abigishwa be baramubaza bati « Mwigisha , uwacumuye ni nde , ari uyu muntu , ari n’ababyeyi be , kugira ngo avuke ari impumyi ? »
43009003	Yezu arabasubiza ati « Ari we , ari n’ababyeyi be , nta wacumuye , ahubwo ni ukugira ngo ibyo Imana ikora bimugaragarireho .
43009004	Ni ngombwa gukora imirimo y’Uwantumye hakibona ; ijoro riraje , kandi muri ryo nta wagira icyo akora .
43009005	Igihe nkiri ku isi , ndi urumuri rw’isi . »
43009006	Amaze kuvuga atyo , acira hasi , amacandwe ye ayatobesha akondo , agasiga ku maso y’impumyi .
43009007	Maze arayibwira ati « Jya kwiyuhagira mu cyuzi cya Silowe » ( bivuga ngo : uwatumwe ) . Nuko impumyi iragenda , iriyuhagira , ihindukira ibona .
43009008	Bituma abaturanyi n’abandi bari barabonye asabiriza bavuga bati « Uriya si wa wundi wajyaga yirirwa yicaye asabiriza ? »
43009009	Bamwe bati « Ni we » , abandi bati « Si we , ahubwo ni usa na we . » Arababwira ati « Ni jye . »
43009010	Ni bwo bamubwiye bati « Amaso yawe yahumutse ate ? »
43009011	Arabasubiza ati « Ni wa muntu bita Yezu : yatobye akondo , akansiga ku maso , maze arambwira ati ’ Jya mu cyuzi cya Silowe maze wiyuhagire . ’ Nuko njyayo , ndiyuhagira , none ndabona . »
43009012	Baramubwira bati « Uwo muntu ari hehe ? » Arabasubiza ati « Simpazi . »
43009013	Nuko uwahoze ari impumyi bamushyira Abafarizayi .
43009014	Hari ku munsi w’isabato igihe Yezu atobye akondo , agahumura amaso ye .
43009015	Abafarizayi na bo bongera kumubaza uko yahumutse . Arababwira ati « Yansize akondo ku maso , ndiyuhagira , none ndabona . »
43009016	Bamwe mu Bafarizayi baravuga bati « Uwo muntu ntakomoka ku Mana , kuko atubahiriza isabato . » Ariko abandi bati « Bishoboka bite ko umunyabyaha yakora ibitangaza nk’ibi ? » Ni bwo biciyemo ibice .
43009017	Barongera babwira impumyi bati « Wowe se , uwaguhumuye umuvugaho iki ? » Arababwira ati « Ni umuhanuzi . »
43009018	Abayahudi banga kwemera ko yari impumyi n’uko yahumutse , bigeza igihe bahamagaje ababyeyi be .
43009019	Barababaza bati « Uyu koko ni umwana wanyu muvuga ko yavutse ari impumyi ? Ubu se ahumutse ate ? »
43009020	Ababyeyi be barasubiza bati « Icyo tuzi , ni uko uyu ari umwana wacu kandi ko yavutse ari impumyi .
43009021	Uko byagenze kugira ngo abone ntitubizi , n’uwamuhumuye amaso ntitumuzi . Nimumwibarize , ni mukuru , niyivugire ubwe » .
43009022	Ababyeyi be bavuze batyo babitewe no gutinya Abayahudi , kuko Abayahudi bari babyumvikanyeho ko umuntu wese uzemera ko Yezu ari Kristu , bazamuca mu isengero .
43009023	Ni cyo cyateye ababyeyi be kuvuga bati « Arakuze , nimumwibarize . »
43009024	Abayahudi bongera guhamagara ubwa kabiri uwo muntu wahoze ari impumyi , baramubwira bati « Singiza Imana , twe tuzi ko uwo muntu ari umunyabyaha . »
43009025	Arababwira ati « Niba ari umunyabyaha , ibyo simbizi ; icyo nzi ni kimwe : ni uko nari impumyi none nkaba mbona ! »
43009026	Bongera kumubaza bati « Yakugenjereje ate ? Yaguhumuye amaso ate ? »
43009027	Arabasubiza ati « Nabibabwiye kandi ntimwabyumva , murashaka kongera kubyumvira iki ? Namwe se murashaka kuba abigishwa be ? »
43009028	Nuko bamuhunda ibitutsi , bati « Urakaba umwigishwa we , twe turi abigishwa ba Musa .
43009029	Tuzi ko Imana yavuganye na Musa , ariko we ntituzi aho aturuka . »
43009030	Wa muntu arabasubiza ati « Ibyo biratangaje , kuba mutazi aho aturuka kandi yampumuye amaso .
43009031	Tuzi neza ko Imana itumva abanyabyaha , tukamenya ko uwubaha Imana , agakora icyo ishaka , imwumva .
43009032	Kuva na kera kose nta wigeze yumva bavuga ko hari uwahumuye uwavutse ari impumyi .
43009033	Uwo muntu iyo adaturuka ku Mana , nta cyo aba yashoboye gukora . »
43009034	Baramusubiza bati « Wazikamye wese mu byaha ukivuka , none ni wowe ugiye kutwigisha ? » Nuko bamusuka hanze .
43009035	Yezu aza kumva ko bamuroshye hanze . Bahuye , Yezu aramubaza ati « Wemera Umwana w’umuntu ? »
43009036	We arasubiza ati « Nyakubahwa , ni nde ngo mwemere ? »
43009037	Yezu aramubwira ati « Wamubonye , kandi ni We muvugana . »
43009038	Ni bwo avuze ati « Ndemera , Nyagasani . » Nuko arapfukama aramuramya .
43009039	Yezu aramubwira ati « Naje mu nsi nje guca urubanza , kugira ngo abatabona bahumuke , maze ababona babe impumyi . »
43009040	Bamwe mu Bafarizayi bari kumwe na we babyumvise , baramubwira bati « Natwe se turi impumyi ? »
43009041	Yezu arabasubiza ati « Iyo muba impumyi , nta cyaha mwajyaga kugira . None ubwo mugize ngo ’ Turabona ’ , icyaha cyanyu kigumyeho .
43010001	Ndababwira ukuri koko : umuntu utinjirira mu irembo ry’urugo rw’intama , ahubwo akuririra ahandi , aba ari umujura n’igisambo .
43010002	Unyura mu irembo we , aba ari umushumba w’intama .
43010003	Uwugarira irembo , aramwugururira , n’intama zikumva ijwi rye ; maze agahamagara intama ze mu mazina yazo , nuko akazahura .
43010004	Intama ze zose iyo amaze kuzikura mu rugo , azijya imbere , zikamukurikira , kuko ziba zisanzwe zizi ijwi rye .
43010005	Ntizikurikira uw’ahandi , ahubwo ziramuhunga , kuko ziba zitazi ijwi ry’ab’ahandi . »
43010006	Yezu yabahaye icyo kigereranyo , ariko bo ntibamenya icyo yashakaga kubabwira .
43010007	Nuko Yezu ati « Ndababwira ukuri koko : ni jye rembo ry’intama .
43010008	Abandi bose baje mbere yanjye , ni abajura n’ibisambo , n’intama zanze kubumva .
43010009	Ni jye rembo ; uzanyuraho yinjira azakizwa , azishyira yizane kandi abone urwuri .
43010010	Umujura agenzwa no kwiba , no kwica , no kurimbura . Jye rero nazanywe no kugira ngo intama zigire ubugingo , kandi zibugire busagambye .
43010011	Ni jye mushumba mwiza . Umushumba mwiza yigurana intama ze .
43010012	Naho umucanshuro utari umushumba , ntabe na nyir’intama , abona ikirura kije , agatererana intama agahunga ; ikirura kikaziraramo kikazitatanya .
43010013	Agenza atyo abitewe n’uko aba ari umucanshuro , maze intama ntizibe zimushishikaje .
43010014	Ni jye mushumba mwiza ; nzi intama zanjye , na zo zikamenya ,
43010015	mbese nk’uko Data anzi , nanjye kandi nkamenya Data . Ndetse nemera guhara ubugingo bwanjye , nkabutangira intama zanjye .
43010016	Mfite n’izindi ntama zitari muri uru rugo , na zo ngomba kuzizana zikazumva ijwi ryanjye , maze hakaba igikumba kimwe n’umushumba umwe .
43010017	Ngicyo igitera Data kunkunda , kuko ntanga ubuzima bwanjye kugira ngo mbusubirane .
43010018	Nta we ubunyaga , ahubwo ni jye ubwanjye ubutanga . Mfite ububasha bwo kubutanga nkagira n’ububasha bwo kubwisubiza . Iryo ni itegeko nahawe na Data . »
43010019	Abayahudi bongera kwicamo ibice babitewe n’ayo magambo .
43010020	Benshi muri bo bati « Yahanzweho na roho mbi , ndetse yasaze ; mumuteze amatwi mushaka iki ? »
43010021	Abandi ariko bati « Aya magambo si ay’uwahanzweho na roho mbi ; roho mbi yashobora ite guhumura amaso y’impumyi ? »
43010022	I Yeruzalemu bahimbazaga umunsi mukuru wo gutaha Ingoro y’Imana . Hari mu itumba .
43010023	Yezu yagendagendaga mu Ngoro yImana mu nsi y’Ibaraza rya Salomoni .

43014008	Filipo ni ko guhita amubwira ati « Nyagasani , twereke So , biraba biduhagije . »
43014009	Yezu aramusubiza ati « Filipo we , n’iminsi yose tumaranye , ukaba utanzi ? Uwambonye aba yabonye na Data . Ushobora ute kuvuga ngo twereke So ?
43014010	Rwose ntimwemera ko ndi muri Data , na Data akaba muri jye ? Amagambo mbabwira sinyavuga ku bwanjye , ahubwo Data uhora muri jye , ni we ukora imirimo ye .
43014011	Nimwemere ko ndi muri Data , na Data akaba muri jye . Byibuze nimwemezwe n’ibyo nkora .
43014012	Ndababwira ukuri koko : unyemera azakora imirimo nkora , ndetse azakora n’ibitambutseho , kuko ngiye kwa Data .

43014014	Nimugira icyo musaba mu izina ryanjye , nzagikora .
43014015	Niba munkunda koko , muzubaha amategeko yanjye .

43014017	Uwo ni Roho Nyir’ukuri isi idashobora kwakira , kuko itamubona kandi ntimumenye . Mwebwe ariko muramuzi , kuko abana namwe kandi akababamo .
43014018	Sinzabasiga muri imfubyi , nzagaruka mbasange .
43014019	Hasigaye igihe gito isi ntizongere kumbona . Ariko mwe muzambona , kuko ndiho kandi namwe mukazabaho .
43014020	Uwo munsi muzamenya ko mba muri Data , kandi namwe mukaba muri jye , nk’uko nanjye ndi muri mwe .
43014021	Umenya amategeko yanjye kandi akayubaha , ni we unkunda . Kandi rero unkunda , azakundwa na Data , nanjye nzamukunda kandi nzamwiyereka . »
43014022	Yuda utari Isikariyoti aramubaza ati « Nyagasani , utewe n’iki kutwiyereka , ntiwiyereke isi ? »
43014023	Yezu aramusubiza ati « Umuntu unkunda , azubaha ijambo ryanjye , Data azamukunda , maze tuzaze iwe tubane na we .
43014024	Utankunda ntamenya n’ijambo ryanjye ; kandi rero ijambo mwumvise si iryanjye , ni irya Data wantumye .
43014025	Ibyo mbibabwiye nkiri kumwe namwe ,
43014026	ariko Umuvugizi Roho Mutagatifu , Data azohereza mu izina ryanjye , ni we uzabigisha byose , kandi abibutse n’ibyo nababwiye byose .
43014027	Mbasigiye amahoro , mbahaye amahoro yanjye . Sinyabahaye nk’uko isi iyatanga . Ntimukuke umutima kandi ntimugire ubwoba .
43014028	Mwumvise ko nababwiye nti ’ Ndagiye kandi nzagaruka mbasange ’ . Iyaba mwankundaga , mwakwishimiye ko nsanze Data , kuko Data anduta .

43015001	Ndi umuzabibu w’ukuri , naho Data akaba umuhinzi .
43015002	Ishami ryose riterera imbuto muri jye , araritema ; naho ishami ryera imbuto , araryicira agira ngo rirusheho kwera imbuto .
43015003	Mwe murakeye kubera ijambo nababwiye .
43015004	Nimube rero muri jyewe , nanjye mbe muri mwe . Uko ishami ridashobora kwera imbuto ku bwaryo ritari ku muzabibu , namwe ni ko mutakwera mutandimo .
43015005	Jye ndi umuzabibu , mwe mukaba amashami . Uba rero muri jye , nanjye nkaba muri we , yera imbuto nyinshi ; koko tutari kumwe nta cyo mwashobora .
43015006	Utaba muri jye , azajugunywa nk’ishami ritera , maze yumagane , kandi bene ayo mashami barayasakuma , bakayajugunya mu muriro , agashya .
43015007	Nimumbamo n’amagambo yanjye akababamo , muzasabe icyo muzashaka cyose muzagihabwa .
43015008	Igihesha Data ikuzo ni uko mwakwera imbuto nyinshi , mukaba n’abigishwa banjye .
43015009	Uko Data yankunze , ni ko nanjye nabakunze . Nimugume mu rukundo rwanjye .
43015010	Nimwubaha amategeko yanjye , muzaguma mu rukundo rwanjye , nk’uko nanjye nubaha amategeko ya Data , maze nkaguma mu rukundo rwe .
43015011	Ibyo mbibabwiye ngira ngo ibyishimo byanjye bibabemo , kandi ngo ibyishimo byanyu bisendere .
43015012	Ngiri itegeko mbahaye : nimujye mukundana nk’uko nanjye nabakunze .
43015013	Nta wagira urukundo ruruta urw’umuntu uhara amagara ye kubera incuti ze .

43015017	Icyo mbategetse ni uko mukundana .
43015018	Isi nibazira , mumenye ko ari jye yabanje kwanga .
43015019	Iyo muba ab’isi , isi yakunze ikiri icyayo ; ariko kuko mutari ab’isi , kandi nkaba narabatoye mbakura mu isi , ni cyo isi izabaziza .
43015020	Mwibuke ijambo nababwiye ko ’ Nta mugaragu uruta shebuja . ’ Niba barantoteje namwe bazabatoteza , niba barubashye amagambo yanjye , n’ayanyu bazayubaha .

43016020	Ndababwira ukuri koko : mwe muzarira ndetse muganye , ariko isi yo izishima . Mwe muzagira ishavu , ariko ishavu ryanyu rizabaviramo ibyishimo .

43017021	kugira ngo bose babe umwe . Nk’uko wowe , Dawe , uri muri jye , nanjye nkaba muri wowe , ndasaba ko na bo bunga ubumwe muri twe , kugira ngo isi yemere ko ari wowe wantumye .

43019009	Asubira mu rugo , maze abaza Yezu ati « Ukomoka he ? » Yezu ariko ntiyagira icyo amusubiza .

43019012	Pilato yumvise ibyo , ashaka uko yamurekura , ariko Abayahudi batera hejuru , bati « Uramutse umurekuye , uraba utakibaye incuti ya Kayizari . Uwigira umwami wese , aba arwanya Kayizari . »
43019013	Nuko Pilato amaze kumva ayo magambo , ajyana Yezu hanze , yicara ku ntebe y’ubucamanza ahantu hiherereye , hitwa « Litostrotosi » , mu gihebureyi « Gabata » .

43019016	Nuko aramutanga , ngo bamubambe ku musaraba .
43019017	Nuko bafata Yezu , maze agenda yikoreye umusaraba we , yerekeza ahantu hitwa « ku Kibihanga » , mu gihebureyi hakitwa « Gologota » .
43019018	Aho ni ho bamubambye ku musaraba , ari kumwe n’abandi babiri , umwe hino , undi hirya , Yezu we akaba hagati .
43019019	Nuko Pilato yandikisha itangazo , arimanikisha hejuru y’umusaraba ; hari handitse ngo « Yezu Umunyanazareti , umwami w’Abayahudi . »
43019020	Abayahudi benshi basoma iryo tangazo , kuko aho hantu Yezu yabambwe hari hafi y’umugi kandi ryari ryanditse mu gihebureyi , mu kilatini no mu kigereki .

43019023	Abasirikare bamaze kubamba Yezu , bafata imyenda ye bayicamo imigabane ine , umusirikare wese ajyana umugabane we . Hari n’ikanzu , ariko iyo kanzu ntigire iteranyirizo , kuko yari iboshywe buzima kuva hejuru kugera hasi . Bajya inama bati
43019024	« Ntituyitanyure , ahubwo reka tuyikorereho ubufindo , tumenye uri bube nyirayo . » Bityo harangira Ibyanditswe , ngo « Bigabanije imyambaro yanjye , maze kanzu yanjye bayikoreraho ubufindo . » Nguko uko abasirikare babigenjeje .

43019029	Aho hakaba hari hateretse urweso rwuzuye divayi irura . Bahambira ku rubingo icyangwe cyinitswe muri iyo divayi irura , bacyegereza umunwa we .

43019031	Ubwo hari ku munsi w’Umwiteguro wa Pasika ; kugira ngo rero imirambo itaguma ku misaraba kuri sabato , kandi iyo sabato ari umunsi mukuru cyane , Abayahudi binginga Pilato ngo bavune amaguru yabo , maze imirambo bayimanure .

43019033	ariko bageze kuri Yezu , basanga yapfuye , we ntibirirwa bamuvuna amaguru ;
43019034	ahubwo umwe mu basirikare amutikura icumu mu rubavu , maze ako kanya havamo amaraso n’amazi .
43019035	Uwabibonye ni we ubyemeza , kandi icyemezo cye ni ukuri ; na we azi ko avuga ukuri kugira ngo namwe mwemere .
