44002017	’ Mu minsi ya nyuma , — uwo ari Nyagasani ubivuga — , nzasendereza Umwuka wanjye ku cyitwa ikiremwa cyose . Abahungu banyu n’abakobwa banyu bazahanure , urubyiruko rwanyu ruzabonekerwe n’abasaza banyu bazabonere mu nzozi .
44002018	Koko muri iyo minsi , abagaragu banjye n’abaja banjye , nzabasenderezamo Umwuka wanjye maze bahanure .
44002019	Nzakora ibintu bitangaje hejuru mu kirere , n’ibimenyetso bikomeye hasi ku isi : hazaboneka amaraso , umuriro n’inkingi y’umwotsi .
44002020	Izuba rizijima n’ukwezi guhinduke amaraso , mbere y’uko haza Umunsi wa Nyagasani , Umunsi ukomeye kandi w’ikuzo .
44002021	Ubwo rero umuntu wese uziyambaza izina rya Nyagasani , azakizwa . ’
44002022	Yemwe Bayisraheli , nimutege amatwi amagambo yanjye : Yezu w’i Nazareti , uwo muntu Imana yemeje muri mwe , imukoresha ibitangaza , ibikorwa n’ibimenyetso bikomeye rwagati muri mwe , nk’uko mubizi ubwanyu ,
44002023	uwo muntu rero , bikurikije umugambi udakuka w’Imana , amaze gutangwa , mwaramwishe mumubambisha ku musaraba amaboko y’abagome .
44002024	Ariko Imana yaramuzuye , imubohora ku ngoyi z’urupfu kuko bitashobokaga ko rumuherana .
44002025	Koko kandi , Dawudi yavuze ibimwerekeyeho ati ’ Narebaga Nyagasani imbere yanjye ubudahwema , kuko ari iburyo bwanjye kugira ngo ntadandabirana .
44002026	Ni cyo gituma umutima wanjye uri mu byishimo , n’ururimi rwanjye rukaba runezerewe , byongeye kandi nzaruhukana icyizere ,
44002027	kuko utazatererana ubugingo bwanjye mu kuzimu , kandi ntuzatume intungane yawe imenyana n’ubushanguke .
44002028	Wamenyesheje inzira zigana mu bugingo , unyuzuzamo ibyishimo unyereka uruhanga rwawe . ’
44002029	Bavandimwe , nta cyambuza kubabwira nta shiti ko umukurambere wacu Dawudi yapfuye , ko yahambwe ndetse n’imva ye ikaba ikiri iwacu kugeza uyu munsi .
44002030	Nyamara , kuba yari umuhanuzi kandi yazirikanaga ko Imana yamusezeranyishije indahiro kuzicaza ku ntebe ye y’ubwami uwo mu bamukomokaho ,
44002031	yabonye atyo mbere y’igihe iby’izuka rya Kristu , maze amuvugaho ati ’ Ntiyatereranywe ikuzimu kandi umubiri we ntiwigeze umenyana n’ubushanguke . ’
44002032	Yezu uwo rero Imana yaramuzuye , twese turi abahamya babyo .
44002033	Aho amariye gukuzwa n’ububasha bw’Imana , no guhabwa na Se Roho Mutagatifu wasezeranywe , amusendereza mu bantu nk’uko mubibona kandi mubyumva .
44002034	Dawudi we n’ubwo atazamutse mu ijuru , nyamara yaravuze ati ’ Nyagasani yabwiye Umutegetsi wanjye ati : Icara iburyo bwanjye ,
44002035	kugeza ko abanzi bawe , mbagira akabaho ukandagizaho ibirenge byawe . ’
44002036	Nuko rero , inzu yose ya Israheli nimenye idashidikanya ko uwo Yezu mwabambye , Imana yamugize Umutegetsi n’Umukiza . »
44002037	Ngo bumve ayo magambo barakangarana , babaza Petero n’izindi Ntumwa bati « Bavandimwe , dukore iki ? »
44002038	Petero arabasubiza ati « Nimwisubireho , buri muntu muri mwe abatizwe mu izina rya Yezu Kristu kugira ngo ababarirwe ibyaha bye , kandi muhabwe ingabire ya Roho Mutagatifu .
44002039	Kuko Isezerano ari mwe ryagenewe kimwe n’abana banyu , ndetse n’abari kure bose , n’abandi batabarika uko Nyagasani Imana yacu azabihamagarira . »
44002040	Ababwira n’andi magambo menshi yo kubemeza no kubakomeza , agira ati « Nimwirokore , mwitandukanye n’aba bantu bayobye . »
44002041	Nuko abemeye izo nyigisho barabatizwa , uwo munsi biyongeraho abantu bagera ku bihumbi bitatu .
44002042	Bahoraga bashishikariye kumva inyigisho z’Intumwa , gushyira hamwe kivandimwe , kumanyurira hamwe umugati no gusenga .
44002043	Abantu bose bagiraga ubwoba kubera ibitangaza n’ibimenyetso bikomeye byakorwaga n’Intumwa .
44002044	Abemera bose bari bashyize hamwe , n’ibyo batunze byose bakabigira rusange .
44002045	Bagurishaga amasambu yabo n’ibintu byabo , bose bakagabana ikiguzi cyabyo bakurikije ibyo buri muntu akeneye .
44002046	Iminsi yose bashishikariraga kujya mu Ngoro y’Imana bashyize hamwe , bakamanyurira umugati imuhira , bagasangira mu byishimo no mu bwiyoroshye bw’umutima .
44002047	Basingizaga Imana kandi bagashimwa n’abantu bose ; nuko Nyagasani akagwiza uko bukeye umubare w’abacunguwe .
44003001	Umunsi umwe , saa cyenda ari cyo gihe cy’isengesho rusange , Petero na Yohani bazamuka bajya mu Ngoro y’Imana .
44003002	Hakaba umuntu wavutse ari ikirema , buri munsi bakamuzana imbere y’umuryango w’Ingoro witwa « Uw’Uburanga » , kugira ngo asabe imfashanyo abinjiraga mu Ngoro bose .
44003003	Ngo abone Petero na Yohani bagiye kwinjira mu Ngoro , abasaba imfashanyo .
44003004	Nuko Petero , ari hamwe na Yohani , aramwitegereza maze aramubwira ati « Ngaho turebe ! »
44003005	Uwo muntu agumya kubahanga amaso , kuko yari ategereje ko hari icyo bari bumuhe .
44003006	Petero aramubwira ati « Ari zahabu , ari na feza , nta byo mfite ; ariko icyo mfite ndakiguhaye : mu izina rya Yezu Kristu w’i Nazareti , haguruka ugende ! »
44003007	Nuko amufata ikiganza cy’iburyo aramuhagurutsa . Ako kanya ibirenge bye n’utugombambari birakomera ;
44003008	arabaduka , arahagarara , aratambuka yinjirana na bo mu Ngoro y'Imana , agenda asimbuka kandi asingiza Imana .
44003009	Nuko rubanda rwose ngo bamubone agenda kandi asingiza Imana ,
44003010	baramumenya : koko yari wa wundi wajyaga asabiriza , yicaye imbere y’Umuryango w’Ingoro y'Imana witwa " Uw'Uburanga " . Nuko abantu barumirwa , batangazwa n’ibimubayeho .
44003011	Kubera ko uwo muntu yanze kuvirira Petero na Yohani , bitangaza cyane rubanda rwose , biruka babasanga ahitwa ku « Ibaraza rya Salomoni » .
44003012	Petero abibonye ni ko kubwira rubanda ati « Bantu ba Israheli , ni iki gitumye mutangazwa n’ibimaze kuba ? Cyangwa se ni iki gitumye muduhanga amaso , nk’aho duhaye uyu muntu kugenda ku bw’ububasha bwacu cyangwa ku bw’ubutungane bwacu bwite ?
44003013	Imana ya Abrahamu , ya Izaki na Yakobo , Imana y’abakurambere bacu yakujije umugaragu wayo Yezu mwebwe mwatanze , mukamwihakanira imbere ya Pilato kandi we yari yiyemeje kumurekura .
44003014	Mwihakanye Umutagatifu n’Intungane , maze musaba ko babarekurira umwicanyi .
44003015	Mwicishije Umugenga w’ubugingo , ariko Imana yamuzuye mu bapfuye , turi abagabo bo kubihamya .
44003016	Kubera ko twiringiye izina rya Yezu , iryo zina ni ryo ryakomeje uyu muntu mubona kandi muzi ; maze ukwemera gukomoka kuri Yezu kumusubiza ubuzima bwe bwose mu maso yanyu mwese .
44003017	None rero , bavandimwe , nzi yuko ibyo mwabikoze mubitewe n’ubujiji kimwe n’abatware banyu .
44003018	Nyamara Imana yujuje ityo ibyo yari yaravugishije Abahanuzi bose mbere y’uko biba , ko Kristu yagombaga kubabara .
44003019	Nimwisubireho rero kandi mugarukire Imana , kugira ngo ibyaha byanyu bihanagurwe ;
44003020	bityo hazabeho ibihe by’ihumure muhawe na Nyagasani , ubwo azaboherereza Kristu wabagenewe , ari we Yezu ,
44003021	Uwo ijuru rigomba kwakira kuzageza ku bihe by’ivugururwa ry’ibintu byose : ngibyo ibyo Imana yavugishije Abahanuzi bayo batagatifu bo mu bihe bya kera .
44003022	Koko Musa yaravuze ati ’ Nyagasani Imana azababonera mu bavandimwe banyu Umuhanuzi umeze nkanjye ; muzamwumvire mu byo azababwira byose .
44003023	Umuntu wese utazumvira uwo Muhanuzi , azacibwa mu muryango wayo . ’
44003024	Kandi n’Abahanuzi bose , uhereye kuri Samweli no ku bamusimbuye , bavuze iby’iy’iminsi turimo .
44003025	Ni mwebwe abaragwa b’Abahanuzi , n’ab’Isezerano Imana yagiranye n’abasekuruza bacu igihe ibwiye Abrahamu iti ’ Imiryango yose y’isi izaherwa umugisha mu rubyaro rwawe . ’
44003026	Ni mwebwe mbere na mbere Imana yahingukirije Umugaragu wayo , iramuboherereza kugira ngo abazanire umugisha ; bityo buri muntu muri mwe abone kuzinukwa ibibi yakoraga . »
44004001	Igihe Petero na Yohani bariho babwira rubanda , abaherezabitambo , umutegeka w’Ingoro n’Abasaduseyi baraza , barabegera .
44004002	Bari barakajwe cyane no kubona bigisha rubanda kandi banamamaza izuka ry’abapfuye , bahereye kuri Yezu .
44004003	Nuko barabafatisha babaraza mu buroko , kuko bwari bugorobye .
44004004	Nyamara abenshi mu bari bumvise izo nyigisho baremera , umubare wabo ugera nko ku bantu ibihumbi bitanu .
44004005	Bukeye bw’uwo munsi , abatware b’Abayahudi , abakuru b’umuryango n’abigishamategeko bakoranira i Yeruzalemu .
44004006	Hari kandi na Ana , umuherezabitambo mukuru , na Kayifa , na Yohani , na Alegisanderi , n’abo mu muryango w’umuherezabitambo mukuru bose .
44004007	Nuko batumiza Petero na Yohani , batangira kubabaza bati « Biriya mwabikoze ku buhe bubasha cyangwa se ku bw’irihe zina ? »
44004008	Ubwo Petero yuzuye Roho Mutagatifu arabasubiza ati
44004009	« Batware , namwe bakuru b’umuryango , uyu munsi turabazwa iby’ineza yagiriwe ikirema , no gusobanura uburyo uyu muntu yakijijwe .
44004010	Nimumenye neza rero , mwebwe mwese n’umuryango wose wa Israheli , ko izina rya Yezu Kristu w’i Nazareti mwebwe ubwanyu mwabambye , Imana ikamuzura mu bapfuye , ari ryo uyu muntu akesha kuba ahagaze imbere yanyu ari mutaraga .
44004011	Yezu uwo ni we rya buye ryajugunywe namwe abubatsi , nyamara rigahinduka insanganyarukuta .
44004012	Bikaba rero nta wundi wundi twakesha umukiro usibye we , kuko ku isi nta rindi zina abantu bahawe , ngo abe ari ryo turonkeramo uburokorwe . »
44004013	Ngo babone ukuntu Petero na Yohani bavuga bashize amanga , kandi bazi ko ari abantu batize , ahubwo ari rubanda rusanzwe , barumirwa . Baza kwibuka ko bagendanaga na Yezu ;
44004014	banitegereje uwo muntu wakijijwe wari uhagararanye na bo , babura icyo babasubiza .
44004015	Nuko bategeka ko babavana imbere y’Inama nkuru , barabazanya bati
44004016	« Bariya bantu tubagenze dute ? Dore bakoze igitangaza kiragaragara , cyanamenyekanye mu batuye Yeruzalemu bose kandi ntidushobora kugihakana .
44004017	Ariko kugira ngo bidakomeza kwamamara muri rubanda , nimucyo tubakange , tubabuze kuzongera kugira uwo babwira bitwaje iryo zina . »
44004018	Ni ko kubahamagaza , bababuza rwose kuzongera kuvuga cyangwa kwigisha mu izina rya Yezu .
44004019	Ariko Petero na Yohani barabasubiza bati « Icyaba kiboneye mu maso y’Imana ni ikihe : ari ukubumvira cyangwa se kumvira Imana ? Ngaho namwe nimwihitiremo !
44004020	Twe rero ntidushobora guceceka ibyo twiboneye kandi tukabyiyumvira . »
44004021	Bamaze kubuka inabi barabarekura , kuko babuze uko babahana kubera rubanda basingizaga Imana bakurije ku byari byabaye .
44004022	Koko kandi , uwo muntu wari wakijijwe ku buryo bw’agatangaza yari arengeje imyaka mirongo ine .
44004023	Petero na Yohani bamaze kurekurwa basanga bagenzi babo , babatekerereza ibyo abatware b’abaherezabitambo n’abakuru b’umuryango bababwiye .
44004024	Ngo bamare kubyumva , bose hamwe n’umutima umwe basenga Imana , bagira bati « Nyagasani , ni wowe waremye ijuru n’isi , inyanja n’ibiyirimo byose ;
44004025	ni wowe kandi ku bwa Roho Mutagatifu wavugiye mu munwa w’umukurambere wacu Dawudi , umugaragu wawe , uti ’ Ni iki giteye amahanga gusakabaka , n’imiryango gutekereza ibidafite umumaro ?
44004026	Abami b’isi barahagurutse n’abatware barakorana , kugira ngo barwanye Nyagasani n’Uwo yisigiye amavuta y’ubutore . ’
44004027	Ni ukuri rwose , Herodi na Ponsiyo Pilato , kumwe n’amahanga yose n’imiryango yose ya Israheli , bakoraniye muri uyu mugi kugira ngo barwanye Yezu , umugaragu wawe mutagatifu , uwo wisigiye amavuta y’ubutore .
44004028	Barangiza batyo imigambi yawe yose wari waragennye kuva kera , ku bw’ububasha bwawe n’ubushake bwawe .
44004029	None rero , Nyagasani , witegereze ibyo badukangisha byose , maze uhe abagaragu bawe kuvuga ijambo ryawe bashize amanga .
44004030	Urambure ikiganza cyawe maze indwara zikizwe , haboneke ibimenyetso n’ibitangaza mu izina rya Yezu , umugaragu wawe mutagatifu . »
44004031	Nuko ngo bamare gusenga , aho bari bateraniye hahinda umushyitsi ; bose buzura Roho Mutagatifu , maze bamamaza ijambo ry’Imana bashize amanga .
44004032	Imbaga y’abemera yari ifite umutima umwe n’amatwara amwe , kandi nta n’umwe wibwiraga ko icyo atunze cyose ari icye bwite , ahubwo byose byari rusange kuri bo .
44004033	Nuko Intumwa zikomeza guhamya izuka rya Nyagasani Yezu n’ububasha bukomeye , kandi ubugwaneza bwinshi bwari bubuzuyemo bose .
44004034	Koko rero , nta mukene wababagamo , kuko ababaga bafite amasambu cyangwa amazu babigurishaga , bakazana ikiguzi cyabyo ,
44004035	bakagishyikiriza Intumwa . Nuko bakabisaranganya , bakurikije ibyo buri muntu akeneye .
44004036	Bityo na Yozefu , uwo Intumwa zari zarahimbye Barinaba — ari byo kuvuga Imaragahinda — , wari n’umulevi ukomoka i Shipure , akaba yari afite umurima .
44004037	Agurisha uwo murima maze ikiguzi cyawo agishyikiriza Intumwa .
44005001	Ariko umuntu witwa Ananiya , amaze kubyumvikanaho n’umugore we Safira , agurisha isambu ye ;
44005002	hanyuma yisigira igice cy’ikiguzi cyayo ndetse n’umugore we abyemeye , maze ajyana igice gisigaye agishyikiriza Intumwa .
44005003	Petero aramubwira ati « Ananiya , ni iki cyatumye Sekinyoma agutaha mu mutima ? Wabeshye Roho Mutagatifu maze usigarana igice cy’ikiguzi cy’isambu yawe .
44005004	Ntiwashoboraga se kugumana isambu yawe ntuyigurishe , cyangwa n’aho umariye kuyigurisha , ntiwari kugumana ikiguzi cyayo uko ubishaka ? Uwo mugambi waje ute mu mutima wawe ? Si abantu wabeshye , ahubwo wabeshye Imana . »
44005005	Ananiya ngo yumve ayo magambo , yitura hasi , araca ; maze ababyumvise bose bashya ubwoba .
44005006	Nuko abasore baraza baramupfunya , maze bajya kumuhamba .
44005007	Hashize nk’amasaha atatu , umugore we na we araza , ariko atazi ibyabaye .
44005008	Petero aramubaza ati « Ni ko ye , koko iki ni cyo kiguzi mwagurishije isambu yanyu ? » Umugore arasubiza ati « Ni icyo ngicyo . »
44005009	Petero ni ko kumubwira ati « Mwaje guhuza mute umugambi , kugira ngo musembure Roho wa Nyagasani ? Umva imirindi y’abavuye guhamba umugabo wawe bageze ku muryango ; nawe bagiye kukujyana . »
44005010	Ako kanya agwa imbere ya Petero , araca . Ba basore ngo binjire basanga amaze gupfa , na we baramujyana bamuhamba iruhande rw’umugabo we .
44005011	Kiliziya yose n’abumvise ibyabaye bose bashya ubwoba .
44005012	Intumwa zikomeza gutanga ibimenyetso no gukora ibitangaza byinshi muri rubanda , kandi bose hamwe n’umutima umwe bagakoranira mu nsi y’Ibaraza rya Salomoni .
44005013	Ariko n’ubwo rubanda babashimaga , ntihagire n’umwe utinyuka kubegera .
44005014	Nyamara abantu batabarika , abagabo n’abagore , bagakomeza kwiyongera ku bemera Nyagasani .
44005015	Byageraga n’aho bazana abarwayi mu mihanda y’umugi , bakabaryamisha ku mariri cyangwa mu ngobyi kugira ngo Petero naza kuhanyura , nibura igicucu cye kigere kuri umwe muri bo .
44005016	Ndetse n’imbaga nyamwinshi y’abantu bagashika , baturutse mu turere dukikije Yeruzalemu , bazanye abarwayi n’abantu bahanzweho na za roho mbi , maze bose bagakira .
44005017	Nuko umuherezabitambo mukuru kimwe n’abari kumwe na we bose — ari byo kuvuga abo mu gatsiko k’Abasaduseyi — bashengurwa n’ishyari ;
44005018	bafatisha Intumwa , bazishyira mu buroko rusange .
44005019	Nyamara muri iryo joro , Umumalayika wa Nyagasani akingura inzugi z’uburoko , abakuramo maze arababwira ati
44005020	« Nimugende muhagarare mu Ngoro y’Imana , maze mubwire rubanda ayo magambo yose azabahesha ubugingo ! »
44005021	Ngo bamare kubyumva , mu museso binjira mu Ngoro , batangira kwigisha . Umuherezabitambo mukuru kimwe n’abari kumwe na we baraza , bahamagaza Inama nkuru igizwe n’abakuru bose b’Abayisraheli ; ni ko gutuma ngo bajye gushaka Intumwa mu buroko .
44005022	Abagaragu baragenda ; ngo bagere mu buroko ntibabasangamo . Nuko bagaruka bababwira bati
44005023	« Twasanze uburoko bufunze neza n’abarinzi bahagaze imbere y’imiryango , ariko dukinguye ntitwagira n’umwe dusangamo . »
44005024	Ngo babyumve , umutegeka w’Ingoro n’abatware b’abaherezabitambo barashoberwa , bibaza uko byabagendekeye .
44005025	Ariko haza umuntu arababwira ati « Dore ba bantu mwari mwashyize mu buroko bahagaze mu Ngoro kandi bariho barigisha rubanda . »
44005026	Nuko umutegeka w’Ingoro ajyana n’abagaragu be kuzana Intumwa , ariko batazakuye , kuko batinyaga ko rubanda babatera amabuye .
44005027	Barabazana rero babahagarika imbere y’Inama nkuru . Umuherezabitambo mukuru arababaza ati
44005028	« Twari twarabihanangirije dukomeje kutazongera kwigisha mwitwaje iryo zina , none dore Yeruzalemu yose mwayujujemo inyigisho zanyu . Murashaka rero kuduhamya amaraso y’uwo muntu ? »
44005029	Petero n’izindi Ntumwa barabasubiza bati « Tugomba kumvira Imana kuruta abantu .
44005030	Imana y’abasekuruza bacu yazuye Yezu , uwo mwishe mumumanitse ku giti .
44005031	Ni we Imana yakurishije ububasha bwayo ngo abe Umutegetsi n’Umukiza , kugira ngo aronkere Israheli ukwisubiraho n’ibabarirwa ry’ibyaha .
44005032	Turi abagabo bo kubihamya , twe na Roho Mutagatifu Imana yahaye abayumvira . »
44005033	Bo ngo babyumve , umujinya urabasya maze batekereza kubica .
44005034	Ariko mu Nama nkuru hahaguruka umugabo w’Umufarizayi witwa Gamaliyeli , yari umwigishamategeko wubahwaga n’abantu bose ; nuko ategeka ko Intumwa zahezwa akanya gato .
44005035	Hanyuma arababwira ati « Bayisraheli , muritondere ibyo mugiye kugirira bariya bantu !
44005036	Dore hambere aha hadutse uwitwa Tewudasi ; aza avuga ko ari umuntu ukomeye , maze abantu nka magana ane baramuyoboka . Nyamara yamaze kwicwa , abari baramuyobotse baratatana , ibyo yari yatangiye birayoyoka .
44005037	Nyuma y’uwo , mu minsi y’ibarura , haduka Yuda w’Umunyagalileya , akurikirwa n’abantu benshi . Ariko na we aza kwicwa , abari baramuyobotse bose baratatana .
44005038	None rero mbibabwire : ntimugire icyo mutwara bariya bantu , nimubareke bagende . Niba umugambi wabo n’ibikorwa byabo bikomoka ku bantu , bizayoyoka ku bwabyo .
44005039	Ariko kandi niba bikomoka ku Mana , ntimuzashobora kubisenya . Muramenye , hato mutavaho murwanya Imana . » Nuko iyo nama barayemera ,
44005040	bahamagara Intumwa bazikubita ibiboko , bazibuza rwose kongera kwigisha mu izina rya Yezu , maze barazirekura .
44005041	Intumwa ngo zive mu Nama nkuru , zigenda zishimye kuko zagize ihirwe ryo kugirirwa nabi , zizira izina rya Yezu .
44005042	Nuko buri munsi ntizisibe kwigishiriza mu Ngoro y’Imana no mu ngo , zamamaza Inkuru Nziza ya Kristu Yezu .
44006001	Muri iyo minsi , umubare w’abigishwa ukomeza kwiyongera ; nuko abavugaga ikigereki muri bo batangira kwinubira Abahebureyi , kuko abapfakazi babo batitabwagaho uko bikwiye mu igabura rya buri munsi .
44006002	Nuko ba Cumi na babiri bahamagaza ikoraniro ry’abigishwa , barababwira bati « Ntibikwiye ko tureka ijambo ry’Imana ngo tujye mu byo kugabura .
44006003	None rero , bavandimwe , nimwishakemo abagabo barindwi b’inyangamugayo buzuye Roho Mutagatifu n’ubuhanga , maze tubashinge uwo murimo .
44006004	Naho twebwe tuzagumya kwibanda ubudahwema ku isengesho no ku murimo wo kwigisha ijambo ry’Imana . »
44006005	Iyo nama ishimisha ikoraniro ryose ; batora Sitefano , umuntu wuzuye ukwemera na Roho Mutagatifu , batora na Filipo na Porokori , Nikanori na Timoni , Parumena na Nikola wo muri Antiyokiya wari umuyoboke w’idini ry’Abayahudi .
44006006	Maze babashyira Intumwa ; zimaze kubasabira , zibaramburiraho ibiganza .
44006007	Nuko ijambo ry’Imana rikomeza gukwira hose , umubare w’abigishwa urushaho kwiyongera i Yeruzalemu , ndetse n’abaherezabitambo benshi bayoboka ukwemera .
44006008	Sitefano , uko Imana yakamusenderejemo ubutoneshwe n’ububasha , yakoraga ibitangaza n’ibimenyetso bikomeye muri rubanda .
44006009	Ariko abantu bo mu isengero ryitwa « iry’ababohowe » , hamwe n’Abanyasireni n’Abanyalegisandiriya , n’abantu bo muri Silisiya n’abo muri Aziya , batangira kujya impaka na Sitefano .
44006010	Nyamara ntibashoboraga guhangara ubuhanga bwe kimwe na Roho wamuvugiragamo ,
44006011	bituma bagurira abantu ngo bavuge bati « Twamwumvise avuga amagambo atuka Musa n’Imana . »
44006012	Nuko bahuruza rubanda hamwe n’abakuru b’umuryango n’abigishamategeko ; baraza bamugwa gitumo baramufata , bamujyana mu Nama nkuru .
44006013	Ni ko kuzana abashinjabinyoma baravuga bati « Uyu muntu ntahwema kuvuga amagambo asebya Ahantu hatagatifu kimwe n’Amategeko ;
44006014	tunamwumva avuga ko uwo Yezu w’i Nazareti azasenya aha Hantu hatagatifu , akanahindura Amategeko twahawe na Musa . »
44006015	Abari mu Nama nkuru bose baramwitegerezaga , maze babona mu ruhanga rwe hasa n’ah’umumalayika .
44007001	Umuherezabitambo mukuru abaza Sitefano ati « Ibyo se koko ni ko biri ? »
44007002	Sitefano arasubiza ati « Bavandimwe kandi babyeyi , nimunyumve : Imana Nyir’ikuzo yabonekeye umukurambere wacu Abrahamu igihe yari muri Mezopotamiya , mbere y’uko atura i Harani .
44007003	Iramubwira iti ’ Wimuke mu gihugu cyawe no mu muryango wawe , maze ujye mu gihugu nzakwereka . ’
44007004	Nuko Abrahamu yimuka mu gihugu cy’Abakalideya , ajya gutura i Harani . Nyuma y’urupfu rwa se , Imana imuzana muri iki gihugu mutuyemo ubu ngubu .
44007005	Nyamara ntiyigera imukebera isambu muri iki gihugu , habe ndetse n’ahangana urwara , ahubwo imusezeranya kuzakimuhaho umurage , we n’urubyaro rwe , n’ubwo Abrahamu atagiraga umwana .
44007006	Imana ni ko kumubwira iti ’ Urubyaro rwawe ruzatura mu gihugu cy’amahanga , babakoreshe imirimo y’agahato kandi babagirire nabi imyaka magana ane .
44007007	Nyamara igihugu kizabagira abacakara , ni jye ubwanjye uzagicira urubanza — iyo ari Imana ibivuga — , hanyuma bazavayo maze bajye bansengera aha hantu . ’
44007008	Nuko igirana na we Isezerano rirangwa no kugenywa ; bityo abyaye Izaki amugenya ku munsi wa munani , hanyuma Izaki na we abigenza atyo kuri Yakobo , na Yakobo abigenza atyo ku basekuruza bacu uko ari cumi na babiri .
44007009	Abo basekuruza bacu bagirira Yozefu ishyari , baramugurisha , ajyanwa mu Misiri . Ariko Imana yari kumwe na we ,
44007010	imugobotora mu magorwa ye yose , maze imuha ubutoni n’ubuhanga imbere ya Farawo , umwami wa Misiri , amugira umutware wa Misiri n’uw’urugo rwe rwose .
44007011	Nuko inzara iza gutera mu Misiri no muri Kanahani ; amagorwa aba yose maze abasekuruza bacu babura ibibatunga .
44007012	Yakobo ngo yumve ko mu Misiri hari ibiribwa , yoherezayo ku ncuro ya mbere abasekuruza bacu .
44007013	Ku ncuro ya kabiri Yozefu yimenyesha abavandimwe be , bityo na Farawo amenyana n’umuryango wa Yozefu .
44007014	Nuko Yozefu abatuma kuzana se Yakobo n’umuryango we wose , bose hamwe bari abantu mirongo irindwi na batanu .
44007015	Yakobo aramanuka ajya mu Misiri , aba ari ho apfira kimwe n’abasekuruza bacu .
44007016	Nuko babajyana i Sikemu , babahamba mu mva Abrahamu yari yaraguze ku giciro cya feza na bene Hemori , i Sikemu .
44007017	Igihe cyegereje kugira ngo Isezerano Imana yagiriye Abrahamu rirangire , umuryango uriyongera maze ugwira mu Misiri ,
44007018	kugeza ubwo mu Misiri hima undi mwami utari uzi Yozefu .
44007019	Uwo mwami apyinagaza umuryango wacu , agirira nabi abasekuruza bacu , kugeza aho abategeka kujugunya abana babo ngo batabaho .
44007020	Muri icyo gihe Musa aravuka , yari umwana mwiza kandi w’igikundiro mu maso y’Imana . Arererwa mu rugo rwa se amezi atatu ;
44007021	amaze gutabwa , umukobwa wa Farawo aramuraruza , maze amurera nk’umwana we bwite .
44007022	Nuko Musa yigishwa ubuhanga bwose bw’Abanyamisiri , aba igihangange mu magambo ye no mu bikorwa bye .
44007023	Igihe Musa yujuje imyaka mirongo ine , igitekerezo kimuzamo cyo kugenderera abavandimwe be , Abayisraheli .
44007024	Ngo abone umwe muri bo agirirwa nabi , aramutabara , maze kugira ngo ahorere umuvandimwe we wagirirwaga nabi , yica wa Munyamisiri .
44007025	Yatekerezaga ko abavandimwe be bazumviraho ko Imana izabarokoresha ikiganza cye , ariko ntibabyumva .
44007026	Bukeye asanga barwana ubwabo , agerageza kubunga agira ati ’ Yemwe bagabo , ko muri abavandimwe ; igituma mugirirana nabi ni iki ? ’
44007027	Ariko uwarenganyaga mugenzi we asunika Musa , avuga ati ’ Ni nde wakugize umutware n’umucamanza wacu ?
44007028	Mbese urashaka kunyica nk’uko ejo wishe wa Munyamisiri ? ’
44007029	Musa ngo yumve ayo magambo arahunga , asuhukira mu gihugu cya Madiyani , ahabyarira abahungu babiri .
44007030	Imyaka mirongo ine ishize , umumalayika amubonekera mu gihuru cyaka umuriro , aho yari ari mu butayu bw’umusozi wa Sinayi .
44007031	Musa ngo abibone biramutangaza , aregera ashaka kwitegereza , maze yumva ijwi rya Nyagasani rigira riti
44007032	’ Ndi Imana y’abasekuruza bawe , Imana ya Abrahamu , ya Izaki na Yakobo . ’ Musa ahinda umushyitsi , ntiyatinyuka kwitegereza .
44007033	Nuko Nyagasani aramubwira ati ’ Kuramo inkweto zawe , kuko aha hantu uhagaze ari ubutaka butagatifu .
44007034	Amagorwa y’umuryango wanjye uri mu Misiri narayitegereje , kandi n’imiborogo yawo narayumvise ; none namanuwe no kubagobotora . Ubu ngubu rero genda , ngutumye mu Misiri . ’
44007035	Musa uwo nyine bari barihakanye bavuga bati ’ Ni nde wakugize umutware n’umucamanza ? ’ , ni we Imana yohereje kubabera umutware n’umutabazi , imutumyeho umumalayika wari wamubonekeye mu gihuru .
44007036	Ni we wabavanye mu Misiri , akora ibitangaza n’ibimenyetso bikomeye muri icyo gihugu , ku Nyanja itukura no mu butayu mu gihe cy’imyaka mirongo ine .
44007037	Musa uwo , ni we wabwiye Abayisraheli ati ’ Imana izababonera mu bavandimwe banyu umuhanuzi umeze nkanjye . ’
44007038	Igihe cy’ikoraniro ryo mu butayu , ni we kandi wari uhagaze imbere y’abasekuruza bacu , akavugana n’Umumalayika ku musozi wa Sinayi ; ni we wakiriye amagambo y’ubugingo kugira ngo ayadushyikirize .
44007039	Ariko abasekuruza bacu banga kumwumvira , baramuhigika maze bifuza kwisubirira mu Misiri !
44007040	Ni ko kubwira Aroni bati ’ Ngaho dukorere imana zo kutugenda imbere ; kuko Musa uriya watuvanye mu gihugu cya Misiri , tutazi uko byamugendekeye ! ’
44007041	Muri iyo minsi ni bwo bacuze ikimasa , batura igitambo icyo kigirwamana kandi bishimira igikorwa cy’ibiganza byabo .
44007042	Nuko Imana irabazibukira , irabareka ngo basenge inyenyeri zo mu kirere , nk’uko byanditswe mu gitabo cy’Abahanuzi ngo ’ Hari ubwo se mwigeze kuntura ibitambo n’amaturo , muryango wa Israheli , mu myaka mirongo ine yose mwamaze mu butayu ?
44007043	Ahubwo mwahetse ihema rya Moloki n’inyenyeri y’imana yanyu Refani , ibyo bishushanyo mwikoreye kugira ngo mubisenge ! Ni cyo gituma nzabajyana bunyago hirya ya Babiloni . ’
44007044	Mu butayu , abasekuruza bacu bari bafite ihema rihamya Isezerano ; Uwavuganaga na Musa yari yaramutegetse kuryubaka akurikije urugero yari yabonye .
44007045	Hanyuma abasekuruza bacu bamaze kurihabwa , bayobowe na Yozuwe , baryinjirana mu gihugu bari bamaze kwigarurira , Imana imaze kwirukanamo amahanga yari agituye ; rirahaguma kugeza mu gihe cya Dawudi .
44007046	Dawudi uwo nyine yatonnye ku Mana , maze ayisaba guteganya Ingoro igenewe Imana ya Yakobo .
44007047	Ariko Salomoni ni we wayubakiye Ingoro .
44007048	Nyamara Umusumbabyose ntaba mu mazu yubatswe n’abantu , nk’uko byavuzwe n’umuhanuzi ati
44007049	’ Ijuru ni intebe yanjye y’ubwami , isi ikaba akabaho nkandagizaho ibirenge byanjye . None rero , muzanyubakira ingoro nyabaki ? — uwo ni Nyagasani ubivuga — Cyangwa se aho nzaruhukira , hazaba hameze hate ?
44007050	Mbese ye , ibiganza byanjye si byo byaremye ibi byose ? ’
44007051	Bantu b’ijosi rishingaraye , bantu banangiye umutima n’amatwi , mugahora murwanya Roho Mutagatifu , muri kimwe n’abasekuruza banyu !
44007052	Ni nde mu bahanuzi , abasekuruza banyu batatoteje ? Ndetse bishe n’abahanuye mbere ukuza kwa ya Ntungane , imwe ubu ngubu mwagambaniye maze mukamwica .
44007053	Mwahawe Amategeko muyashyikirijwe n’abamalayika , nyamara ntimwayakurikiza ! »
44007054	Ayo magambo ya Sitefano arabarakaza , bamuhekenyera amenyo .
44007055	Naho we yuzura Roho Mutagatifu , ahanga amaso ijuru , abona ikuzo ry’Imana na Yezu ahagaze iburyo bw’Imana .
44007056	Nuko aravuga ati « Dore ndabona ijuru rikinguye , n’Umwana w’umuntu ahagaze iburyo bw’Imana . »
44007057	Bahera ko bavuza induru , bipfuka mu matwi maze bamwiroheraho icyarimwe .
44007058	Baramukurubana no hanze y’umugi , bamutera amabuye . Abamushinjaga bari barambitse imyambaro yabo imbere y’umusore witwa Sawuli .
44007059	Igihe bamuteraga amabuye , Sitefano asenga agira ati « Nyagasani Yezu , akira ubuzima bwanjye . »
44007060	Nuko arapfukama maze atera hejuru ati « Nyagasani , ntubahore iki cyaha . » Ngo amare kuvuga ibyo , araca .
44008001	Sawuli na we yari mu bemeye ubwo bwicanyi . Uwo munsi haduka itotezwa rikomeye muri Kiliziya y’i Yeruzalemu , maze bose uretse Intumwa , batatanira mu turere twa Yudeya na Samariya .
44008002	Abantu bubaha Imana bahamba Sitefano , baramuririra cyane .
44008003	Naho Sawuli we agumya kuyogoza Kiliziya , akinjira mu mazu , agafata abagabo n’abagore , akabashyira mu buroko .
44008004	Abari batatanye bagendaga hose , bamamaza Inkuru Nziza y’ijambo ry’Imana .
44008005	Filipo na we aramanuka ajya mu mugi wa Samariya , yigisha abahatuye ibya Kristu .
44008006	Rubanda bashishikariraga n’umutima umwe inyigisho za Filipo , kuko bari barumvise ibitangaza yakoraga kandi bakanabibona .
44008007	Koko rero , roho mbi zasohokaga mu bari bahanzweho zisakuza , ibimuga byinshi n’ibirema bigakira .
44008008	Nuko muri uwo mugi haba ibyishimo byinshi .
44008009	Muri uwo mugi hakaba umugabo witwa Simoni , wari umupfumu , maze agatangaza Abanyasamariya , yiyita akataraboneka .
44008010	Abantu bose kuva ku muto kugera ku mukuru bakamwihambiraho , bavuga bati « Uyu muntu arimo Ububasha bw’Imana , ubwo bita Ubuhangange . »
44008011	Icyatumaga bamwihambiraho batyo , ni uko yari amaze igihe kirekire yarabararuye n’ubwo bupfumu bwe .
44008012	Ariko aho bamariye kwemera Filipo wabamenyeshaga Inkuru Nziza y’Ingoma y’Imana n’izina rya Yezu Kristu , abagabo n’abagore barabatizwa .
44008013	Nuko na Simoni ubwe aremera , arabatizwa , maze yihambira kuri Filipo ; yabona ibimenyetso bikomeye n’ibitangaza byakorwaga , akumirwa .
44008014	Intumwa zari i Yeruzalemu zimenye ko muri Samariya bakiriye ijambo ry’Imana , ziboherereza Petero na Yohani .
44008015	Bagezeyo , basabira Abanyasamariya kugira ngo bahabwe Roho Mutagatifu ,
44008016	kuko ari nta n’umwe muri bo yari yaramanukiyeho ; bakaba bari barabatijwe gusa mu izina rya Nyagasani Yezu .
44008017	Nuko Petero na Yohani babaramburiraho ibiganza , maze bahabwa Roho Mutagatifu .
44008018	Simoni rero ngo abone ko Roho Mutagatifu atangwa no kuramburirwaho ibiganza n’Intumwa , azizanira amafaranga , azibwira ati
44008019	« Nimumpe nanjye ubwo bubasha , kugira ngo uwo nzaramburiraho ibiganza ajye ahabwa Roho Mutagatifu . »
44008020	Petero aramusubiza ati « Uragapfana n’amafaranga yawe , kuko watekereje ko ingabire y’Imana igurwa amafaranga !
44008021	Nta mugabane , nta n’umurage ufite muri ibi , kuko umutima wawe udatunganiye Imana .
44008022	Ngaho rero ihane ubwo bugome bwawe , kandi utakambire Nyagasani ; wenda yakubabarira icyo gitekerezo cyinjiye mu mutima wawe ,
44008023	kuko mbona uri mu ndurwe isharira no mu ngoyi y’icyaha . »
44008024	Simoni ni ko gusubiza ati « Nimunsabire namwe kuri Nyagasani , kugira ngo hatagira ikingwirira mu byo mwavuze . »
44008025	Petero na Yohani bamaze guhamya no kwamamaza ijambo rya Nyagasani , basubira i Yeruzalemu . Bamamaza Inkuru Nziza mu nsisiro nyinshi z’Abanyasamariya .
44008026	Umumalayika wa Nyagasani abwira Filipo , ati « Haguruka , ugende werekeje mu majyepfo , unyure mu muhanda umanuka i Yeruzalemu ujya i Gaza , ubu ngubu ukaba utarimo abagenzi . »
44008027	Filipo ahera ko aragenda . Ubwo Umunyetiyopiya wari icyegera cya Kandasi , umwamikazi wa Etiyopiya , akaba n’umunyabintu we , yari yaje gusengera Imana i Yeruzalemu .
44008028	Yari mu nzira ataha , yicaye mu igare rye , agenda asoma igitabo cya Izayi umuhanuzi .
44008029	Roho Mutagatifu abwira Filipo ati « Genda , wegere ririya gare . »
44008030	Filipo ariruka , yumva uwo mutware asoma mu gitabo cya Izayi umuhanuzi , aramubaza ati « Mbese aho ibyo usoma urabyumva ? »
44008031	Undi aramusubiza ati « Nabyumva nte se , ntabonye unsobanurira . » Nuko asaba Filipo kurira ngo yicare iruhande rwe .
44008032	Muri ibyo Byanditswe yahasomaga ibi ngibi « Bamushoreye nk’intama bajyanye mu ibagiro , cyangwa nk’umwana w’intama wicecekera imbere y’uwupfura ubwoya , na we ntiyaruhije abumbura umunwa .
44008033	Yacishijwe bugufi , acirwa urubanza rw’akarengane . Ni nde uzavuga iby’abazamukomokaho ? Ko ubugingo bwe bwazimanganye ku isi , nta cyo yasize . »
44008034	Uwo mutware abaza Filipo ati « Ndagusabye ngo umbwire : ni nde umuhanuzi avugaho ibi ngibi ? Ni kuri we ubwe , cyangwa se ni undi muntu yavugaga ? »
44008035	Filipo ni ko guterura , ahereye kuri iyo ngingo y’Ibyanditswe , amumenyesha Inkuru Nziza ya Yezu .
44008036	Uko bagakomeje inzira baza kugera ku mugezi , wa mutware aravuga ati « Dore amazi ! Ni iki se kandi cyambuza kubatizwa ? »
44008037	( Filipo aramusubiza ati « Niba wemera Yezu n’umutima wawe wose , birashoboka . » Undi aramubwira ati « Ndemera ko Yezu Kristu ari Umwana w’Imana . » )
44008038	Nuko ategeka ko bahagarika igare , bombi baramanuka bajya mu mazi , Filipo n’umutware , maze Filipo aramubatiza .
44008039	Bamaze kuva mu mazi Roho Mutagatifu ajyana Filipo , uwo mutware ntiyongera kumubona ukundi , ahubwo yikomereza urugendo rwe yishimye .
44008040	Naho Filipo ngo arebe , asanga ari mu mugi wa Azoti , maze yamamaza Inkuru Nziza mu migi yose yanyuragamo , kugeza ko agera i Kayizareya .
44009001	Sawuli nta kindi yatekerezaga kitari ukujujubya no kwica abigishwa ba Nyagasani . Nuko asanga umuherezabitambo mukuru ,
44009002	amusaba inzandiko zo kujya mu masengero y’i Damasi , kugira ngo nagira abo ahasanga bayobotse iyo Nzira , abagabo n’abagore , ababohe abazane i Yeruzalemu .
44009003	Nuko igihe yari mu nzira agiye kugera i Damasi , ako kanya urumuri ruturutse mu ijuru ruramugota .
44009004	Yitura hasi , maze yumva ijwi rimubwira riti « Sawuli , Sawuli ! Urantotereza iki ? »
44009005	Sawuli arabaza ati « Uri nde , Nyagasani ? » Iryo jwi rirasubiza riti « Ndi Yezu , uwo uriho utoteza !
44009006	Ariko haguruka winjire mu mugi , bari bukubwire icyo ugomba gukora . »
44009007	Bagenzi be bari kumwe mu rugendo , bari bahagaze bumiwe , kuko bumvaga ijwi ariko ntibabone umuntu .
44009008	Sawuli arabaduka , nyamara n’ubwo yabumburaga amaso , nta cyo yabonaga . Bagenzi be ni ko kumurandata bamugeza i Damasi .
44009009	Nuko ahamara iminsi itatu atabona , nta cyo arya nta n’icyo anywa .
44009010	Aho i Damasi rero hakaba umwigishwa witwaga Ananiya . Nyagasani aramubonekera , amuhamagara agira ati « Ananiya ! » Undi arasubiza ati « Ndi hano , Nyagasani ! »
44009011	Nyagasani aramubwira ati « Haguruka ujye mu muhanda witwa ’ Ugororotse ’ , ubarize kwa Yuda umuntu witwa Sawuli , ukomoka i Tarisi . Ubu ariho arasenga ,
44009012	kandi mu ibonekerwa , yabonye umuntu witwa Ananiya yinjira iwe , amuramburiraho ibiganza kugira ngo abone . »
44009013	Ananiya arasubiza ati « Nyagasani , numvise benshi bavuga iby’uwo muntu , n’inabi yose yagiriye abatagatifujwe bawe b’i Yeruzalemu ,
44009014	kandi n’ino ahafite ububasha yahawe n’abatware b’abaherezabitambo , kugira ngo abohe abiyambaza izina ryawe bose . »
44009015	Ariko Nyagasani aramubwira ati « Genda ! Kuko uwo muntu ari igikoresho cyanjye nitoranyirije , kugira ngo amenyekanishe izina ryanjye imbere y’abanyamahanga , imbere y’abami n’imbere y’Abayisraheli .
44009016	Ni jye ubwanjye uzamwereka uburyo bwose azagomba kubabazwa , ahorwa izina ryanjye . »
44009017	Nuko Ananiya aragenda , yinjira mu nzu , amuramburiraho ibiganza , maze aramubwira ati « Sawuli muvandimwe ! Nyagasani Yezu wakubonekeye mu nzira uza ino yakuntumyeho , kugira ngo wongere kubona kandi wuzuremo Roho Mutagatifu . »
44009018	Ako kanya , utuntu dusa n’udushishwa duhubuka mu maso ye , yongera kubona maze ahera ko arabatizwa .
44009019	Amaze kurya , yongera kugira intege . Sawuli amarana iminsi mike n’abigishwa b’i Damasi ,
44009020	maze atangira adatinze kwamamaza mu masengero ko Yezu ari Umwana w’Imana .
44009021	Abamwumvaga bose baratangaraga , maze bakabaza bati « Mbese uyu si we wajujubyaga i Yeruzalemu abiyambaza iryo zina ? Hanyuma se ntiyazanywe ino no kubaboha , kugira ngo abashyikirize abatware b’abaherezabitambo ? »
44009022	Ariko Sawuli arushaho gukomera , agatsinda impaka Abayahudi batuye i Damasi , abemeza ko Yezu ari we Kristu .
44009023	Hashize igihe kinini Abayahudi bajya inama yo kumwica .
44009024	Nyamara Sawuli aza kumenya ubwo bugambanyi bwabo , bugeza aho kurinda amarembo y’umugi ijoro n’amanywa , ngo babone uko bamwica .
44009025	Ariko nijoro abigishwa be baramucikisha , bamwururukiriza ku nkike y’umugi , bamumanuriye mu gitebo .
44009026	Sawuli ageze i Yeruzalemu , agerageza kwegera abigishwa ; ariko bose bakamutinya , kuko batemeraga ko na we ari umwigishwa koko .
44009027	Nuko Barinaba aramujyana , amushyikiriza Intumwa , azitekerereza uko yabonanye na Nyagasani mu nzira n’uko yamubwiye , n’ukuntu i Damasi yigishije mu izina rya Yezu ashize amanga .
44009028	Nuko Sawuli agumana na bo , akagenda hose muri Yeruzalemu nta cyo yishisha , ari na ko yigisha mu izina rya Yezu ashize amanga .
44009029	Yakundaga kuganira n’Abayahudi bavugaga ikigereki kandi akajya impaka na bo ; ariko bo bagashaka kumwica .
44009030	Abavandimwe ngo babimenye , baramuherekeza bamugeza i Kayizareya , maze bamwohereza i Tarisi .
44009031	Ubwo Kiliziya yariho mu mahoro muri Yudeya yose , muri Galileya no muri Samariya , ishinga imizi kandi ikomeza kubaha Nyagasani , bityo irushaho kujya mbere ikomejwe na Roho Mutagatifu .
44009032	Ubwo rero Petero wazengurukaga igihugu cyose , aza kugera no ku batagatifujwe bari batuye i Lida .
44009033	Ahasanga umuntu witwa Eneya , wari umaze imyaka umunani atabyuka , kubera ubumuga .
44009034	Petero aramubwira ati « Eneya , Yezu Kristu aragukijije . Haguruka wisasire uburiri bwawe ! » Uwo mwanya arahaguruka .
44009035	Nuko abaturage bose b’i Lida n’abo mu kibaya cya Saroni babibonye , bayoboka Nyagasani .
44009036	Ubwo i Yope hakaba umwigishwakazi witwa Tabita , mu kigereki rikaba Doruka . Yakoraga ibikorwa byiza byinshi , kandi agatanga n’imfashanyo y’abakene .
44009037	Muri iyo minsi aza gufatwa n’indwara , maze arapfa . Bamaze kuhagira umurambo we , bawurambika mu cyumba cyo mu nzu yo hejuru .
44009038	Kuko rero Lida yari bugufi bw’i Yope , abigishwa bakaba barumvise ko Petero ariho ari , bamutumaho abantu babiri kumubwira bati « Ntutindiganye kuza iwacu . »
44009039	Petero ahaguruka uwo mwanya , ajyana na bo . Akihagera , bamujyana muri cya cyumba cyo mu nzu yo hejuru , abapfakazi bose bari bamukikije barira , bereka Petero amakanzu n’ibishura Doruka yadodaga akiri kumwe na bo .
44009040	Nuko Petero aheza abantu bose , arapfukama arasenga ; hanyuma ahindukirira umurambo aravuga ati « Tabita , haguruka ! » Nuko ngo abumbure amaso abona Petero , areguka maze aricara .
44009041	Petero amuhereza ikiganza aramuhagurutsa ; ni ko guhamagara abatagatifujwe n’abapfakazi , aramubereka ari mutaraga .
44009042	Iyo nkuru imenyekana i Yope hose , bituma abantu benshi bemera Nyagasani .
44009043	Nuko Petero amara iminsi myinshi i Yope , acumbitse kwa Simoni w’umukannyi .
44010001	I Kayizareya hakaba umuntu witwa Koruneli , wari umutegeka w’abasirikare bo mu mutwe witwa « uw’Ubutaliyani » .

44010003	Nuko umunsi umwe , nko ku isaha ya cyenda y’amanywa , arabonekerwa : abona umumalayika w’Imana yinjira iwe , maze aramubwira ati « Koruneli ! »
44010004	Undi amuhanga amaso , ubwoba buramutaha , ni ko gusubiza ati « Ni iki se , Nyagasani ? » Umumalayika aramubwira ati « Amasengesho yawe n’ubuntu bwawe byageze ku Mana , ntibyibagirwa .

44010006	Acumbitse ku wundi muntu witwa Simoni w’umukannyi , utuye mu rugo ruri iruhande rw’inyanja . »
44010007	Umumalayika bavuganaga ngo amare kugenda , Koruneli ahamagaza abantu babiri bo mu rugo rwe , n’umusirikare umukoreye igihe kirekire kandi wubaha Imana ;
44010008	amaze kubatekerereza byose , abohereza i Yope .
44010009	Bukeye bw’uwo munsi , ba bantu bakiri mu nzira ahajya kwegera umugi , ubwo na Petero akaba yazamutse ajya ahitaruye hejuru y’igisenge cy’inzu gusenga ; hari nka saa sita .
44010010	Nuko aza gusonza yifuza kurya . Igihe rero bakimutegurira ibyo kurya , ahera ko atwarwa .

44010022	Baramusubiza bati « Twatumwe n’umutegeka w’abasirikare witwa Koruneli , umuntu w’intungane , utinya Imana kandi agashimwa n’umuryango wose w’Abayahudi . Yabwiwe rero n’umumalayika mutagatifu kugutumira , kugira ngo yumve ibyo umubwira . »

44010031	maze arambwira ati ’ Koruneli , isengesho ryawe ryakiriwe n’ubuntu bwawe buribukwa mu maso y’Imana .

44010034	Nuko Petero aterura agira ati « Noneho numvise mu by’ukuri ko Imana itarobanura ,
44010035	ahubwo inyurwa n’umuntu wa buri hanga iryo ari ryo ryose uyitinya kandi agaharanira ubutungane .
44010036	Ubwo butumwa bwayo yabwoherereje Abayisraheli , ari bwo Inkuru Nziza y’amahoro bazaniwe na Yezu Kristu , Umutegetsi w’abantu bose .

44011020	Ariko bamwe muri bo bakomoka muri Shipure no muri Sireni bageze i Antiyokiya , bamenyesha n’Abagereki Inkuru Nziza ya Nyagasani Yezu .

44013027	Koko rero , abaturage b’i Yeruzalemu n’abatware babo birengagije Yezu ; maze mu kumucira urubanza , barangiza batyo ibyo abahanuzi bavuze , bisomwa kuri buri sabato .
44013028	N’ubwo batabonye impamvu n’imwe yo kumwicisha , basabye Pilato ngo amwice .
44013029	Bamaze kurangiza ibyari byaramwanditsweho byose , bamumanura ku musaraba maze bamushyira mu mva .
44013030	Ariko Imana yamuzuye mu bapfuye ,
44013031	amara iminsi myinshi abonekera abari barazamukanye na we kuva muri Galileya kugera i Yeruzalemu , ari na bo bahamya babyo muri rubanda kugeza na n’ubu .
44013032	Natwe rero turabamenyesha iyo Nkuru Nziza : iryo Sezerano Imana yagiranye n’abasekuruza bacu ,
44013033	yararidusohoreje twebwe abana babo , igihe yazuraga Yezu nk’uko byanditswe muri zaburi ya kabiri ngo ’ Uri umwana wanjye , nakwibyariye uyu munsi . ’
44013034	Iby’uko yamuzuye mu bapfuye , akaba adashobora gusubira mu bushanguke , Imana yabivuze muri aya magambo , iti ’ Nzabaha ibyiza nasezeranyije Dawudi , ku buryo budasubirwaho . ’
44013035	Ni cyo gituma n’ahandi havugwa ngo ’ Ntuzareka Intungane yawe imenyana n’ubushanguke . ’
44013036	Dawudi akiriho yarangije ugushaka kw’Imana , arasaza maze ashyingurwa hamwe n’abasekuruza be kandi yarashangutse .
44013037	Nyamara uwo Imana yazuye , we ntarakamenyana n’ubushanguke .
44013038	Nimumenye rero , bavandimwe , ko ari ku bwe mwamenyeshejwe ibabarirwa ry’ibyaha , n’ubwo butungane mutashoboye kubona mu Mategeko ya Musa ,
44013039	uwemera wese akabuherwa muri we .
44013040	Muririnde rero mutagubwaho n’ibyavuzwe n’abahanuzi bagira bati
44013041	’ Nimurebe , mwa banyagasuzuguro mwe , nimutangare maze bibatere gutatana . Koko rero muri iki gihe cyanyu , ngiye gukora igikorwa mutabasha kwemera , n’ubwo hagira ukibabwira ! ’ »
44013042	Pawulo na Barinaba basohotse , abo bantu babasaba ko ku isabato itaha bazongera kubabwira ayo magambo .
44013043	Ikoraniro rimaze gusezererwa , benshi mu Bayahudi no mu banyamahanga bayobotse idini yabo baherekeza Pawulo na Barinaba . Bo rero bakomeza kubaganiriza babashishikariza gukomera ku ngabire y’Imana .
44013044	Ku isabato yakurikiyeho , hafi umugi wose urakorana kugira ngo bumve ijambo ry’Imana .
44013045	Abayahudi rero , ngo babone icyo kivunge cy’abantu , bagira ishyari , ni ko guhinyura ibyo Pawulo yavugaga , babisebya .
44013046	Nuko Pawulo na Barinaba bavuga nta cyo bishisha , bati « Byari ngombwa ko ari mwe mubanza gushyikirizwa ijambo ry’Imana ! None ubwo muryamaganye , mukabona ko mwebwe ubwanyu mudakwiye ubugingo buhoraho , ngaho rero twisangiye abanyamahanga .
44013047	Ni na ko Nyagasani yadutegetse agira ati ’ Nagushyiriyeho kuba urumuri rw’amahanga , kugira ngo uzajyane ijambo ry’umukiro kugeza aho isi igarukira . ’ »
44013048	Abanyamahanga babyumvise barishima , basingiza ijambo rya Nyagasani , n’abari baragenewe ubugingo bose baremera .
44013049	Nuko ijambo rya Nyagasani ryogera muri icyo gihugu cyose ,
44013050	ariko Abayahudi boshya abagore b’abapfasoni bubahaga Imana , kimwe n’abanyacyubahiro bo muri uwo mugi , babateza Pawulo na Barinaba ngo babatoteze , kugeza ubwo babamenesha mu gihugu cyabo .
44013051	Na bo ngo bamare kwihungura umukungugu wo mu birenge byabo , barawubasigira maze bajya mu mugi witwa Ikoniyo .
44013052	Abigishwa b’aho basigaye buzuye ibyishimo na Roho Mutagatifu .
44014001	Aho Ikoniyo na ho ni ko byagenze . Pawulo na Barinaba binjiye mu isengero ry’Abayahudi , baravuga ku buryo Abayahudi n’Abagereki benshi bemeye .
44014002	Ariko bamwe mu Bayahudi bari banze kwemera , batera imidugararo mu banyamahanga , baboshya kugirira nabi abavandimwe .
44014003	Pawulo na Barinaba bahamara igihe kirekire , bakigisha bashize amanga kuko bari biringiye Nyagasani wahamyaga ukuri kw’amagambo yabo , abaha gukora ibimenyetso n’ibitangaza bikomeye .
44014004	Abatuye uwo mugi rero bicamo ibice : bamwe bajya ku ruhande rw’Abayahudi , abandi ku rw’Intumwa .
44014005	Nuko abanyamahanga n’Abayahudi bajya inama n’abatware babo ngo bagirire nabi Intumwa , bazitere amabuye .
44014006	Pawulo na Barinaba babimenye , bashaka ubuhungiro mu migi ya Lisitiri na Deribe yo muri Likawoniya , no mu turere tuyikikije .
44014007	Na ho bakomeza kwamamaza Inkuru Nziza .
44014008	Nuko i Lisitiri hakaba umuntu waremaye ibirenge , kuko yari yaravukanye ubumuga , atigeze atambuka .
44014009	Umunsi umwe , yari ateze amatwi Pawulo yigisha , Pawulo na we amwitegereje , abona ko afite ukwemera guhagije kugira ngo akire ,
44014010	amubwira mu ijwi riranguruye ati « Haguruka , uhagarare wemye ! » Umuntu arabaduka , aragenda .
44014011	Rubanda rero ngo babone ibyo Pawulo amaze gukora , batera hejuru bavuga mu rurimi rwabo kavukire rwo muri Likawoniya , bati « Imana zisa n’abantu zaje muri twe ! »
44014012	Nuko Barinaba bamwita « Zewusi » , naho Pawulo bamwita « Herimesi » , kuko ari we wakundaga gufata ijambo .
44014013	Nuko umuherezabitambo w’ikigirwamana Zewusi , ( ingoro yacyo ikaba yari ku irembo ry’umugi ) , azana ibimasa bitatse indabyo abishyira imbere y’irembo , kuko yashakaga we na rubanda , gutura igitambo .
44014014	Ariko Pawulo na Barinaba , ngo bumve iyo nkuru , bashishimura imyambaro yabo maze biroha muri rubanda batera hejuru , bati
44014015	« Ibyo mukora ni ibiki ? Natwe turi abantu nkamwe . Inkuru Nziza tubamenyesha , irabasaba ko mwigizayo ayo manjwe , ngo mugarukire Imana Nzima yaremye ijuru n’isi , inyanja n’ibiyirimo byose .
44014016	Mu bihe byo hambere , yaretse amahanga yose akora ibyo yishakiye ;
44014017	nyamara ntiyaretse gutanga ibimenyetso bihamya ubugiraneza bwayo : ibaha imvura n’ibihe by’uburumbuke , ikabahaza ibibatunga , n’imitima yanyu ikayuzuza ibyishimo . »
44014018	Ayo magambo yabo atuma rubanda batuza ariko bigoranye , bityo bareka kubatura igitambo .
44014019	Nuko haza kwaduka Abayahudi baturutse Antiyokiya n’Ikoniyo , bigarurira rubanda . Batera Pawulo amabuye , hanyuma bamukururira hirya y’umugi bibwira ko yapfuye .
44014020	Ariko igihe abigishwa bari bamukikije , arahaguruka asubira mu mugi . Bukeye ajyana na Barinaba i Deribe .
44014021	Ngo bamare kwamamaza Inkuru Nziza muri uwo mugi no kuhabona abigishwa benshi , bahera ko basubira i Lisitiri , Ikoniyo n’i Antiyokiya .
44014022	Bakomezaga umutima w’abigishwa , bakabatera umwete ngo bakomere mu kwemera , bababwira bati « Ni ngombwa ko tunyura mu magorwa menshi , kugira ngo tubone kwinjira mu Ngoma y’Imana . »
44014023	Nuko bashyiraho abakuru muri buri Kiliziya , bamaze gusenga no gusiba kurya , babaragiza Nyagasani bari baremeye .
44014024	Hanyuma bambukiranya akarere ka Pisidiya , bagera muri Pamfiliya .
44014025	Bamaze kwamamaza ijambo ry’Imana i Perige , bamanuka berekeza Ataliya .
44014026	Bahavuye , bajya mu bwato berekeza Antiyokiya , ari na wo mugi bari baraturutsemo , ubwo abavandimwe babo babaragizaga Imana , babasabira kuzatunganya uwo murimo nyine bari bamaze kurangiza .
44014027	Bagezeyo , bakoranya Kiliziya , babatekerereza ibyo Imana yari yakoranye na bo byose , ariko cyane cyane ko yugururiye abanyamahanga irembo ry’ukwemera .
44014028	Nuko bamarana iminsi n’abigishwa .
44015001	Nuko abantu bamwe bavuye muri Yudeya , baza bigisha abavandimwe bo muri Antiyokiya bati « Niba mutigenyesheje uko Musa yabitegetse , ntimushobora gukizwa . »
44015002	Nuko havuka amakimbirane n’impaka zikomeye kuri Pawulo na Barinaba bavuguruza abo bantu ; ni ko kwemeza ko Pawulo na Barinaba hamwe n’abandi muri bo , bajya i Yeruzalemu kureba Intumwa n’abakuru b’ikoraniro , bakabagisha inama kuri icyo kibazo .
44015003	Nuko Kiliziya ya Antiyokiya ibafasha ku byo bakeneye mu rugendo , banyura muri Fenisiya na Samariya babatekerereza iby’uguhinduka kw’abanyamahanga , maze iyo nkuru itera abavandimwe bose ibyishimo byinshi .
44015004	Bageze i Yeruzalemu , Kiliziya y’aho irabakira hamwe n’Intumwa n’abakuru b’ikoraniro , hanyuma babatekerereza ibyo Imana yakoranye na bo byose .
44015005	Ariko bamwe mu bemeye bo mu gatsiko k’Abafarizayi batera hejuru bati « Ni ngombwa ko abo banyamahanga bagenywa , kandi bagategekwa kubahiriza Amategeko ya Musa . »
44015006	Intumwa n’abakuru b’ikoraniro bateranira hamwe , kugira ngo basuzume icyo kibazo .
44015007	Bamaze kujya impaka z’urudaca , Petero ni ko guhaguruka , arababwira ati « Bavandimwe , muzi ko kuva mu ntangiriro Imana yantoranyije muri mwe , kugira ngo namamaze Inkuru Nziza mu banyamahanga , maze na bo baremera .
44015008	Ndetse n’Imana imenya imitima yabitangiye icyemezo , igihe ibahaye Roho Mutagatifu kimwe natwe .
44015009	Ntiyabatandukanyije natwe , imitima yabo yayisukurishije ukwemera .
44015010	None rero , ni kuki mushaka kugerageza Imana , mukorera abo bigishwa umutwaro abasekuruza bacu ndetse natwe ubwacu tutabashije kwikorera ?
44015011	Byongeye kandi , twemera ko twakijijwe n’ingabire ya Nyagasani Yezu kimwe na bo ! »
44015012	Nuko ikoraniro ryose riratuza , maze batega amatwi Pawulo na Barinaba babatekererezaga ibimenyetso byose n’ibitangaza Imana yabakoresheje mu banyamahanga .
44015013	Barangije kuvuga , Yakobo afata ijambo agira ati « Bavandimwe , nimunyumve .
44015014	Simewoni amaze kutwibutsa ukuntu kuva mu ntangiriro Imana yagendereye abanyamahanga , ikabatoranyamo umuryango uzubahiriza izina ryayo .
44015015	Ibyo bikaba bihuje n’ibyavuzwe n’Abahanuzi , nk’uko byanditswe ngo
44015016	’ Nyuma y’ibyo nzagaruka , nongere nubake inzu ya Dawudi yasenyutse . Ahasenyutse nzahubaka bundi bushya , maze nyihagarike ,
44015017	kugira ngo abarokotse bazashakashake Nyagasani , kimwe n’amahanga yose izina ryanjye ryambarizwamo . Uwo ni Nyagasani ubivuze , we urangiza imigambi ye
44015018	isanzwe izwi kuva kera kose . ’
44015019	Ni cyo gituma mbona ko badakwiye gutera imitima ihagaze abo mu mahanga bagarukira Imana .
44015020	Ahubwo tubandikire gusa ngo birinde guhumanywa n’ibigirwamana n’ubukozi bw’ibibi , birinde kandi kurya inyamaswa zanizwe , n’amaraso .
44015021	Naho Musa , kuva kera umugi wose awufitemo abigisha ibye , kuko kuri buri sabato babisomera mu masengero . »
44015022	Ubwo byose bamaze kubyumvikanaho , Intumwa n’abakuru b’ikoraniro biyemeza kwitoramo bamwe muri bo , ngo babatume i Antiyokiya kumwe na Pawulo na Barinaba . Nuko hatorwa Yuda witwa Barisaba na Silasi , abantu b’imena mu bavandimwe .
44015023	Urwo rwandiko babahaye rwagiraga ruti « Twebwe Intumwa , abakuru b’ikoraniro n’abavandimwe , turabaramutsa , bavandimwe bacu b’abanyamahanga bari Antiyokiya , muri Siriya no muri Silisiya .
44015024	Twumvise ko bamwe muri twe bababwiye amagambo yo kubakangaranya no kubakura umutima , kandi tutigeze tubatuma .
44015025	None twahuje umugambi wo gutoranya abantu ngo tubabatumeho , bazanye na Pawulo na Barinaba , incuti zacu dukunda ,
44015026	kuko bahaze amagara yabo kubera izina ry’Umwami wacu Yezu Kristu .
44015027	Tubatumyeho rero Yuda na Silasi , kugira ngo na bo ubwabo babasobanurire ibyo tubandikiye .
44015028	Byanogeye rero Roho Mutagatifu kimwe natwe kutagira undi mutwaro tubagerekaho utari aya mabwiriza ya ngombwa :
44015029	mwirinde kurya inyama zatambiwe ibigirwamana , n’amaraso , n’inyama z’inyamaswa zanizwe , mwirinde n’ubukozi bw’ibibi . Nimureka gukora ibyo , muzaba mugenjeje neza . Nimugire amahoro ! »
44015030	Nuko abari batumwe bamanuka berekeza i Antiyokiya ; bahageze bakoranyiriza hamwe ikoraniro ry’aho , babashyikiriza urwandiko .
44015031	Ngo bamare kurusoma , abantu bose bashimishwa n’ubwo butumwa bwo kubakomeza .
44015032	Yuda na Silasi , dore ko na bo bari abahanuzi , bababwira mu magambo arambuye yo kubahugura no kubakomeza .
44015033	Bamarana na bo iminsi , hanyuma abavandimwe bamaze kubifuriza amahoro , barabasezerera basubira ku babatumye . (
44015034	Icyakora Silasi we yiyemeza kuguma aho , Yuda aba ari we usubirayo wenyine . )
44015035	Naho Pawulo na Barinaba baguma i Antiyokiya , bigisha kandi bamamaza Inkuru Nziza y’ijambo rya Nyagasani bifatanyije n’abandi benshi .
44015036	Hashize iminsi , Pawulo abwira Barinaba ati « Reka duhindukire , dusure abavandimwe bo mu migi twamamajemo ijambo rya Nyagasani , turebe uko bameze . »
44015037	Nuko Barinaba ashaka kujyana na Yohani bitaga Mariko .
44015038	Nyamara Pawulo we ntiyishimira kujyana n’umuntu wigeze kubatererana ubwo bari i Pamfiliya , ntabafashe umurimo .
44015039	Impaka ziba urudaca kugeza aho batandukana , Barinaba ajyana na Mariko bafata ubwato berekeza i Shipure ,
44015040	naho Pawulo ahitamo kujyana na Silasi . Abavandimwe bamaze kumusabira no kumuragiza Nyagasani , arahaguruka aragenda .
44015041	Pawulo yambukiranya Siriya na Silisiya , akomeza za Kiliziya .
44016001	Hanyuma aza kugera atyo i Deribe n’i Lisitiri . Aho hakaba umwigishwa witwa Timote , umuhungu w’Umuyahudikazi wemeye , naho se akaba Umugereki .
44016002	Yashimwaga cyane n’abavandimwe b’aho i Lisitiri kimwe n’Ikoniyo .
44016003	Pawulo yifuza kujyana na we , ni ko kumugenya kubera Abayahudi bari muri ako karere , kandi bose bazi ko se ari Umugereki .
44016004	Mu migi yose banyuragamo , Pawulo na Silasi babagezagaho ibyemezo byafashwe n’Intumwa hamwe n’abakuru b’ikoraniro b’i Yeruzalemu , bakabasaba kubukurikiza .
44016005	Bityo Kiliziya zirushaho gukomera mu kwemera , kandi zikiyongera buri munsi .
44016006	Pawulo na Silasi bambukiranya Furujiya n’akarere kose k’Ubugalati , kuko Roho Mutagatifu yari yababujije kwamamaza ijambo ry’Imana muri Aziya .
44016007	Ngo bagere ku mbibi za Misiya , bagerageza kujya muri Bitiniya , ariko Roho wa Yezu arababuza .
44016008	Nuko bambukiranya Misiya , baramanuka bajya i Torowadi .
44016009	Ijoro rimwe , Pawulo arabonekerwa ; abona umuntu wo muri Masedoniya amuhagaze imbere amwinginga , ati « Ambukira muri Masedoniya , uze udutabare ! »
44016010	Pawulo akimara kubonekerwa , dutangira gushaka uko twajya muri Masedoniya , kuko twari tumenye neza ko Imana iduhamagariye kuhamamaza Inkuru Nziza .
44016011	Nuko dufatira ubwato i Torowadi , twambuka tugana kuri Samotirasi , bukeye turakomeza n’i Neyapoli .
44016012	Tuhavuye tujya i Filipi , ari wo mugi mukuru wa Masedoniya , wari utuwe n’Abanyaroma benshi . Muri uwo mugi rero tuhamara iminsi .
44016013	Ku munsi w’isabato , dusohoka mu mugi tugana iruhande rw’umugezi , ahantu twibwiraga ko bagomba kuba bahasengera . Nuko turicara , dutangira kuganira n’abagore bari bahakoraniye .
44016014	Umwe muri bo witwaga Lidiya , ukomoka mu mugi wa Tiyatira , akaba n’umucuruzikazi w’imyenda y’imihemba , yari asanzwe asenga Imana . Nuko atega amatwi kuko Nyagasani yari yamuhaye umutima wo kwita ku byo Pawulo yavugaga .
44016015	Ngo amare kubatizwa kimwe n’abo mu rugo rwe bose , aratwinginga ati « Niba mubona koko ko nemera Nyagasani , nimuze mucumbike iwanjye . » Ni ko kuduhatira kubyemera .
44016016	Umunsi umwe , ubwo twajyaga ahantu basengeraga , duhura n’umukobwa w’umuja wahanzweho na roho mbi yamuteraga kuvuga ibizaba ; ibyo bigatuma aronkera ba shebuja inyungu nyinshi .
44016017	Akomeza kudukurikirana twe na Pawulo , asakuza ati « Aba bantu ni abagaragu b’Imana Isumbabyose ; barabamenyesha inzira y’umukiro . »
44016018	Amara iminsi myinshi abigenza atyo . Pawulo rero bimaze kumurambira , arahindukira abwira iyo roho mbi , ati « Mu izina rya Nyagasani Yezu Kristu , ndagutegetse ngo : sohoka muri uwo mukobwa ! » Ako kanya imuvamo .
44016019	Ba shebuja babonye ko nta nyungu bakimutezeho , bafata Pawulo na Silasi , barabakurubana no ku kibuga cy’umugi , babashyira abategetsi .
44016020	Nuko babashyikiriza abacamanza bakuru , barababwira bati « Aba bantu baratera imvururu mu mugi wacu . Ni Abayahudi
44016021	kandi baramamaza imigenzo tudashobora kwemera no gukurikiza kuko turi Abanyaroma . »
44016022	Ubwo rubanda na bo barabahagurukira . Nuko abacamanza babashishimurira imyambaro , bategeka ko babakubita ibiboko .
44016023	Bamaze kubarema inguma , babajugunya mu buroko , bategeka umurinzi kubarinda abyitayeho .
44016024	Umurinzi ngo abone ko ahawe itegeko rikomeye , abashyira mu nzu yo hirya cyane , amaguru yabo ayaboheye ku biti .
44016025	Ahagana mu gicuku , Pawulo na Silasi barasenga , baririmba ibisingizo by’Imana , izindi mfungwa zibateze amatwi .
44016026	Nuko ako kanya haba umutingito ukomeye w’isi , imfatizo z’uburoko ziranyeganyega , imiryango yose ihita yikingura , iminyururu yari iboshye imfungwa zose iracikagurika .
44016027	Umurinzi w’uburoko akangutse , abona imiryango yose ikinguye . Yibwira ko imfungwa zacitse , ni ko gukura inkota ashaka kwiyica .
44016028	Ariko Pawulo atera hejuru cyane , aramubwira ati « Uramenye ntiwigirire nabi , twese turi hano . »
44016029	Nuko uwo murinzi asaba urumuri , yinjira ahinda umushyitsi , maze yikubita imbere ya Pawulo na Silasi .
44016030	Hanyuma arabasohokana no hanze , arababaza ati « Bategetsi banjye , ngomba gukora iki kugira ngo nkire ? »
44016031	Baramusubiza bati « Wemere Nyagasani Yezu , uzakira , wowe n’urugo rwawe . »
44016032	Nuko bamubwira ijambo rya Nyagasani , we n’abo mu rugo rwe bose .
44016033	Ako kanya muri iryo joro , arabajyana yuhagira inguma zabo , ahera ko abatizwa hamwe n’urugo rwe rwose .
44016034	Hanyuma ajyana Pawulo na Silasi iwe arabazimanira , yishimana n’abo mu rugo rwe bose , kubera ko yemeye Imana .
44016035	Bumaze gucya , abacamanza bakuru batuma abantu kubwira uwo murinzi w’uburoko bati « Rekura abo bantu ! »
44016036	Umurinzi w’uburoko na we amenyesha Pawulo iyo nkuru ati « Abacamanza bantumyeho ngo mbarekure , none rero nimusohoke mwigendere amahoro ! »
44016037	Ariko Pawulo arasubiza ati « Badukubitiye mu ruhame nta rubanza rwadutsinze , ndetse batujugunya mu buroko kandi dufite ubwenegihugu bw’Abanyaroma . None baragira ngo baturekure rwihishwa ? Ibyo ni ibidashoboka ! Ahubwo nibiyizire ubwabo , baturekure ! »
44016038	Abo bantu batumwe bajya kubwira abacamanza bakuru ayo magambo . Ngo bumve ko Pawulo na Silasi bafite ubwenegihugu bw’Abanyaroma bibatera ubwoba .
44016039	Baraza babitwaraho , hanyuma barabarekura , babinginga ngo babavire mu mugi .
44016040	Pawulo na Silasi bamaze kuva mu buroko bajya kwa Lidiya , babonana n’abavandimwe . Bamaze kubakomeza umutima , baragenda .
44017001	Banyura Amfipoli n’i Apoloniya , bagera i Tesaloniki , aho hakaba isengero ry’Abayahudi .
44017002	Pawulo rero yinjira mu isengero nk’uko yari abimenyereye , yikurikiranya amasabato atatu yose ajya impaka na bo , ahereye ku Byanditswe .
44017003	Yasobanuraga kandi akerekana ko Kristu yagombaga kubabara , akazuka mu bapfuye . Yungamo ndetse ati « Kristu ni uwo Yezu ndiho mbamenyesha . »
44017004	Bamwe mu Bayahudi baremera , bifatanya na Pawulo na Silasi kimwe n’Abagereki benshi bubahaga Imana , ndetse n’abagore b’abanyacyubahiro batari bake .
44017005	Nyamara Abayahudi bararakara , bakorakoranya abantu b’ibirara bararuje mu mayira , biremamo inteko maze bateza imidugararo mu mugi . Nuko biroha ku nzu ya Yasoni bashaka Pawulo na Silasi ngo babazane imbere y’ikoraniro rya rubanda .
44017006	Bababuze , bakurubana Yasoni n’abandi bavandimwe , babashyira abatware b’umugi , basakuza bati « Abo bantu bateye isi yose hejuru , none bageze hano Yasoni arabakira .
44017007	Abo bose barakora ibinyuranyije n’amategeko ya Kayizari , bavuga ko hari undi mwami witwa Yezu . »
44017008	Urwo rusaku rutera impagarara muri rubanda no mu batware b’umugi ,
44017009	bategeka Yasoni na bagenzi be gutanga ingurano , hanyuma barabarekura .
44017010	Nuko nijoro abavandimwe bacikisha Pawulo na Silasi , babohereza i Beroya . Ngo bagereyo , binjira mu isengero ry’Abayahudi .
44017011	Abantu b’aho barushaga ubupfura ab’i Tesaloniki , bakirana umutima mwiza ijambo ry’Imana , buri munsi bagasesengura Ibyandi tswe , kugira ngo barebe niba ibyo Pawulo avuga ari ko biri .
44017012	Benshi muri bo baremera , kimwe n’Abagerekikazi b’abanyacyubahiro , n’abagabo batari bake .
44017013	Ariko Abayahudi b’i Tesaloniki ngo bamenye ko Pawulo yamamaza ijambo ry’Imana i Beroya , bahita bajyayo , bateza impagarara n’imidugararo ro muri rubanda .
44017014	Uwo mwanya , abavandimwe bohereza Pawulo ku nyanja , naho Silasi na Timote baguma aho ngaho .
44017015	Abari baherekeje Pawulo barakomeza bamugeza Atene , hanyuma bahindukirana ubutumwa bugenewe Silasi na Timote , bubategeka ko bazamugeraho bidatinze .
44017016	Igihe Pawulo akibategerereje Atene , ashengurwa cyane no kubona uwo mugi ugwiriyemo ibigirwamana .
44017017	Buri munsi yajyaga mu isengero , akajya impaka n’Abayahudi n’abandi bubaha Imana , ndetse no ku karubanda akajya impaka n’abahazaga .
44017018	Hari ndetse n’abahanga bamwe bakurikizaga inyigisho za Epikuri n’iz’Abanyastowa , nuko batangira kujya impaka na we . Bamwe bakabaza bati « Mbese iyo ndondogozi irashaka kuvuga iki ? » Abandi bakavuga bati « Agomba kuba ari umwigisha w’imana z’inyamahanga » , kuko bumvaga Pawulo yamamaza ibyerekeye Yezu n’izuka .
44017019	Nuko baramufata , bamujyana mu rukiko rwabo rwitwa Areyopago , bavuga bati « Dushobora se kumenya iby’izo nyigisho nshya wamamaza ?
44017020	Kuko ibyo utubwira turumva ari ibyaduka , none turifuza kumenya icyo bivuga . »
44017021	Koko rero , Abanyatene bose n’abanyamahanga bahatuye , nta kindi bakoraga uretse kumva no kubara inkuru z’inzaduka .
44017022	Pawulo ahagarara rwagati mu rukiko , araterura ati « Yemwe bantu ba Atene , ndabona ko mushishikarira iyobokamana ku buryo bukataje !
44017023	Koko rero , ubwo nagendagendaga mu mihanda y’umugi wanyu , nagiye mbona amashusho y’Imana zanyu , ndetse ndabukwa n’urutambiro rwanditsweho ngo ’ Urw’imana itaramenyekana . ’ None rero , iyo Mana musenga mutayizi , ni yo nje kubamenyesha .
44017024	Imana yaremye isi n’ibiyirimo byose , yo Mugenga w’ijuru n’isi , ntitura mu ngoro zubatswe n’ibiganza by’abantu ,
44017025	ntikorerwa n’ibiganza by’abantu nk’aho hari icyo ikennye , ahubwo ni yo iha bose ubugingo , ikabaha umwuka n’ibindi bakeneye byose .
44017026	Yaremye amoko yose y’abantu ikurije ku muntu umwe , iyatuza ku bwisanzure bwose bw’isi ; yayashyiriyeho ibihe uko bisimburana , ibakebera imbibi z’aho bagomba gutura .
44017027	Ibyo Imana yabigiriye kugira ngo wenda nibayishakashaka babashe kuyishyikira , kuko mu by’ukuri itari kure ya buri muntu muri twe .
44017028	Ni yo dukesha ubugingo , ubwinyagambure n’ukubaho uko ari ko kose , nk’uko bamwe mu basizi banyu bigeze kubivuga bati ’ Koko turi inkomoko yayo . ’
44017029	Ubwo rero dukomoka ku Mana , ntitugomba gutekereza ko kamere y’Imana imeze nka bya bishushanyo bibajwe muri zahabu , muri feza , cyangwa se mu ibuye , bikomoka ku bukorikori n’ubugenge bya muntu .
44017030	Imana rero yirengagije ibyo bihe by’ubujiji , none irahamagara abantu bose iyo bava bakagera ngo bisubireho ,
44017031	kuko yashyizeho umunsi igomba gucira isi urubanza rutabera , ikoresheje umuntu yabigeneye , nk’uko yahaye bose icyemezo , umunsi imuzura mu bapfuye . »
44017032	Pawulo ngo avuge iby’izuka ry’abapfuye , bamwe muri bo bamuha urw’amenyo , abandi baramubwira bati « Kuri iyo ngingo , tuzakumva ikindi gihe ! »
44017033	Nuko Pawulo abavamo atyo .
44017034	Nyamara bamwe bifatanya na we baremera . Muri bo hakaba Diyoniziyo , umujyanama mu Rukiko , n’umugore witwa Damari , n’abandi .
44018001	Nyuma y’ibyo , Pawulo ava Atene ajya i Korinti .
44018002	Ahasanga Umuyahudi witwa Akwila ukomoka i Ponto , wari uherutse kuva mu Butaliyani n’umugore we Purisila , kuko umwami w’i Roma , Kalawudiyo , yari yategetse Abayahudi bose kuhava . Pawulo amenyana na bo ,
44018003	kandi kubera ko yari ahuje umwuga na bo , — bari ababoshyi b’amahema — , aguma iwabo bagakorana uwo mwuga .
44018004	Buri munsi w’isabato yafataga ijambo mu isengero , akagerageza kwemeza Abayahudi n’Abagereki .
44018005	Nuko Silasi na Timote bamaze kuhagera baturutse i Masedoniya , Pawulo yiyegurira wese ijambo ry’Imana , yemeza Abayahudi ko Yezu ari we Mukiza .
44018006	Nyamara bo bakamurwanya kandi bakamutuka , ni ko gukunguta imyambaro ye , ababwira ati « Amaraso yanyu azabahame ! Jye ndi umwere , ndetse no kuva ubu nigiriye mu banyamahanga . »
44018007	Avuye aho ngaho , ajya ku witwa Tito Yusito , umuntu wubahaga Imana , akaba yari atuye iruhande rw’isengero .
44018008	Kirisipo , umutware w’isengero , yemera Nyagasani n’urugo rwe rwose , ndetse n’Abanyakorinti benshi bumvise amagambo ya Pawulo baremera , barabatizwa .

44018015	ariko ubwo ari impaka zerekeye ku nyigisho , ku mazina no ku mategeko yanyu bwite , nimubyirangirize ubwanyu . Jye sinshaka kuba umucamanza w’ibyo ! »
44018016	Nuko abirukana mu rukiko .

44018019	Bageze Efezi , Pawulo asiga bagenzi be aho ngaho , yinjira mu isengero atangira kwigisha Abayahudi .
44018020	Bamusaba kuhamara igihe kirekire ariko arabyanga ;
44018021	ahubwo abasezeraho ababwira ati « Niba Imana ibishatse , nzagaruka iwanyu . » Afata ubwato ava Efezi ,
44018022	yomokera i Kayizareya ajya gusura Kiliziya y’aho , hanyuma amanuka ajya Antiyokiya ,
44018023	ahamara igihe kirekire . Ahavuye arakomeza azenguruka akarere k’Ubugalati na Furujiya , ashishikaza abigishwa bose .
44018024	Nuko Umuyahudi witwaga Apolo , kavukire ka Alegisandiriya , agera i Efezi . Akaba umuntu w’umuhanga mu Byanditswe .
44018025	Yari yarigishijwe inzira ya Nyagasani , akagira n’umwete mu kuvuga ibyerekeye Yezu , kandi akabyigisha uko biri , n’ubwo yari azi gusa batisimu ya Yohani .
44018026	Ubwo atangira kuvugira mu isengero ashize amanga , Purisila na Akwila ngo bamwumve bamujyana iwabo , bamusobanurira kurushaho inzira y’Imana .
44018027	Hanyuma Apolo ashatse kujya muri Akaya , abavandimwe bamutera inkunga kandi bandikira abigishwa b’aho ngo bamwakire neza . Agezeyo , agirira akamaro abemeye babikesha ubuntu bw’Imana ,
44018028	kuko yatsindaga impaka Abayahudi ku mugaragaro , abereka mu Byanditswe ko Yezu ari we Kristu .
44019001	Igihe Apolo yari i Korinti , Pawulo na we agera i Efezi , aturutse mu bihugu by’amajyaruguru . Ahasanga abigishwa bamwe ,

44019007	Bose hamwe bari bageze nko ku bantu cumi na babiri .

44019009	Ariko bamwe bakomeje kunangira umutima banga kwemera , bagatuka inzira ya Nyagasani mu ruhame . Pawulo ni ko gutandukana na bo , ajyana n’abigishwa akabigishiriza buri munsi mu ishuri ry’umuntu witwa Tirano .

44019011	Imana yakoreshaga Pawulo ibitangaza bidasanzwe ,

44019014	Abakoraga ibyo , ni abahungu barindwi b’Umuyahudi witwaga Seba , akaba n’umuherezabitambo mukuru .

44019016	Nuko uwo muntu wari wahanzweho na roho mbi arabasimbukira , abarusha amaboko bose maze abagirira nabi , kugeza ubwo baturumbuka mu nzu bagahunga bambaye ubusa kandi ari inkomere .
44019017	Abaturage bose b’i Efezi , Abayahudi kimwe n’Abagereki , ngo babimenye bashya ubwoba , basingiza izina rya Nyagasani Yezu .

44019021	Nyuma y’ibyo , Pawulo abwirijwe na Roho Mutagatifu , yiyemeza kujya i Yeruzalemu anyuze muri Masedoniya no muri Akaya . Yaravugaga ati « Nimara kugerayo , bizaba ngombwa no kujya i Roma . »

44019024	Hakaba rero umucuzi witwaga Demetiriyo , wacuraga mu muringa udushushanyo tw’ingoro z’ikigirwamana cyitwa Aritemisi , bikaba byaramuzaniraga we n’abo bakoranaga inyungu zitangaje .

44019026	None rero , nk’uko mubyirebera kandi mukabyiyumvira , Pawulo uwo aroshya rubanda rwose , atari Efezi honyine , ahubwo no muri Aziya yose , ababwira ko imana dukora atari zo .
44019027	Si ugutinya gusa ko umwuga wahinyuka , ahubwo n’ingoro y’imanakazi nkuru Aritemisi ishobora guta agaciro , igasuzugurika kandi ari yo isengwa n’Abanyaziya , ndetse n’abantu b’isi yose . »

44019036	Ubwo rero nta we ubihakana , mugomba gutuza mukareka guhubuka .

44020001	Izo mpagarara zimaze guhosha , Pawulo akoranya abigishwa , abarema agatima , abasezeraho yerekeza muri Masedoniya .
44020002	Amaze kwambukiranya iyo ntara yose , kandi ari na ko agenda abwira abavandimwe amagambo arambuye yo kubakomeza , aza kugera mu Bugereki ,
44020003	ahamara amezi atatu . Nyamara ashaka gufata ubwato ngo ajye muri Siriya , amenya ko Abayahudi bamugambaniye ; ni bwo yiyemeje kongera kunyura muri Masedoniya .
44020004	Muri urwo rugendo yari aherekejwe na Sopateri , mwene Piro w’i Beroya , Arisitariko na Sekundi b’i Tesaloniki , Gayo w’i Deribe na Timote , hamwe na Tushiko na Tirofimo bo muri Aziya .
44020005	Abo batubanje imbere , badutegerereza i Torowadi .
44020006	Naho twebwe , iminsi y’imigati idasembuye irangiye , dufatira ubwato i Filipi , tubasanga i Torowadi nyuma y’iminsi itanu , tuhamara icyumweru cyose .
44020007	Ku wa mbere w’icyumweru , ubwo twari duteraniye hamwe ngo tumanyure umugati , Pawulo wari uraye ari bugende aganira n’abavandimwe kugeza mu gicuku .
44020008	Mu cyumba cyo mu nzu yo hejuru aho twari duteraniye , hakaga amatara menshi .
44020009	Nuko umusore witwa Ewutiko akaba yicaye mu idirishya igihe Pawulo yigishaga . Inyigisho irambiranye , aza gutwarwa n’ibitotsi byinshi ; ni ko guhanuka mu igorofa ya gatatu , yitura hasi , bahaterura uwapfuye .

44020012	Naho wa musore bamuzana ari mutaraga , maze ibyishimo biba byose .
44020013	Twe rero tujya mu bwato tugenda mbere twerekeje ahitwa Aso , aho twagombaga kwakirira Pawulo , kuko we yari yagennye kujyayo anyuze inzira y’ubutaka .
44020014	Nuko adusanga Aso tumushyira mu bwato , turambuka tujya i Mitilena .
44020015	Bukeye , tujya mu bwato tugera ahateganye n’ikirwa cyitwa Kiyo . Ku wundi munsi twambuka tugana i Samosi , ku munsi ukurikiyeho tugera i Mileto .

44020017	Pawulo ari i Mileto , ahamagaza abakuru ba Kiliziya ya Efezi .
44020018	Bamugezeho , arababwira ati « Muzi uko nabanye namwe kuva aho ngereye muri Aziya .
44020019	Nakoreye Nyagasani , niyoroheje ku buryo bwose , mu marira no mu magorwa naterwaga n’ubugambanyi bw’Abayahudi .
44020020	Nta cyo nabakinze mu byo nashoboraga kubabwira cyabagirira akamaro ; byose narabitangaje , mbibigishiriza mu ruhame kimwe no mu ngo .
44020021	Nashishikarizaga Abayahudi kimwe n’Abagereki kugarukira Imana no kwemera Umwami wacu Yezu .
44020022	None dore ngiye i Yeruzalemu mbibwirijwe na Roho Mutagatifu ; ibizambaho ngezeyo simbizi .
44020023	Icyakora , muri buri mugi , Roho Mutagatifu anyemeza ko ingoyi n’amakuba bihantegerereje .
44020024	Nyamara ku bwanjye , ndahamya ko amagara yanjye bwite nta cyo amariye ; icya ngombwa ni ukurangiza isiganwa ryanjye n’umurimo Nyagasani Yezu yanshinze wo guhamya Inkuru Nziza y’ineza Imana ibagirira .
44020025	Nzi neza ko kuva ubu mutazongera kumbona ukundi , mwebwe mwese abo nanyuzemo namamaza Ingoma y’Imana .
44020026	Ni cyo gitumye rero , uyu munsi nshobora kwemeza mu maso yanyu ko ndi umwere w’amaraso yanyu mwese ,
44020027	kuko nabamenyesheje umugambi wose w’Imana , nta cyo mbakinze .
44020028	Murimenye rero ubwanyu , mumenye n’ubushyo mwaragijwe na Roho Mutagatifu , mube abashumba ba Kiliziya y’Imana , Yezu yacunguje amaraso ye bwite .
44020029	Nzi neza ko nimara kugenda , muzinjirwamo n’ibirura by’ibihubuzi bitazababarira n’ubushyo .
44020030	Ndetse no muri mwe hazaduka abantu bavuga amagambo y’ibinyoma , azatuma bigarurira abigishwa .
44020031	Murabe maso rero , mwibuka ko mu myaka itatu yose , ijoro n’amanywa ndetse no mu marira , ntatuje kuburira buri muntu muri mwe .
44020032	Ubu rero mbaragije Nyagasani kugira ngo abababarire , maze abakomereshe ijambo rye , kandi ku bwa ryo abahe umurage hamwe n’abatagatifujwe bose .
44020033	Nta kintu cy’umuntu uwo ari we wese nararikiye , cyaba feza , cyaba zahabu , cyangwa umwambaro .
44020034	Namwe ubwanyu murabizi : ibi biganza byanjye mureba ni byo nkesha ibyo nabaga nkeneye byose , kimwe na bagenzi banjye .
44020035	Naberetse buri munsi ko ari ngombwa kuvunika dutyo , kugira ngo tugoboke abatishoboye , twibuka n’amagambo Nyagasani Yezu yivugiye ubwe ati ’ Utanga arahirwa kuruta uhabwa . ’ »
44020036	Pawulo amaze kuvuga ibyo , arapfukama hamwe n’abo bari kumwe bose , maze arasenga .
44020037	Nuko bose baraturika bararira , bamugwa mu ijosi , baramuhobera .
44020038	Bari bababajwe cyane n’uko yari amaze kuvuga ko batazongera kumubona ukundi . Nuko baramuherekeza bamugeza ku bwato .
44021001	Tumaze kubiyaka , tujya mu bwato tuboneza tugana i Kosi ; bukeye tugera i Rode , tuhava tujya i Patara .
44021002	Tuhasanga ubwato bwajyaga muri Fenisiya , turabwurira buratujyana .
44021003	Ngo tugere ahateganye n’ikirwa cya Shipure , ikirwa tugisiga ibumoso tugenda twerekeje muri Siriya maze twururukira i Tiri , kuko ari ho ubwato bwagombaga gusiga imitwaro .
44021004	Tuhamara iminsi irindwi kuko twari tuhasanze abigishwa , maze bayobowe na Roho Mutagatifu , babwira Pawulo ngo yoye kujya i Yeruzalemu .
44021005	Nyamara ya minsi ngo irangire , turahaguruka dukomeza urugendo , bose baraduherekeza hamwe n’abagore n’abana baturenza umugi . Nuko dupfukama aho ku nkombe y’inyanja turasenga ;
44021006	hanyuma dusezeranaho , twe twurira ubwato naho bo basubira iwabo .
44021007	Ubwo twebwe turangiza urugendo rwacu rwo kuva i Tiri , twururukira i Putolemayida , turamutsa abavandimwe b’aho , dusibira iwabo umunsi umwe .
44021008	Bukeye , turagenda tugera i Kayizareya twinjira kwa Filipo , umwogezi w’Inkuru Nziza , wari umwe muri ba Barindwi , nuko ducumbika iwe .
44021009	Yari afite abakobwa bane b’abari , bahanuraga .
44021010	Mu minsi twahamaze , haza kuza umuhanuzi wo muri Yudeya , akitwa Agabo .
44021011	Ngo agere aho turi , afata umukandara wa Pawulo , awibohesha amaguru n’amaboko avuga ati « Roho Mutagatifu aravuze ngo ’ Nyir’uy’umukandara , uku ni ko Abayahudi bazamubohera i Yeruzalemu , maze bamugabize abanyamahanga . ’ »
44021012	Tubyumvise , twe n’abavandimwe bo muri uwo mugi , twinginga Pawulo ngo yoye kujya i Yeruzalemu .
44021013	Nuko aradusubiza ati « Ikibateye kurira no kunshengura umutima ni iki ? Jye siniteguye kubohwa byonyine , ahubwo niteguye no gupfira i Yeruzalemu , mporwa izina rya Nyagasani Yezu . »
44021014	Kuko tutari dushoboye kubimwemeza , ntitwahatiriza turavuga tuti « Icyo Nyagasani ashaka nigikorwe ! »
44021015	Nyuma y’iyo minsi rero , tumaze kwegeranya ibintu byacu , turazamuka n’i Yeruzalemu .
44021016	Abigishwa b’i Kayizareya bari baduherekeje , batujyana gucumbika ku muntu witwa Munasoni ukomoka i Shipure , wari umwigishwa kuva kera .
44021017	Tugeze i Yeruzalemu , abavandimwe batwakirana ibyishimo .
44021018	Bukeye , Pawulo ajyana natwe kwa Yakobo , n’abakuru bose barahateranira .
44021019	Pawulo amaze kubaramutsa , abatekerereza ku buryo burambuye ibyo Imana yamukoresheje byose mu banyamahanga .
44021020	Abamwumvaga basingiza Imana , maze baramubwira bati « Muvandimwe , urabona ibihumbi by’Abayahudi bemeye uko bingana , nyamara dore bose barakiziritse ku Mategeko ya Musa .
44021021	Nuko rero , bumvise ko wigisha Abayahudi bose batuye mu mahanga kuzinukwa inyigisho ze , uvuga ngo ntibazongere ukundi kugenya abana babo no gukurikiza imigenzo yacu .
44021022	Byagenda bite rero ? Byanze bikunze kandi , bazamenya ko wageze ino .
44021023	None rero , ukore ibyo tugiye kukubwira . Dufite abantu bane bahize umuhigo ;
44021024	bajyane ukore umuhango wo kwisukura hamwe na bo , kandi ubishyurire ibyo bari gutanga kugira ngo bogoshwe . Bityo abantu bose bazamenya ko ibyo bakumviseho bidafite ishingiro , ahubwo ko nawe ubwawe witondera Amategeko .
44021025	Naho ku byerekeye abanyamahanga bemeye , twabandikiye tubabwira ibyemezo byacu : kwirinda inyama zatambiwe ibigirwamana , n’amaraso , n’inyama z’ibyanizwe , no kwirinda ubukozi bw’ibibi . »
44021026	Bukeye bw’uwo munsi , Pawulo ajyana na ba bantu , atangira umuhango wo kwisukura hamwe na bo . Hanyuma ajya mu Ngoro y'Imana kugira ngo bemeranywe umunsi ituro rya buri wese rizaherezwaho , barangije kwisukura .
44021027	Iminsi irindwi ijya kurangira , Abayahudi bo muri Aziya ngo babone Pawulo mu Ngoro , babyutsa imvururu muri rubanda rwose , maze baramufata .
44021028	Barasakuzaga bavuga bati « Bayisraheli , nimudutabare ! Dore uyu muntu agenda hose yigisha abantu bose , arwanya umuryango wacu kimwe n’Amategeko n’aha Hantu . Byongeye kandi , yinjije Abagereki mu Ngoro , ahumanya aha Hantu hatagatifu ! »
44021029	Koko rero , bavuze batyo kuko bari barabonye Tirofimo w’i Efezi ari kumwe na we mu mugi , bakeka ko Pawulo yamwinjije mu Ngoro .
44021030	Umugi wose ni ko kuvurungana , maze rubanda rwose rurahurura , bafata Pawulo bamuvana mu Ngoro bamujyana hanze , bahita bakinga imiryango .
44021031	Igihe bagishaka kumwica , iyo nkuru iba yageze ku mugaba w’ingabo , bamubwira bati « Yeruzalemu yose yavurunganye ! »
44021032	Aherako akoranya abasirikare n’abategeka babo , yihuta asanga icyo kivunge cy’abantu . Ngo babone uwo mugaba w’ingabo n’abasirikare , bareka gukubita Pawulo .
44021033	Nuko umugaba w’ingabo aramwegera , aramufata , maze ategeka ko bamuboha n’iminyururu ibiri ; hanyuma abaza uwo ari we n’icyo yakoze .
44021034	Ariko rubanda bagasakuza , umwe avuga ibye undi ibye . Umugaba w’ingabo abonye ko nta cyo ashoboye kumenya kubera uwo muvurungano , ategeka abasirikare kumujyana mu kigo cyabo .
44021035	Igihe bageze ku mabaraza , abasirikare bagombye guterura Pawulo babitewe n’ukuntu rubanda bari barakaye ,
44021036	kuko imbaga y’abantu uko yakabaye yari imukurikiye , basakuza bati « Nimumukureho ! »
44021037	Igihe bajyaga kumwinjiza mu kigo cy’abasirikare , Pawulo abaza umugaba w’ingabo ati « Mbese nshobora kugira icyo nkubwira ? » Undi aramusubiza ati « Uzi ikigereki ?
44021038	Aho none ntiwaba wa Munyamisiri uherutse gutera impagarara , agacikisha abantu ibihumbi bine b’abishi , akabajyana mu butayu ? »
44021039	Pawulo ni ko kumusubiza ati « Jyewe ndi Umuyahudi , ukomoka i Tarisi ho muri Silisiya , nkaba umuturage w’uwo mugi w’ikirangirire . None ndakwinginze ngo ureke ngire icyo mbwira iyi mbaga . »
44021040	Umugaba w’ingabo amaze kumwemerera , Pawulo ahagarara ku mabaraza , arambura ukuboko kugira ngo acecekeshe imbaga . Bamaze gutuza , ababwira mu rurimi rw’igihebureyi ati
44022001	« Bavandimwe kandi babyeyi , nimwumve ukwiregura kwanjye ngiye kubagezaho . »
44022002	Nuko ngo bumve avuze mu rurimi rw’igihebureyi , ituze rirushaho kuba ryose .
44022003	Arakomeza ati « Ndi Umuyahudi , navukiye i Tarisi ho muri Silisiya , ariko narerewe muri uyu mugi ; nigishwa na Gamaliyeli , antoza kwita byuzuye ku Mategeko y’abasekuruza . Imana nyirwanira ishyaka nk’uko namwe murirwana uyu munsi .
44022004	Natoteje abantu bakurikiraga iyi Nzira kugeza ubwo mbica , mboha abagabo n’abagore mbashyira mu buroko .
44022005	Umuherezabitambo mukuru hamwe n’abakuru b’umuryango ni bo ntanzeho abagabo , bo bampaye inzandiko nshyikiriza abavandimwe bacu b’i Damasi , ubwo najyagayo , ntumwe kuboha abariyo no kubazana i Yeruzalemu kugira ngo bahanwe .
44022006	Nuko igihe nkiri mu nzira negereje kugera i Damasi , ako kanya amanywa ava , urumuri ruturutse mu ijuru rurangota .
44022007	Nikubita hasi , maze numva ijwi rimbwira riti ’ Sawuli , Sawuli ! Urantotereza iki ? ’
44022008	Ndasubiza nti ’ Uri nde , Nyagasani ? ’ Iryo jwi rirongera riti ’ Ndi Yezu w’i Nazareti , uwo uriho utoteza . ’
44022009	Bagenzi banjye twari kumwe babonye urumuri , ariko ntibumve ijwi ry’uwo tuvugana .
44022010	Ni ko kubaza nti ’ Nkore iki se , Nyagasani ? ’ Nyagasani aransubiza ati ’ Haguruka ujye i Damasi , ni ho bazakubwira ibyo wagenewe gukora byose . ’
44022011	Ariko kubera ko icyezezi cy’urwo rumuri cyari cyampumye amaso , abo twari kumwe bagombye kundandata , ngera i Damasi .
44022012	Aho i Damasi hakaba umuntu witwa Ananiya , yari umuntu wubaha Imana , agakurikiza Amategeko kandi agashimwa n’Abayahudi bose bari bahatuye .
44022013	Aza kundeba maze arambwira ati « Sawuli , muvandimwe , humuka . ’ Ako kanya ndahumuka , maze ndamureba .
44022014	Nuko arambwira ati ’ Imana y’abasekuruza bacu yakugeneye kumenya icyo ishaka , kubona Intungane no kumva ijwi ryayo bwite .
44022015	Ugomba rero kuyibera umugabo mu bantu bose , ubamenyesha ibyo wabonye n’ibyo wumvise .
