44022016	None se kandi utegereje iki ? Haguruka wambaze Nyagasani , ubatizwe kandi uhanagurweho ibyaha byawe . ’
44022017	Nuko ngaruka i Yeruzalemu , igihe nari mu Ngoro nsenga nza gutwarwa ,
44022018	maze mbona Nyagasani wambwiraga ati ’ Ihute uve i Yeruzalemu bidatinze , kuko batazakira ibyo uzahamya binyerekeyeho . ’
44022019	Ubwo ndasubiza nti ’ Nyagasani , barabizi neza ko ari jye wajyaga mu masengero yose gufunga no gukubita abakwemera .
44022020	Ndetse n’igihe bamennye amaraso ya Sitefano umuhamya wawe , nanjye nari mpari nshyigikiye abo bishi be , kandi ndinze n’imyambaro yabo . ’
44022021	Ariko Nyagasani arambwira ati ’ Genda , kuko jyewe nshaka kugutuma ku bo mu mahanga ya kure . ’ »
44022022	Abayahudi bari bagumye kumutega amatwi kugeza ko avuze ayo magambo , batera hejuru bati « Umuntu nk’uyu agomba kuvanwa ku isi ! Ntakwiye kubaho ! »
44022023	Igihe bariho basakabaka , bajugunya ibishura byabo , ari na ko batumura umukungugu mu kirere ,
44022024	umugaba w’ingabo ategeka ko binjiza Pawulo mu kigo cy’abasirikare , no kumubaza babanje kumukubita ibiboko , kugira ngo amenye impamvu ituma rubanda bamuvugiriza induru .
44022025	Igihe babohaga Pawulo kugira ngo bamukubite , abaza umutegeka w’abasirikare wari umuhagarikiye ati « Mbese mufite uburenganzira bwo gukubita umuntu ufite ubwenegihugu bw’Abanyaroma , atari yanacirwa urubanza ? »
44022026	Uwo mutegeka w’abasirikare ngo abyumve , asanga umugaba w’ingabo , aramubaza ati « Ibyo ugiye gukora ni ibiki ? Ko uriya mugabo ari Umunyaroma ! »
44022027	Umugaba w’ingabo araza , abaza Pawulo ati « Ngaho mbwira , koko se uri Umunyaroma ? » Pawulo aramusubiza ati « Ni koko . »
44022028	Umugaba w’ingabo ni ko kuvuga ati « Nyamara jyewe narishye byinshi , kugira ngo mpabwe ubwo bwenegihugu ! » Pawulo aravuga ati « Jyewe rero narabuvukanye ! »
44022029	Abari bagiye kumukubita bahita bamureka ; umugaba w’ingabo agira ubwoba , aho amariye kumenya ko ari Umunyaroma kandi akaba yamuboshye .
44022030	Bukeye bw’uwo munsi , umugaba w’ingabo ashaka kumenya neza icyo Abayahudi barega Pawulo , aramubohora , hanyuma ategeka ko abatware b’abaherezabitambo n’Inama nkuru yose baterana , azana Pawulo amuhagarika imbere yabo .
44023001	Pawulo ahanga amaso Inama nkuru , ni ko guterura ati « Bavandimwe , kugeza uyu munsi ndumva nta kibi mfite ku mutima . »
44023002	Ariko Ananiya , umuherezabitambo mukuru , ategeka abari bakikije Pawulo kumukubita ku munwa . Nuko Pawulo aramubwira ati
44023003	« Ni wowe Imana izakubita , wa nkike we irabye ingwa ! Wicajwe no kuncira urubanza ukurikije Amategeko , none uhinyuye Amategeko , utegeka ko bankubita ! »
44023004	Abari bahagaze aho baravuga bati « Uratuka umuherezabitambo mukuru w’Imana ! »
44023005	Pawulo arabasubiza ati « Bavandimwe , nta bwo nari nzi ko ari umuherezabitambo mukuru , kuko byanditswe ngo ’ Ntugatuke umutware w’umuryango wawe . ’ »
44023006	Pawulo ngo amenye ko iryo koraniro rigizwe n’igice kimwe cy’Abasaduseyi , n’ikindi cy’Abafarizayi , avuga aranguruye imbere y’Inama nkuru ati « Bavandimwe , ndi Umufarizayi , nkaba umwana w’Abafarizayi . Icyatumye nshyirwa mu rubanza , ndazira ko niringira izuka ry’abapfuye . »
44023007	Ngo amare kuvuga ibyo , havuka amakimbirane mu Bafarizayi n’Abasaduseyi , ikoraniro risubiranamo .
44023008	Koko rero , Abasaduseyi bavugaga ko nta zuka , nta mumalayika , nta na roho bibaho , naho Abafarizayi bakemera ko bibaho .
44023009	Haba urusaku rwinshi , bituma bamwe mu bigishamategeko bo mu gice cy’Abafarizayi bahaguruka , barwana ishyaka bikomeye bagira bati « Nta kibi tubona kuri uyu muntu . Mbese none roho yaba yaravuganye na we , cyangwa se umumalayika ? »
44023010	Kubera ko amakimbirane yarushagaho gukomera , umugaba w’ingabo atinya ko bari butanyaguze Pawulo , ni ko gutegeka abasirikare ngo bamanuke bamuvane hagati yabo , bamusubize mu kigo cyabo .
44023011	Mu ijoro rikurikiyeho , Nyagasani abonekera Pawulo aramubwira ati « Komera ! Uko wambereye umugabo i Yeruzalemu , ni ko ugomba no kuzambera umugabo n’i Roma . »
44023012	Bukeye mu gitondo , bamwe mu Bayahudi bajya inama , ndetse barahira ko batazagira icyo barya cyangwa ngo banywe , batabanje kwica Pawulo .
44023013	Abari bahuje uwo mugambi bari abantu basaga mirongo ine .
44023014	Basanga abatware b’Abaherezabitambo n’abakuru b’umuryango , barababwira bati « Twarahiye dukomeje ko nta cyo turi bukoze ku munwa , tutabanje kwica Pawulo .
44023015	None rero mwebwe , mwumvikane n’Inama nkuru , musabe umugaba w’ingabo amubazanire , nk’aho hari ikindi mushaka kumenya ku bimwerekeyeho . Ubwo natwe turaba twiteguye kumwica , atari yabageraho . »
44023016	Ariko mwishywa wa Pawulo ngo amenye iby’icyo gico , araza yinjira mu kigo cy’abasirikare , abibwira Pawulo .
44023017	Pawulo ni ko guhamagara umwe mu bategeka b’abasirikare , aramubwira ati « Jyana uyu musore ku mugaba w’ingabo , kuko hari icyo ashaka kumumenyesha . »
44023018	Nuko aramujyana amugeza ku mugaba w’ingabo , maze aravuga ati « Imfungwa yitwa Pawulo yampamagaye , insaba kukugezaho uyu musore , ngo afite icyo akubwira . »
44023019	Umugaba w’ingabo ni ko kumufata ukuboko , amujyana ahiherereye , aramubaza ati « Icyo ushaka kumenyesha ni iki ? »
44023020	Uwo musore aramusubiza ati « Abayahudi bumvikanye ko ejo bazagusaba kuzana Pawulo mu Nama nkuru , bitwaje ko hari ibindi bashaka kumenya ku bimwerekeyeho .
44023021	Ntuzabemerere , kuko abantu basaga mirongo ine bamwubikiye , bakaba barahiye ko batazagira icyo barya cyangwa banywa batabanje kumwica . Bategereje gusa igisubizo cyawe . »
44023022	Nuko umugaba w’ingabo asezerera uwo musore , ariko abanje kumwihanangiriza ati « Uramenye ntugire umuntu n’umwe ubwira ibyo wamenyesheje ! »
44023023	Hanyuma ahamagara babiri mu bategeka b’abasirikare , arababwira ati « Nimutegure abasirikare magana abiri , abanyamafarasi mirongo irindwi , n’izindi ngabo magana abiri zitwaje amacumu , mwitegure guhaguruka saa tatu z’ijoro mujya i Kayizareya .
44023024	Mutegure kandi n’amafarasi yo guheka Pawulo , mumushyikirize umutware Feligisi , akiri mutaraga . »
44023025	Nuko umugaba w’ingabo yandikira umutware Feligisi muri aya magambo
44023026	« Jyewe Kalawudiyo Liziya , kuri Nyakubahwa umutware Feligisi : ndakuramutsa .
44023027	Uyu muntu nkoherereje yafashwe n’Abayahudi bashaka kumwica , ni bwo mpagobotse n’umutwe w’abasirikare ndamubaka , kuko nari maze kumenya ko afite ubwenegihugu bw’Abanyaroma .
44023028	Nashatse kumenya icyo bamurega , mujyana mu Nama nkuru ,
44023029	nsanga rero bamurega impaka z’ibyerekeye amategeko yabo , ariko nta kindi kintu na kimwe yakoze cyatuma apfa cyangwa ngo abohwe .
44023030	Aho menyeye ko bari biteguye kumwica , niyemeje kumukoherereza . Menyesheje kandi n’abamurega ko bazakugezaho ibirego byabo . Gira amahoro ! »
44023031	Nuko abasirikare bakora uko bategetswe , bajyana Pawulo muri iryo joro , bamugeza Antipatiri .
44023032	Bukeye , abanyamafarasi baba ari bo bakomeza kujyana na we , abandi bagaruka mu kigo cyabo .
44023033	Bageze i Kayizareya , bahereza umutware Feligisi urwandiko , bamushyikiriza na Pawulo .
44023034	Feligisi amaze gusoma urwandiko , abaza akarere Pawulo akomokamo . Aho amenyeye ko akomoka muri Silisiya ,
44023035	aravuga ati « Nzaba numva ibyawe , abakurega bamaze kugera hano . » Nuko ategeka ko arindirwa mu ngoro ya Herodi .
44024001	Hashize iminsi itanu , Ananiya umuherezabitambo mukuru amanukana na bamwe mu bakuru b’umuryango , hamwe n’umuburanyi wabo witwa Teritulo ; basanga umutware Feligisi kugira ngo bamuregere Pawulo .
44024002	Pawulo amaze guhamagarwa , Teritulo atangira kumurega agira ati « Nyakubahwa Feligisi , aya mahoro atuganjemo ni wowe tuyakesha , kandi n’ibyavuguruwe byinshi muri iki gihugu tubikesha umwete wawe .
44024003	Aho turi hose , ntidusiba buri gihe kwakira ibyo byiza , kandi turabigushimira cyane .
44024004	Ariko kugira ngo ntakurambira , ndagusaba ko watwihanganira uko ubisanganywe , ukumva muri make ibyo dushaka kukubwira .
44024005	Uyu muntu twasanze ari icyorezo , acumba urugomo mu Bayahudi bo ku isi yose , kandi akaba n’umutware w’agatsiko kayobye k’Abanyanazareti .
44024006	Ndetse yagerageje no guhumanya Ingoro y’Imana yacu , turamufata . ( Dushatse kumucira urubanza dukurikije amategeko yacu ,
44024007	ni bwo umugaba w’ingabo Liziya ahagobotse , amutwambura ku ngufu ,
44024008	ategeka ko abamuregaga bazagusanga ) . Nawe ubwawe umubajije , ushobora kumenya neza ko ibyo tumurega ari impamo . »
44024009	Abayahudi na bo baryungamo , bahamya ko ibyo byose ari ko biri .
44024010	Umutware Feligisi amaze kumuha ikimenyetso cyo kuvuga , Pawulo araterura ati « Nzi neza ko umaze imyaka myinshi ucira imanza abaturage b’iki gihugu cyacu , ni yo mpamvu nishimiye kwiregurira imbere yawe .
44024011	Nk’uko wowe ubwawe ushobora kubyigenzurira , iminsi ntirarenga cumi n’ibiri kuva aho nzamukiye i Yeruzalemu , njyanyweyo no gusenga .
44024012	Haba mu Ngoro , haba mu masengero cyangwa mu mugi , muri aba bantu nta wigeze ambona hari uwo tujya impaka , cyangwa ngo basange nteza imvururu muri rubanda .
44024013	Aba bantu nta n’ubwo bashobora kubona ibimenyetso byemeza ibyo bandega ubu ngubu .
44024014	Nyamara icyo nemereye imbere yawe , ni uko nkorera Imana y’abasekuruza , nkurikije Inzira aba bita agatsiko k’abayobye , nkaba nemera n’ibyanditswe byose mu Mategeko no mu Bahanuzi .
44024015	Mfite icyo cyizere ku Mana — kandi na bo turagisangiye — , ko hazabaho izuka ry’intungane kimwe n’iry’abagome .
44024016	Ni cyo gituma nihatira ubudatuza kugira umutimanama udahinyuka imbere y’Imana n’imbere y’abantu .
44024017	Nyuma y’imyaka myinshi , nagarutse i Yeruzalemu nzaniye umuryango wanjye imfashanyo z’abakene , ndetse n’amaturo .
44024018	Igihe nkiri muri ibyo , bansanga mu Ngoro maze kwisukura , ariko nta bantu benshi twari kumwe , yemwe nta n’urusaku ;
44024019	uretse bamwe mu Bayahudi bo muri Aziya . . . Abo ni bo bagombaga kuza kukundegaho , iyo bajya kugira ikibi bambonaho !
44024020	Cyangwa se aba na bo nibavuge ikosa bansanganye , igihe nari mpagaze imbere y’Inama nkuru !
44024021	Naba se nzira iri jambo navugiye rwagati muri bo ndanguruye nti ’ Mbese byaba ari uko nemera izuka ry’abapfuye , byatumye uyu munsi munshyira mu rubanza ? ’ »
44024022	Feligisi wari uzi neza iby’iyo Nzira , asubika urubanza avuga ati « Umugaba w’ingabo Liziya namara kuza , nzarangiza ibyanyu . »
44024023	Nuko ashinga umutegeka w’abasirikare kurinda Pawulo aho yari ari mu buroko , ariko ngo amureke yishyire yizane , kandi ngo ntabuze n’umwe mu be kumuha icyo akeneye .
44024024	Hashize iminsi mike Feligisi azana n’umugore we Durusila , wari Umuyahudikazi . Ahamagaza Pawulo , maze amutega amatwi ngo amubwire ibyerekeye kwemera Yezu Kristu .
44024025	Ariko ngo ikiganiro kigere ku byerekeye ubutabera , ukwifata n’urubanza ruzaza , Feligisi agira ubwoba , ni ko kuvuga ati « Ba urekeye aho wigendere , ninongera kubona igihe nzagutumaho . »
44024026	Yari yizeye kandi ko Pawulo yazamuha amafaranga , ni yo mpamvu yahoraga amutumiza kenshi ngo baganire .
44024027	Imyaka ibiri ishize , Feligisi asimburwa n’uwitwa Porikiyo Fesito ; maze Feligisi ashaka kwikundisha ku Bayahudi , asiga Pawulo mu buroko .
44025001	Nyuma y’iminsi itatu Fesito ageze muri ako karere , ava i Kayizareya ajya i Yeruzalemu .
44025002	Abatware b’abaherezabitambo n’abanyacyubahiro bo mu Bayahudi bamusanganiza ibirego barega Pawulo ; bamwinginga
44025003	bamusaba kubagirira ubuntu ngo amutumize aze i Yeruzalemu , kuko bari baciye ibico byo kumwubikira ngo bamutsinde mu nzira .
44025004	Nuko Fesito abasubiza ko Pawulo afungiye i Kayizareya , kandi ko na we ubwe agomba gusubirayo bidatinze .
44025005	Arongera ati « Kandi ababa babishoboye muri mwe , baze tujyane i Kayizareya , barege uwo muntu niba hari ikibi yakoze ! »
44025006	Fesito amara iwabo iminsi itarenze umunani cyangwa icumi , asubira i Kayizareya . Bukeye ajya mu rukiko , maze ategeka ko bazana Pawulo .
44025007	Bamugejeje aho , Abayahudi bamanutse i Yeruzalemu baramukikiza , batangira kumurega byinshi kandi bikomeye , badashobora no kubonera gihamya .
44025008	Nuko Pawulo ariregura ati « Nta kosa nigeze nkora , haba ku Mategeko y’Abayahudi , haba ku Ngoro cyangwa se kuri Kayizari . »
44025009	Ariko Fesito ashatse kwikundisha ku Bayahudi , abaza Pawulo ati « Mbese uremera kujya i Yeruzalemu kugira ngo abe ariho ucirirwa urubanza mu maso yanjye ? »
44025010	Pawulo arasubiza ati « Dore ndi mu rukiko rwa Kayizari , ni ho ngomba gucirirwa urubanza . Nta kibi nakoreye Abayahudi nk’uko nawe ubizi neza .
44025011	Niba koko ibyo bimpama , cyangwa se niba narakoze icyaha gikwiriye urupfu , sinanga gupfa . Ariko niba ibirego aba bantu bandega nta kuri kurimo , nta muntu ufite uburenganzira bwo kubangabiza . Njuririye Kayizari ! »
44025012	Nuko Fesito amaze kuvugana n’abajyanama be , arasubiza ati « Ubwo ujuririye Kayizari , uzajye kwa Kayizari . »
44025013	Hashize iminsi mike , umwami Agripa na Berenisa bagera i Kayizareya , baje gusura Fesito .
44025014	Bahamaze igihe , Fesito atekerereza umwami ibya Pawulo , agira ati « Hano hari umuntu Feligisi yasize mu buroko .
44025015	Igihe nari i Yeruzalemu , abatware b’abaherezabitambo n’abakuru b’Abayahudi baramundegera , bansaba ko yakwicwa .
44025016	Mbasubiza ko atari akamenyero ku Banyaroma gucira umuntu urubanza , nta we uhingutse ngo amushinje na we abone umwanya wo kwiregura , ngo yiyezeho icyaha .
44025017	Ubwo rero baje hano , nanjye sinazarira , bukeye nicara mu rukiko mpamagaza uwo muntu .
44025018	Abamuregaga baramukikiza , ariko ntibagira ikirego gikomeye na kimwe bahingutsa mu byo nakekaga .
44025019	Ahubwo bafite ibyo bapfa byerekeye idini yabo , ariko ku buryo bw’umwihariko bagapfa umuntu witwa Yezu wapfuye , nyamara Pawulo akaba yemeza ko ari muzima .
44025020	Mbonye ko ntashobora gukemura ibyo bibazo byabo , mbaza Pawulo niba yemera kujya i Yeruzalemu , ngo abe ari ho acirirwa urubanza ku byo bamuregaga .
44025021	Ariko Pawulo arajurira , ashaka ko urubanza rwe rwarangizwa na Nyir’icyubahiro ; ubwo nanjye ntegeka ko bamurinda kugeza igihe nzamwohereza kwa Kayizari . »
44025022	Agripa ni ko kubwira Fesito ati « Nanjye ndashaka kumva uwo muntu ! » Undi aramusubiza ati « Ejo uzamwumva . »
44025023	Nuko bukeye , Agripa na Berenisa binjirana ishema mu rukiko , bashagawe n’abagaba b’ingabo hamwe n’abanyacyubahiro bo muri uwo mugi , maze Fesito ategeka ko bazana Pawulo .
44025024	Fesito afata ijambo , agira ati « Mwami Agripa , namwe mwese abateraniye hano , murabona uyu muntu . Imbaga yose y’Abayahudi yaje kumundegera i Yeruzalemu , ndetse na n’ubu baracyasakuza , bavuga ko adakwiye kubaho .
44025025	Jye nasanze nta cyo yakoze cyatuma akwiye gupfa . Nyamara kuko we yajuririye Nyir’icyubahiro , niyemeza kumumwoherereza .
44025026	Icyakora , nta kintu na kimwe cy’ukuri nabonye naheraho nandikira Kayizari ku bimwerekeyeho . Ni cyo gitumye muzana imbere yanyu , cyane cyane wowe , mwami Agripa , kugira ngo nimumara kumubaza mbonereho kugira icyo nandika .
44025027	Kuko nasanze bidafututse kohereza imfungwa , ntagaragaje neza icyo iregwa . »
44026001	Nuko Agripa abwira Pawulo ati « Ngaho iregure . » Pawulo arambura ukuboko , atangira kwiregura ati
44026002	« Mwami Agripa , biranshimishije kurushaho , kuko ibyo Abayahudi bandega byose , uyu munsi ngiye kubyiregurira imbere yawe ,
44026003	cyane cyane kuko nawe usanzwe uzi neza imico y’Abayahudi n’ibyo bajyaho impaka . Ni cyo gitumye ngusaba ngo wihangane unyumve .
44026004	Abayahudi bose bazi imibereho yanjye uhereye mu buto bwanjye , uko nabayeho rwagati mu muryango wanjye , ndetse n’i Yeruzalemu .
44026005	Baranzi kuva kera , babishatse bashobora guhamya ko nabaye umuyoboke w’ishyaka rikomeye ry’idini yacu , nkurikije umuco w’Abafarizayi .
44026006	None ubu ndaregwa ko nizera amasezerano Imana yagiriye abasekuruza bacu .
44026007	Ayo masezerano ni yo nyine imiryango yacu uko ari cumi n’ibiri idahwema kwizera ko azasohozwa , bigatuma ishishikarira gusenga Imana amanywa n’ijoro . None rero , Mwami , iby’ayo mizero ni byo ndegwa n’Abayahudi .
44026008	Mbese ye , ni mpamvu ki mudashobora kwemera ko Imana ishobora kuzura abapfuye ?
44026009	Nanjye ubwanjye , natekerezaga ko ngomba kurwanya ku buryo bwose izina rya Yezu w’i Nazareti .
44026010	Ni na byo nakoze i Yeruzalemu ; nashyize mu buroko abenshi mu batagatifujwe , mpawe uburenganzira n’abatware b’abaherezabitambo ; igihe kandi babaciraga urwo gupfa nkabishyigikira .
44026011	Nazengurutse amasengero yose mbatoteza bikomeye , ndetse nkanabahatira gutuka Imana . Narabarakariraga bikabije , ku buryo nabakurikiraga kugeza no mu migi yo mu mahanga .
44026012	Ni cyo cyatumye umunsi umwe njya i Damasi , mfite ububasha n’amabwiriza by’abatware b’abaherezabitambo .
44026013	Nuko ndi mu nzira rero , Mwami , amanywa ava mbona urumuri rutambukije izuba kwaka ruturutse mu ijuru , rurangota hamwe n’abo twari kumwe .
44026014	Ubwo twese twikubita hasi , maze numva ijwi rimbwira mu rurimi rw’igihebureyi , riti ’ Sawuli , Sawuli ! Urantotereza iki ? Biragukomereye kwishita ku rubambo . ’
44026015	Nuko ndabaza nti ’ Uri nde , Nyagasani ? ’ Nyagasani aransubiza ati ’ Ndi Yezu , uwo uriho utoteza .
44026016	Ariko byuka , maze uhagarare ! Igitumye nkubonekera ni uko nakugeneye kuba umugaragu wanjye n’umuhamya w’ibyo ubonye , n’uw’ibyo nzakwereka hanyuma .
44026017	Nzakugobotora umuryango wawe kimwe n’iy’abanyamahanga nkoherejemo ,
44026018	kugira ngo ubahumure amaso , ubahindure bave mu mwijima bagane urumuri , bave mu ngoma ya Sekibi bagarukire Imana ; kugira ngo nibanyemera bagirirwe imbabazi z’ibyaha , kandi bahabwe umurage hamwe n’abatagatifujwe . ’
44026019	Kubera iyo mpamvu rero , mwami Agripa , nta cyari kumbuza kumvira ibyo neretswe biturutse mu ijuru .
44026020	Mpera ko mbanziriza ku bantu b’i Damasi , ngera i Yeruzalemu no mu karere kose ka Yudeya no mu mahanga yose , menyesha abo bose ngo bisubireho kandi bagarukire Imana , babeho ku buryo bukwiriye abicujije .
44026021	Ni cyo cyatumye Abayahudi bamfata igihe nari mu Ngoro , bakagerageza kunyica .
44026022	Nyamara no kugeza uyu munsi Imana iracyantabara , nkaba ngikomeza guhamya mu maso ya bose , abato kimwe n’abakuru , ibyavuzwe n’abahanuzi na Musa ku bigomba kuzaba kandi nta cyo nongeyeho :
44026023	bityo mpamya ko Kristu yagombaga kubabara , kandi ko aho amariye kuzuka uwa mbere mu bapfuye , azasakaza urumuri mu muryango wacu no mu mahanga . »
44026024	Pawulo , ngo ageze aho yiregura , Fesito atera hejuru ati « Pawulo , wasaze ! Wize byinshi byo kugutera ibisazi ! »
44026025	Pawulo aramusubiza ati « Nyakubahwa Fesito , sinasaze , ahubwo ndavuga amagambo y’ukuri kandi ashyira mu gaciro .
44026026	Ni yo mpamvu mvuga nta cyo nishisha kuko umwami mbwira abizi neza byose , nkaba mpamya ko nta na kimwe cyamusobye , kuko bitakorewe mu bwihisho .
44026027	Mwami Agripa , mbese waba wemera iby’abahanuzi ? Na ko ndabizi : urabyemera . »
44026028	Nuko Agripa abwira Pawulo , ati « Erega ndabona uko utekereza , hari hato ukanyemeza kuba umukristu ! »
44026029	Pawulo aramusubiza ati « Byaba iby’akanya gato cyangwa se igihe kinini , ndasaba Imana ngo , uretse nawe wenyine , n’abanyumva uyu munsi bose bamere nkanjye . . . , usibye iyi minyururu imboshye ! »
44026030	Nuko umwami n’umutware na Berenisa n’abo bari kumwe barahaguruka .
44026031	Bigiye hirya baravugana bati « Uriya muntu , nta kibi yakoze gikwiriye kumwicisha , cyangwa kumufungisha ! »
44026032	Agripa abwira Fesito ati « Uriya muntu yajyaga kurekurwa , iyo atajuririra Kayizari . »
44027001	Bamaze kwemeza ko dufata ubwato tukajya mu Butaliyani , Pawulo n’izindi mfungwa bashingwa umutegeka w’abasirikare witwa Yuli , akaba uwo mu mutwe w’abasirikare witwa « uwa Ogusito » .
44027002	Twurira ubwato buvuye Aduramiti bwajyaga mu byambu bya Aziya , maze tugera mu mazi magari . Ubwo twari kumwe na Arisitariko , Umumasedoniya ukomoka i Tesaloniki .
44027003	Bukeye duhagarara i Sidoni ; Yuli rero wagiriraga neza Pawulo , amwemerera kujya gusura incuti ze kugira ngo zimwakire .
44027004	Tuvuye aho , tunyura mu majyepfo y’ikirwa cya Shipure , kuko umuyaga waturwanyaga .
44027005	Tuhavuye , tunyura mu nyanja iherereye kuri Silisiya na Pamfiliya , maze twambukira i Mira ho muri Lisiya .
44027006	Tugeze aho ngaho , umutegeka w’abasirikare abona ubwato buturutse Alegisandiriya bugana mu Butaliyani , nuko turabwurira .
44027007	Tumara iminsi myinshi tugenda buhoro , tuza kugera ahateganye n’umugi wa Kinida , ariko bibanje kutugora . Umuyaga utubujije gukomeza , tunyura mu majyepfo y’ikirwa cya Kireta , ahateganye na Salimoni .
44027008	Tumaze kuhanyura ariko bitugoye , tugera ahitwa « Myaro myiza » , hafi y’umugi wa Lasaya .
44027009	Twari tumaze igihe kirekire kandi gukomeza urugendo rwo mu bwato bikaba byatera amakuba , kuko umunsi w’igisibo wari wararangiye ; Pawulo ni ko kutubwira ati
44027010	« Ncuti zanjye , ndabona uru rugendo rwo mu bwato rugiye gukurura amakuba ndetse rugahitana byinshi , atari ku mitwaro n’ubwato byonyine , ahubwo ndetse no ku bantu . »
44027011	Umutegeka w’abasirikare , aho kwita ku byo Pawulo avuga , yiringira inama z’umusare na nyir’ubwato .
44027012	Nyamara icyo cyambu nticyari kimeze neza muri ayo mezi y’imbeho ; abenshi bahuza umugambi wo gukomeza bakavayo , ngo barebe ko bagera i Fenike , babe ari ho bamara ayo mezi y’imbeho . Fenike ni icyambu cyo mu kirwa cya Kireta , aherekera mu burengerazuba .
44027013	Ngo bumve umuyaga woroshye uturuka mu majyepfo utangiye guhuhera , bibwira ko umugambi wabo wagezweho ; ni ko kuzitura ubwato bagerageza kugenda , bakikiye ikirwa cya Kireta .
44027014	Ariko bidatinze , inkubi y’umuyaga witwa « Majyaruguru y’uburasirazuba » utangira guhuhera uturutse mu kirwa ,
44027015	ukubita ubwato bunanirwa kuwurwanya ; nuko twemera kujyanwa aho umuyaga ushaka .
44027016	Twabonye aho twikinga umuyaga akanya gato , ubwo twahitaga mu majyepfo y’akarwa kitwa Kawuda . Aho ni ho twashoboye kwiyegereza ubwato buto bwari buziritse ku bunini twarimo .
44027017	Abasare barabwuriza babushyira mu bunini ; maze ubwo bunini babuzengurutsa imigozi ikomeye , barabuhambira ngo budasandara . Ubwo barekurira mu mazi ibifatabwato kugira ngo bugende buhoro , babitewe no gutinya kujugunywa ku nkombe ya Sirita .
44027018	Uko twagakomeje gucundabatwa bikomeye n’inkubi y’umuyaga , bukeye bw’aho batangira kuroha imitwaro mu nyanja ,
44027019	naho ku munsi wa gatatu abasare ubwabo bafata ibikoresho by’ubwato , na byo barabiroha .
44027020	Hari hashize iminsi myinshi nta zuba nta n’inyenyeri biboneka , umuyaga ukomeza kuba mwinshi kandi mubi kugeza ubwo tutari tukiringiye kurokoka .
44027021	Bari bamaze igihe kirekire nta cyo bakoza ku munwa , Pawulo ni ko guhagarara hagati yabo , arababwira ati « Ncuti zanjye , byari kuba byiza iyo mujya kunyumva ntimutirimuke i Kireta , kuko mutari kubona aya makuba cyangwa ngo mugire igihombo kingana gitya .
44027022	Ariko noneho ndabasabye ngo mushyire umutima hamwe , kuko ari nta muntu n’umwe muri mwe uzagira icyo aba , keretse ubwato bwonyine .
44027023	Iri joro nyine , umumalayika w’Imana niyeguriye kandi nkorera yambonekeye ,
44027024	arambwira ati ’ Pawulo , witinya ! Ni ngombwa ko ugera imbere ya Kayizari , kandi Imana ikugiriye ubuntu bwo kugukiriza ubuzima , hamwe n’abo mufatanyije urugendo bose . ’
44027025	Nimukomere rero ncuti zanjye , kuko nizeye Imana , bizaba nk’uko yabimbwiye .
44027026	Amaherezo ariko , ubwato buzadusuka ku kirwa . »
44027027	Ijoro rya cumi na kane tugicundabatwa n’inkubi y’umuyaga mu nyanja ya Adiriyatika , ahagana mu gicuku , abasare bibwira ko bari hafi kugera ku butaka .
44027028	Bajugunya mu mazi umugozi uziritseho icyuma , basanga uburebure bw’amazi bureshya n’imikono makumyabiri ; ngo bigire imbere gato babona uburebure bw’imikono cumi n’itanu .
44027029	Batinya ko ubwato bwasekura ku mabuye yo mu nyanja , bajugunya mu mazi ibifatabwato bine by’inyuma ngo ahari bwahagarara , maze bagategereza ko bucya .
44027030	Bigeze aho abasare bashaka guhunga , basubiza bwa bwato buto mu mazi , bitwaje ko bagiye kumanurira mu mazi ibindi bifatabwato by’imbere .
44027031	Pawulo abwira umutegeka w’abasirikare n’ingabo ze , ati « Aba bantu nibataguma mu bwato , mwebwe ntimushobora kurokoka . »
44027032	Nuko abasirikare batema imigozi iziritse bwa bwato buto , barabureka buragenda .
44027033	Bujya gucya , Pawulo asaba ko bagira icyo bafungura agira ati « Dore uyu munsi ni uwa cumi n’ine muhagaritse umutima , mutagira icyo mukoza ku munwa .
44027034	Ndabasabye rero ngo mugire icyo murya , maze mubashe kubaho . Nongeye kandi kubabwira ko nta n’agasatsi k’umwe muri mwe kazazimira . »
44027035	Amaze kuvuga atyo , afata umugati , ashimira Imana imbere ya bose , arawumanyura maze atangira kurya .
44027036	Bose ni ko kugarura umutima , na bo baratangira bararya .
44027037	Abari mu bwato twese , twari magana abiri na mirongo irindwi na batandatu .
44027038	Bamaze kwijuta , baroha ingano mu nyanja , kugira ngo borohereze ubwato .
44027039	Ngo bumare gucya , abasare ntibabasha kumenya ubutaka bari bagezeho , ariko babona akagobe k’inyanja gafite inkuka y’umusenyi , batekereza ko bishobotse ari ho bakwerekeza ubwato .
44027040	Bazitura bya bifatabwato birokera mu nyanja , bahambura n’ibiyoborabwato by’inyuma ; hanyuma bazamura umwenda wo ku ruhembe rw’imbere , bityo bagana ku nkombe bakurikiye icyerekezo cy’umuyaga .
44027041	Ariko ubwato ngo bugere ku gashoro k’ubutaka karengewe n’amazi , butikura mu musenyi . Uruhembe rw’imbere rurigitamo ku buryo budatirimuka , naho urw’inyuma rusandazwa n’umuhengeri wo mu nyanja .
44027042	Abasirikare rero bagira igitekerezo cyo kwica imfungwa , ngo hatagira uwoga agacika .
44027043	Ariko umutegeka w’abasirikare washakaga gukiza Pawulo , ababuza kurangiza uwo mugambi , ahubwo ategeka ko abazi koga bakwiroha aba mbere , bagafata ku nkombe ;
44027044	abasigaye na bo bakabakurikira , bogeye ku mbaho cyangwa ku bimene by’ubwato . Uko ni ko bose babashije gufata imusozi , ari bataraga .
44028001	Tumaze rero guhonoka icyo cyago , tumenya ko icyo kirwa tugezeho cyitwa Malita .
44028002	Abaturage b’aho batwakira neza cyane , kubera ko imvura yagwaga hariho n’imbeho , baducanira umuriro turawukikiza .
44028003	Pawulo atoragura umuganda w’inkwi azishyira mu muriro , inzoka y’impiri isohorokamo yikanze ubushyuhe , maze imusumira ikiganza .
44028004	Abaturage babonye icyo gikoko kimunagana ku kiganza , baravugana bati « Rwose uyu muntu agomba kuba ari umwicanyi ! Kubona yarokotse inyanja , ariko ubutabera bw’Imana bukaba bukimukurikiranye ! »
44028005	Ariko Pawulo akungutira ya mpiri mu muriro , kandi ntiyagira icyo aba .
44028006	Abo bantu bategereza ko ari bubyimbirwe , cyangwa se ko yikubita hasi agapfa , ariko ngo bamare umwanya bategereje , babona nta cyo abaye . Ni ko kwigarura bavuga bati « Ni imana ! »
44028007	Hafi aho , hakaba amasambu y’umutware w’icyo kirwa witwa Pubuliyo , atwakira gicuti , iwe tuhamara iminsi itatu .
44028008	Se w’uwo Pubuliyo yari mu buriri ari indembe , ahinda umuriro kandi na macinya imuri nabi . Pawulo ajya kumusura , amaze gusenga amuramburiraho ibiganza , aramukiza .
44028009	Ibyo bimaze kuba , abandi barwayi bo muri icyo kirwa na bo baraza , abakiza uburwayi bwabo .
44028010	Abantu b’aho baduha icyubahiro cyinshi , nuko igihe twuriye ubwato , baduha impamba twari dukeneye mu rugendo .
44028011	Hashize amezi atatu , twurira ubwato bwavaga Alegisandiriya , bwitiriwe ibigirwamana by’impanga , Kasitori na Polugisi , bwari bumaze amezi yose y’imbeho muri icyo kirwa .
44028012	Tugeze i Sirakuza tuhamara iminsi itatu ,
44028013	tuhavuye tugenda dukikiye inkombe , tugera ahitwa Regiyo . Bukeye bw’uwo munsi , umuyaga utangira guhuhera uturuka mu majyepfo , maze tugera i Puzoli ku munsi wa kabiri .
44028014	Tuhasanga abavandimwe , badusaba kumara icyumweru iwabo . Nuko tugera i Roma dutyo .
44028015	Abavandimwe b’i Roma bumvise ko tuje , baza kudusanganirira ku Iguriro rya Apiyo , n’ahitwa ku Macumbi atatu . Pawulo ngo ababone ashimira Imana , yongera kugira icyizere .
44028016	Tugeze i Roma , bemerera Pawulo kwicumbikira ukwe , hamwe n’umusirikare wo kumurinda .
44028017	Hashize iminsi itatu , Pawulo atumiza abanyacyubahiro b’Abayahudi bahatuye ; ngo bamare guterana arababwira ati « Bavandimwe , n’ubwo nta kibi nagiriye umuryango wacu , cyangwa se ngo ncishe ukubiri n’imigenzo y’abasekuruza , nyamara nafungiwe i Yeruzalemu , nshyikirizwa Abanyaroma !
44028018	Bamaze gusuzuma ibyo ndegwa bashaka kundekura , kuko basanze nta kibi nakoze gikwiye urupfu .
44028019	Ariko mbonye Abayahudi babyanze , biba ngombwa ko njuririra Kayizari , nyamara nta cyo ngamije kurega bene wacu .
44028020	Ngicyo rero icyatumye mbatumiza ngo tuganire . Mu by’ukuri , naboheshejwe iminyururu ku mpamvu y’amizero ya Israheli . »
44028021	Nuko baramusubiza bati « Nta rwandiko twigeze tubona ruturutse mu Yudeya rukuvuga , ndetse nta n’umwe mu bavandimwe waje ngo abitumenyeshe cyangwa se ngo akuvuge nabi .
44028022	Ariko rero , turashaka kumva icyo wowe ubwawe ubitekerezaho , kuko tuzi ko hose barwanya izo nyigisho z’ako gatsiko urimo . »
44028023	Ubwo bemeranya umunsi bazongera guterana , uwo munsi ugeze bamusanga ari benshi ku icumbi rye . Ahera mu gitondo ageza nimugoroba abasobanurira iby’Ingoma y’Imana , anagerageza kubemeza ku byerekeye Yezu , ahereye ku Mategeko ya Musa no ku Bahanuzi .
44028024	Bamwe muri bo bemezwa n’ibyo yavugaga , abandi ariko banga kubyemera .
44028025	Bagera igihe bataha batarumvikana ubwabo , Pawulo ni ko kongeraho iri jambo ati « Mbega ngo riraba irinyakuri , rya jambo Roho Mutagatifu yabwiye abasekuruza banyu , arivugishije umuhanuzi Izayi ati
44028026	’ Sanga umuryango wawe , maze ubabwire uti : Kumva muzumva , ariko mwe gusobanukirwa ; muzitegereze , ariko mwe kubona .
44028027	Kuko uwo muryango winangiye umutima , biziba amatwi , bihuma n’amaso , kugira ngo batagira icyo babona , amatwi yabo akagira icyo yumva , n’umutima wabo ukagira icyo umenya , ngo batavaho bangarukira maze nkabakiza . ’
44028028	Nuko rero , mumenye ko uwo mukiro Imana yawoherereje abanyamahanga , kandi bo bakazawakira ! »
44028029	Pawulo ngo amare kubabwira ibyo , Abayahudi bataha bajya impaka z’urudaca .
44028030	Pawulo amara imyaka ibiri yose mu icumbi yirihirira , akakira abamugendereraga bose ,
44028031	yamamaza Ingoma y’Imana kandi yigisha ibyerekeye Yezu Kristu nta nkomyi kandi ashize amanga .
45001001	Jyewe Pawulo , umugaragu wa Yezu Kristu , ndabaramutsa . Koko natorewe kuba intumwa , nteganyirizwa kwamamaza Inkuru Nziza
45001002	Imana yari yarateguje abahanuzi bayo mu Byanditswe bitagatifu .
45001003	Iyo Nkuru Nziza yerekeye Umwana wayo , Yezu Kristu Umwami wacu , wabayeho ku bw’umubiri ari mwene Dawudi ,
45001004	ariko izuka rye ava mu bapfuye rikagaragaza ko ari Umwana w’Imana mu bubasha bwose ku bwa Roho Mutagatifu .
45001005	Ni na We waduhesheje ubutumwa bwo kuyobora mu ikuzo ry’izina rye amahanga yose ku kwemera ,
45001006	ari yo mubarirwamo namwe , abahamagawe na Yezu Kristu .
45001007	Mwebwe rero , batoni b’Imana muri i Roma , mwebwe abatagatifujwe no gutorwa n’Imana : nimugire ineza n’amahoro bituruka ku Mana Umubyeyi wacu , no kuri Nyagasani Yezu Kristu .
45001008	Mbere na mbere , ndashimira Imana yanjye muri Yezu Kristu ku mpamvu yanyu , kuko ukwemera kwanyu kuratwa n’isi yose .
45001009	Imana nyitanzeho umugabo , Yo nkeza mu mutima wanjye namamaza Inkuru Nziza y’Umwana wayo : sinsiba kubibuka ,
45001010	ngasaba iteka mu masengesho yanjye ko nazagira amahirwe yo kuzashyira nkagera iwanyu niba Imana ibishatse .
45001011	Koko kandi , ndifuza cyane kubabona ngo mbe nabaha ku ngabire ndengakamere yabakomeza ,
45001012	bambe kugira ngo mumare igishyika mu kwemera duhuriyeho , mwebwe nanjye .
45001013	Sinabahisha kandi , bavandimwe , ko kenshi nagambiriye kuza iwanyu — nyamara kugeza ubu byaramburiye — ngo ngire imbuto namwe mbasaruraho , nk’uko byagenze no ku yandi mahanga .
45001014	Ngomba kwita ku Bagereki no ku batari bo , ku bajijutse no ku batajijutse :
45001015	ikaba ari yo mpamvu nshishikajwe no kubigisha Inkuru Nziza namwe ab’i Roma .
45001016	Koko rero , nta bwo nshishwa n’Inkuru Nziza kuko ari yo bubasha bw’Imana burokora uwemera wese uhereye ku Muyahudi ukageza ku Mugereki .
45001017	Koko kandi ni muri yo ubutungane bw’Imana buhishurirwa , bishingiye ku kwemera , bigakomeza ukwemera , nk’uko byanditswe ngo « Intungane izabeshwaho n’ukwemera . »
45001018	Koko rero uburakari bw’Imana bwihishura buva mu ijuru burwanya abagomeramana bose , n’abagizi ba nabi bose bapfukirana ukuri muri iyo nabi .
45001019	Kuko icyo umuntu yamenya ku Mana kirabigaragariza : Imana yarakibahishuriye .
45001020	Koko rero , kuva isi yaremwa , ubwenge buhera ku byaremwe , bugashyikira ibitagaragara by’Imana , ni ukuvuga ububasha bwayo buhoraho na kamere yayo bwite . Bityo rero ntibabona uko biregura ,
45001021	kuko bamenye Imana , ariko ntibayiha ikuzo , ngo bayishimire uko bikwiriye Imana ; ahubwo babaye abapfu bishinga ibitekerezo by’amanjwe , maze umutima wabo w’igipfapfa ucura umwijima .
45001022	Birataga kuba abanyabwenge , bahinduka abapfayongo ,
45001023	maze ikuzo ry’Imana idapfa barigurana ishusho isa n’umuntu uzapfa , isa n’ibiguruka , n’inyamaswa , n’ibikurura inda hasi .
45001024	Ngiyo impamvu yatumye Imana ibagabiza iby’umutima wabo urarikira , bakora ibiterasoni , kugira ngo bihumanye umubiri .
45001025	Bo baguranye ukuri kw’Imana ikinyoma , basenga ikiremwa baranagikorera , bahigika Rurema , Nyagusingizwa iteka ryose ! Amen .
45001026	Ni cyo cyatumye Imana ibagabiza ingeso z’urukozasoni : dore abagore babo bateshejwe gukoresha imibiri yabo ibihuje na kamere ,
45001027	abagabo na bo aho kugana umugore uko kamere ishaka , ubwabo bagurumanirana irari , umugabo agakorana n’undi ibiterasoni , bityo bikururira ingaruka mbi ikwiranye n’ubuyobe bwabo .
45001028	Byongeye kandi , nk’uko banze kumenya Imana , Imana yabagabije ubwenge bwabo bucuramye ngo bakore ibidakorwa .
45001029	Buzuye icyitwa inabi cyose , ubugome , umururumba , ububisha ; buzuye ishyari , ubwicanyi , intonganya , uburiganya , ubugambanyi ; barasebanya ,
45001030	batera urubwa , banga Imana , barasuzugura , barirata , barirarira , bahimbahimba ibibi , bananira ababyeyi ;
45001031	ni ibiburabwenge , abahemu , ibiburamutima , intababarira .
45001032	N’ubwo bazi iteka ry’Imana ricira urwo gupfa abakora bene ibyo , bo ntibabikora gusa , bashima ndetse n’ababikora .
45002001	Nuko rero nta cyo uzabona wireguza , wowe muntu uca urubanza , uwo uri we wese : kuko iyo ucira undi urubanza , uba witsindisha ubwawe , kuko ugenza utyo nawe wowe uca urubanza .
45002002	Tuzi ko Imana izacira urubanza abagenza batyo ikurikije ukuri .
45002003	None se , muntu ucira urubanza abakora ibyo bintu kandi nawe ubikora , wibwira ko uzasimbuka ute urubanza rw’Imana ?
45002004	Cyangwa se waba usuzugura impuhwe zayo zitabarika , ubwihangane n’ubugwaneza bwayo , ukirengagiza ko ubuntu bwayo bukureshya ngo wicuze ?
45002005	Noneho rero , kuko wanangiye umutima wawe ukanga kwicuza , urihunikira uburakari bwa wa munsi w’uburakari Imana izahishura ko ica imanza zitabera ,
45002006	Yo izitura buri wese ikurikije ibikorwa bye :
45002007	ubugingo bw’iteka ku batacogoye mu gukora ikiri cyiza bashakashaka ikuzo , icyubahiro n’ukutazapfa ;
45002008	naho uburakari n’umujinya ku bivumbuye , ntibumve ukuri , bakayoboka inabi .
45002009	Impagarara n’ishavu birakokama buri mutima w’umuntu ukora ikibi , uhereye ku Muyahudi ukageza ku Mugereki ;
45002010	naho ikuzo , icyubahiro n’amahoro kuri buri wese ukora icyiza , uhereye ku Muyahudi ukageza ku Mugereki .
45002011	Kuko Imana itareba igihagararo cy’abantu .
45002012	Koko rero , abazaba baracumuye nta mategeko , bazorama nta mategeko ; naho abazaba baracumuye bazi amategeko , bazacirwa urubanza hakurikijwe amategeko .
45002013	Kuko abumva amategeko atari bo ntungane ku Mana , ahubwo abakurikiza amategeko ni bo bazagirwa intungane .
45002014	Iyo abanyamahanga bakora ku bwa kamere ibihuje n’amategeko , kandi nyamara batagira amategeko , bibera ubwabo amategeko , bo badafite amategeko .
45002015	Bagaragaza batyo ko icyo amategeko agamije cyanditswe mu mitima yabo . N’umutimanama wabo na wo ni intangamugabo hamwe n’imitima ibarwanamo , imwe ishinja , indi irengera .
45002016	Nk’uko nabivuze mu Nkuru Nziza yanjye , bizagaragara umunsi Imana izakoresha Yezu Kristu , Imana igacira urubanza ibyo abantu bahishahisha bakora rwihishwa .
45002017	Wowe rero witwa Umuyahudi , ukitwaza amategeko , ukiratana Imana ,
45002018	wowe uzi kandi ugushaka kwayo , ukamenya guhitamo ikiruta ibindi kuko wigishijwe n’amategeko ,
45002019	wowe wiyemera ngo ni wowe warandata impumyi , wamurikira abari mu mwijima ,
45002020	wahugura injiji , wakwigisha abana , ngo kuko wasanze mu mategeko hakubiyemo ubumenyi n’ukuri . . .
45002021	Ko wigisha abandi , ntiwiyigishe ubwawe ; ko ubwiriza kutiba , nyamara ukiba ;
45002022	ko ubuza gusambana , ugasambana ; ko uzira ibigirwamana , kandi ugasahura amasengero yabyo ;
45002023	ko wiratana amategeko , ariko ugasuzuguza Imana urenga ku mategeko ,
45002024	nk’uko byanditswe ngo : « Izina ry’Imana bararituka mu mahanga ku mpamvu yanyu » .
45002025	Koko kuba waragenywe byagira akamaro ukurikije amategeko , naho niba ugomera amategeko , ukugenywa kwawe kwabaye ukutagenywa .
45002026	Niba se utagenywe akurikije ibitunganiye amategeko , nta bwo se ukuba atagenywe bizaba bihwanye n’ukugenywa ?
45002027	Ndetse utagenywe umubiri , ariko agakurikiza amategeko , azagucira urubanza , wowe uzaba warenze ku mategeko witwaje ibyanditswe n’ukugenywa .
45002028	Kuko Umuyahudi ntumubwirwa n’ibigaragara , n’ukugenywa si uko ku mubiri ahagaragara ;
45002029	ahubwo Umuyahudi nyakuri ni uri we muri kami ye , n’ukugenywa nyakuri ni uk’umutima muri roho bitari mu nyandiko . Uwo ntakura ishimwe rye ku bantu , ahubwo ku Mana .
45003001	Umuyahudi arusha iki abandi ? Ukugenywa bimaze iki ?
45003002	Bifite akamaro kanini kandi ku buryo bwose . Mbere na mbere kuko ari bo baragijwe amagambo y’Imana .
45003003	Bite rero ? Niba bamwe muri bo barahemutse , ubuhemu bwabo bwahindura ubusa ubudahemuka bw’Imana ?
45003004	Ntibikabeho ! Imana irabe imvugakuri , naho umuntu wese abe umubeshyi , nk’uko byanditswe ngo « Urabe intungane mu magambo yawe , uzatsinde nushyirwa mu rubanza . »
45003005	Ariko se niba inabi yacu igaragaza ubutungane bw’Imana , tuvuge ngo iki ? Mbese Imana ntirenganya , Yo ihanira ko yarakaye ?
45003006	Ndavuga ku buryo bw’abantu . Ntibikabe ! Naho ubundi se , Imana yazacira ite isi urubanza ?
45003007	Nyamara se , niba ukuri kw’Imana kurushaho kugaragara ku mpamvu y’ikinyoma cyanjye , maze Imana igahabwa ikuzo , ni uruhe rubanza rwampamya kuba umunyabyaha ?
45003008	Kandi ni iki kitubuza gukora ibibi ngo bibyare ibyiza , nk’uko batubeshyera bavuga ko ari yo nyigisho yacu ? Abo ngabo bazacirwa urubanza rubakwiriye .
45003009	Bite rero ? Hari icyo turusha abandi se ? Habe na mba ! Dore tumaze guhamya bose icyaha , ari Abayahudi , ari Abagereki ,
45003010	nk’uko byanditswe ngo « Nta ntungane wabona , habe n’imwe ,
45003011	nta we uzi ubwenge , nta we ushaka Imana .
45003012	Bose barayobye , babereye ibigoryi icyarimwe , nta n’umwe ukora icyiza , habe n’umwe .
45003013	Umuhogo wabo ni imva irangaye , indimi zabo zisuka ibinyoma . Iminwa yabo ijunditse ubumara nk’ubw’impiri ,
45003014	akanwa kabo kuzuyemo imivumo n’amagambo asesereza .
45003015	Ibirenge byabo byihutira kumena amaraso ,
45003016	amatongo n’imiborogo ni byo biranga aho banyuze .
45003017	Ntibazi inzira y’amahoro ,
45003018	nta gitinyiro cy’Imana mu maso yabo .
45003019	Nyamara tuzi ko ibyo amategeko avuze byose , bibwirwa abagengwa n’amategeko kugira ngo akanwa kose kazibe , maze isi yose yemezwe kuba yaragomeye Imana .
45003020	Ni yo mpamvu nta n’umwe uzagirwa intungane mu maso yayo n’uko yubahiriza amategeko , kuko amategeko afasha gusa kumenya icyaha .
45003021	Ubu ngubu ariko ubutungane bw’Imana bwarahishuwe hatagombye amategeko ; intangamugabo ni amategeko n’abahanuzi .
45003022	Ni ubutungane bw’Imana butangwa no kwemera Yezu Kristu , bukaba bugenewe abemera bose nta vangura .
45003023	Kuko bose bagomye , bakivutsa ikuzo ry’Imana .
45003024	Ariko bahabwa kuba intungane n’ineza yayo ku buntu , babikesha gucungurwa na Kristu Yezu .
45003025	Ni We Imana yagize intangacyiru mu maraso ye ku bw’ukwemera , kugira ngo igaragaze ubutungane bwayo , Yo yarenze ku byaha bya kera ,
45003026	mu gihe yabyihanganiraga . Ubu ngubu rero igaragaza ubutungane bwayo kugira ngo ibe intungane , kandi ihe kuba intungane ugengwa no kwemera Yezu .
45003027	Wa mwirato ushingiye he se noneho ? Warashize . Uzize irihe teka ? Iryo kubahiriza amategeko ? Oya ! Ahubwo itegeko ry’ukwemera .
45003028	Koko rero , turahamya ko umuntu ahabwa kuba intungane n’ukwemera hatagombye ibikorwa by’amategeko .
45003029	Mbese Imana yaba iy’Abayahudi bonyine ? Nta bwo se ari n’iy’abanyamahanga ? Yego , ni n’iy’abanyamahanga .
45003030	Ubwo ari Imana imwe , izaha uwagenywe kuba intungane abikesha ukwemera , n’utagenywe na we abikesha ukwemera .
45003031	Ubwo se turambura amategeko agaciro kayo tuvuga ukwemera ? Ntibikabe ! Ahubwo tuyahaye ishingiro .
45004001	Twavuga iki ku mukurambere wacu Abrahamu ? Hari icyo yaba yararonse ku bw’umubiri ?
45004002	Niba Abrahamu yarabaye intungane abikesheje ibyo yakoze , akwiriye kubyirata , usibye imbere y’Imana .
45004003	None se ibyanditswe bivuga iki ? Ngo « Abrahamu yemera Uhoraho , bituma aba intungane . »
45004004	Umuntu kandi ukoze umurimo , igihembo ntagihabwa ku buntu , ahubwo barakimugomba .
45004005	Naho utagize icyo akora , ariko akemera uha umunyabyaha kuba intungane , uko kwemera kwe kuzamuha ubutungane .
45004006	Nk’uko Dawudi avuga amahirwe y’umuntu Imana iha kuba intungane kandi nta bikorwa , ati
45004007	« Hahirwa abababariwe ibicumuro , maze ibyaha byabo bikarenzwaho .
45004008	Hahirwa umuntu Nyagasani adashinja icyaha . »
45004009	Mbese ayo mahirwe ni ay’abagenywe bonyine cyangwa ni n’ay’abatagenywe ? Tuvuga ko « ukwemera kwahaye Abrahamu kuba intungane . »
45004010	Kwabimuhaye buryo ki ? Mbere cyangwa nyuma yo kugenywa ? Si nyuma , ahubwo ni mbere yo kugenywa .
45004011	Nyuma ukugenywa yaguhaweho ikimenyetso , irango ry’ubutungane akesha ukwemera yagize ataragenywa , kugira ngo abe umubyeyi w’abemera bose batagenywe , ngo bahabwe kuba intungane ,
45004012	n’umubyeyi kandi w’abagenywe , batari abangenywe bonyine , ahubwo n’abashyira ikirenge mu cya Abrahamu bakurikiza ukwemera yari afite ataragenywa .
45004013	Koko rero , nta bwo ari amategeko yatumye Abrahamu cyangwa urubyaro rwe basezeranywa guhabwa isi yose ho umurage , ahubwo ni ubutungane butangwa n’ukwemera .
45004014	Kuko niba abiringiye amategeko ari bo ngenerwamurage , ukwemera kwaba nta mumaro , n’isezerano rikaba risheshwe .
45004015	Kuko amategeko akurura uburakari . Ariko ahataba amategeko , nta we ucumura .
45004016	Ni yo mpamvu , ari ku bw’ukwemera isezerano ryabaye ihame , ritangwa ku buntu , rigenerwa urubyaro rwose , atari abishingikirije amategeko bonyine , ahubwo ndetse n’abishingikirije ukwemera kwa Abrahamu , we mubyeyi wacu twese ,
45004017	nk’uko byanditswe ngo « Nakugize sekuru w’amahanga menshi . » Yemeye Imana , Yo isubiza ubuzima abapfuye , igaha kubaho ibitariho .
45004018	Yizeye ibidashoboka nyamara aremera , maze aba atyo umubyeyi w’amahanga menshi bikurikije rya jambo ngo « Dore uko urubyaro rwawe ruzangana . »
45004019	Ntiyigeze acogora mu kwemera areba umubiri we washaje — yakabakabaga imyaka ijana — n’inda ya Sara yumiranye , kuko urupfu rwari rwarabatashye bombi .
45004020	Ntiyabura ubwizere ngo ashidikanye isezerano ry’Imana , ahubwo akomezwa n’ukwemera maze yiragiza ikuzo ry’Imana .
45004021	Yiyemeza rwose ko ishobora kuzuza icyo yasezeranye .
45004022	Ni yo mpamvu ibyo byatumye agirwa intungane .
45004023	Nyamara si we wenyine byandikiwe ko ukwemera kugeza ku butungane ;
45004024	natwe ni uko bizamera , twe twemera Uwazutse mu bapfuye , Yezu umwami wacu ,
45004025	watangiwe ibyaha byacu , akazukira kutugira intungane .
45005001	Ubwo rero twagizwe intungane n’ukwemera , dufite amahoro ku Mana , muri Yezu Kristu Umwami wacu .
45005002	Ku bwe twashyikiriye , mu kwemera , iyi neza tuganjemo , none twiratira gutegereza ikuzo ry’Imana .
45005003	Si ibyo byonyine , twiratana ndetse n’ibitotezo , kuko tuzi ko ibitotezo bitera kwihangana ,
45005004	ukwihangana kugatera kudahemuka , ukudahemuka na ko kugatera kwizera ,
45005005	ukwizera ntigutamaze , kuko urukundo rw’Imana rwabuganijwe mu mitima yacu na Roho Mutagatifu twahawe .
45005006	Koko rero igihe twari tugifite intege nke , Kristu yapfiriye abanyabyaha ku munsi wagenwe .
45005007	Birakomeye ko hagira upfira intungane ; sinzi niba hagira uwemera gupfira inyangamugayo .
45005008	Imana rero yerekanye urukundo idufitiye kuko Kristu yadupfiriye kandi twari abanyabyaha .
45005009	None ubwo twagizwe intungane n’amaraso ye , tuzarokorwa na We uburakari ku buryo busumbijeho .
45005010	Koko rero , niba twariyunze n’Imana mu rupfu rw’Umwana wayo kandi nyamara twari abanzi , ubwo twiyunze , tuzarokorwa mu buzima bwe ku buryo busumbijeho .
45005011	Si n’ibyo ngibyo gusa : twishimiye Imana muri Yezu Kristu Umwami wacu , ari We ubu ngubu wadufashije kwiyunga .
45005012	Nk’uko icyaha cyadutse mu nsi gikuruwe n’umuntu umwe , kandi n’urupfu rukuruwe n’icyaha , bityo urupfu rucengera abantu bose , kuko bose bacumuye . . .
45005013	Koko rero na mbere y’uko amategeko atangazwa , icyaha cyariho mu nsi , n’ubwo nta we cyahama iyo nta mategeko ariho .
45005014	Nyamara urupfu rwaraganje kuva kuri Adamu kugera kuri Musa , ndetse no ku batakoze icyaha kingana n’icya Adamu , ari we washushanyaga Uwari ugiye kuzaza .
45005015	Ariko ineza ntigira ihuriro n’icyaha . Koko rero n’ubwo abenshi bapfuye bazize icyaha cy’umuntu umwe , ineza y’Imana n’ingabire y’ubuntu bw’umwe , Yezu Kristu , zasesekaye kuri benshi ku buryo busumbijeho .
45005016	Kandi rero ingabire ntiyagereranywa n’icyaha cy’umwe : kuko icyaha cy’umwe cyaciriwe urubanza rwo gucibwa , naho impuhwe zigiriwe ibyaha byinshi , zigeza ku butungane .
45005017	Niba koko urupfu rwaraganje rutewe n’umuntu umwe , rutewe n’icyaha cy’umuntu umwe , ku buryo busumbijeho abahabwa ineza n’ingabire zitabarika z’ubutungane , bazaganza mu bugingo babikesha umuntu umwe , Yezu Kristu .
45005018	Bityo rero , nk’uko icyaha cy’umwe cyatumye abantu bose bacibwa , ni ko n’igikorwa cy’ubutungane bw’umuntu umwe kizatuma abantu bose bahabwa ubutungane butanga ubugingo .
45005019	Koko rero , nk’uko ukutumvira k’umuntu umwe kwatumye benshi icyaha kibahama , ni ko n’ukumvira k’umwe kuzatuma benshi baba intungane .
45005020	Amategeko yaje agwiza icyaha , ariko aho icyaha cyakwiriye , ineza yarushijeho kuhasendera
45005021	kugira ngo , nk’uko icyaha cyari cyaraganje mu rupfu , n’ineza izaganze mu butungane butanga ubugingo bw’iteka muri Yezu Kristu umwami wacu .
45006001	Twabivugaho iki rero ? Twigumire mu cyaha se ngo ineza ikunde igwire ?
45006002	Ntibikabeho ! Ko twebwe twapfuye ku cyaha , twakomeza dute kubaho muri cyo ?
45006003	Ntimuzi se ko twebwe twese ababatijwe muri Kristu Yezu , ari mu rupfu rwe twabatirijwemo ?
45006004	Koko rero ku bwa batisimu twahambanywe na we mu rupfu rwe kugira ngo , uko Kristu yazuwe mu bapfuye n’ikuzo rya Data , bityo natwe tugendere mu bugingo bushya .
45006005	Niba koko twarabaye umwe na We dusangira urupfu rwe , ni ko bizagenda no mu izuka .
45006006	Tumenye neza ko muntu w’igisazira twari we kera yabambanywe na We , kugira ngo umubiri w’icyaha utsiratsizwe , bityo twoye kuzongera ukundi kuba abagaragu b’icyaha .
45006007	Kuko upfuye , aba ahanaguweho icyaha .
45006008	Niba rero twarapfanye na Kristu , twemera ko nanone tuzabaho hamwe na We .
45006009	Tuzi ko Kristu yazutse mu bapfuye akaba atazongera gupfa ukundi , urupfu rukaba rutakimufiteho ububasha .
45006010	Kuko igihe apfuye , yapfuye ku cyaha rimwe rizima ; naho kuba ariho , abereyeho Imana .
45006011	Bityo namwe mumenye ko ubwanyu mwapfuye ku cyaha mukaba mubereyeho Imana muri Kristu Yezu .
45006012	Icyaha rero nticyongere kugenga umubiri wanyu uzapfa ngo gitume mwumvira irari ryawo .
45006013	Kandi imibiri yanyu ntimukayegurire icyaha ngo ibe intwaro z’ukugira nabi , ahubwo nimugandukire Imana nk’abazima bavuye mu bapfu , imibiri yanyu muyegurire Imana ibe intwaro z’ubutungane .
45006014	Koko rero icyaha ntikikibafiteho ububasha , kuko mutakigengwa n’amategeko , ahubwo mugengwa n’ineza .
45006015	Bite rero ? Tuzacumure se ngo aha ntitukigengwa n’amategeko , tugengwa n’ineza ? Oya ntibikabe !
45006016	Mbese ntimuzi ko uwo mwiyeguriye mukamubera abagaragu bamwumvira , muba mumubereye koko abagaragu bagomba kumwumvira , cyaba icyaha gishyira urupfu , kwaba ukumvira gutanga ubutungane ?
45006017	Imana ishimwe kuko mwahoze muri abagaragu b’icyaha none mukaba mwarayobotse mubikuye ku mutima inyigisho mwaragijwe .
45006018	Mwarokowe ubucakara bw’icyaha , muhinduka abagaragu b’ubutungane .
45006019	Ndavuga ku buryo bw’abantu mbitewe n’intege nke zanyu . Ubwo mwari mwareguriye imibiri yanyu gukora ibiterasoni n’ubwigomeke , noneho rero nimuyegurire ubutungane butanga ubutagatifu .
45006020	Koko rero , igihe mwari abagaragu b’icyaha , ntimwagengwaga n’ubutungane .
45006021	Mbese byabunguye iki icyo gihe ? Ko ahubwo ubu ngubu bibateye isoni , kuko amaherezo yabyo ari urupfu .
45006022	Ariko ubu ngubu , kuva aho mugobotorewe icyaha , mukaba abagaragu b’Imana , mweze imbuto zigeza ku butagatifu , amaherezo akazaba ubugingo bw’iteka .
45006023	Nuko rero ingaruka y’icyaha ni urupfu , naho ingabire y’Imana ni ubugingo bw’iteka muri Kristu Yezu Umwami wacu .
45007001	Bavandimwe muyobewe se ko umuntu agengwa n’amategeko igihe cyose akiriho ? ( Ndabwira abahanga mu mategeko ) .
45007002	Umugore wubatse , itegeko rimuhambira ku mugabo igihe akiriho ; iyo umugabo apfuye , umugore aba abohowe itegeko ry’umugabo .
45007003	Ni yo mpamvu yitwa umusambanyi iyo ari ku wundi mugabo kandi uwe akiriho ; ariko iyo umugabo apfuye , aba abohowe itegeko ku buryo ataba akiswe umusambanyi iyo acyuwe n’undi mugabo .
45007004	Namwe rero , bavandimwe , mwarapfuye ku byerekeye amategeko mubikesheje umubiri wa Kristu ngo mube ab’undi , ari We wazutse mu bapfuye , kugira ngo turumbukire Imana imbuto .
45007005	Koko rero , igihe twari mu cyaha , irari ryacyo ryaduteraga kwera imbuto z’urupfu , ryishingikirije itegeko .
45007006	Naho ubu ngubu , twapfuye ku byerekeye itegeko , tugobotorwa n’ibyo ryatuboheshaga ku buryo tugengwa na roho nshya , aho kugengwa n’inyandiko ishaje .
45007007	Twavuga iki rero ? Ko amategeko ari yo cyaha ? Oya ntibikabe ! Ariko sinari kumenya icyaha ntabihawe n’amategeko . Simba naramenye irari iyo amategeko atavuga ngo « Ntuzararikire ikibi . »
45007008	Nyamara icyaha cyitwaje itegeko , kintera icyitwa irari cyose . Nuko rero hatabayeho amategeko , icyaha nticyabaho .
45007009	Kera , amategeko atarabaho , nari muzima . Aho itegeko rihingukiye , icyaha kirabaduka ,
45007010	nuko jyewe ndapfa , nsanga itegeko rinkururira urupfu kandi ubundi ryaragenewe gutanga ubuzima .
45007011	Koko icyaha cyitwaje itegeko , kiranyoshya kirinyiciramo .
45007012	Bityo rero , amategeko ni matagatifu , ndetse itegeko ryose ni ritagatifu , riratunganye kandi ni ryiza .
45007013	Mbese noneho icyo cyiza kibe cyarambereye urupfu ? Oya ntibikabeho ! Ahubwo ni icyaha , kugira ngo cyigaragaze ko ari icyaha koko : kuko cyitwaje icyiza maze kinkururira urupfu , kugira ngo kandi cyerekane ububi bwacyo bwose bitewe n’itegeko .
45007014	Tuzi neza ko amategeko aturuka kuri Roho ; jyewe ariko ndi umunyamubiri , naraguzwe mba umucakara w’icyaha .
45007015	Koko rero sinumva ibyo nkora : icyo nshaka gukora , si cyo nkora , ahubwo ndetse icyo ndashaka , ngicyo icyo nkora .
45007016	Ubwo noneho rero nkora icyo ndashaka , mpuje n’amategeko kandi nkemera ko ari meza .
45007017	Ubwo rero si jyewe ukora ibyo , ahubwo ni icyaha cyaritse muri jye .
45007018	Koko kandi nzi neza ko icyiza kitandimo , kubera intege nke z’umubiri wanjye . Nshobora kwifuza icyiza , ariko kugikora bikananira .
45007019	Kuko icyiza nifuza ntagikora , naho ikibi ndashaka akaba ari cyo nkora .
45007020	Niba rero icyo ndashaka ari cyo nkora , ntibikibaye jyewe ugikora ahubwo ni icyaha gituye muri jye .
45007021	Jyewe ushaka gukora icyiza , nsanga hari iri tegeko ko ikibi ari cyo kimbangukira .
45007022	Nishimira amategeko y’Imana mu mutima wanjye ,
45007023	nyamara nkabona irindi tegeko muri jyewe rirwanya itegeko ry’umutima wanjye , ku buryo ndi imbohe y’itegeko ry’icyaha rindimo .
45007024	Mbega ngo ndaba umunyabyago ! Ni nde uzankiza uyu mubiri wagenewe gupfa ?
45007025	Imana ishimwe muri Yezu Kristu Umwami wacu ! Naho ubundi jyewe ndasanga ndi umugaragu w’itegeko ry’Imana ku bw’umutima , n’uw’itegeko ry’icyaha ku bw’umubiri .
45008001	Ubu ngubu noneho abari muri Kristu Yezu ntibagiciwe .
45008002	Kuko itegeko rya Roho utanga ubugingo muri Kristu Yezu ryaturokoye itegeko ry’icyaha n’urupfu .
45008003	Koko rero , ikitashobokeraga amategeko kuko intege nke z’umubiri zayacogozaga , Imana yaragishoboye : igihe yohereje Umwana wayo mu mubiri usa n’uw’icyaha ngo abe igitambo cy’icyaha , yagitsindiye mu mubiri ,
45008004	kugira ngo ubutungane bushakwa n’amategeko budusenderezwemo , twebwe abatagengwa n’ibitekerezo by’umubiri ahubwo na roho .
45008005	Koko rero abagengwa n’umubiri bita ku by’umubiri ; naho abagengwa na roho , bo bita ku bya roho .
45008006	Irari ry’umubiri rishyira urupfu , naho ibyifuzo bya roho bigashyira ubugingo n’amahoro .
45008007	Kuko irari ry’umubiri rirwanya Imana : nta bwo ryayoboka amategeko y’Imana , ntiryanabishobora .
45008008	N’abagengwa n’umubiri ntibashobora kunyura Imana .
45008009	Mwebwe ariko , ntimugengwa n’umubiri , ahubwo mugengwa na roho , kuko Roho w’Imana atuye muri mwe . Umuntu udafite Roho wa Kristu , uwo ntaba ari uwe .
45008010	Niba Kristu ari muri mwe , umubiri wanyu wo ugomba gupfa ku mpamvu y’icyaha , ariko mubeshejweho na Roho ku mpamvu y’ubutungane .
45008011	Niba kandi Roho y’Uwazuye Kristu Yezu mu bapfuye abatuyemo , Uwazuye Kristu Yezu mu bapfuye azabeshaho imibiri yanyu igenewe gupfa ku bwa Roho we utuye muri mwe .
45008012	None rero , bavandimwe , turimo umwenda , ariko si uw’umubiri byatuma tugomba kubaho tugengwa n’umubiri .
45008013	Kuko nimubaho mugengwa n’umubiri , muzapfa ; ariko niba ku bwa roho , mucitse ku bikorwa by’umubiri , muzabaho .
45008014	Abayoborwa na Roho w’Imana , abo ni bo bana b’Imana .
45008015	Kandi rero ntimwahawe roho y’ubucakara ibasubiza nanone mu bwoba , ahubwo mwahawe roho ibagira abana bishingiwe kibyeyi , igatuma dutera hejuru tuti « Abba ! Data ! »
45008016	Roho uwo nyine afatanya na roho yacu guhamya ko turi abana b’Imana .
45008017	Kandi ubwo turi abana , turi n’abagenerwamurage ; abagenerwamurage b’Imana , bityo n’abasangiramurage ba Kristu niba ariko tubabarana na We ngo tuzahabwe ikuzo hamwe na We .
45008018	Koko rero nsanga amagorwa y’igihe cy’ubu ngubu atagereranywa n’ikuzo rizatugaragarizwamo .
45008019	Ndetse n’ibiremwa byose birarekereje ngo birebe igaragazwa ry’abana b’Imana :
45008020	n’ubwo ibyo biremwa bitagifite agaciro , atari ku bushake bwabyo , ahubwo ku bw’Uwabigennye atyo , biracyafite amizero .
45008021	Kuko n’ibyaremwe ubwabyo bizagobotorwa ingoyi y’ubushanguke maze bigasangira ubwigenge n’ikuzo by’abana b’Imana .
45008022	Tuzi neza ko na n’ubu ibiremwa byose binihira icyarimwe , nk’ibiri mu mibabaro yo kuramukwa .
45008023	Nyamara si byo byonyine , ndetse natwe abahawe Roho Mutagatifu ho umuganura , turaganyira mu mutima , dutegereje kugirwa abana b’Imana , ugucungurwa kw’imibiri yacu .
45008024	Koko rero twarakijijwe mu bwizere ; nyamara kureba ibyo wizeraga , ntibiba bikiri ukwizera . Iyo umuntu yirebera , aba acyizeye iki kindi ?
45008025	Niba rero twizeye icyo tutareba ubu ngubu , twihanganiye kugitegereza .
45008026	Bityo , ni ko na Roho atabara intege nke zacu , kuko tutazi icyo twasaba uko bikwiye , maze Roho ubwe akadutakambira mu miniho irenze imivugirwe .
45008027	Kandi Nyirugusuzuma imitima akaba azi icyo Roho yifuza , kuko atakambira abatagatifujwe ku buryo buhuje n’Imana .
45008028	Tuzi kandi ko byose bihira abakunda Imana , ari bo yihamagariye ku bwende bwayo .
45008029	Abo yamenye kuva kera , yanabageneye guhabwa isura y’Umwana wayo ngo abe umuvukambere mu bavandimwe benshi .
45008030	Abo yabigeneye kandi , abo ngabo yarabahamagaye ; abo yahamagaye kandi , abo ngabo yabahaye kuba intungane ; abo yahaye kuba intungane , abo ngabo yanabahaye ikuzo .
45008031	Ibi twabyongeraho iki ? Niba Imana turi kumwe , ni nde waduhangara ?
45008032	Yo itimanye ndetse n’Umwana wayo , ahubwo ikamudutangira twese , yabura ite kandi kutugabira byose kumwe na We ?
45008033	Ni nde wagira icyo ashinja intore z’Imana ? Ko Imana iziha kuba intungane .
45008034	Ni nde uzazicira urubanza ? Ko Kristu Yezu yapfuye , ndetse ko yazutse , We uri iburyo bw’Imana , akaba anadutakambira .
45008035	Ni iki cyadutandukanya n’urukundo rwa Kristu ? Ibyago se , agahinda se , ibitotezo se , inzara se , ubukene se , imitego se , cyangwa inkota ?
45008036	Nk’uko byanditswe ngo « Ku mpamvu yawe , baratwica umusubizo ; batugize intama z’imbagwa . »
45008037	Nyamara muri ibyo byose tugatsinda kakahava , tubikesha Uwadukunze .
45008038	Koko rero simbishidikanya : ari urupfu , ari ubugingo , ari abamalayika , ari ibinyabubasha , ari iby’ubu , ari ibizaza , ari ibinyamaboko ,
45008039	ari iby’ejuru , ari iby’ikuzimu , ari n’ikindi kiremwa cyose , nta na kimwe kizashobora kudutandukanya n’urukundo Imana idukunda muri Kristu Yezu Umwami wacu .
45009001	Ndavuga ukuri muri Kristu rwose simbeshya : icyemezo ndagitangana umutimanama wanjye muri Roho Mutagatifu .
45009002	Mfite agahinda kenshi n’intimba inshengura umutima ubutitsa .
45009003	Koko rero nakwiyifuriza kuba ikivume jyewe ubwanjye ngatandukana na Kristu , nigurana abavandimwe banjye dusangiye ubwoko ku bw’umubiri ,
45009004	ari bo Abayisraheli . Ni bo batowe , bahabwa ikuzo n’amasezerano , amategeko , imihango n’ubuhanuzi .
45009005	Abasekuruza babo ni bo Kristu akomokaho ku bw’umubiri , We usumba byose , Imana isingizwa iteka ryose . Amen .
45009006	Nyamara ariko ijambo ry’Imana ntiryapfuye ubusa . Koko rero abakomoka kuri Israheli , si ko bose ari Israheli y’ukuri .
45009007	No kuba inkomoko ya Abrahamu , si byo kuba bose ari abana be . Ahubwo « Abakomoka kuri Izaki ni bo bazitwa abawe . »
45009008	Ari byo kuvuga ko kuba abana be ku bw’umubiri , atari byo kuba abana b’Imana , ahubwo abana b’isezerano ni bo babarwa mu rubyaro .
45009009	Ngiri rero ijambo ry’isezerano « Igihe nk’iki nzahindukira , kandi Sara azabyara umuhungu . »
45009010	Si n’ibyo gusa . Hari na Rebeka wasamye inda imwe kuri Izaki , umubyeyi wacu .
45009011	Igihe abana bataravuka , nta cyiza cyangwa ikibi barakora , kugira ngo umugambi w’Imana ukomeze ushingire ku butore ,
45009012	atari ku bikorwa , ahubwo kuri Nyiruguhitamo , yarabwiwe ngo « Gakuru azaba umugaragu wa Gatoya » ,
45009013	nk’uko byanditswe ngo « Nikundiye Yakobo , maze ndeka Ezawu . »
45009014	Twabivugaho iki rero ? Ko Imana ibera ? Oya , ntibikabeho .
45009015	Yabwiye Musa iti « Nzagirira ineza uwo nzashaka kuyigirira , nzagirire impuhwe uwo nzashaka kuzigirira . »
45009016	Nuko rero , si iby’umwete cyangwa ubushake by’umuntu , ahubwo ni iby’Imana igira impuhwe .
45009017	Kuko Ibyanditswe bibwira Farawo biti « Dore icyatumye ngushyiraho , kwari ukugira ngo nzakwerekanireho ububasha bwanjye maze izina ryanjye ribe ikirangirire ku isi yose . »
45009018	Nuko rero Imana ibabarira uwo ishaka , ikanangira umutima w’uwo ishaka .
45009019	Ubwo rero wagira uti « Imana iracyadushakaho iki ? » Mbese ni nde warwanya ugushaka kwayo ?
45009020	Mbe muntu , uri nde wo gushyogoranya n’Imana ? Mbese ikintu cy’ikibumbano cyabwira uwakibumbye ngo « Kuki wankoze utya ? »
45009021	Mbese umubumbyi ntashobora kuvana mu ibumba rimwe igikoresho cy’agaciro n’igikoresho gisanzwe ?
45009022	Bityo rero Imana yashatse kwerekana uburakari bwayo no kugaragaza ububasha bwayo . Yihanganiye bihagije ibibumbano bibi byari bikwiriye kujanjagurwa .
45009023	Ibyo kwari ukugira ngo ibibumbano bikwiriye impuhwe byateganyirijwe ikuzo , ibigaragarize uburumbuke bw’ikuzo ryayo bwite :
45009024	ibyo bibumbano ni twebwe yahamagaye tutavuye mu Bayahudi gusa , ahubwo ndetse no mu Banyamahanga .
45009025	Nk’uko yabivuze muri Hozeya ati « Umuryango utari uwanjye nzawita umuryango wanjye , utari inkundwakazi nzamwita inkundwakazi ;
45009026	kandi ahantu babwiriwe ngo ntimuri umuryango wanjye , ni ho bazitirwa abana b’Imana Nyir’ubugingo . »
45009027	Izayi na we yavuze ibyerekeye Israheli ati « Naho umubare w’abana ba Israheli wangana n’umusenyi wo ku nyanja , agasigisigi konyine ni ko kazarokoka ,
45009028	kuko Nyagasani azasohoza ijambo rye ku isi , ku buryo bunonosoye kandi adatindiganyije . »
45009029	Ni nk’uko kandi Izayi yabihanuye ati « Iyo Nyagasani Umutegetsi w’ingabo atatuzigamira imbuto , tuba twarabaye nka Sodoma , tukagereranywa na Gomora . »
45009030	Twabivugaho iki ? Ko abanyamahanga batashakashakaga ubutungane babushyikiriye , ubutungane ariko bukomoka ku kwemera ,
45009031	naho Israheli yashakaga itegeko ritanga ubutungane , ntiyarishyikira .
45009032	Ni ku mpamvu ki rero ? Ni uko itashakiye ubutungane ku kwemera , ahubwo mu bikorwa . Batsitaye ku ibuye ry’ubutsikire
45009033	nk’uko byanditswe ngo « Dore nshyize muri Siyoni ibuye ry’ubutsikire n’urutare rugusha , ariko uzemera akarushingaho ibirindiro ntazakorwa n’isoni . »
45010001	Bavandimwe , icyo umutima wanjye wifuza n’icyo nsaba Imana ni uko barokoka .
45010002	Ndahamya rwose ko bafitiye Imana ishyaka , ariko nta bushishozi ,
45010003	kuko bayobewe ubutungane buturuka ku Mana , bashaka gushyiraho ubwabo bwite , ntibayoboka ubutungane bw’Imana .
45010004	Kuko amategeko agarukira kuri Kristu , kugira ngo uwemera wese ahabwe kuba intungane .
45010005	Koko rero Musa yanditse ko ubutungane buturuka ku mategeko , kandi ko umuntu uzayubahiriza , azabeshwaho na yo .
45010006	Naho ubutungane buturuka ku kwemera bwo bukavuga buti « Ntukavuge mu mutima wawe ngo ’ Ni nde uzazamuka mu ijuru ? ’ » ari byo kuvuga kumanurayo Kristu ,
45010007	cyangwa ngo « Ni nde uzamanuka ikuzimu ? » ari byo kuvuga kuzamura Kristu mu bapfuye .
45010008	Ni ukuvuga iki se ahubwo ? « Ijambo rikuri bugufi cyane , riri mu kanwa kawe no mu mutima wawe . » Iryo jambo ni iry’ukwemera twamamaza .
45010009	Kuko niba wamamarisha umunwa wawe ko Kristu ari Nyagasani kandi ukemera mu mutima wawe ko Imana yamuzuye mu bapfuye , uzarokorwa .
45010010	Nuko rero umuntu yemera n’umutima bikamuha ubutungane , yakwamamarisha umunwa bikamuha uburokorwe .
45010011	Kuko Ibyanditswe bivuga ngo « Umwemera wese ntazakozwa isoni . »
45010012	Nta tandukanyirizo rero hagati y’Umuyahudi n’Umugereki : Nyagasani ni umwe kuri bose , akungahaza abamwambaza bose .
45010013	Kuko « umuntu wese uzambaza izina rya Nyagasani , azarokorwa . »
45010014	Bakwiyambaza bate rero Uwo bataremera ? Bakwemera bate se Uwo batarumva ? Bamwumva bate ntawamwamamaje ?
45010015	Bamwamamaza bate niba batatumwe ? Nk’uko byanditswe ngo « Mbega ngo biraba byiza ibirenge by’abogeza inkuru nziza ! »
45010016	Nyamara si ko bose bumviye Inkuru Nziza . Koko rero Izayi yaravuze ati « Nyagasani , ni nde wemeye inyigisho zacu ? »
45010017	Bityo rero , ukwemera gushingira ku nyigisho , inyigisho na yo ku ijambo rya Kristu .
45010018	Reka nanjye mbaze : mbese ntibumvise ? Barumvise . Ahubwo ndetse ngo « Ijwi ryabo ryakwiriye isi yose , n’ijambo ryabo rigera ku mpera z’isi . »
45010019	Nongere mbaze : mbese Israheli yaba itarasobanukiwe ? Musa ni we wabanje kuvuga ati « Nzabaharika ikitari umuryango muterwe ishyari n’ihanga ritagira ubwenge . »
45010020	Izayi we ntatinya kuvuga ati « Nabonywe n’abatanshakashakaga , nigaragariza abatambaririzaga » ;
45010021	naho Israheli akayibwira ati « Nirije umunsi ntegeye amaboko umuryango utanyumvira , wigometse . »
45011001	Reka mbaze rero : mbese Imana yaba yaraciye umuryango wayo ? Oya ntibikabe ! Nanjye ndi Umuyisraheli wo mu rubyaro rwa Abrahamu , mu nzu ya Benyamini .
45011002	Nta bwo Imana yaciye umuryango wayo kandi ari wo yari yaratoye . Cyangwa se ntimuzi icyo Ibyanditswe bivuga aho Eliya arega Israheli ku Mana , agira ati
45011003	« Nyagasani , bishe abahanuzi bawe , basenya intambiro zawe , none nsigaye ndi jyenyine kandi nanjye barahigira amagara yanjye ! »
45011004	Mbese Imana imusubiza iki ? « Nsigaranye abantu ibihumbi birindwi batapfukamiye Behali . »
45011005	Bityo rero no muri ibi bihe , hari agasigisigi katoranijwe ku buntu .
45011006	Ubwo rero ari ku buntu , ntibikiri ku bw’ibikorwa , naho ubundi ubuntu ntibwaba bukiri bwo .
45011007	Bite rero ? Ko icyo Israheli yashakashakaga itagishyikiriye ! Nyamara abatowe bo baragishyikiriye , naho abandi baranangira ,
45011008	nk’uko byanditswe ngo « Imana yabahaye umutima uhumye , n’amaso atabona , n’amatwi atumva , kugeza na n’ubu . »
45011009	Na Dawudi aravuga ati « Ameza yabo arakababera umutego , urushundura , urutsitariro n’igihano bikwiriye !
45011010	Amaso yabo arakijima boye kubona n’umugongo wabo ube umuheto iteka ryose . »
45011011	Reka nongere mbaze : batsitariye kugwa ngo bahere hasi ? Oya , ntibikabe ! Ahubwo ugutsitara kwabo kwatumye uburokorwe bugera ku banyamahanga kugira ngo bibatere ishyari .
45011012	Ubwo se ugutsitara kwabo kwakungahaje isi , n’ukugwa kwabo kugakungahaza amahanga , ntibizahebuza nibagera ku burokorwe bwuzuye ?
45011013	Mwebwe abanyamahanga , dore icyo mbabwira : mu rugero jyewe ndi intumwa mu mahanga , nubahiriza ubutumwa nahawe ,
45011014	nizera gutera ishyari abo dusangiye ubwoko ngo ngire bamwe muri bo ndokora .
45011015	Kuko niba ugucibwa kwabo kwararonkeye isi kwiyunga n’Imana , ukugarurwa kwabo kuzacura iki kitari ukuzuka kw’abari barapfuye ?
45011016	Iyo ifu y’umuganura ari ntagatifu , n’irobe ni ko riba ; n’iyo imizi ari mitagatifu , amashami na yo ni ko aba .
45011017	Niba amwe mu mashami yaratemwe , maze wowe , n’ubwo wari ishami ry’agasozi , ukahagemekwa maze ugasangizwa amakakama azamurwa n’umuzi w’umuzeti ,
45011018	ntukitere hejuru wigamba kuri ya mashami . Niba witeye hejuru , wibuke ko atari wowe uhagaritse umuzi , ko ahubwo ari umuzi uguhagaritse .
45011019	Ahari wavuga uti « Batemye amashami kugira ngo ngemekwe . »
45011020	Ni byo koko . Yatemwe ku mpamvu y’ukutemera , naho wowe uhahagaritswe n’ukwemera . Ntukitere hejuru rero , ahubwo tinya .
45011021	Kuko ubwo Imana itasoneye amashami ya kamere , nawe ntizagusonera .
45011022	Irebere nawe ubugwaneza n’ubutabera by’Imana : ku baguye ikurikira ubutabera , kuri wowe igira ubuntu , niba ariko ugumye muri ubwo bugwaneza , naho ubundi nawe izagukorora .
45011023	Nyamara na bo umunsi bemeye , bazongera bagemekwe : kuko Imana ishobora kongera kubagemeka .
45011024	Ko wowe watemwe ku giti cy’agasozi muhuje ubwoko , maze ukagemekwa ku muzeti mwiza mudahuje ubwoko , nkanswe bo bazagemekwa ku muzeti wabo bwite bahuje ubwoko !
45011025	Koko rero , bavandimwe , sinshaka ko muyoberwa iri banga hato mutazirata : igice kimwe cya Israheli kizanangira umutima kugeza igihe abanyamahanga bose bazaba bakoranyijwe .
45011026	Bityo rero Israheli yose izarokorwa nk’uko byanditswe ngo « Umucunguzi azaturuka i Siyoni , yamaganire kure ya Yakobo icyitwa ubugomeramana .
45011027	Ngiryo isezerano nzagirana na bo , maze kubakuraho ibyaha byabo . »
45011028	Kuba batakiriye Inkuru Nziza , babaye abanzi b’Imana , naho kuba baratowe , ni abatoni bayo babikesha abasekuruza .
45011029	Koko rero igihe Imana imaze gutanga no gutora , ntiyisubiraho .
45011030	Nk’uko namwe kera mutumviraga , none ubu ngubu mukaba mwaragiriwe impuhwe ku mpamvu y’ukutumvira kwabo ,
45011031	bityo na bo ubu ngubu banze kumvira kugira ngo mugirirwe impuhwe , mu gihe cyabo na bo bazazigirirwe .
45011032	Imana yakoranirije abantu bose mu bwigomeke kugira ngo bose hamwe ibagirire imbabazi .
45011033	Mbega ukuntu ubukungu n’ubuhanga n’ubwenge by’Imana birengeje urugero ! Mbega ukuntu imigambi yayo ari inshoberabantu , n’inzira zayo zikaba urujijo !
45011034	« Koko rero , ni nde wamenye igitekerezo cya Nyagasani , cyangwa ni nde wamubereye umujyanama ,
45011035	cyangwa se wabanje kugira icyo amuha ngo azagombe kumwitura ? »
45011036	Ko byose bikomoka kuri We bikabeshwaho na We , bikaberaho We . Nahabwe ikuzo iteka ryose ! Amen .
45012001	Bavandimwe rero , mbinginze ku bw’impuhwe z’Imana : nimuture imibiri yanyu , ibe igitambo nyabuzima , gitagatifu kandi kinyuze Imana ; ngiryo iyobokamana ryabava ku mutima .
45012002	Kandi ntimukigane ibi bihe turimo , ahubwo nimuhinduke , mwivugururemo ibitekerezo , kugira ngo muzajye mumenya neza ugushaka kw’Imana , ikiri cyiza , icyashimisha n’ikiboneye .
45012003	Ku bw’ingabire nahawe , reka ngire icyo mbwira buri wese muri mwe : ntimukirebe ibisumbye uko mugomba kwireba , ahubwo muzirikane ibifasha kwiyoroshya , buri wese mu rugero rw’ukwemera Imana yamugeneye .
45012004	Mbese nk’uko mu mubiri umwe tugira ingingo nyinshi kandi ingingo zose ntizikore umurimo umwe ,
45012005	bityo turi benshi , ariko tugize umubiri umwe muri Kristu , buri wese ku buryo bwe akabera abandi urugingo .
45012006	Dufite ingabire zinyuranye bikurikije ineza twagiriwe . Uwahawe ingabire y’ubuhanuzi , ajye ahanura akurikije ukwemera ;
45012007	uwahawe ingabire yo kwita ku bandi , abiteho ; uwahawe kwigisha , niyigishe ;
45012008	uwahawe gutera abandi inkunga , nayibatere . Utanga , atange nta kindi akurikiranye ; uyobora , ayoborane umwete ; utabara abatishoboye , nabafashe anezerewe .
45012009	Urukundo rwanyu ruzire uburyarya . Ikibi kibashishe mugihunge , naho icyiza mukihambireho .
45012010	Mukundane urukundo rwa kivandimwe , mushyire imbere icyahesha buri wese icyubahiro .
45012011	Muragire umwete ntimukabe abanebwe , nimushishikare , mube abagaragu ba Nyagasani .
45012012	Mwishimire amizero mufite , mwiyumanganye mu magorwa , ntimugahweme gusenga .
45012013	Musangire n’abatagatifujwe bakennye , muharanire gufata neza abashyitsi .
45012014	Musabire umugisha ababatoteza , mubasabire umugisha aho kubavuma .
45012015	Mwishimane n’abishimye , murirane n’abarira .
45012016	Muhuze imitima ; ntimukararikire ibibasumbye , ahubwo mwimenyereze ibiciye bugufi . « Ntimukishime ubwenge bwanyu . »
45012017	Ntihakagire uwo mwitura inabi ; « mwihatire kugaragariza abantu bose ibyiza mukora . »
45012018	Bishobotse , mu rugero byabaturukaho mwebwe , mubane mu mahoro n’abantu bose .
45012019	Ntimukihorere ubwanyu , nkoramutima zanjye , ahubwo muhe akanya uburakari bw’Imana nk’uko byanditswe ngo « Kumara inzigo ni ibyanjye , ni jye uzatanga inyiturano » , uwo ari Nyagasani ubivuga .
45012020	Ahubwo rero « niba umwanzi wawe ashonje , muhe icyo kurya ; niba afite inyota , muhe icyo kunywa . Kuko nugenza utyo , uzaba umurahuriye ku mutwe amakara agurumana . »
45012021	Ntukareke inabi ikuganza , ahubwo inabi uyiganjishe ineza .
45013001	Umuntu wese yumvire ubutegetsi bumusumbye , kuko nta butegetsi budaturuka ku Mana kandi n’uburiho bukaba bwarashinzwe n’Imana .
45013002	Bityo urwanya ubutegetsi aba arwanya icyo Imana yagennye , kandi ababurwanya baba bikururira urubanza .
45013003	Kuko ugira neza si we utinya abatware , ahubwo ni ugira nabi . Mbese urashaka kudatinya ubutegetsi ? Kora icyiza , na bwo buzagushima .
45013004	Kuko Imana ibukoresha ngo ugere ku cyiza . Ariko niba ukoze ikibi , utinye ; nta bwo bwitwaza inkota ku busa . Kuko Imana ikoresha ubutegetsi ngo ibuhanishe ugira nabi .
45013005	Ni yo mpamvu ari ngombwa kuyoboka ubutegetsi , bidatewe no gutinya umujinya wabwo gusa , ahubwo ubibwirijwe n’umutimanama .
45013006	Ni na yo mpamvu burya mutanga imisoro : abayakirana ubwitonzi , baba bakorera Imana .
45013007	Mujye muha buri muntu ikiri icye : uwo mugomba umusoro , mumuhe umusoro ; uwo mugomba ihazabu , muyimuhe ; ugomba gutinywa , mumutinye ; ugomba kubahwa , mumwubahe .
45013008	Ntihakagire uwo mubamo umwenda , atari uwo gukundana . Kuko ukunda undi , aba yujuje amategeko .
45013009	Kuko kuvuga ngo « Ntuzasambane , ntuzice , ntuzibe , ntuzararikire ikibi » , kimwe n’andi mategeko , yose akubiye muri iri jambo ngo « Uzakunde mugenzi wawe nkawe ubwawe . »
45013010	Ukunda ntiyagirira mugenzi we inabi . Urukundo rero ni rwo rubumbye amategeko .
45013011	Cyane cyane mumenye ko aya magingo turimo , ari igihe cyo gushiguka mu bitotsi , kuko ukurokorwa kuturi hafi ubu ngubu kurusha igihe twakiriye ukwemera .
45013012	Ijoro rirakuze , umunsi ugiye gucya . Nitwiyake rero ibikorwa by’umwijima maze twambare intwaro z’urumuri .
45013013	Tugendane umurava nk’abagenda ku mugaragaro amanywa ava , nta busambo , nta businzi , nta busambanyi , nta biterasoni , nta ntonganya , nta shyari .
45013014	Ahubwo nimwiyambike Nyagasani Yezu Kristu kandi ntimukishinge umubiri ngo mukore ibyo wifuza .
45014001	Mujye mwakira ugifite intege nke mu kwemera , mwoye kumugisha impaka mu byo ashidikanyaho .
45014002	Kuko hari uwemera ko ashobora kurya ibibonetse byose , naho uw’intege nke yibwira ko agomba kurya imboga gusa .
45014003	Uwirira ibibonetse byose , ntagasuzugure utabirya ; utabirya na we ntazacire ubirya urubanza , kuko Imana yamwakiriye .
45014004	Uri nde mbese , wowe ucira urubanza umugaragu utari uwawe ? Yahagarara cyangwa yagwa , ibyo bireba shebuja ; nyamara azagumya ahagarare kuko Nyagasani afite ububasha bwo kumushyigikira .
45014005	Hari usumbanya umunsi umwe n’indi , hari n’ubona yose ari kimwe . Buri wese ajye akurikiza icyo umutima we wemera .
45014006	Usumbanya iminsi ayisumbanyiriza Nyagasani ; uwirira ibibonetse byose , abirira Nyagasani kuko aba ashimira Imana . Utarya na we , ni Nyagasani abigirira , na we ashimira Imana .
45014007	Koko rero nta n’umwe muri twe ubereyeho we ubwe , kandi nta n’umwe upfira we ubwe .
45014008	Niba turiho , tubereyeho Nyagasani ; niba kandi dupfuye , dupfira Nyagasani . Twabaho , twapfa , turi aba Nyagasani .
45014009	Koko rero ni cyo cyatumye Kristu apfa akazuka , kwari ukugira ngo abe ari we ugenga abapfuye n’abazima .
45014010	Wowe rero , ni iki gituma ucira umuvandimwe wawe urubanza ? Cyangwa ni iki gituma usuzugura umuvandimwe wawe ko twese tuzashyikirizwa urukiko rw’Imana ?
45014011	Kuko byanditswe ngo « Ndahiye ubuzima bwanjye — uwo ari Nyagasani ubivuga — icyitwa ivi cyose kizampfukamira , n’icyitwa ururimi cyose kizamamaze Imana . »
45014012	Nuko rero , umuntu wese azisobanurira ibye imbere y’Imana .
45014013	Ntitukongere rero gucirana imanza ; ahubwo twitondere icyabera umuvandimwe intandaro yo kugwa cyangwa gucumura .
45014014	Nzi neza , rwose sinshidikanya muri Nyagasani Yezu , ko nta kintu gihumanya ku bwacyo ; nyamara hagize utekereza ko ikintu gihumanya , kuri we koko kiba gihumanya .
45014015	Niba rero umuvandimwe wawe atewe agahinda n’icyo uriye , ntuba ukigengwa n’urukundo . Irinde kugira icyo urya cyagusha uwo Kristu yapfiriye .
45014016	Ikiri cyiza kuri mwe ntikigasebe .
45014017	Kuko Ingoma y’Imana itagizwe n’ibiribwa n’ibinyobwa , ahubwo irangwa n’ubutungane , amahoro n’ihirwe muri Roho Mutagatifu .
45014018	Ukorera Kristu atyo , anyura Imana kandi agashimwa n’abantu .
45014019	Nuko rero niduharanire ibishyigikira amahoro n’ibidufasha guterana inkunga .
45014020	Ntugasenye igikorwa cy’Imana ku mpamvu y’ibyo kurya . Ibintu byose ntibihumanya , ariko ni bibi ko umuntu arya icyatera undi gucumura .
45014021	Ibyiza ni ukutarya inyama no kutanywa divayi , mbese ni ukwirinda icyabera umuvandimwe impamvu yo kugwa .
45014022	Wowe rero , icyo wabwirijwe n’ukwemera ufite ugihorane mu mutimanama wawe no mu maso y’Imana . Hahirwa utigaya ubwe mu byo yahisemo yabisuzumye .
45014023	Naho urya kandi agishidikanya , uwo yatsinzwe n’urubanza kuko ibyo akora biba bidaturutse ku kwemera , kandi rero icyo umuntu akoze kidaturutse ku kwemera , kiba ari icyaha .
45015001	Twebwe abakomeye tugomba kugoboka intege nke z’abadashoboye , aho kwishimira gusa ibitworoheye .
45015002	Buri muntu muri twe nashimishe mugenzi we , akore icyiza cyose cyamukomeza .
45015003	Kuko na Kristu atakoze icyamushimishaga gusa , nk’uko byanditswe ngo « Ibitutsi by’abagutukaga byanguyeho . »
45015004	Koko rero ibyanditswe kera byose , byandikiwe kutubera inyigisho kugira ngo tugire icyizere , twihangane kandi duhumurizwe na byo .
45015005	Imana soko y’ukwihangana n’uguhumurizwa , irabahe no guhuza ibitekerezo nk’uko Kristu Yezu abishaka ,
45015006	kugira ngo , mu mutima umwe no mu ijwi rimwe , muhe ikuzo Imana , Se w’Umwami wacu Yezu Kristu .
45015007	Ku mpamvu y’ibyo rero , nimwakirane nk’uko na Kristu ubwe yabakiriye agirira ikuzo ry’Imana .
45015008	Ndahamya ko Kristu yigize umugaragu w’abagenywe kugira ngo yerekane ubudahemuka bw’Imana maze yuzuze ibyo abasokuruza basezeranijwe .
45015009	Naho amahanga ahe Imana ikuzo ayishimira impuhwe zayo , nk’uko byanditswe ngo « Ni yo mpamvu nzakwamamaza mu mahanga , kandi nzasingiza izina ryawe » ,
45015010	kandi ngo « Mahanga , nimwishimane n’umuryango we » ,
45015011	nanone ngo « Mahanga mwese , nimusingize Nyagasani ; miryango mwese , nimumuhimbaze . »
45015012	Izayi na we akongera ati « Azashyira aze inkomoko ya Yese ; ni we uzabadukira kugenga amahanga , kandi ni we bose bazizera . »
45015013	Imana , Yo soko y’amizero , nibuzuze ihirwe ryose n’amahoro mu kwemera kugira ngo musenderezwe ukwizera ku bw’ububasha bwa Roho Mutagatifu .
45015014	Bavandimwe banjye , nzi neza ko namwe ubwanyu mwuje ingeso nziza , ko mwuzuye ubumenyi bwose , ko mushobora ubwanyu kujijurana .
45015015	Nyamara hamwe na hamwe muri iyi baruwa hari aho nagiye mbandikira ku buryo bwubahutse , nsa n’ubibutsa , kuko nahawe ingabire n’Imana
45015016	yo kuba umugaragu wa Kristu mu mahanga , nkegurirwa umurimo w’Inkuru Nziza kugira ngo amahanga atagatifuzwe na Roho Mutagatifu , maze yakirweho ituro rinyuze Imana .
45015017	Ni cyo gituma nshobora kwirata muri Kristu Yezu ibyo nkorera Imana .
45015018	Kuko ntagira icyo niratana usibye icyo Kristu ubwe yankoresheje , ari mu magambo , ari mu bikorwa ,
45015019	mu bubasha bw’ibimenyetso n’ibitangaza , no mu bubasha bwa Roho , kugira ngo amahanga yumvire Imana . Bityo uhereye i Yeruzalemu ukazenguruka ukagera muri Iliriya , nahakwije Inkuru Nziza ya Kristu .
45015020	Nirinze ariko kuyamamaza ahandi handi usibye aho izina rya Kristu ritazwi , kugira ngo ntavaho nubaka mu kibanza cy’undi ,
45015021	nk’uko byanditswe ngo « Abatamumenyeshejwe bazamubona , n’abatamwumvise bazamumenya . »
45015022	Ngicyo icyambujije kenshi kuza iwanyu .
45015023	None ubu ngubu , ubwo ntagifite ahandi nshigaje mu birere by’ino , nkaba kandi narifuje kuza iwanyu kuva imyaka n’imyaka ,
45015024	igihe nzerekeza muri Hispaniya . . . Koko rero ndizera kuzababona mpita , nyuma mukamperekeza , maze kubashira urukumbuzi ho gato .
45015025	Ubu ngubu ariko ngiye i Yeruzalemu kwita ku batagatifujwe .
45015026	Kuko ab’i Masedoniya n’abo muri Akaya biyemeje kugira icyo basaranganya n’abatagatifujwe b’i Yeruzalemu bakennye .
45015027	Koko rero barabyiyemeje kandi barabibagombaga . Kuko niba amahanga yarasangiye na bo ibyiza byabo by’umutima , agomba kubafashisha ibyiza by’umubiri .
45015028	Ibyo rero nimbirangiza , maze kubashyikiriza ku mugaragaro uwo musaruro , nzabanyuraho njya muri Hispaniya .
45015029	Kandi nzi ko ninza iwanyu , nzazana umugisha wose wa Kristu .
45015030	Bavandimwe kandi , ndabinginga ku bw’Umwami wacu Yezu Kristu no ku bw’urukundo rwa Roho Mutagatifu , ngo muntabaze amasengesho munturira Imana ,
45015031	kugira ngo nkire abo mu Yudeya batemera , maze imfashanyo njyanye i Yeruzalemu izanyure abatagatifujwe ;
45015032	bityo nshobore kuza iwanyu nishimye , maze Imana nibishaka , nzaruhukane namwe .
45015033	Imana , Yo soko y’amahoro , nibane namwe mwese ! Amen .
45016001	Mbashinze mushiki wacu Foyibe , umudiyakonikazi mu Kiliziya y’i Kenkireya ,
45016002	kugira ngo mumwakire muri Nyagasani nk’uko bikwiriye abatagatifujwe , kandi ngo muzamufashe mu byo yabakeneraho byose , kuko na we yatabaye benshi , barimo jye .
45016003	Mutashye Purisika na Akwila , abafasha banjye muri Kristu Yezu ;
45016004	abo ni bo bishyize mu kaga , kugira ngo barwane ku buzima bwanjye . Si jye jyenyine ubashimira , ahubwo na Kiliziya zose z’abanyamahanga .
