45016005	Mutashye na Kiliziya ijya iteranira mu rugo rwabo . Mutashye incuti yanjye Epayineto , we muganura Aziya yahaye Kristu .
45016006	Mutashye Mariya wabavunikiye cyane .
45016007	Mutashye bene wacu Andironiki na Yuniya , twasangiye umunyururu ; ni intumwa z’ibirangirire kandi babaye aba Kristu mbere yanjye .
45016008	Mutashye Ampiliyato , incuti yanjye muri Nyagasani .
45016009	Muntahirize Urubano umufasha wanjye muri Kristu , ndetse na Sitaki incuti yanjye .
45016010	Muntahirize kwa Arisitobuli .
45016011	Muntahirize mwene wacu Herodiyoni . Muntahirize abo kwa Narisisi bari muri Nyagasani .
45016012	Muramutse Tirifayina na Tirifoza baruhira cyane Nyagasani . Mundamukirize inkoramutima Perisida , na we uvunikira cyane Nyagasani .
45016013	Muramutse Rufo , intore muri Nyagasani , ndetse na nyina ari we wanjye .
45016014	Mutashye Asinkirito , Filegonti , Erimesi , Patiroba , Herimasi n’abavandimwe bari kumwe na bo .
45016015	Muramutse Filologo na Yuliya , Nereyi na mushiki we , na Olimpiya n’abatagatifujwe bari kumwe na bo .
45016016	Nimuramukanye mu muhoberano mutagatifu . Kiliziya zose za Kristu zirabatashya .
45016017	Ndabinginze kandi , bavandimwe , mwitondere abazana amacakubiri n’ingero mbi , bakanyuranya n’inyigisho mwahawe ; mubagendere kure .
45016018	Bene abo ntibakorera Kristu Umwami wacu , ahubwo inda yabo , maze amagambo yabo y’uburyarya n’ubucakura akayobya imitima itagira iribi .
45016019	Ukumvira kwanyu kwamenyekanye hose ; ndabishimiye rero ariko ndashaka ko muba abahanga mu gukora icyiza n’abaswa mu gukora ikibi .
45016020	Imana , Yo soko y’amahoro , izajanjagurira Sekibi mu nsi y’ibirenge byanyu vuba . Ineza y’Umwami wacu Yezu Kristu ibane namwe !
45016021	Timote , umufasha wanjye , arabatashya , na bene wacu Lusiyo , na Yasoni , na Sosipateri .
45016022	Nanjye ndabatashya muri Nyagasani , jyewe Teritiyo wanditse uru rwandiko .
45016023	Arabatashya Gayusi uncumbikiye jye na Kiliziya yose .
45016024	Arabaramutsa Erasito umubikamari w’umugi , n’umuvandimwe Kuwariti .
45016025	Nihasingizwe Imana , Yo ifite ububasha bwo kubakomeza bihuje n’Inkuru Nziza nabashyikirije namamaza Yezu Kristu , nkurikije iyobera ryari ryaracecetswe kuva kera kose ,
45016026	ubu rikaba ryahishuriwe abanyamahanga bose , rikagaragarira mu byanditswe by’abahanuzi . Nguko uko Imana Ihoraho yabigennye kugira ngo na bo ibageze ku kwemera bayumvire .
45016027	Imana Nyir’ubuhanga nihabwe ikuzo muri Yezu Kristu , uko ibihe bihora bisimburana iteka . Amen .
46001001	Jyewe Pawulo , watorewe kuba intumwa ya Yezu Kristu , uko Imana yabishatse , hamwe n’umuvandimwe wacu Sositeni ,
46001002	kuri Kiliziya y’Imana iri i Korinti , ari yo mwebwe abatagatifurijwe muri Yezu Kristu , mugahamagarirwa kuba intungane hamwe n’abandi bose biyambaza , aho bari hose , izina rya Nyagasani Yezu Kristu , Umwami wabo n’uwacu :
46001003	tubifurije ineza n’amahoro biva ku Mana , Umubyeyi wacu , no kuri Nyagasani Yezu Kristu .
46001004	Mpora nshimira Imana yanjye kubera mwebwe , nibuka ineza yayo mwaherewe muri Kristu Yezu .
46001005	Koko rero Imana yabasenderejeho ingabire z’amoko yose muri We , cyane cyane iyo kumumenya no kumumenyesha abandi .
46001006	Bityo guhamya Kristu mukaba mwarabyikomejemo ,
46001007	ku buryo nta ngabire n’imwe y’Imana mubuze , mu gihe mugitegereje ukwigaragaza kwa Yezu Kristu Umwami wacu .
46001008	Ni we uzabakomeza kugeza mu ndunduro , kugira ngo muzabe muri indakemwa , kuri uwo munsi wa Nyagasani Yezu Kristu .
46001009	Ni indahemuka , Imana yabahamagariye kugirana ubumwe n’Umwana wayo Yezu Kristu , Umwami wacu .
46001010	Bavandimwe , mbinginze mu izina ry’Umwami wacu Yezu Kristu , ngo muhuze ibitekerezo , mwirinde kwicamo ibice ; ahubwo muhuze umutima n’umugambi .
46001011	Koko rero , bavandimwe , abo kwa Kolowe bambwiye ko mwifitemo amakimbirane .
46001012	Icyo nshaka kuvuga ni uko buri muntu muri mwe agira ati « Jyewe ndi uwa Pawulo ! » Undi ati « Jyewe ndi uwa Apolo ! » Undi ati « Jyewe , ndi uwa Kefasi ! » Undi ati « Jyewe ndi uwa Kristu ! »
46001013	Mbese Kristu yaba agabanijemo ibice ? Mbese ni Pawulo wababambiwe ku musaraba ? Cyangwa se mwabatijwe mu izina rya Pawulo ?
46001014	Ndashimira Imana kuba nta n’umwe muri mwe nabatije , usibye Kirisipo na Gayo ;
46001015	ku buryo nta n’umwe uzavuga ko yabatijwe mu izina ryanjye !
46001016	Cyakora koko nabatije n’umuryango wa Sitefana , nkaba numva nta wundi wundi nabatije .
46001017	Kuko Kristu atanyohereje kubatiza , ahubwo yantumye kwamamaza Inkuru Nziza , atari mu magambo y’ubuhanga ngo hato umusaraba wa Kristu udakurizaho guta agaciro .
46001018	Mu by’ukuri , kwamamaza urupfu rwa Kristu ku musaraba bisa n’amahomvu ku bari mu nzira yo korama , ariko ku bari mu nzira yo gukira ari bo twe , ni ububasha bw’Imana .
46001019	Kuko handitswe ngo « Nzasenya ubuhanga bw’abahanga kandi nzarimbura ubwenge bw’abanyabwenge . »
46001020	Mbese uw’umuhanga ari he ? Uw’umunyabwenge ari hehe ? Uw’intyoza mu by’iyi si ari he ? Ko ubanza ubuhanga bw’iyi si Imana yarabuhinduye amahomvu ?
46001021	Koko rero , isi ku bwenge bwayo ntiyashoboye kumenyera Imana mu bigaragaza ubuhanga bwayo ; ni yo mpamvu Imana yihitiyemo gukiza abemera , ikoresheje ubusazi bw’iyamamazabutumwa .
46001022	Mu gihe Abayahudi bigomba ibitangaza , naho Abagereki bashimikiriye iby’ubuhanga ,
46001023	twebweho twamamaza Kristu wabambwe ku musaraba , bigashengura Abayahudi , kandi bikitwa ibisazi ku Bagereki .
46001024	Naho ku batowe , baba Abayahudi cyangwa Abagereki , Kristu uwo ni we bubasha bw’Imana n’ubuhanga bwayo .
46001025	Kuko icyakwitwa ibisazi ariko giturutse ku Mana gitambutse kure ubuhanga bw’abantu , kandi icyakwitwa intege nke giturutse ku Mana gisumbye imbaraga z’abantu .
46001026	Bavandimwe rero , mwebwe abatowe n’Imana , nimurebe uko muteye : murasanga ku bw’abantu nta bahanga benshi babarimo , nta n’ibihangange byinshi bibarimo , ndetse nta na benshi bafite amavuko y’ikirenga .
46001027	Ahubwo rero ibyo abantu bita ibisazi , ni byo Imana yihitiyemo ngo irindagize abiyita abahanga ; kandi ibinyantege nke ku bantu , ni byo Imana yitoreye ngo isuzuguze abanyamaboko ;
46001028	byongeye , abatagira amavuko b’insuzugurwa ni bo Imana yihitiyemo ngo ihindure ubusa abiyita imbonera ;
46001029	kugira ngo hatagira umuntu n’umwe wikuza imbere y’Imana .
46001030	Ni yo mukesha kuba muri Kristu Yezu , we watubereye ku bw’Imana ubuhanga n’ubutungane , akaba ari we kandi udutagatifuza akanaturokora .
46001031	Mbese nk’uko byanditswe ngo « Ushaka kwirata wese , niyiratire muri Nyagasani . »
46002001	Bavandimwe , igihe niyiziye ubwanjye iwanyu kwamamaza amabanga y’Imana , sinakoresheje amagambo y’akarimi keza cyangwa y’ubwenge .
46002002	Koko rero nta kindi kindi nashatse kwibandaho usibye kubamenyesha Yezu Kristu , kandi Yezu Kristu wabambwe ku musaraba .
46002003	Igihe nari kumwe namwe , nari mfite intege nke , ntinya kandi ndagadwa ,
46002004	kandi amagambo nakoresheje mbamamazamo Inkuru Nziza nta ho yari ahuriye n’iby’ubwenge buhanitse , ahubwo yabemeje ku bw’ububasha bwa Roho w’Imana .
46002005	Bityo , ukwemera kwanyu kukaba kudashingiye ku bwenge bw’abantu , ahubwo ku bubasha bw’Imana .
46002006	Nyamara , abamaze gukomera mu kwemera turababwira iby’ubuhanga , ariko butari ubuhanga bw’iyi si , cyangwa bukomoka ku bagenga b’iyi si kuko bariho batariho .
46002007	Ubuhanga bw’Imana tubagezaho ni ibanga Imana yari yarazigamiye kuva kera kose kuduhesha ikuzo .
46002008	Nta n’umwe wo mu bagenga b’iyi si wigeze aritahura , kuko iyo baza kuritahura , ntibaba barabambye Umwami w’ikuzo .
46002009	Ariko bihuje n’uko byanditswe ngo « Icyo ijisho ritabonye , icyo ugutwi kutumvise , kandi ntikizamuke mu mutima wa muntu , ni cyo Imana yateguriye abayikunda . »
46002010	Ni twebwe rero Imana yabiseruriye ku bwa Roho wayo ; kandi Roho uwo acengera byose , kugeza no ku mayobera y’Imana .
46002011	Koko rero , ni nde wundi wamenya akari mu mutima w’umuntu , uretse nyirawo nyine ? Ni na ko rero nta wamenya amabanga y’Imana , uretse Roho wayo nyine .
46002012	Twebwe koko si ubwenge bw’isi twahawe , ahubwo ni Roho ukomoka ku Mana twahawe kugira ngo tumenye ibyiza Imana yatugabiye ku buntu .
46002013	Ibyo turabibigisha , tutifashishije imvugo y’ubuhanga bw’abantu , ahubwo twishingikirije ubuhanga bwa Roho uduha gusobanura ibya Roho mu magambo abigenewe .
46002014	Umuntu ugengwa na kamere ye gusa ntashobora kwumva ibya Roho w’Imana ; koko rero , kuri we ni nk’ibisazi , maze ntashobore kubyumva , kuko bene ibyo biserurirwa muri Roho wenyine .
46002015	Naho umuntu uyoborwa na Roho w’Imana asobanukirwa muri byose , akaba kandi nta we ushobora kumuhinyuza .
46002016	Koko se « Ni nde wamenye ibitekerezo bya Nyagasani ngo akurizeho kumwungura inama ? » Nyamara twebwe twifitemo ibitekerezo bya Kristu .
46003001	Bavandimwe , sinashoboye kuvugana namwe nk’ubwira abantu bayoborwa na Roho w’Imana , ahubwo nababwiye nk’uvugana n’abantu bakigengwa na kamere yabo gusa , mbese nk’abakiri ibitambambuga muri Kristu .
46003002	Nabatungishije amata , sinabagaburira ibyo kurya bikomeye , kuko mutari kubibasha . Ndetse n’ubu ntimurabibasha ,
46003003	kuko mukiri ab’iyi si . None se ko mukirangwa n’ishyari n’amakimbirane , ibyo ntibigaragaza ko mukiri ab’iyi si , mukaba mwitwaye bya runtu ?
46003004	Iyo umwe avuga ati « Ndi uwa Pawulo » , undi ati « Ndi uwa Apolo » , ubwo se ntimukurikiza amatwara ya runtu ?
46003005	Ngaho nimumbwire : Apolo ni iki ? Pawulo ni iki ? Si abagaragu babagejeje ku kwemera ; buri wese akoresheje ingabire yahawe na Nyagasani !
46003006	Jyewe nateye imbuto , Apolo arayuhira , ariko Imana yonyine ni yo yayikujije .
46003007	Bityo , uwateye nta cyo ari cyo , n’uwuhiye ni uko ; Imana yonyine irihagije , yo itanga gukura .
46003008	Nyir’ukubiba na nyir’ukuhira nta ho bataniye ; buri wese azahabwa igihembo gihwanye n’umurimo yakoze .
46003009	Twembi turi abafasha b’Imana , mwe mukaba umurima wayo n’inzu yiyubakira .
46003010	Ku bw’ingabire nahawe n’Imana , nashije ikibanza nk’umufundi w’umuhanga , undi acyubakamo . Nyamara buri wese yitondere uburyo yubaka .
46003011	Nta kindi kibanza kindi gishobora guhangwa , usibye igisanzwe : Yezu Kristu .
46003012	Niba rero kuri icyo kibanza umuntu yubakishijemo zahabu , feza , amabuye y’agaciro , ibiti , ibyatsi cyangwa ibikenyeri ,
46003013	umurimo wa buri wese uzagaragazwa ku munsi w’urubanza . Ni bwo byose bizasuzumwa n’umuriro , ari wo uzatangaza agaciro k’umurimo wa buri wese .
46003014	Uzaba yarubatse muri icyo kibanza kandi umurimo we ugahonoka , azahembwa .
46003015	Naho nyir’umurimo uzaba wakongotse , azabura igihembo ; gukira we azakira , ariko nk’uwiyatse umuriro .
46003016	Ubwo se ntimuzi ko muri ingoro y’Imana , kandi ko Roho w’Imana abatuyemo ?
46003017	Nihagira rero usenya ingoro y’Imana , Imana na we izamusenya . Kuko ingoro y’Imana ari ntagatifu , kandi iyo ngoro ni mwebwe .
46003018	Ntihakagire uwihenda : niba hari uwikekaho kuba umuhanga ku bw’iyi si , nabanze yihindure umusazi kugira ngo abe umunyabwenge nyakuri ;
46003019	kuko ubuhanga bw’iyi si ari ubusazi mu maso y’Imana , nk’uko byanditswe ngo « Ni Yo ifatira abanyabwenge mu mutego w’uburiganya bwabo » ,
46003020	kandi ngo « Nyagasani acengera ibitekerezo by’abahanga , agasanga byose ari amanjwe . »
46003021	Ku bw’iyo mpamvu rero , ntihakagire ushingira ikuzo rye ku bantu , kuko byose ari ibyanyu :
46003022	yaba Pawulo , yaba Apolo cyangwa Kefasi , yaba isi , bwaba ubugingo cyangwa urupfu , byaba ibiriho cyangwa ibizaza , byose ni ibyanyu ,
46003023	naho mwebwe muri aba Kristu , na We Kristu akaba uw’Imana .
46004001	Buri wese rero natubonemo abagaragu ba Kristu n’abagabuzi b’amabanga y’Imana .
46004002	Kandi icyo abagabuzi batezweho si ikindi kindi atari ukuba indahemuka .
46004003	Jyeweho , sintewe inkeke n’uko mwancira urubanza , cyangwa ko narucirwa n’urukiko rw’abantu , ndetse nanjye ubwanjye sindwicira .
46004004	Nyamara n’ubwo nta kibi niyumva mu mutima , ibyo si byo bingira umwere ; Nyagasani wenyine ni we uncira urubanza .
46004005	Namwe rero ntimugace imanza igihe kitaragera , mutegereze ko Nyagasani azaza , agashyira ahabona ibihishwe mu mwijima , akanatangaza ibyo umutima ubundikiye . Ubwo ni bwo Imana izaha buri wese ishimwe rimukwiye .
46004006	Muri ibyo byose , bavandimwe , nifuje ko tubabera urugero , ari jyewe , ari n’Apolo , kugira ngo mwitoze kutirata murwanirira ishyaka uyu cyangwa uriya .
46004007	Mu by’ukuri , ni iki kigusumbije abandi ? Ni iki utunze , waba utahawe ? Niba se waragihawe , ni iki cyatuma wirata nk’aho utagihawe ?
46004008	Dore muratengamaye ! Dore mwarikungahaje ! Yewe mwabaye abami , twe tutarimo . Ubonye mwakwimitswe , kugira ngo natwe twimikanwe namwe !
46004009	Jye uko mbibona , twebwe intumwa , Imana isa n’iyadushyize inyuma y’abandi , nk’abaciriwe urwo gupfa ; koko rero twahinduwe agashungero k’isi , n’ak’abamalayika n’abantu .
46004010	Twebweho turi abasazi ku mpamvu ya Kristu , naho mwe mukaba abanyabwenge muri Kristu ; twebwe turi abanyantege nke , naho mwe murakomeye ; murubashywe , naho twe turasuzuguritse .
46004011	Kugeza magingo aya , turicwa n’inzara , dufite inyota , twambaye ubusa , turakubitwa , turabuyerezwa ,
46004012	kandi turacogozwa no gukoresha amaboko yacu . Baradutuka tukabifuriza umugisha ; baradutoteza tukihangana ;
46004013	baradusebya twe tugahoza abandi ! Twahinduwe nk’icyavu cy’isi , kugeza na n’ubu batugize ibicibwa mu bantu .
46004014	Ibyo simbyandikiye kubakoza isoni , ahubwo ni ukubaburira nk’abana banjye nkunda .
46004015	N’aho mwagira ibihumbi n’ibihumbi by’abarezi muri Kristu , ababyeyi banyu si benshi , kuko ari jyewe wabibyariye muri Yezu Kristu ku bw’Inkuru Nziza .
46004016	Ndabinginze rero , nimukurikize urugero nabahaye .
46004017	Ni na yo mpamvu mboherereje Timote , umwana wanjye nkunda kandi indahemuka muri Nyagasani ; azabibutsa imibereho yanjye muri Kristu , mbese nk’uko mbyigisha muri za kiliziya zose .
46004018	Bamwe muri mwe bibwiye ko ntazagaruka iwanyu , batangira kwitera hejuru .
46004019	Nyamara , Nyagasani nabishaka , nzabagarukamo vuba , maze aho kwibanda ku magambo y’abo birasi , nzirebere ibikorwa byabo .
46004020	Kuko Ubwami bw’Imana atari amagambo , ahubwo bushingiye ku bikorwa .
46004021	Mbese icyo mwahitamo ni iki ? Ko nabazanamo inkoni , cyangwa se urukundo n’umutima ugwa neza ?
46005001	Inkuru yaramamaye hose y’uko muri mwe hari ubusambanyi , ndetse ubusambanyi bukabije , butaraboneka no mu banyamahanga : baravuga ko umwe muri mwe atunze muka se !
46005002	None mwe muritera hejuru ! Aho kuba mwaragize ishavu , ngo nyir’ugukora ibyo abirukanwemo !
46005003	Jyewe rero , n’ubwo ku bw’amaso mbari kure , ku mutima turi kumwe , nkaba nararangije gucira urubanza uwakoze ayo mahano , nk’aho nahibereye .
46005004	Ngaho rero , nimukoranire mu izina rya Nyagasani Yezu Kristu , maze ku bubasha bwe , nanjye mbashyigikiye ,
46005005	uwo muntu yegurirwe Sekibi ngo ababazwe muri ubu buzima , maze ahazaza azarokoke ku munsi wa Nyagasani .
46005006	Ibyo mwiratana nta byo ! Mbese ntimuzi ko agasemburo gake gatutumbya ifu yose ?
46005007	Nimwiyunyuguzemo rero umusemburo wose ushaje , kugira ngo mubone kuba nk’umugati mushya , udasembuye . Kuko Kristu , ari we Ntama ya Pasika yacu , yishweho igitambo .
46005008	Niduhimbaze rero uwo munsi mukuru , tudakoresheje umusemburo ushaje ari wo w’ubugiranabi n’ubukozi bw’ibibi , ahubwo dukoreshe imigati idasembuye , ari yo ubumanzi n’ukuri .
46005009	Hanyuma kandi , mu ibaruwa mperutse kubandikira , mbihanangiriza kutivanga n’abasambanyi ,
46005010	sinashakaga kuvuga abasambanyi bose iyo bava bakagera , cyangwa se abanyabugugu , abambuzi , n’abasenga ibigirwamana , kuko bibaye ibyo mwagombye kuva kuri iyi si .
46005011	Mu by’ukuri rero , nabandikiye mbabuza kugenderana n’umuntu wiyita umuvandimwe , kandi ari umusambanyi , umunyabugugu , usenga ibigirwamana , usebanya , umusinzi , cyangwa umwambuzi ndetse n’umuntu nk’uwo nguwo ntimukanasangire .
46005012	Mpuriye he no gucira imanza abo tudafitanye isano ? Mwebwe se abo mukemanga si ababarimo rwagati ?
46005013	Abo hanze ni Imana izabacira urubanza . ( Mugenze rero nk’uko byanditswe ngo ) « Nimuvane inkozi z’ibibi muri mwe rwagati . »
46006001	Igihe umwe muri mwe afite icyo apfa n’undi , atinyuka ate kumuregera abadatunganye , aho kumuhanisha mu batagatifujwe ?
46006002	Cyangwa se , ntimuzi ko abatagatifu ari bo bazacira isi urubanza ? Niba rero ari mwe muzacira isi urubanza , mwananirwa mute gukiranura ibyoroheje ?
46006003	Ntimuzi ndetse ko n’abamalayika tuzabacira urubanza , nkanswe rero ibyo muri iki gihe ?
46006004	Niba rero mufite imanza z’ubwo bwoko , kuki mutinyuka kuzegurira abo Kiliziya itizeye ?
46006005	Mbivugiye kubakoza isoni , ubwo koko nta muntu n’umwe muri mwe waba usheshe akanguhe ngo akiranure abavandimwe ?
46006006	Dore umuvandimwe araburanya umuvandimwe , kandi bikabera imbere y’abatemera !
46006007	Ibyo ari byo byose muba mwiyandaritse igihe mukurubana mu nkiko . Kuki mutihanganira kurenganywa ? Kuki mutihanganira ko babahuguza ?
46006008	Nyamara ni mwe murenganya kandi mugahuguza abandi , abo bandi kandi ni abavandimwe banyu !
46006009	Mbese ntimuzi ko abadatunganye batazagira umugabane mu Ngoma y'Imana ? Muramenye ntimwishunge ! Ari abasambanyi , ari abasenga ibigirwamana , ari indaya , ari abararikirana nyamara bahuje ibitsina , ari abakora ingeso mbi bose ,
46006010	kimwe n’abajura , abanyabugugu , abasinzi , abasebanya , abambuzi , abo bose ntibazagira umugabane mu Ngoma y'Imana .
46006011	Nguko uko bamwe muri mwe bari bameze . None , mwarasukuwe , mwaratagatifujwe muba intungane ku bw’izina rya Nyagasani Yezu Kristu , no ku bwa Roho w’Imana yacu .
46006012	( Bamwe muri mwe baravuga bati ) « Byose mbifitiye uburenganzira » ; nyamara byose ntibimfitiye akamaro . « Byose mbifitiye uburenganzira » ; yee ! ariko jye sinzemera ko hagira ikintu na kimwe kinziga .
46006013	Ibiribwa byagenewe inda , inda na yo igenerwa ibiribwa , simbihakana ; nyamara byombi Imana izabisenya . Cyakora umubiri ntiwagenewe gusambana , ni uwa Nyagasani ; Nyagasani akaba ari we uwugenga .
46006014	None rero Imana yazuye Nyagasani , izatuzura natwe ku bw’ububasha bwayo .
46006015	Ntimuzi se ko imibiri yanyu ari ingingo za Kristu ? Hanyuma rero nzafate ingingo za Kristu maze nzigire ingingo z’ihabara ? Ntibikavugwe !
46006016	Ntimuzi se ko usambanye n’ihabara aba abaye umubiri umwe na yo ? Ni ko byanditswe ngo « Bombi bazaba umubiri umwe . »
46006017	Naho uwibumbira kuri Nyagasani , aba agize umutima umwe na we .
46006018	Ubusambanyi nimubugendere kure . Icyaha cyose umuntu akoze , usibye icyo , ntikigera ku mubiri we ; ariko usambana aba acumuriye umubiri we bwite .
46006019	Ubundi se ntimuzi ko umubiri wanyu ari ingoro ya Roho Mutagatifu ubatuyemo , kandi ukomoka ku Mana , maze mukaba nta bubasha mwifiteho ?
46006020	Mwacungujwe igiciro gihambaye ! Nimusingirize rero Imana mu mubiri wanyu .
46007001	Noneho ngeze ku byo mwanyandikiye . Uko mbona , ibyiza ni uko umugabo atakwegera umugore .
46007002	Ariko kugira ngo mwirinde ingeso mbi , buri mugabo nagire umugore we , na buri mugore agire umugabo we .
46007003	Umugabo ntakwiriye kwiyima umugore we , bityo n’umugore ku mugabo we .
46007004	Umugore ntiyigenga ku mubiri we , ugengwa n’umugabo we ; n’umugabo ntiyigenga ku mubiri we , ugengwa n’umugore we .
46007005	Ntihakagire uwiyima undi , keretse mubyumvikanyeho , na bwo by’igihe gito , kugira ngo muhugukire gusenga ; hanyuma musubirane , ngo hato mutananirwa kwigomwa , Sekibi agakurizaho kubashuka .
46007006	Ibyo mbabwiye , ndabibemereye gusa ; simbibategetse .
46007007	Nakwifuza yuko abantu bose bamera nkanjye , ariko buri wese afite ingabire ye bwite yiherewe n’Imana , umwe iye , undi iye .
46007008	Icyo mbwira abatarashaka n’abapfakazi ni uko bakwigumira batyo , kimwe nanjye .
46007009	Nyamara niba badashoboye kwihangana , nibashake ; kuko ikiruta ari ugushyingirwa aho kwicwa n’irari .
46007010	Dore icyo ntegetse abashakanye , atari jyewe ahubwo ni Nyagasani : umugore ntagatandukane n’umugabo we .
46007011	— niba batandukanye , ntakongere gushaka cyangwa yigorore n’umugabo we — n’umugabo ntakirukane umugore we .
46007012	Abandi basigaye mbabwiye ku giti cyanjye , si Nyagasani ubwe ubivuga : niba hari umuvandimwe ufite umugore utaremera Kristu maze akishimira ko babana , ntakamwirukane .
46007013	Niba kandi umugore afite umugabo utaremera , maze akishimira ko babana , ntagatandukane n’uwo umugabo .
46007014	Kuko umugabo utemera atagatifuzwa n’umugore we , kimwe n’uko umugore utemera atagatifuzwa n’umugabo we . Byaba bitabaye ibyo , abana banyu baba babuze ubuntungane , kandi ubundi baratagatifujwe .
46007015	Niba utemera ashatse gutandukana , nabigire ! Icyo gihe umuvandimwe wacu , cyangwa mushiki wacu , aba abohowe , kuko Imana yabahamagariye kubaho mu mahoro .
46007016	Ni ko se , wa mugore we , wabwirwa n’iki ko uzakiza umugabo wawe ? Nawe wa mugabo we , wabwirwa n’iki ko uzakiza umugore wawe ?
46007017	Ubundi rero buri muntu akomeze kubaho nk’uko Nyagasani yabimugeneye , mbese uko yari ari igihe Imana imuhamagaye ; ni yo mabwiriza mpaye za Kiliziya zose .
46007018	Niba hari uwahamagawe yarabanje kugenywa , ntakabihishahishe . Niba kandi hari utagenywe , ntakigenyeshe .
46007019	Ari ukugenywa , cyangwa ukutagenywa , byose nta kavuro ; icya ngombwa ni ugukurikiza amategeko y’Imana .
46007020	Buri wese nagume uko yari ameze igihe ahamagawe .
46007021	Mbese wahamagawe uri umucakara ? Ibyo ntibiguhangayike ; ndetse n’iyo waba wizeye kuzigobotora , ntibikubuze ituze mu bucakara bwawe .
46007022	Kuko uwo Nyagasani yahamagariye mu bucakara , aba ari umwigenge muri Nyagasani . Kimwe n’uko uwahamagawe yigenga , aba ari umugaragu wa Kristu .
46007023	Mwacungujwe igiciro gihambaye ; ntimukisubize mu bucakara bw’abantu .
46007024	Buri wese , bavandimwe , nagume uko yari ameze igihe atowe n’Imana .
46007025	Ku byerekeye ingaragu n’inkumi nta tegeko rya Nyagasani mbafitiye ; ahubwo ndabagira inama y’umuntu wagiriwe impuhwe na Nyagasani kandi ukwiye kwizerwa .
46007026	Ibyiza ni uko baguma uko bameze , kubera ingorane zo muri iki gihe . Rwose ndabona ko ibyiza ari uko umuntu yakwigumira uko ameze .
46007027	Mbese usanganywe umugore ? Witandukana na we . Mbese nta mugore washatse ? Wigira uwo ushaka .
46007028	Nyamara niba umushatse , nta cyaha ukoze ; n’umukobwa aramutse ashyingiwe , nta cyaha aba akoze . Ariko abo ngabo bazahura n’ingorane z’urudaca , ari zo nifuzaga kubarinda .
46007029	Mbibabwire rero , bavandimwe , igihe kirabashirana . Aho bigeze , abafite abagore nibabeho nk’aho batabagize ;
46007030	abarira bamere nk’aho batarira ; abanezerewe bamere nk’aho batanezerewe ; n’abacuruza bamere nk’aho nta cyo batunze ;
46007031	n’abakoresha iby’iyi si ntibagatwarwe na byo , kuko imisusire y’iyi si ihita bwangu .
46007032	Icyo nabifuriza ni ukubaho nta mpagarara . Umuntu utashatse ahihibikanira ibyerekeye Nyagasani , ashaka uko yanyura Imana .
46007033	Naho ufite umugore aharanira iby’isi , ashakashaka uko yanyura umugore we ,
46007034	maze akaba yisatuyemo kabiri . Bityo , n’umugore cyangwa umukobwa batashatse bahihibikanira ibyerekeye Nyagasani , ngo bamutunganire ku mubiri no ku mutima . Naho umugore washatse aharanira iby’isi , ashakashaka uko yashimisha umugabo we .
46007035	Ibyo mbibabwiriye kubafasha , atari umutego mbagushamo , ahubwo ari ukugira ngo mukore ikirushijeho gutungana kandi mwegukire Nyagasani , nta nkomyi .
46007036	Niba umusore asanze ko yaba ahemukiye umukobwa yasabye badashyingiranwe kandi yumva amufitiye irari , nibashyingiranwe uko bisanzwe , kuko ari ko abishaka , kandi nta cyaha kirimo .
46007037	Nyamara niba uwo musore yiyemeje mu mutima we kudashakana n’uwo mukobwa , nta gahato kamuriho , ahubwo abikuye ku bwende bwe , azaba agize neza .
46007038	Bityo , ushyingiwe aba agize neza , ariko udashyingiwe aba arushijeho kugira neza .
46007039	Umugore ahambiriye ku mugabo we igihe cyose akiriho . Nyamara uwo mugabo aramutse apfuye , umugore afite uburenganzira bwo kwishakira undi mugabo yishimiye , ariko wo mu bemera gusa .
46007040	Cyakora uko mbyumva , yarushaho kugubwa neza yigumiye aho ; kandi ndakeka ko nanjye mfite Roho w’Imana .
46008001	Ku byerekeye inyama zatuwe ibigirwamana ni koko : twese tubifitemo ubujijuke ( nk’uko mubivuga ) . Nyamara ubumenyi butera kwirata , naho urukundo rukajijura .
46008002	Niba hari uwibwira ko hari icyo azi , ntarageza aho kumenya uko bikwiye .
46008003	Ariko niba hari ukunda Imana , uwo nguwo azwi n’Imana .
46008004	None se byaba byemewe kurya inyama zatuwe ibigirwamana ? Tuzi ko nta kigirwamana kibaho ku isi , kandi ko nta yindi mana iriho , usibye Imana imwe rukumbi .
46008005	Koko , n’ubwo hariho ibyitwa imana byinshi mu ijuru no ku isi — koko kandi ibigirwamana n’ibikomerezwa ntibibarika ! —
46008006	kuri twe habaho Imana imwe , ari yo Mubyeyi , byose biturukaho , ari na Yo tugana ; hakabaho na Nyagasani umwe , Yezu Kristu , ari We ubeshaho byose , natwe tukabeshwaho na We .
46008007	Ariko bose si ko babifitemo ubujijuke . Hariho bamwe bakiva mu by’ibigirwamana , maze baba bariye inyama zabituwe , umutimanama wabo udakomeye ukabemeza ko bahumanye .
46008008	Mu by’ukuri si ibiribwa bizatugeza ku Mana ; tubiriye , tutabiriye , nta cyo tuzaba duhombye cyangwa twungutse .
46008009	Cyakora mwitondere ubwo burenganzira mubifitemo , ngo hato butagusha abanyantege nke .
46008010	Koko se umunyantege nke aramutse akubonye urira mu ngoro y’ibigirwamana , kandi witwa ko ujijutse , ntiyaboneraho akarya izo nyama zatuwe ibigirwamana , kandi umutima we utabimwemerera ?
46008011	Bityo rero ubujijuke bwawe buzaba bugushije umunyantege nke , kandi ari umuvandimwe Kristu yapfiriye .
46008012	Muri uko gucumurira abavandimwe banyu mubakomeretsa ku mutima usanzwe udakomeye , ubwo ni Kristu muba mucumuriye .
46008013	Kubera iyo mpamvu , niba ibyo kurya bigusha umuvandimwe wanjye , nzazinukwa inyama burundu , aho kugusha umuvandimwe wanjye .
46009001	Mbese jye simfite ubwigenge ? Mbese sindi intumwa ? Mbese jye sinabonye Yezu Umwami wacu ? Mbese si mwe musaruro wanjye muri Nyagasani ?
46009002	Niba ku bandi ntari intumwa , nibura ndi yo kuri mwebwe , kuko ukuri k’ubutumwa Nyagasani yanshinze kubagaragariramo .
46009003	Dore icyo nsubiza abaninura .
46009004	Mbese twebwe ntitwagira uburenganzira bwo guhabwa ibyo kurya no kunywa ?
46009005	Mbese twe ntitwashobora kugendana n’umugore duhuje ukwemera , nk’uko izindi ntumwa , n’abavandimwe ba Nyagasani , na Kefasi babigenza ?
46009006	Cyangwa se tuzabe ari twe twenyine , jyewe na Barinaba , duhatirwa gukorera ibidutunga ?
46009007	Ni iyihe ngabo yagiye ku rugamba , kandi igomba no kwigemurira ? Ni nde wahinga umuzabibu , ntawuryeho imbuto ? Cyangwa se ni nde wakorora ubushyo , maze ntanywe amata yabwo ?
46009008	Ibyo se byaba bishingiye gusa ku matwara y’abantu , cyangwa ahubwo bishyigikiwe n’Amategeko y’Imana ?
46009009	Koko mu Mategeko ya Musa haranditswe ngo « Ntuzahambire umunwa w’ikimasa kivungagura ingano . » Ubwo se Imana yaba koko ishishikajwe n’ibimasa ?
46009010	Ahubwo si twebwe ibivugira ? Ni koko , ibyo ni twebwe byandikiwe ; kuko uhinga wese ahingana icyizere , n’uhura ingano akagira icyizere cyo guhabwa umugabane we .
46009011	Ubwo twababibyemo imbuto z’Imana , murasanga bikabije ko dusarura ku byo mutunze ?
46009012	Niba abandi babafiteho ubwo burenganzira , twe twabuzwa n’iki kububagiriraho ? Nyamara nta bwo twigeze tubwitwaza ! Twihanganiye byose , ngo hato tudatera imbogamizi Inkuru Nziza ya Kristu .
46009013	Ariko se ntimuzi ko abakorera Ingoro y’Imana batungwa n’iyo Ngoro nyine , n’abahereza ku rutambiro , bagahabwa umugabane ku byo batuye ?
46009014	Bityo rero , n’abogeza Inkuru Nziza , Nyagasani yabageneye gutungwa na yo .
46009015	Icyakora nta cyo nigeze nitwaza muri ibyo byose ; kandi simbibandikiye ngo mukurizeho kugira icyo mumpa ; ahubwo nahitamo gupfa , aho gucuzwa iryo shema n’ubonetse wese .
46009016	Kuba naramamaje Inkuru Nziza , si byo byatuma nirata , kuko ari umurimo ngombwa nashinzwe ; ndiyimbire rero niba ntamamaje Inkuru Nziza !
46009017	Yabaye rero nabikoraga ku bwende bwanjye , nari nkwiye kubihemberwa ; ariko ubwo mbitegetswe , ni umuzigo nahawe .
46009018	Ubwo se ishimwe ryanjye rishingiye he ? Rishingiye mu kwamamaza Inkuru Nziza ku buntu , ntarambirije ku burenganzira mpabwa na yo .
46009019	N’ubwo nigenga kuri bose , nahisemo kwigira umugaragu wa bose , kugira ngo nigarurire benshi muri bo .
46009020	Nigize Umuyahudi mu Bayahudi , kugira ngo nshobore gushyikira Abayahudi ; kandi jyewe utakigengwa n’amategeko nemeye kumvira Amategeko nk’abayagenewe , ari ukugira ngo nigarurire abagengwa n’amategeko .
46009021	Kandi jyewe utabuze itegeko ry’Imana ringenga , kuko Kristu ari we ungenga , nigize nk’utagira amategeko , rwagati mu batagira amategeko , ari ukugira ngo mbigarurire na bo .
46009022	Nigize umunyantege nke mu banyantege nke , ngo niyegereze abanyantege nke . Nihwanyije na bose muri byose , kugira ngo ngire abo mbarokoramo .
46009023	Ibyo kandi mbikorera Inkuru Nziza kugira ngo nzayigireho uruhare .
46009024	Ntimuzi se ko abasiganwa ku kibuga cy’imikino biruka bose ariko igihembo kikegukana umwe ? Ngaho rero nimwiruke namwe kugira ngo mwese mugitsindire .
46009025	Urushanwa wese yigomwa byinshi , kandi aba aharanira ikamba rizayoka ; naho twebwe iryo duharanira , ntirizashira .
46009026	Nguko rero uko jye niruka , sinkora hirya no hino ; nguko kandi uko ndwana , sinigera mpusha .
46009027	Ahubwo umubiri wanjye ndawuhana nkawukandamiza kugira ngo ntazavaho mpigikwa , maze kwamamaza Inkuru Nziza mu bandi .
46010001	Bavandimwe , sinshaka ko muyoberwa ukuntu abasekuruza bacu bose bagendaga bayobowe n’igihu cyererana , bose bakambuka inyanja ,
46010002	bose bakabatirizwa muri cya gihu na ya nyanja , bifatanyije na Musa .
46010003	Bose basangiye ibyo kurya bimwe bikomoka mu ijuru ;
46010004	kandi bose bashoka iriba rimwe rikomoka mu ijuru ; nuko bakanywa amazi avubuka mu rutare bahawe n’Imana , rukagenda rubaherekeje , kandi urwo rutare rwarangaga Kristu .
46010005	Nyamara benshi muri bo si ko banyuze Imana , ni yo mpamvu intumbi zabo zararitswe mu butayu .
46010006	Ibyo byose byabereye kuducira amarenga , kugira ngo tutararikira ikibi , nk’uko na bo bakirarikiye .
46010007	Ntimugasenge ibigirwamana , nk’uko bamwe muri bo babigize , mbese nk’uko byanditswe ngo « Nuko imbaga iricara , bararya , baranywa , nyuma barahaguruka , barabyina » .
46010008	Twirinde gusambana , nk’uko bamwe muri bo babikoze , maze bagapfamo abageze ku bihumbi makumyabiri na bitatu umunsi umwe .
46010009	Twirinde no kwinja Nyagasani , nk’uko bamwe muri bo bamugerageje , maze batsembwa n’inzoka z’ubumara .
46010010	Ntimukitotombe , nk’uko bamwe muri bo binubye , maze Umunyacyorezo akaboreka .
46010011	Ibyababayeho biraducira amarenga , kandi byandikiwe kutuburira , twe twegereje amagingo ya nyuma .
46010012	Bityo rero uwibwira ko ahagaze , aritonde atagwa .
46010013	Nta bwo mwigeze muterwa n’ibishuko bibarenze . Imana ni indahemuka ; ntiyakwemera ko mushukwa birenze imbaraga zanyu ; ahubwo izabaha uburyo bwo kwivana mu bishuko n’imbaraga zo kubyihanganira .
46010014	Kubera iyo mpamvu rero , nkoramutima zanjye , nimwirinde gusenga ibigirwamana .
46010015	Reka mbabwire nk’abaciye akenge , namwe ubwanyu mwirebere ukuri kw’ibyo mvuga .
46010016	Mbese inkongoro y’umugisha tunyweraho dushimira Imana , si ugusangira amaraso ya Kristu ? N’umugati tumanyurira hamwe , si ugusangira Umubiri wa Kristu ?
46010017	Kubera uwo mugati umwe , n’ubwo twebwe turi benshi , tugize umubiri umwe , kuko twese nyine duhujwe n’umugati umwe .
46010018	Nimurebere ku rubyaro rwa Israheli : mbese abarya ku bitambo byatuwe ntibaba bunze ubumwe n’urutambiro ?
46010019	Mbese mvuge ngo iki ? Ko inyama zatuwe ibigirwamana , hari icyo zivuze ? Cyangwa se ko ikigirwamana hari icyo kimaze ?
46010020	Ashwi da ! Kuko ibyo bitambo byabo , atari Imana babitura , ahubwo biturwa Sekibi , kandi sinshaka ko mugirana ubusabane na we .
46010021	Ntimushobora kunywera icyarimwe ku nkongoro ya Nyagasani no ku nkongoro ya Sekibi ; ntimushobora kubangikanya ameza ya Nyagasani n’aya Sekibi .
46010022	Cyangwa se twaba dushaka kwikururira ishyari ry ’ Imana ? Twaba se tuyirusha amaboko ?
46010023	« Byose tubifitiye uburenganzira ! » ( nk’uko bamwe babivuga ) , nyamara byose ntibidufitiye akamaro ; « Byose tubifitiye uburenganzira » , ariko byose si ko bitera inkunga .
46010024	Ntihakagire uwikurikiranira inyungu ye bwite , ahubwo aharanire iy’abandi .
46010025	Nimwirire rero ibigurirwa ku isoko byose , mutiriwe musiganuza aho biturutse ngo bibakure umutima ,
46010026	« kuko isi yose ari iy’Imana , n’ibiyiriho byose . »
46010027	Niba kandi uwo mudasangiye ukwemera aramutse agutumiye , irire ibyo akuzimaniye byose , utiriwe usiganuza ngo bigukure umutima .
46010028	Ariko hagize ukubwira ati « Izi nyama zatuwe ibigirwamana » , ntuziryeho ubigiriye uwakuburiye ngo utamutera guhagarika umutima ;
46010029	umutima mvuga rero si uwawe , ahubwo ni umutimanama w’undi . Kuki ubwigenge bwanjye bwaba bushingiye ku mutimanama w’undi ?
46010030	Niba ngize icyo ndya nshimira Imana , kuki hagira ungayira ibyo nakurijeho gushimira ?
46010031	Ari igihe rero murya , ari n’igihe munywa , icyo mukoze cyose , mujye mugikorera guhesha Nyagasani ikuzo .
46010032	Ntimukagire uwo mutera imbogamizi , yaba Umuyahudi , yaba Umugereki , yaba uwo mu Kiliziya y’Imana .
46010033	Nguko uko nanjye ngerageza gushimisha bose muri byose , ntaharanira inyungu yanjye bwite , ahubwo ifitiye abenshi akamaro ngo bakurizeho gukira .
46011001	Nimube rero abakurikiza banjye , nk’uko nanjye nkurikiza Kristu .
46011002	Ndabashimira ko muhora munyibuka , kandi mu budahemuka mukikomezamo ibyo nababwirije byose .
46011003	Nyamara dore icyo mukwiye kumenya : Kristu ni we mugenga wa buri mugabo , umugore na we akagengwa n’umugabo ; na we Kristu akagengwa n’Imana .
46011004	Umugabo wese usenga cyangwa uhanura yitwikiriye umutwe , aba asuzuguye umutegetsi we .
46011005	Naho umugore wese usenga cyangwa uhanura atitwikiriye umutwe , aba asuzuguye umutegetsi we ; mbese ni nk’aho yaba yimojeho umusatsi .
46011006	Niba rero umugore adateze igitambaro , n’imisatsi yose nayimareho ! Nasanga ariko bimuteye isoni kwimoza cyangwa kwikemuza , natege igitambaro !
46011007	Umugabo we ntagomba kwipfuka mu mutwe , kuko ari ishusho n’uburanga bw’Imana ; naho umugore akaba ikuzo ry’umugabo we .
46011008	N’ubundi umugabo si we wakomotse ku mugore , ahubwo umugore ni we wakomotse ku mugabo .
46011009	Kandi umugabo koko si we waremewe umugore , ahubwo umugore ni we waremewe umugabo .
46011010	Ngiyo impamvu umugore agomba kwambara ku mutwe ikimenyetso cy’uko agengwa , mbese abigiriye n’abamalayika .
46011011	Nyamara muri Nyagasani umugabo wese agizwe n’umugore , n’umugore agizwe n’umugabo we .
46011012	N’ubwo umugore yavuye ku mugabo , umugabo na we akabyarwa n’umugore , bombi baturuka ku Mana .
46011013	Ngaho namwe nimumbwire : bishoboka bite ko umugore asenga Imana atitwikiriye umutwe ?
46011014	N’ubusanzwe biteye isoni ko umugabo atendeza imisatsi ,
46011015	nyamara ni ishema ry’umugore ko ayitunga atyo , bikurikije kamere yabo bombi , kuko umugore yayiherewe kumutwikira .
46011016	Ahasigaye ushaka guhariranya , amenye ko atari umuco wacu , si n’uwa Kiliziya z’Imana .
46011017	Tuvuye muri ibyo hari n’ibindi ntabashimaho : amakoraniro yanyu , aho kubagirira akamaro , abagwa nabi .
46011018	Icya mbere cyo , bambwiye ko , iyo muhuriye mu ikoraniro , mwiremamo ibice kandi bisa n’aho ari byo :
46011019	wagira ngo ni ngombwa ko muri mwe habamo amakimbirane , kugira ngo ababakomeyemo bigaragaze .
46011020	Igihe rero muteraniye hamwe , ntimuhuzwa n’isangira rya Nyagasani ,
46011021	kuko buri wese amaranira kurya ibyo yizaniye , ku buryo umwe yicwa n’inzara , undi yasinze .
46011022	Mbese nta mazu mugira yo kuriramo no kunyweramo ? Cyangwa muzanwa no gusuzugura imbaga y’Imana , no gukoza isoni abatagira icyo bafite ? Mbabwire iki se ? Mbashime se ? Oya , muri ibyo simbashimye .
46011023	Jyewe rero dore ibyo nashyikirijwe na Nyagasani , bikaba ari byo nabagejejeho : Nyagasani Yezu , araye ari butangwe , yafashe umugati ,
46011024	amaze gushimira , arawumanyura , avuga ati « Iki ni umubiri wanjye ubatangiwe ; mujye mubikora namwe bibe urwibutso rwanjye . »
46011025	Barangije kurya , n’inkongoro ayigenzereza atyo , avuga ati « Iyi ni inkongoro y’Isezerano rishya , rishingiye ku maraso yanjye ; mujye mubikora namwe , kandi igihe cyose muyinywereyeho , bibe urwibutso rwanjye . »
46011026	Kuko igihe cyose murya uyu mugati , mukanywa no kuri iyi nkongoro , muba mwamamaza urupfu rwa Nyagasani , kugeza igihe azazira .
46011027	Ni cyo gituma uzarya uyu mugati , akanywa no kuri iyi nkongoro ya Nyagasani , atabikwiye , azaba acumuriye umubiri n’amaraso bya Nyagasani .
46011028	Buri wese nabanze yisuzume rero , maze abone kurya uwo mugati no kunywa kuri iyo nkongoro ;
46011029	kuko uwarya cyangwa akanywa atubahirije umubiri wa Nyagasani , aba ariye kandi anyoye ikizamubyarira ubucibwe .
46011030	Ni cyo gituma benshi muri mwe barwaye kandi bamugaye , ndetse bamwe bakaba barapfuye .
46011031	Iyaba twabanzaga kwisuzuma ubwacu , nta rundi rubanza twacirwa .
46011032	Ariko Nyagasani adutonganyiriza kutugorora , kugira ngo tutarohamana n’iyi si .
46011033	Bityo rero , bavandimwe , igihe muhuriye gusangira , nimurindirane .
46011034	Niba hari ushonje , nabanze ahembukire iwe , kugira ngo ikoraniro ryanyu ritababyarira ubucibwe . Ibisigaye nzabitunganya , igihe nzaba naje .
46012001	Bavandimwe , sinshaka ko muba injiji mu byerekeye ingabire za Roho .
46012002	Mwibuke ko igihe mwari mutarayoboka Imana , mwagendaga mutwawe n’ibigirwamana bijunjamye .
46012003	Ni yo mpamvu mbamenyesha ko nta we ubwirizwa na Roho w’Imana , ngo agire ati « Yezu arakaba ikivume » , nk’uko nta wavuga ngo « Yezu ni Nyagasani » , atabibwirijwe na Roho Mutagatifu .
46012004	Ingabire ziranyuranye , ariko Roho ni umwe ;
46012005	muri Kiliziya kwitangira abandi biri kwinshi , ariko Nyagasani ni umwe ;
46012006	uburyo bwo gukora buri kwinshi , ariko Imana ni Yo itunganya byose muri bose .
46012007	Koko rero , buri wese ahabwa kugaragaza ibyo Roho w’Imana amukoreramo , ngo bigirire akamaro bose .
46012008	Ku bwa Roho , umwe ahabwa kuvuga amagambo yuje ubushishozi , undi agahabwa kuvugana ubumenyi , muri uwo Roho nyine ;
46012009	umwe ahabwa ukwemera guhebuje abikesha uwo Roho , undi agahabwa ingabire yo gukiza abarwayi na none muri uwo Roho nyine ;
46012010	umwe yegurirwa ububasha bwo gukora ibitangaza , undi akagabirwa guhanura ; umwe ahabwa kurobanura ibiturutse ku Mana n’ibiyitambamiye , undi agahabwa kuvuga mu ndimi nyinshi , hakaba n’uhabwa kuzisobanura .
46012011	Ariko ibyo byose bikorwa na Roho umwe rukumbi , ugabira buri wese uko abyishakiye .
46012012	Mu by’ukuri umubiri ni umwe , kandi ugizwe n’ingingo nyinshi ; ariko izo ngingo zose , n’ubwo ari nyinshi , zigize umubiri umwe : ni ko bimeze no muri Kristu .
46012013	Twese twabatirijwe muri Roho umwe , ngo tube umubiri umwe . Twaba Abayahudi cyangwa Abagereki , twaba abacakara cyangwa abigenga , twese twuhiwe Roho umwe .
46012014	Koko rero umubiri ntugizwe n’urugingo rumwe gusa , ahubwo ugizwe na nyinshi .
46012015	Niba ikirenge kivuze kiti « Ubwo ntari ikiganza , nta ho mpuriye n’umubiri » , byakibuza kuba urugingo rw’umubiri ?
46012016	Niba ugutwi kuvuze kuti « Ubwo ntari ijisho , nta ho mpuriye n’umubiri » , byakubuza kuba urugingo rw’umubiri ?
46012017	Niba umubiri wose ubaye ijisho , kumva byaherera he ? Niba byose bibaye ugutwi , uguhumurirwa kwaherera he ?
46012018	Noneho rero Imana yagennye umwanya wa buri rugingo mu mubiri uko yabyishakiye .
46012019	Yabaye byose byarabaye urugingo rumwe , umubiri wari kuba he ?
46012020	Ingingo rero ni nyinshi , ariko umubiri ukaba umwe .
46012021	Ijisho ntirishobora kubwira ikiganza ngo « Singukeneye » , n’umutwe ngo ubwire ibirenge uti « Simbakeneye » .
46012022	Byongeye kandi n’ingingo zisa nk’aho ari nta ntege , na zo ziba ngombwa ,
46012023	ndetse n’izo dukeka ko zisuzuguritse , ni zo twubaha cyane , maze izirusha izindi gutera isoni , tukarushaho kuzubahiriza .
46012024	Naho ingingo zacu zisanzwe ntizijya ziduhangayika . Cyakora Imana yateye umubiri ku buryo buha icyubahiro ingingo zari zitacyifitemo ,
46012025	ari ukugira ngo umubiri utibyaramo amakimbirane , ahubwo ingingo zose zibe magirirane .
46012026	Niba hari urugingo rubabaye , izindi zose zisangira ako kababaro ; niba hari urugingo rumerewe neza , izindi na zo zirishima .
46012027	Namwe rero muri umubiri umwe ari wo Kristu , kandi mukaba ingingo ze , buri muntu ku giti cye .
46012028	Bityo rero , abo Imana yashyizeho muri Kiliziya , aba mbere ni intumwa , aba kabiri ni abahanuzi , aba gatatu ni abigisha . Hanyuma ikurikizaho abakora ibitangaza ; abafite ingabire yo gukiza abarwayi , iyo gutabarana , iyo kuyobora n’iyo kuvuga mu ndimi .
46012029	Mbese bose ni intumwa ? Bose se ni abahanuzi ? Cyangwa ni abigisha ? Mbese bose bakora ibitangaza ?
46012030	Cyangwa bafite ingabire yo gukiza ? Bose se bavuga mu ndimi ? Cyangwa bose bazi kuzisobanura ?
46012031	Nimuharanire ingabire zisumbuye , kandi ngiye kubereka izitambutse zose .
46013001	N’aho navuga indimi z’abantu n’iz’abamalayika , ariko singire urukundo , naba ndi nk’icyuma kibomborana cyangwa inzogera irangira .
46013002	N’aho nagira ingabire y’ubuhanuzi , ngahishurirwa amayobera yose n’ubumenyi bwose ; n’aho nagira ukwemera guhambaye , kumwe gushyigura imisozi , ariko ndafite urukundo , nta cyo mba ndi cyo .
46013003	N’aho nagabiza abakene ibyo ntunze byose , n’aho nahara umubiri wanjye ngo utwikwe , ariko nta rukundo mfite , nta cyo byaba bimariye .
46013004	Urukundo rurihangana , rwitangira abandi , ntirugira ishyari ; urukundo ntirwirarira , ntirwikuririza ;
46013005	nta cyo rukora kidahwitse , ntirurondera akari akarwo , ntirurakara , ntirugira inzika ;
46013006	ntirwishimira akarengane , ahubwo ruhimbazwa n’ukuri .
46013007	Urukundo rubabarira byose , rwemera byose , rwizera byose , rukihanganira byose .
46013008	Urukundo ntiruteze gushira . Ubuhanuzi se ? Buzashira . Indimi zo se ? Zizaceceka . Ubumenyi se ? Buzayoka .
46013009	Koko ubumenyi bwacu buracagase , kimwe n’uko ubuhanuzi bwacu bucagase .
46013010	Igihe rero ibyuzuye bizahinguka , iby’igicagate bizazimira !
46013011	Mu gihe nari umwana , navugaga ay’abana , ngatekereza nk’abana , nkazirikana nk’abana ; aho mbereye umugabo , nikuyemo ibya rwana byose .
46013012	Ubu ngubu turasa n’abarebera mu ndorerwamo , ku buryo budafututse , ariko hari igihe tuzarebana imbonankubone . Ubu ngubu ibyo nzi biracagase , ariko icyo gihe nzamenya nk’uko nzwi .
46013013	Kugeza ubu , ukwemera , ukwizera n’urukundo uko ari bitatu , birabangikanye ; ariko icy’ingenzi muri byo ni urukundo .
46014001	Ngaho rero nimukurikirane urukundo , kandi muharanire ingabire za Roho , cyane cyane iy’ubuhanuzi .
46014002	Kuko uvuga mu ndimi aba atabwira abantu , ahubwo Imana ; koko kandi nta we uba amwumva ; aba avuga ibimuri mu mutima ariko by’amayobera .
46014003	Nyamara uhanura we , aba abwira abantu , akabakomeza , akabashishikaza , akabahumuriza .
46014004	Uvuga mu ndimi ni we ubwe wiyungura , naho uhanura aba agiriye akamaro ikoraniro ry’abavandimwe .
46014005	Nakwifuza ko mwese muvuga mu ndimi , ariko icyo nahitamo ni uko mwahanura . Uhanura asumbye uvuga mu ndimi , keretse rero nyirukuzivuga ashoboye no kuzisobanura , bigakomeza ikoraniro .
46014006	Tuvuge nk’ubu , bavandimwe , nje iwanyu nkivugira mu ndimi , naba mbamariye iki , ijambo ryanjye ritagize icyo ribahishurira , mu bumenyi , mu buhanuzi , cyangwa mu nyigisho ?
46014007	Ni kimwe n’ibyo bacurangisha , nk’umwirongi cyangwa inanga ; bibaye bidasobanuye amajwi yabyo , watandukanya ute imicurangire y’umwirongi n’iy’inanga ?
46014008	Akarumbeti kataranguruye ijwi , ni nde wakwitegura kujya ku rugamba ?
46014009	Namwe rero : niba indimi zanyu zidasobanura amagambo , ibyo muvuga bizumvikana bite ? Mwaba mucurangira abahetsi .
46014010	Amagambo akoreshwa ku isi ni menshi , kandi nta n’ijambo na rimwe ridafite icyo risobanura .
46014011	Habaye rero umbwira amagambo ntumva , naba mubereye nk’umunyamahanga , na we kandi akambera umunyamahanga .
46014012	Namwe rero nimuharanire ingabire za Roho , ndetse muzikenukeho cyane , ariko murarikiye gukomeza ikoraniro .
46014013	Ni yo mpamvu uvuga mu ndimi akwiye no gusaba Imana ingabire y’ubusobanuzi .
46014014	Kuko iyo nsenga mu ndimi , umutima wanjye uba usenga , ariko ubwenge bwanjye nta cyo buhungukira .
46014015	Bigende bite rero ? Nzasengera mu mutima , ariko n’ubwenge bwanjye bushyireho akabwo . Nzaririmbira mu mutima , ariko n’ubwenge bushyireho akabwo .
46014016	Naho ubundi niba ushimiye Imana mu mutima gusa , uri kumwe n’umuntu utabisobanukiwemo , yasubiza ate « Amen » kuri uko gushimira kwawe , kandi atumva icyo uvuga ?
46014017	Ugushimira kwawe yego ni kwiza , ariko nta cyo kumariye uwo nguwo .
46014018	Nanjye ubwanjye mvuga mu ndimi , ndetse mbibarusha mwese — Imana ishimwe —
46014019	ariko iyo ndi mu ikoraniro mpitamo kuvuga amagambo make cyane yumvikana , afitiye abandi akamaro , aho gusukiranya menshi mu ndimi .
46014020	Bavandimwe , mu byo gushishoza ntimukigire nk’abana ; mu byo gukora nabi ho , nimube abana koko , ariko mu byo gushishoza , mugenze nk’abantu bakuze .
46014021	Mu Mategeko haranditse ngo « Uyu muryango nzawubwiza izindi ndimi mu munwa w’abanyamahanga , ariko na bwo ntibazanyumva , uwo ari Nyagasani ubivuga . »
46014022	Nuko rero kuvuga mu ndimi si ikimenyetso kigenewe abemera , ahubwo kireba abatemera ; naho ubuhanuzi bwo si ikimenyetso kireba abataremera ; ahubwo kigenewe abemera .
46014023	Tuvuge nk’igihe Kiliziya yose ikoranye , maze mwese mukavuga mu ndimi , nyuma hakinjira uwo tudasangiye ukwemera cyangwa udasobanukiwe mu byacu , ntiyakurikizaho kubita abasazi ?
46014024	Ibiri amambu , hagize usanga mwese muhanura , yaba uwo tudasangiye ukwemera cyangwa udasobanukiwe mu byacu , azumva bose bamuhurijeho ijambo rimutera kwisuzuma no kwicuza ,
46014025	nuko ibyari byihishe mu mutima we bigaragare ; maze agwe yubitse uruhanga , aramye Imana , yemeza ko Imana muri kumwe koko .
46014026	Turangirize ku ki rero , bavandimwe ? Igihe mukoraniye hamwe , umwe ashobora gutera indirimbo , undi akigisha , undi agatangaza ibyo yahishuriwe , undi akavuga mu ndimi , undi akazisobanura ; ibyo byose kandi bikagirirwa akamaro rusange .
46014027	Niba hari abavuga mu ndimi , babe babiri cyangwa batatu gusa , kandi bavuge umwe umwe , ndetse habe n’uzisobanura .
46014028	Niba nta musobanuzi uhari , babyihorere ; aho kuvuga mu ndimi , muzirikane mu mutima gusa kandi mubwira Imana .
46014029	Abahanuzi na bo , havuge babiri cyangwa batatu , maze abandi basuzume ibyo bavuga .
46014030	Hagize uwo mu ikoraniro ugize atya agahishurirwa ikintu , uwavugaga ahite aceceka .
46014031	Mwese mushobora guhanura , ariko mugahana umwanya kugira ngo buri wese abonereho kujijuka no gushishikazwa .
46014032	Umuhanuzi wese agenga ingabire yahawe .
46014033	Kuko Imana yacu atari iy’akajagari , ahubwo ni iy’amahoro .
46014034	Nk’uko bimeze muri za Kiliziya zose z’abatagatifujwe , abagore bajye baceceka mu makoraniro ; ntibemerewe kuhafatira ijambo , ahubwo bajye batuza nk’uko Amategeko ubwayo abivuga .
46014035	Niba hari icyo bifuza kujijukirwaho , bajye basobanuza abagabo babo mu rugo . Kuko bidakwiye ko umugore avugira mu ruhame .
46014036	Mbese mwibwira ko Ijambo ry’Imana rikomoka iwanyu ? Cyangwa se ko ari mwe mwenyine ryashyikirijwe ?
46014037	Niba hari uwikekaho ubuhanuzi , cyangwa ko ahishurirwa na Roho , amenyereho ko ibyo mbandikiye ari itegeko rya Nyagasani .
46014038	Niba atabizi , ni uko na we Imana itamuzi !
46014039	Nuko rero , bavandimwe , nimuharanire ingabire y’ubuhanuzi , kandi ntimukange ko bavuga mu ndimi .
46014040	Ariko byose bikorwe neza nk’uko bikwiye .
46015001	Bavandimwe , ndabibutsa Inkuru Nziza nabagejejeho , ari yo mwakiriye kandi mukaba muyihambiriyeho ,
46015002	ikaba ari na yo izabakiza niba muyikomeyeho nk’uko nayibigishije ; naho ubundi ukwemera kwanyu kwaba ari impfabusa .
46015003	Koko rero icya mbere cyo nabagejejeho , ni icyo nanjye nashyikirijwe : ko Kristu yapfuye azize ibyaha byacu , nk’uko byari byaranditswe .
46015004	Ko yahambwe , ko yazutse ku munsi wa gatatu , nk’uko byari byaranditswe .
46015005	Ko yabonekeye Kefasi , hanyuma akabonwa na ba Cumi na babiri .
46015006	Hanyuma yongeye kubonwa n’abavandimwe magana atanu icya rimwe ; abenshi muri bo baracyariho , abandi barapfuye .
46015007	Hanyuma yabonekeye Yakobo , nyuma abonekera intumwa zose icyarimwe .
46015008	Ubw’imperuka , nanjye arambonekera , jye umeze nk’uwavutse imburagihe .
46015009	Koko jyewe ndi uwa nyuma mu ntumwa zose ; sinkwiriye no kwitwa intumwa , kuko natoteje Kiliziya y’Imana .
46015010	Ariko uko ndi kose , mbikesha ingabire y’Imana , kandi iyo ngabire ntiyambayemo impfabusa . Ahubwo ndetse nakoreye kubarusha bose ; nyamara si ku bwanjye , ni ku bw’ingabire y’Imana indimo .
46015011	Uko biri kose , yaba jye , cyangwa bo , ngibyo ibyo twamamaza , kandi ari na byo mwemeye .
46015012	Ubwo hamamazwa ko Kristu yazutse mu bapfuye , bishoboka bite ko bamwe muri mwe bavuga ko abapfuye batazazuka ?
46015013	Niba abapfuye batazazuka , Kristu na we ubwo ntiyazutse .
46015014	Niba kandi Kristu atarazutse , ibyo twigisha nta shingiro , n’ukwemera kwanyu gufashe ku busa .
46015015	Bikaba ndetse twaba abahamyabinyoma b’Imana , kuko twemeje ko yazuye Kristu , kandi itaramuzuye , niba ari byo ko abapfuye batazuka .
46015016	Koko niba abapfuye batazuka , na Kristu ubwo ntiyazutse .
46015017	Kandi niba Kristu atarazutse , ukwemera kwanyu ni amanjwe , mukaba mukiri mu byaha byanyu .
46015018	Bityo rero , n’abapfuye bizeye Kristu barayoyotse .
46015019	Niba kwizera Kristu kwacu guhagarariye kuri ubu bugingo gusa , twaba dukwiye kubabarirwa bitambukije abandi bose .
46015020	Oya kandi , Kristu yazutse koko mu bapfuye , aba umuzukambere mu bapfuye bose .
46015021	Nk’uko kandi urupfu rwakuruwe n’umuntu umwe , ni na ko izuka ry’abapfuye ryazanywe n’umuntu umwe .
46015022	Kimwe n’uko bose boramye bitewe na Adamu , ni na ko bose bazasubizwa ubugingo biturutse kuri Kristu ;
46015023	nyamara buri wese mu rwego rwe : uw’ibanze ni Kristu , nyuma hateho abamuyobotse , igihe azazira .
46015024	Nuko byose bizarangire , igihe azegurira Ubwami Imana se , amaze gusenyagura icyitwa ubuhangange , ubutegetsi n’ububasha cyose .
46015025	Kuko agomba kwima ingoma kugeza ko azashyira abanzi be bose mu nsi y’ibirenge bye .
46015026	Umwanzi w’imperuka uzarimburwa , ni urupfu ,
46015027	kuko byanditswe ngo « byose yabishyize mu nsi y’ibirenge bye . » Igihe rero Kristu azavuga ati « Byose biranyeguriwe » , birumvikana ko hatabariwemo Uwabimweguriye byose .
46015028	Nuko rero igihe byose bizaba bimaze kumuyoboka , ubwo Mwana na we aziyegurire Se wamweguriye byose , kugira ngo Imana ibe byose muri bose .
46015029	Bitabaye ibyo , ababatirizwa abapfuye baba bashaka kugera ku ki ? Niba koko abapfuye batazuka , ni iki gituma bababatirizwa ?
46015030	Natwe ubwacu kuki twahora twishyira mu makuba ?
46015031	Buri munsi ruhora rungera amajanja ! Simbeshya , bavandimwe , mwe kuzo ryanjye muri Kristu Yezu Umwami wacu .
46015032	Biba byaramariye iki kurwanya inyamaswa zo muri Efezi , iyo nza kuba niringiye ubu bugingo gusa ? Niba abapfuye batazuka nimwemere koko « twirire kandi twinywere , kuko ejo tuzapfa ! »
46015033	Ntimukishuke : kubana n’ababi byonona imigenzo myiza .
46015034	Nimwice ku businzi burundu , mwirinde gucumura . Kuko muri mwe harimo abatazi Imana na busa , ibyo mbivugiye kubakoza isoni .
46015035	Ubwo ntihabuze uwibaza ati « Abapfuye bazazuka bate ? Bazahingukana umubiri uteye ute ? »
46015036	Mbega injiji ! Ese icyo ubibye ntikibanza gushanguka ngo kibyare ubuzima !
46015037	Kandi icyo ubibye gitandukanye n’urubuto ruzaza ; ni akabuto gasa k’ingano cyangwa k’ikindi kindi .
46015038	Nyuma Imana ikakihera imisusire uko ishaka , buri rubuto ku buryo bwihariye .
46015039	Nta kinyabuzima gihuje kamere n’ikindi : abantu batandukanye n’inyamaswa , n’inyoni , n’amafi .
46015040	Hari ibyagenewe kuba mu kirere , n’ibyagenewe kuba ku isi ; ariko byose ntibinganya umucyo .
46015041	Ububengerane bw’izuba butandukanye n’ubw’ukwezi , n’ubw’inyenyeri ; ndetse nta n’inyenyeri ishashagira nk’indi .
46015042	Ni na ko bimeze mu kuzuka kw’abapfuye : umubiri ujyira mu gitaka gushanguka , ukazukira mu budashanguka ;
46015043	ushyirwa mu gitaka ari nta kamaro , ukazukana ikuzo ; ushyirwa mu gitaka ari nta ntege , ukazukana ibakwe ;
46015044	hahambwa umubiri usanzwe wa muntu , hakazuka umubiri wahinduwe na Roho . Ubwo koko habaho imibiri ya kamere gusa , hashobora no kubaho n’imibiri yahinduwe na Roho .
46015045	Ni na ko byanditswe ngo : Muntu wa mbere , Adamu , yagabiwe ubuzima bw’umubiri , ariko Adamu wa kabiri , ugizwe na Roho , atanga ubuzima .
46015046	Cyakora habanza ubuzima bw’umubiri , hagakurikiraho ubuzima bwa Roho .
46015047	Muntu wa mbere wavuye mu gitaka ni umunyagitaka ; Muntu wa kabiri , we , aturuka mu ijuru .
46015048	Uko umunyagitaka yabaye , ni na ko abanyagitaka bameze ; uko uwaturutse mu ijuru ameze , ni na ko abagenewe ijuru bazaba .
46015049	Nk’uko twabayeho mu misusire ya Muntu w’umunyagitaka , ni na ko kandi tuzagira imisusire y’Uwaturutse mu ijuru .
46015050	Icyo nemeza cyo , bavandimwe , ni uko muntu , ku bw’umubiri n’amaraso , adashobora kwironkera umugabane mu Ngoma y’Imana , kimwe n’uko ubushanguke butakwigeza ku budashanguka .
46015051	Ngiye noneho kubahishurira ibanga . Twese ntituzapfa ; ahubwo twese tuzahindurwa ukundi ,
46015052	mu kanya gato , nk’uhumbije ijisho , akarumbeti k’imperuka kavuze . Koko akarumbeti kazavuga maze abapfuye bazukire kudashanguka , nuko natwe duhindurwe ukundi .
46015053	Ni ngombwa ariko ko uyu mubiri wagenewe kubora ugezwa ku budashanguka , kandi uyu mubiri wagenewe gupfa ukagabirwa ukutazapfa .
46015054	Igihe rero uyu mubiri ugenewe kubora uzagezwa ku budashanguka , kandi uyu mubiri ugenewe gupfa ukagabirwa ukutazapfa , ubwo ngubwo ibyanditswe bizaba byujujwe ngo « Urupfu rwaburijwemo n’umutsindo .
46015055	Rupfu we ! Ugutsinda kwawe kuri he ? Urubori rwawe ruri hehe , wa Rupfu we ? »
46015056	Koko rero urubori rw’urupfu ni icyaha , naho ububasha bw’icyaha buturuka ku mategeko .
46015057	Dushimire Imana yaduhaye gutsinda ku bw’Umwami wacu Yezu Kristu .
46015058	Nuko rero , bavandimwe nkunda , nimukomere , mwe guhungabana , mukomeze gukorera Nyagasani , muzi neza ko kuruhira Nyagasani bitazabapfira ubusa .
46016001	Ku byerekeye imfashanyo zigenewe abatagatifujwe , muzakurikize namwe amabwiriza nahaye Kiliziya zo mu Bugalati .
46016002	Ku munsi wa mbere ukurikira isabato , ari ho ku cyumweru , buri wese ajye azigama icyo yashoboye gusagura , ku buryo mutazarindira igihe nzazira ngo mwegeranye amaturo .
46016003	Ubwo ningera iwanyu nzohereza abo muzaba mwihitiyemo , bajyane amabaruwa n’amaturo yanyu i Yeruzalemu .
46016004	Nibiba ngombwa ko nanjye njyayo , tuzafatanya urugendo .
46016005	Nzaza iwanyu maze kwambukiranya Masedoniya , kuko nzayinyuramo gusa .
46016006	Birashoboka ko nzatinda iwanyu , ndetse nkahaguma itumba ryose , kugira ngo munshakire uburyo bwo gukomeza urugendo rwanjye .
46016007	Sinshaka noneho kubakubita urubandu , ahubwo nizeye kuzagumana namwe umwanya uringaniye , Nyagasani nabinyemerera .
46016008	Icyakora nzaguma Efezi kugeza kuri Pentekositi ,
46016009	kuko umurimo wanjye wahugururiwe amarembo magari , n’ubwo hari abantambamiye benshi .
46016010	Niba Timote aramutse aje iwanyu , muramenye ntazagire icyo abishishaho , kuko dufatanyije gukorera Nyagasani .
46016011	Ntihazagire rero umusuzugura . Ahubwo muzamufashe mu rugendo rwe , ngo angarukire amahoro ; ndamutegereje hamwe n’abandi bavandimwe .
46016012	Naho umuvandimwe wacu Apolo , namusabye nkomeje ngo azane n’abandi bavandimwe iwanyu , ariko yabaye abyanze muri iki gihe , ngo azaza nabona umwanya umutunganiye .
46016013	Murabe maso rero , mukomere mu kwemera , mube abagabo , mube intwari ;
46016014	ibyanyu byose mubikorane urukundo .
46016015	Indi nama nabungura , bavandimwe , ni ukutibagirwa ko Sitefana n’urugo rwe babaye uburiza muri Akaya , bakaba baritangiye rwose abatagatifujwe .
46016016	Nimushobokere abantu nk’abo , kimwe n’abandi bose bafatanyije imirimo n’imiruho .
46016017	Nanyuzwe n’uko Sitefana , Forutunati , na Akayikusi baje kunsura ; barahababereye rwose .
46016018	Batwuruye umutima , ari jye , ari namwe . Mujye mumenya gushimira bene abo bantu .
46016019	Kiliziya zo muri Aziya zirabaramutsa . Akwila na Purisika barabatashya cyane muri Nyagasani , hamwe na Kiliziya ikoranira iwabo .
46016020	Abavandimwe bose barabatashya . Namwe rero muramukanye mwese , mu muhoberano mutagatifu .
46016021	Iyi ndamutso ni jye uyiyandikiye , jyewe Pawulo .
46016022	Niba hari udakunda Nyagasani , uwo arakaba ikivume . Marana ta ! Ngwino , Nyagasani !
46016023	Ineza ya Nyagasani Yezu Kristu ihorane namwe .
46016024	Ni jye , ubakundira mwese muri Kristu Yezu .
47001001	Jyewe Pawulo , intumwa ya Kristu Yezu , uko Imana yabishatse , n’umuvandimwe wacu Timote , kuri Kiliziya iri i Korinti , no ku batagatifujwe bose muri Akaya :
47001002	tubifurije ineza n’amahoro biva ku Mana , Umubyeyi wacu no kuri Nyagasani Yezu Kristu .
47001003	Haragasingizwa Imana , Se w’Umwami wacu Yezu Kristu , Umubyeyi w’impuhwe zose kandi utanga ihumure ryuzuye .
47001004	Ni yo iduhumuriza mu magorwa yacu yose ikaduha natwe guhumuriza abashavuye bose , tubagezaho ihumure twiherewe n’Imana .
47001005	Nk’uko twahawe gusangira na Kristu imibabaro ye yose , ni na ko yadusenderejeho ihumure rishyitse muri We .
47001006	Mbese amagorwa turimo , si yo ababyarira guhumurizwa no kurokoka ? Kandi se iyo duhumurijwe , si byo bibabyarira kwihanganira imibabaro dusangiye , maze mukagira ituze ?
47001007	Turabizeye bihagije : kuba dusangiye imibabaro , bizatuma dusangira n’ihumurizwa .
47001008	Koko , bavandimwe , ntitwabahisha akaga twagiriye muri Aziya ; twakutse umutima birenze imivugire , tugeza n’aho twiheba nk’abagiye gupfa .
47001009	Koko twari tumeze nk’abaciriwe urwo gupfa , ku buryo amizero yari yadushizemo , dusigaye twiringiye Imana gusa , Yo izura abapfuye .
47001010	Ni Yo koko yatwaruye mu nzara z’urupfu , kandi izahora irutwaruramo . Twizeye rwose ko nta na rimwe izigera idutererana .
47001011	N’amasengesho yanyu azabidufashamo , bityo umukiro wacu tuzawukeshe gusabirwa na benshi , maze twese hamwe tuzafatanye gushimira Imana ubwo buntu izatugirira .
47001012	Dore ishema ryacu aho rishingiye : ni uko umutimanama wacu utwizeza ko twabayeho kuri iyi si , cyane cyane muri mwe , mu bwiyoroshye no mu butaryarya biva ku Mana , tudakurikije ubwenge bw’abantu , ahubwo tuyobowe n’ineza y’Imana .
47001013	Ntimukeke kandi ko mu mabaruwa yacu , tubandikira ibiciye ukubiri n’ibyo musoma kandi muhita mwumva ; nizeye ko noneho muzatwumva neza ,
47001014	kuko kugeza ubu mwatwumvise amahushuka . Muzasanga ku munsi wa Nyagasani mutwishimira , nk’uko natwe tuzabishimira .
47001015	Nari nizeye kubanza kunyura iwanyu , ngo mwongere mwishime ;
47001016	noneho ngahaguruka iwanyu njya muri Masedoniya , ndetse nkongera kugaruka iwanyu , ngo muntegurire urugendo rwanjye rwo muri Yudeya .
47001017	Mbese uwo mugambi nawufashe nsa n’ukina ? Cyangwa se imigambi yanjye irasa n’idafashe , nk’umuntu wemeye atemeye ?
47001018	Imana irandeba : ibyo nababwiye sinari ngambiriye guhita mbihindagura .
47001019	Koko rero , Umwana w’Imana , Kristu Yezu , twamamaje iwanyu , jyewe , Silivani na Timote , si uko ateye . Ntiyabaye icyarimwe « yego » na « oya » , yabaye « yego » gusa !
47001020	Ku buryo amasezerano yose y’Imana yabaye muri we « yego » , natwe tugakurizaho gukuza Imana , tuvuga tuti « Amen » .
47001021	Ni Yo ubwayo idukomeza muri Kristu , ikadutorera kuba abayo ,
47001022	idushyiramo ikimenyetso cyayo , ikaduha no gutunga Roho wayo mu mitima yacu kugira ngo atubere ingwate y’ibyiza yatugeneye .
47001023	Imana imbeshaho ni Yo ntanzeho umugabo : nirinze kugaruka iwanyu i Korinti ngo ntabatera ibibazo .
47001024	Nta bwo dushaka kubagora mu byerekeye ukwemera , kuko ukwemera kwanyu kutajegajega , ahubwo turabafasha ngo muhimbarwe .
47002001	Niyemeje rero kutagaruka iwanyu , mu gihe tukibabaye .
47002002	Niba se koko ari jye ubababaza , ni nde wundi wangarurira ibyishimo , usibye nyine uwo nababaje ?
47002003	Ubwo mperutse kubandikira nashakaga gukiranura ibintu , ngo hato ninza iwanyu ntababazwa n’abagombaga kuntera ibyishimo ; sinshidikanya rwose ko igihe nishimye , namwe muba mwishimye .
47002004	Simbabeshya , nabandikiye mfite ishavu ryinshi n’umutima wuzuye agahinda , ndetse amarira yisuka , atari ukugira ngo mbababaze , ahubwo ngo mumenye ukuntu mbakunda .
47002005	Niba hari uwahemutse , si jye jyenyine yababaje , ndetse mubirebye neza nanone tudakabije , namwe mwese yarabababaje .
47002006	Birahagije kuba uwo muntu yaratonganyirijwe mu ikoraniro ;
47002007	ni na yo mpamvu , aho bigeze , mukwiye kumubabarira , mukamuhumuriza , ngo hato adashengurwa n’agahinda gakabije , akiheba .
47002008	Ndabibasabye rero , nimukomeze kumugaragariza urukundo .
47002009	Icyatumye kandi mbandikira , ni uko nashakaga kubagerageza ngo ndebe ukuntu mukurikiza amabwiriza yanjye .
47002010	Iyo mugize uwo mubabarira , nanjye mba mubabariye ! Kandi jye mubabariye , mu rugero yaba abikwiye , ni mwe mba mbigiriye , mu maso ya Kristu ,
47002011	ngo tudaha Sekibi urwaho ; imigambi yayo ntituyiyobewe .
47002012	Ubwo ngeze i Torowadi nje kuhamamaza Inkuru Nziza ya Kristu , n’ubwo Nyagasani yari yahankinguriye amarembo ,
47002013	nakomeje guhagarika umutima , kuko ntahasanze umuvandimwe wanjye Tito ; mpita mbasezeraho , njya muri Masedoniya .
47002014	Ariko Imana ishimwe , Yo ihora iduha gutsinda muri Kristu , ikanatuma twogeza ubwamamare bwe , nk’impumuro nziza isakara hose .
47002015	Kandi koko imbere y’Imana , turi impumuro nziza ya Kristu rwagati mu barokorwa no mu bacibwa .
47002016	Kuri bamwe tubanukira urupfu bikazabageza ku rupfu ; ku bandi turi impumuro y’ubuzima bikazabageza ku bugingo . Ni nde muntu rero waba ukwiye guhabwa ubutumwa nk’ubwo ?
47002017	Koko rero ntitumeze nk’abandi benshi bagenda barisha Ijambo ry’Imana ; ahubwo , ku bwa Yo n’imbere yayo , turivugana ubutaryarya , muri Kristu .
47003001	Mbese twongere kandi kwishingana ? Cyangwa se dukeneye kugenza nka bamwe bitwaza inzandiko zibashingana iwanyu , cyangwa aho mubohereje ?
47003002	Ibaruwa idushingana ni mwe , ikaba kandi yanditse mu mutima wacu , izwi kandi isomwa na bose .
47003003	Biragaragara rwose ko muri urwandiko rwa Kristu yandikishije umurimo wacu , rutandikishijwe wino ahubwo Roho w’Imana Nyirubuzima , atari ku bisate by’amabuye , ahubwo rwanditswe ku mitima y’abantu .
47003004	Ngicyo icyizere dufitiye Imana ku bwa Kristu .
47003005	Bityo ku bwacu tukaba nta cyo dushobora kwiratana kidukomotseho , kuko ubushobozi bwacu buturuka ku Mana .
47003006	Ni Yo yatugize abogeza b’Isezerano Rishya ridashingiye ku Mategeko yanditswe , ahubwo kuri Roho ; kuko Amategeko yanditswe akurura urupfu , naho Roho we agatanga ubuzima .
47003007	Niba gushingwa ubutumwa butarindaga urupfu , busharazwe ku bisate by’amabuye , kwaramuhesheje ikuzo ringana rityo kugeza aho Abayisraheli badahangara kureba uruhanga rwa Musa , kubera ububengerane bw’akanya gato bwo mu maso he ,
47003008	bishoboka bite ko uwashinzwe ubutumwa bwa Roho atamutambukije kure ikuzo ?
47003009	Ubwo ubutumwa bwavanyeho ubucibwe bwagize ikuzo , ubutumwa bugeza ku butungane busumbijeho kure ikuzo risesuye .
47003010	Uko byamera kose , ibyahoranye ikuzo , byarayoyotse , ubigereranyije n’ibifite ikuzo rihanitse ryo kuri ubu .
47003011	Niba rero ibyamaze akanya gato byarahawe ikuzo , bishoboka bite ko ibigenewe guhoraho , bitarushaho kugira ikuzo ?
47003012	Kuba rero dufite ayo mizero , bituma tudahungabana .
47003013	Ntitumeze nka Musa wipfukaga igitambaro mu maso ngo Abayisraheli batabona uko ikuzo rimweyurukaho .
47003014	Nyamara ubwenge bwabo bwahumiye ko ! Koko rero kugeza na n’ubu , iyo basoma Isezerano rya kera , icyo gitambaro cyakomeje kubapfukirana ; ntikiratamururwa kuko Kristu wenyine ari We ukivanaho .
47003015	Mu by’ukuri , kugeza magingo aya , uko basoma ibya Musa , hari nk’igihu kibambitse ku mutima wabo .
47003016	Uwo mubambiko uzavanwaho n’uko bagaruriye Nyagasani umutima wabo .
47003017	Mu by’ukuri Nyagasani ni We Roho , kandi aho Roho wa Nyagasani ari , ni ho haba ubwisanzure .
47003018	Nuko rero twebwe twese , abo uruhanga rudapfukiranye , turashashagira ikuzo rya Nyagasani , bigatuma tugira imisusire ye , mu ikuzo rigenda ryisumbura , ku bwa Nyagasani , ari we Roho .
47004001	Ku mpuhwe zayo , Imana yatweguriye uwo murimo , bigatuma tudacika intege .
47004002	Ni yo mpamvu twirinze amatwara afifitse kandi ateye isoni ; twanga kuryaryana no guhindagura Ijambo ry’Imana , ahubwo tugatangaza ukuri kwaryo kugira ngo abantu bose batwizere imbere y’Imana .
47004003	Nyamara , niba Inkuru Nziza yacu yaba itumvikana , abatayumva ni aborama ,
47004004	n’abemeragato imana y’iyi si yahumye ubwenge , ku buryo batagerwaho n’umucyo w’Inkuru Nziza n’ububengerane bwa Kristu , We buranga nyakuri bw’Imana .
47004005	Si twe twiyamamaza na gato , ahubwo twamamaza Nyagasani Yezu Kristu . Twebwe twiyiziho kuba abagaragu banyu , tubigiriye Yezu .
47004006	Kuko Imana yivugiye iti « Urumuri nirwakire mu mwijima » , ni Yo ubwayo yamurikiye mu mitima yacu , ngo tumenye ikuzo ryayo ribengerana ku ruhanga rwa Kristu .
47004007	Ariko uwo mukiro tuwutwaye mu tubindi tumeneka ubusa , bigatuma bose babona ko ubwo bubasha buhanitse buturuka ku Mana , aho kutwitirirwa .
47004008	Baraduhutaza hirya no hino , ariko ntidutembagara ; turagirijwe , ariko tugatambuka ;
47004009	turaburagizwa , ariko ntidushyikirwa ; twatuwe hasi , ariko ntiduheranwa .
47004010	Igihe cyose tugendana imibabaro y’urupfu rwa Kristu , kugira ngo n’ubuzima bwe bwigaragaze mu mubiri wacu .
47004011	N’ubwo turi bazima bwose , duhora tugabizwa urupfu , duhorwa Yezu , kugira ngo ubugingo bwe bugaragarire muri iyi mibiri yacu y’impfabusa .
47004012	Twebwe ariko urupfu ruratubungamo , naho muri mwe ubuzima ni bwose .
47004013	Ubwo dushyigikiwe n’ukwemera kw’Ibyanditswe bivuga biti « Naremeye , bintera kwamamaza » , natwe turemera ikaba ari yo mpamvu twamamaza .
47004014	Koko turabizi , Uwazuye Nyagasani Yezu , natwe azatuzurana na We , kandi twese azatwakire iruhande rwe .
47004015	Ibyo byose ni mwe bigirirwa , kugira ngo musenderezwe ineza y’Imana , maze murusheho kuba benshi bashimira Imana , bayihesha ikuzo .
47004016	Ni cyo gituma tudacogora ; kabone n’ubwo umubiri ugenda uyonga , umutima wo wivugurura buri munsi .
47004017	Kandi n’amagorwa yacu muri iki gihe gihita nta cyo adutwaye , uyagereranije n’ikuzo adutegurira ry’akataraboneka kandi rizahoraho .
47004018	Bityo tukaba tutarangamiye ibigaragara , ahubwo ibitagaragara , kuko ibigaragarira amaso bihitana n’igihe , naho ibitagaragara bigahoraho iteka .
47005001	Tuzi neza ko uyu mubiri utubereye nk’icumbi kuri iyi si . Umunsi ryasenyutse , tukazimukira mu ngoro ihoraho yo mu ijuru , itubatswe n’ukuboko k’umuntu , ahubwo yubatswe n’Imana .
47005002	Tukaba rero duhangayikishijwe no kwifuza cyane igihe tuzatungira hirya y’ubu buzima , iwacu ho mu ijuru ,
47005003	niba ariko dusanganywe umwambaro aho kuba dutumbuje .
47005004	Koko rero twebwe abakiri muri uyu mubiri , turaganya dushenguka , kuko tudashaka kuwucuzwa , ahubwo twifuza kuwambikirwaho kugira ngo uwo mwambaro w’akanya gato , uduhindurirwemo uw’ubuzima .
47005005	Bityo , Imana , yaduteganyirije ibyo , yabaye iduhaye Roho Mutagatifu ho umuganura .
47005006	N’ubwo ariko duhorana icyizere , tuzi neza ko igihe tuzaba dutuye muri uyu mubiri , tuzasa n’abari ishyanga , kure ya Nyagasani .
47005007	— Kuko ubu tugendera mu kwemera , tutayobowe n’uko tubona neza . —
47005008	Koko duhorana icyizere , bigatuma duhitamo kwimuka muri uyu mubiri , ngo twigire gutura iruhande rwa Nyagasani .
47005009	Twaba muri uyu mubiri , cyangwa twawimukamo , icyo tugambiriye ni uko tumushimisha .
47005010	Kuko twese tuzahinguka imbere y’urukiko rwa Kristu , ngo buri wese ahabwe igikwiye ibyo yakoze akiri mu buzima bw’umubiri , byaba ibyiza cyangwa ibibi .
47005011	Ubwo dufitiye Nyagasani igitinyiro ; turashishikariza abantu kumwemera , kandi rwose , nta buryarya dufite imbere y’Imana . Nizeye ko namwe mutabunziho .
47005012	Ntitugiye kongera kubishinganaho , ahubwo turashaka kubaha uburyo bwo kutwishimira , kugira ngo mubone icyo musubiza abiratana ibihenda amaso , ariko bidafite ishingiro mu mutima .
47005013	Niba twaragaragaweho n’ibisazi , twabigiriye Imana ; niba kandi twarashyize mu gaciro , ni mwebwe twabigiriye .
47005014	Urukundo rwa Kristu ruraduhihibikanya , iyo tuzirikanye ukuntu umwe yapfiriye bose , bikaba rero ko bose bapfuye .
47005015	Kandi koko yapfiriye bose , kugira ngo abariho bataberaho bo ubwabo , ahubwo babereho uwabapfiriye kandi akazukira kubakiza .
47005016	Ni cyo gituma kuva ubu nta muntu n’umwe tukimenya ku buryo busanzwe ; ndetse na Kristu , niba twarigeze kumumenya ku buryo bw’abantu , ubu ntitukimumenya dutyo .
47005017	Bityo , umuntu wese uri muri Kristu , yabaye ikiremwa gishya . Ibishaje byarayoyotse , none ngaha byose byahindutse bishya .
47005018	Byose biva ku Mana , yo yiyunze natwe ikoresheje Kristu ; nyuma idushinga umurimo w'ubwiyunge .
47005019	Uko biri kose , Imana ubwayo ni yo yiyunze n’ab'isi bose muri Kristu , ntiyaba ikibabaraho ibicumuro byabo ; nuko natwe idushinga ubutumwa bwo kubwira abantu ngo biyunge na Yo .
47005020	Ubu rero duhagarariye Kristu , ku buryo Imana ubwayo ari yo ibahamagara ari twe ikoresheje . Ngaho rero turabinginze mu izina rya Kristu : Nimwemere mwiyunge n'Imana !
47005021	Kristu utarigeze akora icyaha , Imana yamubazeho ibyaha bya muntu , kugira ngo muri We tubarweho ubutungane bw'Imana .
47006001	Ubwo turi abafasha b’Imana , turabashishikariza kudapfusha ubusa ubuntu bwayo .
47006002	Kuko ubwayo yivugira iti « Mu gihe gikwiye , numvise isengesho ryawe ; no ku munsi w’uburokorwe , naragutabaye . » Ngiki rero koko igihe gikwiye ; nguyu koko umunsi w’uburokorwe .
47006003	Nta we rero dushaka guhungabanya , kugira ngo ubutumwa bwacu butagira amakemwa .
47006004	Ahubwo twihatira kugaragaza muri byose ko turi abagaragu b’Imana , turihangana bihagije , ari mu magorwa , mu mage no mu ishavu ,
47006005	ari mu ikubitwa , mu buroko no mu midugararo , ari mu minaniro , mu kutagoheka no mu isonza ;
47006006	tukitabaza ubuziranenge n’ubuhanga , ubwiyumanganye n’ubugwaneza , muri Roho Mutagatifu ; dukoresha urukundo rutaryarya ,
47006007	ijambo ry’ukuri n’ububasha bw’Imana ; turwanisha intwaro z’ubutungane , zo mu kuboko kw’iburyo n’ibumoso .
47006008	Rimwe turubahwa , ubundi tugasuzugurwa ; baradusebya , ubundi bakadushimagiza . Batwita ababeshyi , kandi tuvugisha ukuri .
47006009	Dusa nk’intamenyekana , kandi tuzwi neza . Dufatwa nk’indembe , kandi turi bazima . Baraduhana , ariko ntibageze aho kutwica .
47006010	Turashavuzwa , nyamara duhora twishimye . Turi abakene , nyamara dukungahaza benshi . Batugize abinazi , kandi ari twe dutunze byose !
47006011	Bavandimwe b’i Korinti , twababwiye ukuri kose , tubaranguriza umutima wacu .
47006012	Muwufitemo umwanya mugari : uwanyu ubanza ari wo ufunganye !
47006013	Nimutwishyure rwose , ndababwira nk’abana banjye : nimutwugururire namwe umutima wanyu !
47006014	Ntimukagirane urunana rw’insumbane n’abatemera ! Mbese ubutungane hari isano bugirana n’ubukozi bw’ibibi ? Urumuri rwabangikana rute n’umwijima ?
47006015	Kristu na Beliyari bakumvikana bate ? Uwemera n’utemera bahuriye he ?
47006016	Mbese ingoro y’Imana yasangirwa ite n’ibigirwamana ? Erega , ni twe ngoro y’Imana Nzima , nk’uko ubwayo ibyivugira iti « Nzatura muri bo , nzatambagire rwagati muri bo , maze nzabe Imana yabo , na bo bazambere umuryango .
47006017	Nimuve muri abo bantu , mwitandukanye na bo , uwo ari Nyagasani ubivuga . Mwirinde gukora ku cyabahumanya , maze ubwanjye nzabakire .
47006018	Nzababera umubyeyi , namwe mumbere abahungu n’abakobwa , uwo ni Nyagasani ubivuze . »
47007001	Ncuti nkunda , ubwo twashyikirijwe ayo masezerano nitwivaneho ubwandu bwose bw’umubiri n’ubw’umutima ; twirundurire ubutungane , mu gitinyiro cy’Imana .
47007002	Natwe , nimuduhe umwanya mu mitima yanyu . Nta we twigeze duhemukira ; nta we twigeze ducuza ikiri icye ; nta n’uwo twigeze turya imitsi .
47007003	Ibyo simbivugiye kubahamya icyaha ; nk’uko nakomeje kubibabwira : muri inkoramutima zacu bigeze n’aho urupfu rutadutandukanya .
47007004	Mbafitiye ubwizere buhagije , kandi muhora muntera akanyamuneza . Mu magorwa yacu yose , mpora niyumvamo ihumure , ndetse nsendereye ibyishimo .
47007005	Mu by’ukuri , kuva twagera muri Masedoniya , nta gahenge twigeze tugira , ahubwo twahuye n’ingorane zitabarika , ari intambara zo hanze , ari n’inkeke zo ku mutima .
47007006	Ariko Imana ihoza abiyoroshya , yaduhumurije ituzanira Tito .
47007007	Si ukuza kwe gusa , ahubwo no kumva ukuntu mwamwakiriye , akanadutekerereza iby’urukumbuzi mumfitiye , amarira yanyu , n’ukuntu mundwanirira ishyaka , ibyo byose byatumye nishima kurushaho .
47007008	N’ubwo wenda ibaruwa nabandikiye yabababaje , sinicuza kuba narayanditse . Nanone ndabona ko yabababaje mu gihe cy’akanya gato ,
47007009	n’ubwo naba narabyicujije , ubu nshimishijwe n’uko yabateye kwisubiraho . Agahinda kanyu kanyuze Imana , bityo ku bwanjye nkaba nta nabi nabagiriye .
47007010	Kuko akababaro kanyuze Imana gatera kwisubiraho bigeza ku mukiro . Ibyo rero nta n’umwe wabyicuza . Naho akababaro gaheze mu by’isi gusa , gakurura urupfu .
47007011	Nimwirebere namwe icyo akababaro kanyu kanyuze Imana , kabagejejeho ! Mbega umwete mwagize ! Ukuntu mwitwaye ! Ukuntu mwigaye , mwagize igishyika ! Mbega ubushake , ukuntu mwagize isyaka , mwifuza gucyaha ikibi ! Muri ibyo byose mwerekanye ko muri abere ku byabaye .
47007012	Muri make , ubwo mperutse kubandikira , sinabigiriye uwahemutse , cyangwa uwahemukiwe , ahubwo kwari ukugira ngo mbagaragarize ishyaka mudufitiye imbere y’Imana .
47007013	Ngicyo icyatumaze agahinda . Uretse ihumurizwa bwite mwaduteye , twanyuzwe cyane n’ukuntu Tito yishimiye ko mwamwuruye umutima .
47007014	Niba kandi hari ikintu nabamuratiyeho , sinigeze mbyicuza . Muzi neza ko mpora mbabwiza ukuri : ukuntu nabamuratiye ni ko yabasanze .
47007015	Na we yarushijeho kubakunda , iyo abona ukuntu mumwumvira mwese , n’ukuntu mwamwakiranye icyubahiro n’igitinyiro .
47007016	Nishimiye ko nshobora kubiringira muri byose .
47008001	Bavandimwe , turifuza kubamenyesha ubuntu Imana yagiriye Kiliziya zo muri Masedoniya .
47008002	N’ubwo bari mu ruhuri rw’amagorwa y’ibigeragezo , hakubitiyeho ubukene bukabije , ariko kandi bari no mu byishimo byinshi , ibyo byabateye kugira ubuntu cyane .
47008003	Nanjye ndahamya ko batanze ku bwende bwabo , ndetse birenze uko bashoboye .
47008004	Ahubwo banyingingiraga kubareka ngo bagire uruhare ku mfashanyo yagenewe abatagatifujwe ( bo muri Yudeya ) .
47008005	Baritanze , biyegurira Imana natwe baratwiha , birenze ndetse uko twari tubyizeye , nk’uko Imana yabishatse .
47008006	Ni cyo cyatumye nsaba Tito nshishikaye ngo akomeze iwanyu icyo gikorwa yabatangiyemo cyo kugira ubuntu .
47008007	Kandi ubwo musanganywe ubukungahazwe muri byose , haba mu kwemera no mu kuvuga neza , mu bumenyi n’ishyaka muri byose , ndetse no mu rukundo twabatoje , nimukataze no muri iyo ngabire yo kugira ubuntu .
47008008	Simbibahayemo itegeko , ahubwo ndabamenyesha imyifatire y’ahandi , mukurizeho kugaragaza ukuri k’urukundo rwanyu .
47008009	Musanzwe muzi ubugiraneza bw’Umwami wacu Yezu Kristu , We mukire wemeye kwigira umukene , ari mwe abigirira , ngo abakungaharishe ubukene bwe .
47008010	Ni akanama mbagira muri ibyo : ni byiza ko mukomeza icyo gikorwa cy’urukundo mwatangiye umwaka ushize ; ntimwabaye aba mbere gusa mu kubitekereza , ahubwo no mu kubikurikiza .
47008011	Ngaho nimugere ku cyo mwiyemeje , maze uko mubishoboye , ibikorwa byanyu byuzuze ugushaka kwanyu .
47008012	Utangana umutima mwiza ntagayirwa icyo adafite , ashimirwa icyo yatanze !
47008013	Si ukuvuga ko mugomba kwikokora ngo murarwana ku bandi , ahubwo muharanire kuringaniza .
47008014	Kuri ubwo buryo , icyo akarusho mutunze kizatabarure abari mu bwinazi ; maze umunsi umwe icyo na bo bazabarusha kizabatabare mu bukene bwanyu , mukomeze mutyo kuba magirirane .
47008015	Koko byaranditswe ngo « Uwayoye byinshi nta cyo yarengejeho , n’uwayoye bike nta cyo yabuzeho . »
47008016	Imana ishimwe , Yo yahaye na Tito uwo mutima wo kubakunda .
47008017	Igihe musabye kujya iwanyu , yahise abyemera , ndetse yihutira kubageraho .
47008018	Twamwohereje hamwe n’umuvandimwe ushimwa na Kiliziya zose kubera ishyaka afitiye Inkuru Nziza .
47008019	Si n’ibyo gusa , Kiliziya zose zamutoreye kuduherekeza mu rugendo tujyanye imfashanyo zanyu , zihesha Imana ikuzo kandi zikagaragaza umutima wacu wo gufasha abandi .
47008020	Nirinda rwose ko hagira untera urubwa mu buryo ngenga iyo mfashanyo itubutse mwanshinze .
47008021	Turaharanira kuba indakemwa , bitari imbere y’Imana gusa , ndetse no mu maso y’abantu .
47008022	Tubatumanye kandi n’undi muvandimwe wacu twagerageje ku buryo bwinshi , twasanze ari umunyeshyaka , maze ubu akaba arushijeho kurigira , kubera icyizere cyinshi abafitiye .
47008023	Muzi ko Tito ari mugenzi wanjye dufatanya imirimo yose tubakorera . Naho abandi bavandimwe , bo bahagarariye za Kiliziya , kandi bakaba ikuzo rya Kristu .
47008024	Ngaho rero , nimubagaragarize urukundo rwanyu , n’impamvu zidutera kubarata , bimenyekane muri za Kiliziya zose .
47009001	Si ngombwa ko ngira icyo mbandikira ku byerekeye imfashanyo igenewe abatagatifujwe .
47009002	Nzi imigambi myiza mufite , ndetse nabaratiye n’abo muri Masedoniya , nti « Kuva mu mwaka ushize , abo muri Akaya biteguye gutanga imfashanyo » , kandi ishyaka ryanyu ryateye inkunga za Kiliziya nyinshi .
47009003	Mboherereje aba bavandimwe , kugira ngo iryo shema mbafitiye muri ibyo ritaba impfabusa , muzasangwe koko mwiteguye , nk’uko nabibavuzeho .
47009004	Mfite ubwoba ko , ndamutse nzanye n’abo muri Masedoniya , twasanga nta cyo mwateguye , kandi twari tubafitiye icyizere gihagije ; twakorwa n’ikimwaro , ntiriwe mvuga ko namwe mwaba mugayitse .
47009005	Nasanze ibyiza ari uko abo bavandimwe bambanziriza ngo begeranye amaturo yanyu , maze ibyo mwiyemeje gutanga ku buntu bimaze kuringanizwa , bizabe iby’ubuntu koko , atari ibyo mutanze mugononwa .
47009006	Muramenye ko « Uwabibye ubusa , asarura ubusa , naho uwabibye byinshi agasarura byinshi ! »
47009007	Buri wese rero atange uko umutima we ubimubwira , atinuba , adahaswe , kuko Imana ikunda utanga yishimye .
47009008	Imana ifite ububasha bwo kubasenderezaho ibyiza by’ubwoko bwose , kugira ngo muhorane ibya ngombwa igihe cyose no muri byose , mugasagura ndetse n’ibibafasha gukora ibikorwa byiza .
47009009	Nk’uko byanditswe ngo « Yatanze ku buntu , akwiza abakene ; ubutungane bwe buzahoraho iteka . »
47009010	Uha umuhinzi imbuto zo kubiba , akanamuha umugati wo kurya , azabaha namwe imbuto , azirumbure , kandi agwize umusaruro w’ubutungane bwanyu .
47009011	Muzakungahazwa ku buryo bwose , bizatume mutanga mutizigamye maze imfashanyo tuzaba tubashyikirije , zitere benshi gushimira Imana .
47009012	Umurimo w’ayo maturo , ntugamije gusa mu gukenura abatagatifujwe , ahubwo ugenewe no kugwiza amasengesho yo gushimira Imana .
47009013	Abanyuzwe n’uwo murimo bazakurizaho gusingiza Imana kubera ukuntu mwumviye Inkuru Nziza ya Kristu , banayishimire kandi ubuntu mugira bwo gusangira byose na bose .
47009014	Bityo mu kubasabira , babagaragarize ubwuzu babafitiye , ku mpamvu z’ingabire Imana yabasesekarije .
47009015	Imana ishimirwe ubuntu bwayo butagereranywa !
47010001	Ni jyewe Pawulo ubibisabiye ubwanjye , mu bugwaneza n’ituze bya Kristu . Muvuga ko iyo turi kumwe niyoroshya , naba ndi kure nkabisha .
47010002	Nyamara ndabinginze , igihe nzazira iwanyu , sinzagombe gukoresha amakare , n’ubwo nifuza gukangara bamwe bibwira ko tucyitwara bya runtu .
47010003	Kuba abantu ko turi abantu , ariko ntitukirwana ibi bisanzwe by’abantu .
