47010004	Oya , intwaro zacu ntizikomoka kuri muntu , ahubwo ububasha bwazo buturuka ku Mana , bugasenyagura ibyari intamenwa . Abiyemera tubakura ku izima ,
47010005	kimwe n’abatambamiye ubumenyi bw’Imana . Twigarurira ibitekerezo byose ngo bigomokere Kristu ,
47010006	kandi twiteguye gucyaha icyitwa agasuzuguro cyose , igihe mwebwe muzaba mwumviye muri byose .
47010007	Nimurebe ibintu uko biri ! Uwibwira wese ko ari uwa Kristu , namenye bidasubirwaho ko natwe turi aba Kristu , kimwe na we !
47010008	Niba naba nkabya mu kwiratana ububasha Nyagasani yaduhereye kubakomeza , atari ubwo kubadindiza , nta soni binteye .
47010009	Sinshaka gusa n’ubakangaranya mu nzandiko zanjye ,
47010010	— kuko hari abavuga ngo « Inzandiko ze zifite ireme kandi zirakaze , nyamara iyo ari muri twe , usanga agayitse n’ijambo rye ari nta ryo . » —
47010011	Uwibwira ibyo amenye neza ko , uko tumeze mu mvugo , turi kure , twandika , nta ho bitandukaniye n’ibyo tuzakora tugeze iwanyu .
47010012	Kuko tutahangara kwireshyeshya no kwigereranya n’abo biyogeza ubwabo ; ni abirasi rwose gukeka ko ari bo kamara n’igipimo cya byose .
47010013	Twebwe tuzirinda kwirata birengeje urugero rw’umurimo Imana yadushinze itwohereza iwanyu .
47010014	Iyo tuza kuba tutaraje iwanyu twaba koko dutandukiriye ; none twabaye aba mbere bageze iwanyu tubazaniye Inkuru Nziza ya Kristu .
47010015	Nta bwo twikabiriza nk’abiratana imirimo yakozwe n’abandi , ahubwo dufite icyizere ko , nimukomeza gutera imbere mu kwemera , tuzarushaho kwagura umurimo wacu muri mwe ,
47010016	ndetse Inkuru Nziza ya Kristu tukayirenza imbibi z’iwanyu , uko tubishinzwe ; bityo ntituziratane imirimo abandi bakoze mu murima wabo .
47010017	« Ushaka kwirata wese , niyiratire muri Nyagasani ! »
47010018	Uwiyemezaho agaciro wese , si we ugakwiye , ahubwo uwo Nyagasani akemejeho , ni we ugakwiye .
47011001	Icyampa ngo mushobore kwihanganira ubusazi bwanjye ho gato ! Ngaho se nimunyihanganire !
47011002	Mbakunda byansajije , nk’uko Imana ibakunda . Nabashyingiye umukwe umwe rukumbi , mbashyikiriza Kristu muri nk’umugeni w’isugi .
47011003	Nyamara , nk’uko Eva yaguye mu mutego w’inzoka , ndatinya ko namwe , imitima yanyu izahuma mugateshuka ku bupfura mukwiriye kugirira Kristu .
47011004	Dore nawe , uwadutse wese abamenyesha undi Yezu utari uwo twabigishije , cyangwa se akabarohamo umwuka wundi utari Mwuka w'Imana mwahawe , cyangwa se akabazanira indi nkuru nziza itari Iyo twabashyikirije , uwo muntu mumutega yombi .
47011005	Ndibwira ko izo ntumwa z’akataraboneka nta cyo zindusha .
47011006	Ndi umuswa koko mu byo kuvuga neza , nyamara sindi we mu by’ubuhanga . Ibyo twabibagaragarije muri byose no ku buryo bwose .
47011007	Ubwo se cyabaye icyaha cyo kubicishaho bugufi , mbamamariza Inkuru Nziza y’Imana ku buntu , kugira ngo mbaheshe agaciro ?
47011008	Nacuje za Kiliziya z’ahandi , nemera gutungwa na zo ngo mbone uko mbakorera .
47011009	Iyo nagiraga icyo nkenera ndi iwanyu , nta we nigeze ndushya , kuko ibyo nari mbuze nabihabwaga n’abavandimwe baturutse muri Masedoniya . Iteka ryose nirinze kubagora , kandi nzakomeza kubyirinda .
47011010	Mbarahirije ukuri kwa Kristu undimo , nta we uzanyaga iryo shema mu turere twose two muri Akaya .
47011011	Kuki se ? Kuko se ntabakunda ? Imana ni Yo ibizi !
47011012	Nzakomeza uko nsanzwe ngenza , kugira ngo ndaha urwaho abarunshakaho , babure impamvu yo kwirata ko duhwanyije agaciro .
47011013	Bene abo bantu ni ingirwantumwa , ni abahendanyi biyoberanyamo intumwa za Kristu .
47011014	Ibyo kandi ntibitangaje : Sekibi na yo yihinduramo umumalayika w’urumuri .
47011015	Nta gitangaje rero ko abagaragu bayo bihinduramo abaharanira ubutungane . Nyamara amaherezo yabo ni ukugarukwa n’ibyo bakoze .
47011016	Nongere mbisubiremo , ntihakagire ukeka ko ndi umusazi , cyangwa se nimunyemerere kuba we maze nanjye nshobore kwirataho gato .
47011017	Ibyo ngiye kuvuga , simbibwirijwe na Nyagasani , ahubwo mu bisazi byanjye nishimiye kugira icyo niratana .
47011018	Ubwo benshi biratana ibyo bakesha kamere , reka nanjye nirate .
47011019	Mwebwe muzwiho ubwitonzi , mwihanganira abasazi nta ngorane !
47011020	Mwihanganira ko babagira abacakara , ko babaryana utwanyu , ko babacuza , ko babishongoraho , ko babakubita mu maso .
47011021	Mfite isoni zo kubabwira ko twagize intege nke nka bo ! Ibyo abandi batinyutse kwivuga — noneho mvuge nk’umusazi — nanjye ndabitinyutse .
47011022	Mbese ni Abahebureyi ? Nanjye ndi we ! Ni Abayisraheli ? Nanjye ndi we ! Inkomoko ya Abrahamu ? Nanjye ndi yo !
47011023	Mbese bakorera Kristu ? — Reka mvuge amateshwa — Ndabarusha bose ! Mu miruho ? Narabarushije ! Mu buroko ? Incuro nyinshi kubarusha ! Inkoni ? Nakubiswe izitabarika ! Amakuba y’urupfu ? Nayagize hato na hato !
47011024	Incuro eshanu Abayisraheli bankubise ibiboko mirongo itatu n’icyenda .
47011025	Nakubiswe inkoni incuro eshatu , rimwe mpondaguzwa amabuye , ndohama gatatu mu mazi , ndetse mara ijoro n’umunsi rwagati mu nyanja .
47011026	Mu ngendo zanjye nyinshi nagiriye amakuba mu nzuzi , mpura n’abambuzi , ngira akaga k’abo dusangiye ubwoko n’ako ntewe n’abanyamahanga , ngirira ingorane mu mugi , mu butayu no mu nyanja , nkubitiraho imitego y’abagambanyi biyita abavandimwe !
47011027	Mu miruho n’iminaniro , mu kurara irondo kenshi , mu nzara n’inyota , mu gusiba kurya kenshi , mu kwicwa n’imbeho no kubura icyo nambara ;
47011028	ntavuze n’ibisigaye : inkeke ya buri munsi mpagaritswe umutima na za Kiliziya zose !
47011029	Ni nde wacogoye , sincike intege ? Ni nde wateshutse , maze simpinde umushyitsi ?
47011030	Niba kwirata ari ngombwa , nziratana intege nke zanjye .
47011031	Imana , Se wa Nyagasani Yezu , yogahora isingizwa iteka , izi ko ntabeshya .
47011032	I Damasi , igisonga cy’Umwami Areta cyarindishije umugi ngo bamfate .
47011033	Nuko bancisha mu idirishya , bamanurira ku rukuta mu gitebo , murokoka ntyo .
47012001	Mbese ni ngombwa kwirata ? Ubanza ari nta cyo bimaze ! Nyamara reka ngere ku ibonekerwa no ku byo nahishuriwe na Nyagasani .
47012002	Hari umuntu nzi ku bwa Kristu , hashize imyaka cumi n’ine , — niba byari mu mubiri we , simbizi ; niba bitari mu mubiri we , jye simbizi ; Imana ni Yo ibizi — , uwo muntu rero yarajyanywe , agezwa mu bushorishori bw’ijuru .
47012003	Kandi nzi ko uwo muntu , — niba ari mu mubiri we , niba atari mu mubiri we , simbizi ; Imana ni Yo ibizi — ,
47012004	uwo muntu yajyanywe mu ijuru maze ahumvira amagambo arengeje imivugirwe , umuntu ndetse adafitiye uruhusa rwo gusubiramo .
47012005	Bene uwo muntu namwiratana koko , usibye ko jyewe nta kindi nziratana kitari intege nke zanjye .
47012006	Rwose , nshatse kwirata sinaba ndi umusazi , kuko naba mvuga ibiri ukuri ; ariko na byo ndabyirinze , ngo hato batankekaho kuba nsumbye uko bambona cyangwa uko mvuga .
47012007	Maze , kugira ngo ibyo bintu bihanitse nahishuriwe bitantera kwirarika , nashyizwe umugera mu mubiri , ari yo ntumwa ya Sekibi ngo ijye inkubita , nirinde kwikuza .
47012008	Ibyo byatumye nsaba Nyagasani gatatu kose ngo ayinkize .
47012009	Maze aransubiza ati « Ingabire yanjye iraguhagije ; kuko ububasha bwanjye bwigaragariza cyane cyane mu banyantegenke . » Ni yo mpamvu mpisemo kwiratira mu ntege nke zanjye , kugira ngo ububasha bwa Kristu bunyituriremo .
47012010	Bityo mpimbarirwe mu ntege nke zanjye , mu bitutsi , mu mage , mu bitotezo no mu ihagarikamutima , mbigirira Kristu . Kuko igihe cyose mba mfite intege nke , ari bwo nyine mba nkomeye .
47012011	Ngaho rero nabaye umusazi ! Ariko ni mwe mwabinteye . Ni mwe muba mwarandwanyeho , kuko nta cyo izo ntumwa z’akataraboneka zinsumbije , n’ubwo nta cyo ndi cyo .
47012012	Ibiranga intumwa nyayo byarabagaragariye , ari byo ibi : ukwihangana kudahinyuka , ibimenyetso , ibitangaza , n’ibikorwa by’ububasha .
47012013	Izindi Kiliziya zabarushije iki , usibye ko jye ntigeze mbasahura ? Niba muri ibyo narabarenganyije , nimubimbabarire !
47012014	Ubu niteguye kugaruka iwanyu ubwa gatatu , kandi nta bwo nzabagora ; kuko atari ibintu byanyu ndangamiye , ahubwo ari mwebwe ubwanyu . Si abana bagomba kuzigamira ababyeyi , ahubwo ababyeyi ni bo babikorera abana babo .
47012015	Ku binyerekeye , nahara ibyanjye byose , nanjye nkitanga wese ntizigamye , mbigirira mwe . Ese kuba mbakunze by’agahebuzo byamviramo gukundwa urumamo ?
47012016	Ni koko , sinabashatsemo indonke ! Ariko nabaye inyaryenge mbafatisha amayeri ?
47012017	Murebe mu bo nabatumyeho , uwo nikingirije ngo mbacuze .
47012018	Ningingiye Tito kuza iwanyu , n’undi muvandimwe mutayobewe . Tito se yaba ari we wabamazeho ibintu ? Twaba se tutaragize umutima umwe ? Cyangwa tutaraciye inzira imwe ?
47012019	Hashize umwanya mutekereza ko turiho tubireguraho ? Oya da ! Turavugira imbere y’Imana , muri Kristu . Kandi ibyo byose , nkoramutima zacu , bibere kubagwa neza .
47012020	Cyakora mfite ubwoba ko , ninza , ntazabasanga uko mbyifuza , cyangwa se ko jyewe mutazasanga meze uko munyifuza ; ndatinya ko nzabasangana ubwumvikane buke , ishyari , uburakari , ubushyamirane , amazimwe , ubutiriganya , ugusuzugurana n’imvururu .
47012021	Ndatinya rwose ko , igihe nzagaruka iwanyu , Imana yanjye izankoza isoni imbere yanyu , nkarizwa na benshi muri mwe bacumuye , ariko ntibisubireho ngo biyake ingeso mbi , ubusambanyi n’ubuhabara .
47013001	Ubu ni ubwa gatatu ngiye kuza iwanyu . ( Nk’uko Ibyanditswe bibivuga ) « Urubanza rwose ruzasozwa ari uko rukemuwe n’abagabo babiri cyangwa batatu » .
47013002	Narabivuze ubwo nabasuraga bwa kabiri , n’ubu nkiri kure nongeye kubisubiramo , abaherutse gucumura n’abandi bose , ko nindamuka nje , nta mpuhwe nzabagirira ,
47013003	kuko ngo mushaka ikimenyetso cy’uko ari Kristu umvugiramo . Kristu si inganzwa kuri mwe , ahubwo azabagaragariza ububasha bwe .
47013004	Ni koko yabambwe ku musaraba bishingiye ku ntege nke ze , ariko ubu ni muzima bishingiye ku bubasha bw’Imana . Natwe kandi muri We turi abanyantege nke , ariko nk’uko muzabyibonera , tuzabana na We ku bw’ububasha bw’Imana buzabagaragarizwa .
47013005	Nimwisuzume ubwanyu , mwigerageze , murebe ko mutacogoye mu kwemera . Mwaba se mwariyibagije ko Kristu abatuyemo nyirizina ? Keretse rero , musanze mwaratsinzwe !
47013006	Nizeye ko mudashidikanya ko twe twatsinze .
47013007	Turasaba Imana ngo mutazavaho mukora nabi . Icyo tugamije si ukugaragaza ko mwatsinzwe n’igeragezwa , ahubwo ni uko twababona mukora neza , maze tukaba ari twe twibeshya .
47013008	Nta ntege dufite zo kurwanya ukuri , ahubwo tuzifitiye kugushyigikira .
47013009	Duhora twishimye iyo twe ducogoye ariko mwe mukaba mukomeye . Impamvu y’amasengesho yacu ni uko mwatera imbere .
47013010	Ni cyo gitumye mbandikiye nkiri kure , ngo ntazazanwa no guca urubanza , nkoresheje ububasha Nyagasani yampereye kubakomeza aho kubacogoza .
47013011	Ahasigaye rero , bavandimwe , muhorane ibyishimo , mutere imbere , muterana inkunga , mushyire hamwe , mubane mu ituze , bityo Imana yuje urukundo n’amahoro izabana namwe .
47013012	Muramukanye mu muhoberano mutagatifu . Abatagatifujwe bose b’ino barabaramutsa .
47013013	
47013014	Ineza y’Umwami wacu Yezu Kristu , n’urukundo rw’Imana Data , n’ubusabane kuri Roho Mutagatifu , bihorane namwe mwese .
48001001	Jyewe Pawulo intumwa , itari iy’abantu cyangwa kubw’umuntu , ahubwo ku bushake bwa Yezu Kristu n’Imana Umubyeyi wacu wamuzuye mu bapfuye ,
48001002	n’abavandimwe bose turi kumwe , kuri za Kiliziya zo mu Bugalati :
48001003	tubifurije ineza n’amahoro biva ku Mana Umubyeyi wacu , no kuri Nyagasani Yezu Kristu ,
48001004	witangiye ibyaha byacu ngo aturokore iyi si mbi , akurikije ugushaka kw’Imana , ari Yo Umubyeyi wacu .
48001005	Nahabwe ikuzo uko ibihe bihora bisimburana . Amen .
48001006	Ntangazwa n’ukuntu , mu kanya gato , mutangiye gucika ku wabahamagariye ineza ya Kristu , mugashikira indi Nkuru Nziza .
48001007	Si uko haba hari indi Nkuru Nziza ibaho . Ni uko hadutse abantu bashaka ko muhagarika imitima , bashaka no guhindura Inkuru Nziza ya Kristu .
48001008	Ariko rero , hagize ubigisha Inkuru Nziza itari iyo twabigishije , kabone n’aho yaba umwe muri twe , cyangwa umumalayika umanutse mu ijuru , arakaba ikivume !
48001009	Mbese nk’uko twababwiye , kandi n’ubu ngubu mbisubiyemo : uzabigisha Inkuru Nziza itari iyo mwakiriye , arakaba ikivume !
48001010	Mbese ubu ngubu nkurikiranye gushimwa n’abantu cyangwa n’Imana ? Aho ntimugira ngo mparanira kuneza abantu ? Mbaye nkigamije kuneza abantu , sinaba nkiri umugaragu wa Kristu .
48001011	Mbibamenyeshe rero , bavandimwe , iyo Nkuru Nziza nabigishije si iy’umuntu ,
48001012	si n’umuntu nyikesha , kandi si umuntu wayinyigishije : ni Yezu Kristu wayimpishuriye .
48001013	Mwumvise kandi imigirire yanjye kera nkiri mu kiyahudi : ko natotezaga bikabije Kiliziya y’Imana nshaka kuyitsemba .
48001014	Kandi benshi mu bo tungana , dusangiye n’ubwoko nabarushaga gukurikiza idini ya kiyahudi , nkabasumbya ishyaka mu guharanira umuco karande w’abasokuruza .
48001015	Nyamara umunsi Uwanyitoranyirije nkiri mu nda ya mama , yampamagaye kubw’ineza ye
48001016	ngo ampishurire Umwana we , kugira ngo mwamamaze mu mahanga , ako kanya nahise mpaguruka nta we niriwe ngisha inama ,
48001017	habe no kuzamuka i Yeruzalemu ngo nsange abantanze kuba intumwa ; ahubwo nagiye muri Arabiya , nyuma ngaruka i Damasi .
48001018	Nyuma y’imyaka itatu , ni bwo nazamutse i Yeruzalemu kureba Petero , tumarana iminsi cumi n’itanu .
48001019	Nta yindi ntumwa twabonanye , uretse Yakobo umuvandimwe wa Nyagasani .
48001020	Ibi mbandikira , dore ndi mu maso y’Imana , simbeshya .
48001021	Hanyuma naje mu ntara ya Siriya na Silisiya .
48001022	Kiliziya za Kristu ziri mu Yudeya zari zitarambona ,
48001023	usibye ko zumvaga bavuga ngo « wa wundi wadutotezaga kera , asigaye yamamaza ukwemera yahoze arwanya . »
48001024	Nuko zigasingiza Imana kubera jye .
48002001	Nyuma y’imyaka cumi n’ine , nongera kuzamuka i Yeruzalemu , ndi kumwe na Barinaba , na Tito ndamujyana .
48002002	Nazamutseyo ari uko Imana yabimpishuriye . Mbanyuriramo ibyerekeye Inkuru Nziza nigishaga mu mahanga ; abayobozi bo nyibasobanurira birambuye twiherereye . Kwari ukugira ngo menye niba nirukira cyangwa narirukiye ubusa .
48002003	Yewe , kabone na Tito mugenzi wanjye utari Umuyahudi , ntibamuhatiye kugenywa ;
48002004	nyamara ariko hari indyarya ziyita abavandimwe zitwihishamo ngo zitubuze ubwigenge bwacu twifitiye muri Kristu Yezu , bityo ngo zidusubize mu bucakara .
48002005	Ntitwigeze n’akanya na gato tuganzwa n’abo , kugira ngo ukuri kw’Inkuru Nziza kuzagume muri mwe .
48002006	Naho abayobozi — icyo bari cyo nticyari kinshishikaje kuko Imana itareba ubusumbane bw’abantu — abo bayobozi nta kindi bantegetse .
48002007	Ahubwo ndetse babonye ko nashinzwe kwamamaza Inkuru Nziza mu batagenywe nk’uko Petero yayishinzwe mu bagenywe ,
48002008	kuko Uwahaye Petero kuba intumwa mu bagenywe , ni na We wampaye kuba intumwa mu banyamahanga .
48002009	Nuko Yakobo , Petero na Yohani , kandi ari na bo bitwa inkingi , bamaze kumenya ingabire nahawe , turumvikana baduhereza ukuboko , jyewe na Barinaba , ngo twebwe tujye mu banyamahanga , naho bo mu bagenywe .
48002010	Batwihanangirije ikintu kimwe rudori : ko tuzajya twibuka abakene ; ari na cyo nihatiye gukora .
48002011	Nyamara ariko , ubwo Petero yazaga Antiyokiya , nahanganye na we kuko byari ngombwa kumugaya .
48002012	Koko rero , mbere y’uko haza abantu bo mu gice cya Yakobo , yasangiraga n’abanyamahanga . Aho baziye , aravunura , aritarura , byo gutinya abagenywe .
48002013	N’abandi Bayahudi bigana uburyarya bwe , bigeza aho na Barinaba yoshywa na bo kuryarya bene ako kageni .
48002014	Jye rero mbonye ko batagororokeye ukuri kw’Inkuru Nziza , mbwira Petero bose barora nti « Niba wowe w’Umuyahudi ugenza nk’abanyamahanga aho kugenza kiyahudi , ushobora ute guhatira abanyamahanga kugenza kiyahudi ? »
48002015	Twebwe turi Abayahudi kavukire , ntituri abanyamahanga b’abanyabyaha .
48002016	Tuzi ariko ko umuntu atagirwa intungane no kubahiriza amategeko , ahubwo no kwemera Yezu Kristu byonyine . Natwe rero twemeye Yezu Kristu , ngo tuzagirwe intungane no kwemera Kristu , tutabitewe no kuzuza amategeko kuko nta n’umwe uba intungane abikesheje kubahiriza amategeko .
48002017	Kuba se dushaka kuba intungane muri Kristu , ariko kandi bikagaragara ko natwe ubwacu tukiri abanyabyaha , bizabe byerekana ko Kristu ari we utuma abantu bagwa mu cyaha ? Oya ntibikabe !
48002018	Mbaye ari jye wubaka bundi bushya ibyo nashenye , naba nihamije icyaha .
48002019	Nyamara rero , jyewe napfuye ku byerekeye kugengwa n’amategeko , kandi ari amategeko abinteye , kugira ngo mbeho ngengwa n’Imana . Nabambanywe na Kristu ku musaraba .
48002020	Yego ndiho , ariko mu by'ukuri si jye ukiriho , ahubwo ni Kristu uriho muri jye . Kuba ubu ngubu ndiho mu mubiri , ni uko ndiho mu kwemera Umwana w’Imana wankunze , ubwe akigabiza urupfu ari jye agirira .
48002021	Jye sinasuzuguza ineza y’Imana . Kuko niba ari itegeko rituma umuntu aba intungane , noneho Kristu yapfiriye akamama !
48003001	Mbega ngo muraba abapfu , Banyagalati ! Ni nde wabararuye kandi mwareretswe uko Kristu yabambwe ?
48003002	Ndifuza ko mumenyesha iki cyonyine : ari ukuzuza amategeko , ari no kwakira ukwemera , icyabahesheje Roho ni ikihe ?
48003003	Mbese mwabaye abapfu bigejeje aho ? Mwatangiye ibintu mufashijwe na Roho , none mwibwiye ko bizuzurizwa mu ruhu rw’umubiri ?
48003004	Mbega kuruhira ubusa ? Ubonye n’iyo biba ku busa nyine !
48003005	Mbese nyine , Ubaha Roho , akabakoramo ibitangaza , abigirira ko mwujuje amategeko cyangwa ko mwakiriye ukwemera ?
48003006	Nk’uko Abrahamu yemeye Uhoraho bigatuma aba intungane ,
48003007	mubimenye rero : abemera ni bo bana ba Abrahamu .
48003008	Ibyanditswe byabibonye kare ko Imana izatagatifuza amahanga ku mpamvu y’ukwemera , byo byahanuriye Abrahamu ngo « Imiryango yose y’isi izaguherwamo umugisha . »
48003009	Bityo rero , abemera bahabwa umugisha hamwe na Abrahamu w’umwemezi .
48003010	Naho abitwaza ibikorwa by’amategeko , bikururira umuvumo kuko byanditswe ngo « Arakaba ikivume utuzuza ibyanditswe byose mu Gitabo cy’Amategeko . »
48003011	Ni ikintu kigaragara kandi ko mu maso y’Imana , nta muntu n’umwe waba intungane abikesha amategeko kuko « intungane izabeshwaho n’ukwemera . »
48003012	Amategeko kandi ntahuje n’ukwemera yo avuga ngo « umuntu uzubahiriza ibyo , bizamubeshaho . »
48003013	Kristu yadukijije umuvumo w’amategeko , yihindura umuvumo ari we , ari twe agirira , kuko byanditswe ngo « Umanitse ku giti wese ni umuvumo . »
48003014	Ibyo ari ukugira ngo umugisha wa Abrahamu usesekare ku mahanga muri Kristu Yezu , kandi duhabwe mu kwemera Roho twasezeranijwe .
48003015	Bavandimwe , mvuge mpereye ku mico y’abantu : indagano umuntu akoze , nta wundi uyisesa cyangwa ngo agire icyo ayongeraho .
48003016	Abrahamu rero ni we wahawe amasezerano , we n’urubyaro rwe . Ntibavuga imbyaro ze nk’aho ari nyinshi : ahubwo ni nk’aho ari urubyaro rumwe rukumbi : « n’urubyaro rwawe » , ari rwo Kristu .
48003017	Icyo nshaka kuvuga rero ni iki : indagano ihamye y’Imana nta bwo yaseswa n’itegeko ryashyizweho hashize imyaka magana ane na mirongo itatu ; bibaye ibyo , iyo ndagano yaba ibaye ubusa .
48003018	Kuko iyaba umurage watangwaga ku bw’itegeko , ntibyaba bikibaye ku bw’isezerano . Nyamara ineza Imana yagiriye Abrahamu , yayigiriye isezerano .
48003019	Itegeko rero ni iry’iki ? Ryongereweho hanyuma ngo rijye rigaragaza uwacumuye , kuzageza igihe hazahinguka urubyaro rwagenewe isezerano . Itegeko ryatangajwe n’abamalayika barishinga umuhuza .
48003020	Nyamara umuhuza ntiyabaye uw’umwe . Imana yo ni imwe rukumbi .
48003021	Noneho se , itegeko ryaba ritambamiye amasezerano y’Imana ? Oya ntibikabe ! Iyaba koko haratangajwe itegeko ritanga ubugingo , ubutungane buba mu by’ukuri buriturukaho .
48003022	Ahubwo rero Ibyanditswe byabohesheje byose ingoyi y’icyaha kugira ngo isezerano rizuzurizwe abemera Yezu Kristu .
48003023	Mbere y’uko igihe cy’ukwemera kigera , twari nk’imfungwa turinzwe n’amategeko , dutegereje uko kwemera kwagombaga guhishurwa .
48003024	Bityo rero , amategeko yaradushoreye adushyikiriza Kristu kugira ngo tuzahabwe ubutungane tubikesha ukwemera .
48003025	Ubu rero , kuva aho haziye ukwemera , ntitugishorewe ,
48003026	kuko mwese muri abana b’Imana mubikesha kwemera Kristu Yezu .
48003027	Kandi ni koko , mwebwe mwese ababatijwe muri Kristu , mwambaye Kristu .
48003028	Nta Muyahudi ukiriho , nta Mugereki , nta mucakara , nta mwigenge , nta mugabo , nta mugore , kuko mwese muri umwe muri Kristu Yezu .
48003029	Ubwo rero muri aba Kristu , noneho ni mwe rubyaro rwa Abrahamu , ni mwe rero muzegukana umurage wasezeranywe .
48004001	Dore icyo nshaka kuvuga : igihe cyose uwagenewe umurage akiri muto , nta ho aba atandukaniye n’umugaragu n’ubwo aba ari we mutware wa byose ,
48004002	ahubwo agumya kugengwa n’abamurera n’abashinzwe ibintu bye kugeza igihe se yategetse .
48004003	Natwe ni uko : igihe twari tukiri bato , twategekwaga n’ibigenga isi , twari abagaragu ,
48004004	ariko igihe cyagenwe kigeze , Imana yohereje Umwana wayo , avuka ku mugore , kandi avuka agengwa n’amategeko ,
48004005	kugira ngo acungure abari bakigengwa n’amategeko , maze duhabwe kuba abana Imana yihitiyemo .
48004006	Kandi koko muri abana b’Imana , yo yohereje Roho w’Umwana wayo mu mitima yanyu ngo arangurure ijwi agira ati « Abba , Data . »
48004007	Bityo rero ntukiri umugaragu , ahubwo uri umwana ; kandi ubwo uri umwana , Imana iguha kuba n’umugenerwamurage .
48004008	Kera mutaramenya Imana , mwari abacakara bakorera ibidafite kamere y’Imana .
48004009	Ubu ngubu ariko muzi Imana , ndetse na Yo irabazi . Mwongeye mute kugarukira ibyo bintu bitagira intege , bitagira uko byigira na byo ? Mwakwiyemeza mute kongera kubibera abagaragu bundi bushya ?
48004010	Mwubahiriza imihango n’imiziririzo yerekeye iminsi , amezi , ibihembwe n’imyaka .
48004011	Munteye agahinda , nkibaza niba ntaravunikiye ubusa iwanyu .
48004012	Bavandimwe , ndabinginze , nimumere nkanjye ubwo nanjye nigize nkamwe . Nta kibi mwigeze mungirira .
48004013	Muzi ko nari ndwaye igihe nje kubigisha Inkuru Nziza bwa mbere na mbere .
48004014	Uwo muruho mwatewe n’umubiri wanjye , ntimwigeze muwuhungana ishozi cyangwa ngo muwuvumire ku gahera . Ahubwo mwanyakiriye nk’umumalayika w’Imana , nka Kristu Yezu ubwe .
48004015	Ubu uri he wa munezero ? Jyewe ndahamya rwose ko , iyo biba ibishoboka , muba mwarinogoyemo amaso yanyu ngo muyanyihere .
48004016	Ubu se noneho mbaye umwanzi wanyu kuko mbabwije ukuri ?
48004017	Abo bantu babitayeho cyane , nyamara si icyiza babashakira , kuko bashaka kudutandukanya ngo abe ari bo mwikundira .
48004018	Ni byiza kugira urugwiro , iyo murutewe n’umutima mwiza kandi mukarugira iteka , atari igihe ndi kumwe namwe gusa .
48004019	Twana twanjye , ndacyari ku gise mbabyara kugeza igihe Kristu abaremwemo .
48004020	Iyaba ubu ngubu nari ndi kumwe na mwe , nari kumenya imvugo nakoresha kuko ibyanyu binshobeye .
48004021	Ngaho nimumbwire mwebwe mushaka kugengwa n’amategeko : mbese ntimwumvise amategeko ?
48004022	Koko rero biranditswe ko Abrahamu yagize abahungu babiri ; umwe yavutse ku muja , undi ku mugore utigeze ubuja .
48004023	Ariko uw’umuja yavutse ku bwa kamere mubiri , naho uw’umugore utari umuja avuka ku bw’isezerano .
48004024	Ibyo ni incamarenga . Abo bagore bashushanya amasezerano uko ari abiri : rimwe ryo ku musozi wa Sinayi , rikabyarira ubuja , ni Hagara .
48004025	Hagara ashushanya umusozi Sinayi wo muri Arabiya , ashushanya kandi Yeruzalemu y’ubu ngubu kuko ari umuja , we n’abana be .
48004026	Naho Yeruzalemu yo mu ijuru irigenga , ni yo umubyeyi wacu .
48004027	Koko rero byanditswe ngo « Ishime mugore w’ingumba , wowe utigeze ubyara , rangurura maze uvuze impundu , wowe utamenye ububabare bw’igise , kuko abana b’intabwa baruta ubwinshi ab’ubana n’umugabo » .
48004028	Mwebwe rero , bavandimwe , muri abana b’isezerano nka Izaki .
48004029	Kandi uko byabaye icyo gihe , uwavutse ku bwa kamere mubiri yatotezaga uwavutse ku bwa roho , na n’ubu ni ko bimeze .
48004030	Nyamara se Ibyanditswe bibivugaho iki ? « Irukana umuja n’umuhungu we , umwana w’umuja ntagahabwe umurage hamwe n’umwana w’umugore wigenga » .
48004031	Bityo rero , bavandimwe , ntituri abana b’umuja , turi abana b’umugore wigenga .
48005001	Kristu yaratubohoye kugira ngo tugire ubwo bwigenge . Nimwemarare rero , mwirinde ko umutwaro w’ubucakara wakongera kubagonda ijosi .
48005002	Ngaha jyewe Pawulo ndabibabwiye : muramutse mwigenyesheje , Kristu nta cyo yaba akibamariye .
48005003	Nongeye kandi kwerurira umuntu wese wigenyesha , ko agomba gukurikiza amategeko iyo ava akagera .
48005004	Muzaba mwitandukanije na Kristu rero , nimushakira ubutungane mu mategeko ; muzaba mwivukije ineza .
48005005	Naho twebwe , ni ku bwa Roho no mu kwemera dutegereje ubutungane twizeye .
48005006	Kuko , ku muntu uri muri Kristu , nta cyo bivuze kuba yaragenywe cyangwa atagenywe ; igifite akamaro ahubwo , ni ukwemera kujyana n’urukundo .
48005007	Ko mwirukaga neza , ni nde ubabambiye ngo mudakurikiza ukuri ?
48005008	Igishuko nk’icyo nticyaturuka ku Uwabahamagaye .
48005009	N’ubundi agasemburo gake gatutumbya irobe ryose .
48005010	Jyewe ndabizeye muri Nyagasani , nzi ko mutatekereza ukundi . Naho ubatera guhagarika imitima , uwo azatsindwa n’urubanza , uwo ari we wese .
48005011	Naho jyewe , bavandimwe , niba nkigisha ukugenywa , naba se kandi ngitoterezwa iki ? Ubwo rero , umusaraba nta we waba ugiteye kwibaza .
48005012	Mbese abo babatera guhagarika umutima , bakwishahuye bakamaraho !
48005013	Mwebweho , bavandimwe , mwahamagariwe ubwigenge . Gusa rero ubwigenge ntibukabere umubiri urwitwazo , ahubwo umwe abere undi umugaragu mugirirana urukundo .
48005014	Kuko amategeko yose abumbiye muri iri jambo rimwe rukumbi ngo « Uzakunde mugenzi wawe nkawe ubwawe » .
48005015	Naho niba mushihana , mugacagagurana , muramenye ntimuzamarane .
48005016	Mureke mbabwire : Roho nabayobore , ni bwo mutazakora ibyo umubiri urarikira .
48005017	Kuko umubiri urarikira ibirwanya Roho , na Roho igakurikirana ibyo umubiri wangira . Ibyo byombi koko birazirana ku buryo namwe mutagenza uko mwishakiye kose .
48005018	None rero , niba muyoborwa na Roho , nta bwo mukigengwa n’amategeko .
48005019	Ibikorwa by’umubiri birigaragaza : ubusambanyi , ubuhabara , ubwomanzi ,
48005020	gusenga ibigirwamana , kuroga , kwangana , gukurura intonganya , ishyari , uburakari , kwikuza , amazimwe , amakimbirane ,
48005021	inzika , ubusinzi , ubusambo , n’ibindi nk’ibyo . Ndababuriye nk’uko nigeze kubibabwira : abakora bene ibyo , nta murage bazahabwa mu Ngoma y'Imana .
48005022	Naho imbuto ya Roho ni urukundo : ibyishimo , amahoro , kwihangana , ubugwaneza , ubuntu , ubudahemuka ,
48005023	imico myiza , kumenya kwifata . Nta tegeko ribuza imigirire nk’iyo .
48005024	Aba Kristu Yezu babambye ku musaraba umubiri wabo n’ingeso mbi ndetse n’irari .
48005025	Niba tubeshejweho na Roho , nituyoborwe na Roho .
48005026	Twoye kurarikira ikuzo ry’amanjwe , twirinde gushotorana no kugirirana ishyari .
48006001	Bavandimwe , niba hagize ufatirwa mu cyaha , mwebwe abayoborwa na Roho , nimumuhane ariko mumworoheye . Nawe ubwawe witonde , maze utazavaho ushukwa .
48006002	Nimwakirane imitwaro yanyu , bityo muzaba mwumviye byuzuye itegeko rya Kristu .
48006003	Naho uwakwirebamo kuba akataraboneka , kandi nta cyo ari cyo , uwo yaba yibeshya .
48006004	Ahubwo buri muntu asuzume ibikorwa bye bwite . Niba hari icyo abonye yakwiratana , abikore ku giti cye atigereranya n’abandi .
48006005	Kuko buri wese azitwarira uwe muzigo .
48006006	Uwigishwa ijambo , nahe ku bye byose urimwigisha .
48006007	Ntimuzibeshye : Imana ntireregwa . Icyo umuntu azaba yarabibye ni cyo azasarura .
48006008	Ubibira umubiri , azawusaruraho urupfu . Naho ubibira roho , azayisaruraho ubugingo bw’iteka .
48006009	Nitwihatire gukora icyiza tutadohoka , bityo , niba tudacogoye , tuzasarura igihe kigeze .
48006010	Nuko rero , ubwo tukibifitiye umwanya , nitugirire neza abantu bose , cyane cyane abo dusangiye ukwemera .
48006011	Nimwitegereze noneho izi nyuguti nini : ni jye ubwanjye ubandikira n’ukuboko kwanjye .
48006012	Abashaka gushimwa biratana ibikorwa by’umubiri , abo ngabo ni bo babahatira kugenywa , gusa ngo badatotezwa bahorwa umusaraba wa Kristu .
48006013	Nyamara n’abigenyesha , na bo ubwabo ntibakurikiza amategeko , none barashaka ko mugenywa kugira ngo birate ibyabaye mu mubiri wanyu .
48006014	Naho jyewe nta kindi nakwiratana kitari umusaraba wa Nyagasani wacu Yezu Kristu : ni wo iby’isi bimbambiweho , nanjye nkaba mbibambiweho .
48006015	Kuko nta cyo bimaze kugenywa cyangwa kutagenywa , ahubwo ukuba ikiremwa gishya .
48006016	Abakurikiza iri tegeko bose , bahorane amahoro n’impuhwe , bo na Israheli y’Imana .
48006017	Ahasigaye , ntihakagire undushya , dore ngendana mu mubiri wanjye inguma za Yezu .
48006018	Ineza y’Umwami wacu Yezu Kristu isakare imitima yanyu , bavandimwe . Amen .
49001001	Jyewe Pawulo , intumwa ya Yezu Kristu , uko Imana yabishatse , ku batagatifujwe b’indahemuka muri Yezu Kristu :
49001002	mbifurije ineza n’amahoro biva ku Mana , Umubyeyi wacu , no kuri Nyagasani Yezu Kristu .
49001003	Nihasingizwe Imana , Se w’Umwami wacu Yezu Kristu , Yo yadusakajemo imigisha y’amoko yose , ituruka kuri Roho , mu ijuru , ku bwa Kristu .
49001004	Nguko uko yadutoreye muri We nyine , mbere y’ihangwa ry’ibiriho byose , kugira ngo tuzayihore imbere mu rukundo , turi intungane n’abaziranenge .
49001005	Igena ityo mbere y’igihe , ko tuzayibera abana yihitiyemo , tubikesheje Yezu Kristu . Uko ni ko yabyishakiye ku buntu bwayo ,
49001006	kugira ngo izahore isingirizwa ingabire yaduhereye ubuntu mu Mwana wayo w’Inkoramutima .
49001007	Ni We dukesha ugucunguzwa amaraso ye , tukamuronkeramo imbabazi z’ibyaha byacu , ku rugero rw’ubusendere bw’ineza yayo ,
49001008	ikaba yarabudusesekajemo ibigiranye ubuhanga n’ubumenyi bwose .
49001009	Yaduhishuriye ibanga ry’ugushaka kwayo , wa mugambi wuje urugwiro yari yifitemo kuva kera ,
49001010	ngo izawuzuze ibihe bigeze : umugambi wo gukoranyiriza ibintu byose ku Mutware umwe rukumbi , Kristu , ari ibiri mu ijuru , ari n’ibiri ku isi .
49001011	Ni we kandi twatorewemo tugenwa mbere y’igihe ku buryo buhuye n’umugambi w’Ugenga byose ,
49001012	kugira ngo twebwe abashyize amizero muri Kristu , tubonereho gusingiza ikuzo ryayo .
49001013	Namwe rero , aho mumariye kumvira ijambo ry’ukuri , ari yo Nkuru Nziza y’ugukizwa kwanyu , mukaryemera , ni We mukesha kuba mwarashyizweho ikimenyetso cya Roho Mutagatifu wasezeranywe ,
49001014	ari na We musogongero w’umugabane twagenewe , ubanziriza icungurwa ry’umuryango Imana yironkeye , ngo ihore isingirizwa ikuzo ryayo .
49001015	Ni cyo gituma nanjye , kuva aho menyeye ukwemera mufitiye Nyagasani Yezu , n’urukundo mugirira abatagatifujwe bose ,
49001016	ntahwema gushimira Imana kubera mwe , mbibuka mu masengesho yanjye .
49001017	Imana y’Umwami wacu Yezu Kristu , Yo Mubyeyi wuje ikuzo , nibahe umutima w’ubwenge n’ubujijuke , maze muyimenye rwose .
49001018	Ubonye yamurikiye amaso y’umutima wanyu , mugasobanukirwa n’ukwizera mukesha ubutorwe bwanyu , n’ikuzo rihebuje muzigamiweho umurage hamwe n’abatagatifujwe ,
49001019	mugasobanukirwa kandi n’ububasha bwayo butagereranywa yadusesuyeho , twebwe abemera !
49001020	Izo mbaraga zitagira urugero yanazigaragarije muri Kristu , igihe imuzuye mu bapfuye , ikamwicaza iburyo bwayo mu ijuru ,
49001021	hejuru y’ibyitwa Ibikomangoma , Ibihangange , Ibinyabubasha n’Ibinyabutegetsi byose , ndetse no hejuru y’irindi zina ryose ryashobora kuvugwa ubu no mu bihe bizaza .
49001022	« Ishyira rero byose mu nsi y’ibirenge bye » , kandi mbere ya byose imugira umutwe wa Kiliziya ,
49001023	ari yo mubiri n’umusendero w’Uwo Imana ubwayo isendereyemo ku buryo bwose .
49002001	Namwe kandi mwari mwarapfuye muzize ibicumuro n’ibyaha mwiberagamo kera ,
49002002	igihe mwakurikizaga imigenzo y’iyi si , n’Umugenga w’ibyo mu nsi y’ikirere , wa mwuka ukorera mu bagomera Imana . . .
49002003	Kandi natwe twese kera twari tumeze nka bo , dukurikira irari ry’umubiri wacu , dukora gusa ibyo umubiri ushaka n’ibyifuzo byawo bibi ; yewe , ku bwacu twari twikururiye uburakari bw’Imana kimwe na bo .
49002004	Ariko Imana ni Nyir’impuhwe zihebuje ; kubera urukundo rwinshi yadukunze ,
49002005	n’ubwo twari twarapfuye tuzize ibyaha byacu bwose , yadushubije ubugingo hamwe na Kristu : rwose , kuba mwarakijijwe , mubikesha ubuntu bwayo !
49002006	Nuko hamwe na We iratuzura , maze itwicaza mu ijuru turi muri Kristu Yezu .
49002007	Bityo , igiriye ubuntu bwayo yatugaragarije muri Yezu Kristu , yashatse kwerekana mu bihe bizaza ubukungu butagereranywa bw’ineza yayo .
49002008	Koko mwakijijwe ku buntu , mubikesha ukwemera ; nta bwo ari ku bwanyu rero , ahubwo ni ku bw’ingabire y’Imana .
49002009	Ntibyatewe n’ibyo mwakoze , kugira ngo hatazagira uwirata .
49002010	Koko rero , Imana ni Yo yaduhanze , kandi twaremewe muri Kristu Yezu , kugira ngo dushishikarire ibikorwa byiza Imana yateguye kuva kera igira ngo bijye bituranga iteka .
49002011	Nuko rero , mwebwe b’abanyamahanga , mwebwe abasuzugurwaga n’Abayahudi kubera umubiri wanyu utagenywe warangaga ukutemera kwanyu , naho bo bakiratana iryo genywa ryabo ryakozwe n’abantu ,
49002012	nimwibuke uko mwari mumeze kera : icyo gihe mwari mwibereye aho mutagira Umukiza , nta sano mufitanye na Israheli , nta ho muhuriye n’Amasezerano y’Imana , ndetse mutanayizi , kandi nta cyo mwizeye kuri iyi si .
49002013	Naho ubu ngubu , muri Yezu Kristu , mwebwe abari kure y’Imana kera , mwigijwe bugufi yayo mubikesha amaraso ya Kristu .
49002014	Koko rero ni We mahoro yacu ; Abayahudi n’abatari bo yabahurije mu muryango umwe , maze aca urwango rwabatandukanyaga , rwari rumeze nk’urukuta ruri hagati yabo .
49002015	Yakuyeho itegeko n’amabwiriza ariherekeza , kimwe n’imigenzo yabyo , kugira ngo bombi , ari Umuyahudi , ari n’utari we , abahindure umuntu umwe mushya muri We , bityo agarure amahoro ,
49002016	maze bombi abagire umubiri umwe , abagorore n’Imana abigirishije umusaraba we , awutsembeshe inzangano zose .
49002017	Yazanywe no kubamamazamo inkuru nziza y’amahoro , mwebwe mwari kure , kimwe n’abari hafi .
49002018	Ubu rero twese , uko twari amoko abiri , tumukesha guhinguka imbere y’Imana Data , tubumbwe na Roho umwe .
49002019	Nuko rero ntimukiri abanyamahanga n’abasuhuke ; ahubwo musangiye ubwenegihugu n’abatagatifujwe , mubarirwa mu muryango w’Imana .
49002020	Muri inzu yubatswe mu kibanza cy’intumwa n’abahanuzi , maze Yezu Kristu ubwe akaba ibuye riyishyigikira .
49002021	Ibimwubatseho byose bizamuka bisobekeranye neza , bigahinduka ingoro ntagatifu ibereye Nyagasani .
49002022	Namwe kandi ni We mukesha gusobekwa kuri iyo nzu imwubatseho , kugira ngo muhinduke ingoro y’Imana ku bwa Roho Mutagatifu .
49003001	Ngicyo igituma , jyewe Pawulo , ndi imbohe ya Kristu Yezu kubera mwebwe , abavuye ishyanga . . .
49003002	Ngira ngo mwamenye ingabire Imana yampaye ku buntu , ari mwe ibigirira , kugira ngo isohoze umugambi wayo ,
49003003	ikampishurira ibanga ryayo nk’uko maze kubibandikira muri make .
49003004	Nimubisoma , muziyumvira ubwanyu ukuntu nacengewe n’ibanga rya Kristu .
49003005	Iryo banga , Imana ntiyigeze iribwira abantu bo hambere , nk’uko ubu imaze kurihishurira intumwa zayo ntagatifu n’abahanuzi bayo , ku bwa Roho Mutagatifu .
49003006	None dore n’abanyamahanga na bo bemerewe gusangira umurage umwe natwe , bakaba ingingo z’umubiri umwe hamwe natwe , kandi bakabona uruhare ku isezerano rimwe hamwe natwe muri Kristu Yezu , babikesha Inkuru Nziza .
49003007	Kandi iyo Nkuru Nziza ni yo nshinzwe kwamamaza ku bw’ingabire Imana yampaye ku buntu no ku bubasha bwayo .
49003008	Jyewe w’intamenyekana mu batagatifujwe bose , nahawe iyo ngabire yo kogeza mu banyamahanga ibyiza bitagereranywa bituruka kuri Kristu ,
49003009	no gusobanurira bose ukuntu Imana isohoza wa mugambi wari uhishe kuva kera na kare muri Yo , Rurema wahanze ibintu byose .
49003010	Bityo , guhera ubu ngubu , Ibikomangoma n’Ibihangange byo mu ijuru bimenyera kuri Kiliziya ubuhanga bw’Imana buteye kwinshi ,
49003011	nk’uko yabigambiriye kuva kera na kare muri Kristu Yezu Umwami wacu .
49003012	Nuko ku bw’ukwemera tumufitiye , duhabwa gutunguka imbere y’Imana tuyiringiye .
49003013	Ni cyo gituma mbinginga ngo mwoye gucika intege mubitewe n’amagorwa ndimo mbaruhira , kuko ari yo abahesha ishema .
49003014	Ngiyo impamvu itumye mpfukama imbere y’Imana Data ,
49003015	Yo icyitwa ububyeyi cyose gikomokaho , ari mu ijuru , ari no ku isi ,
49003016	ikaba na Nyir’ikuzo ryose , nkabasabira kugira ngo ibatere imbaraga ibigirishije Roho wayo , inakomeze umutima wa buri wese .
49003017	Kristu nabaturemo mubikesha ukwemera ; mushore imizi mu rukundo , murushingemo n’imiganda ,
49003018	maze hamwe n’abatagatifujwe bose , mushobore gusobanukirwa n’urukundo ruhebuje rwa Kristu , mumenye ubugari n’uburebure , ubujyejuru n’ubujyakuzimu byarwo .
49003019	Ni bwo muzagera ku bumenyi busumba byose bw’urwo rukundo , maze musenderezwemo mutyo ubukungahare bw’Imana .
49003020	Nyir’ububasha bwose , ugirira muri mwe ibyiza bisumba kure cyane ibyo twasaba , ndetse n’ibyo twakwibwira ,
49003021	naherwe ikuzo muri Kiliziya no muri Kristu Yezu , uko amasekuruza n’ibihe bigenda bisimburana iteka ! Amen .
49004001	Ubu rero , jyewe uri ku ngoyi nzira Nyagasani , ndabinginga ngo mugenze mu buryo bukwiranye n’ubutore bwanyu :
49004002	nimubane mu rukundo , murangwe n’ubwiyoroshye , n’ituze , n’ubwiyumanganye , mwihanganirane muri byose ,
49004003	kandi mwihatire kugumana umutima umwe ubahuza mu mahoro .
49004004	Nk’uko Umubiri ari umwe na Roho akaba umwe , ni na ko mwahamagariwe gusangira ukwizera kumwe .
49004005	Nyagasani ni umwe , ukwemera ni kumwe , batisimu ni imwe ;
49004006	n’Imana ni imwe , Yo Mubyeyi wa bose , usumba bose , agakorera muri bose , kandi agatura muri bose .
49004007	Buri wese muri twe yahawe ingabire ye bwite , uko Kristu yayimugeneye .
49004008	Ni cyo gituma mu Byanditswe hari ahavuga ngo « Yarazamutse atumbagira ashoreye imbohe , maze aha abantu ingabire » .
49004009	Kuba yarazamutse bivuga iki atari uko yabanje kumanuka akagera ku isi yacu ?
49004010	Uwari waramanutse ni na We wazamutse mu bushorishori bw’ijuru kugira ngo aganze muri byose .
49004011	Ni na We wahaye bamwe kuba intumwa , abandi abaha kuba abahanuzi , abandi abaha kuba abogezabutumwa , abandi abaha kuba abashumba cyangwa se abigisha .
49004012	Nguko uko yatunganyije abatagatifujwe be , anabategurira gukomeza umurimo bashinzwe wo kungura umubiri wa Kristu ,
49004013	kugeza igihe twese tuzunga ubumwe mu kwemera no mu kumenya Umwana w’Imana , tukazaba abantu bashyitse , bageze ku rugero ruhamye , ruyingayinga igihagararo cya Kristu .
49004014	Ubwo rero ntituzaba tukiri abana basabayangwa , maze ngo twangaranwe n’umuyaga ubonetse wose w’inyigisho ziturutse ku buhendanyi bw’abantu no ku buriganya bwabo bubayobya .
49004015	Ahubwo nitubaho mu rukundo rutaryarya , tuzakura kandi twiyongere ubudahwema twifatanyije na Kristu utubereye umutwe .
49004016	Ni We uha umubiri wose gutera hamwe mu ngingo nyinshi ziwugize , zikawutunga , zikawucunga , buri rugingo ku rugero rwarwo , akanawuha gukura no kwiyubaka mu rukundo .
49004017	Dore rero icyo mbabwira kandi mbashishikariza muri Nyagasani : ntimuzongere kugenza nk’abatazi Imana , bikurikirira ubupfu bwabo .
49004018	Koko ibitekerezo byabo bigandiyemo umwijima ; bitandukanyije n’ubugingo buva ku Mana kubera ubujiji baterwa no kunangira umutima wabo ;
49004019	bataye isoni maze biroha mu busambanyi , bigeza aho batwarwa n’ingeso mbi zose nta cyo bikanga .
49004020	Mwebweho si uko mwigishijwe kumenya Kristu :
49004021	niba koko ari We mwabwiwe , niba ari We mwigishijwe kumenya , mukumva ibihuje n’ukuri kuganje muri Yezu .
49004022	Mugomba rero guca ukubiri n’imibereho yanyu yo hambere , mukivanamo imigenzereze ya muntu w’igisazira ugenda yiyangiza mu byifuzo bibi bimuroha .
49004023	Ahubwo nimuvugurure imitima yanyu hamwe n’ibitekerezo byanyu ,
49004024	muhinduke muntu mushya waremwe uko Imana ibishaka mu budakemwa no mu butungane nyakuri .
49004025	Nibitume rero mucika ku binyoma , buri muntu abwire mugenzi we ukuri , kuko bamwe turi ingingo z’abandi .
49004026	Nimufatwa n’uburakari , ntibikabaviremo gucumura ; izuba ntirikarenge mugifite umujinya .
49004027	Ntimugahe Sekibi urwaho .
49004028	Uwari umujura ntakongere kwiba , ahubwo ajye yihatira gukoresha amaboko ye imirimo ifite akamaro , kugira ngo abone n’icyo afashisha abari mu bukene .
49004029	Ntihakagire ijambo ribi riva mu kanwa kanyu , ahubwo hajye hava ijambo ryiza ryahumuriza abandi , rikagirira akamaro abaryumva .
49004030	Muramenye , ntimugashavuze Roho Mutagatifu w’Imana , wa wundi mwahawe ngo abe ikimenyetso kizabaranga ku munsi w’ukubohorwa kwanyu .
49004031	Icyitwa ubwisharirize cyose , n’umwaga , n’uburakari , n’intonganya , no gutukana , kimwe n’icyitwa ububisha cyose , bicibwe muri mwe .
49004032	Ahubwo nimugirirane ineza n’impuhwe , mubabarirane ibyaha nk’uko Imana yabababariye muri Kristu .
49005001	Nimwigane rero Imana , ubwo muri abana bayo ikunda ;
49005002	mujye mukundana nk’uko Kristu yadukunze , maze ubwe akatwitangira aba igitambo n’ituro bimeze nk’umubavu uhumura neza , bigashimisha Imana .
49005003	Naho ibyerekeye ubusambanyi , ubwandavure iyo buva bukagera , kimwe n’ubugugu , ibyo ntibikanavugwe muri mwe ; ni ko bikwiye mu batagatifujwe .
49005004	Kandi amagambo ateye isoni , ay’amanjwe , n’amahomvu , na byo ni uko ; ahubwo muhore mushimira Imana .
49005005	Koko rero mubimenye neza : nta musambanyi , cyangwa uwandavuye , cyangwa umunyabugugu — we uhindura iby’isi ikigirwamana cye — , abo bose , nta wuzagira umugabane mu Ngoma ya Kristu n’Imana .
49005006	Kandi ntihazagire ubahendesha amagambo atagira aho ashingiye , kuko ari ibyo ngibyo bitera Imana kurakarira abayigomera .
49005007	Ntimugafatanye n’abo bantu .
49005008	Koko rero , kera mwigeze kuba umwijima , naho ubu ngubu mwagizwe urumuri muri Nyagasani ; nimugenze nk’abana b’urumuri .
49005009	Imbuto kandi y’urumuri ni icyitwa ubugiraneza cyose , n’ubutungane n’ukuri .
49005010	Nimushishoze , mumenye ibishimisha Nyagasani .
49005011	Mureke kugira uruhare ku bikorwa by’umwijima bitagira icyo bibyara , ahubwo mubyamagane ;
49005012	kuko ibyo bene abo bakora rwihishwa , yewe ndetse no kubivuga biteye isoni .
49005013	Mubyamagane rero , maze mubishyire ku mugaragaro , kuko urumuri rugaragaza byose uko bimeze .
49005014	Ni cyo gituma bajya bavuga ngo « Kanguka , wowe usinziriye ! Haguruka , uve mu bapfuye , maze Kristu akumurikire ! »
49005015	Nuko rero nimwitondere imibereho yanyu , ntimube abapfayongo , ahubwo mube abantu bashyira mu gaciro ,
49005016	bakoresha neza igihe barimo , kuko iminsi ari mibi .
49005017	Ntimukabe rero abapfu , ahubwo mwihatire kumenya icyo Nyagasani ashaka .
49005018	Ntimugasindishwe na divayi , kuko byabatera kwifata nabi , ahubwo nimwuzure Roho Mutagatifu .
49005019	Nimufatanye kuvuga zaburi , ibisingizo n’indirimbo mubwirijwe na Roho Mutagatifu ; muririmbe , mwogeze Nyagasani n’umutima wanyu wose .
49005020	Igihe cyose no muri byose , mushimire Imana Data mu izina ry’Umwami wacu Yezu Kristu .
49005021	Mujye mworoherana kubera igitinyiro mufitiye Kristu .
49005022	Abagore borohere abagabo babo nk’aho babigirira Nyagasani ;
49005023	koko rero umugabo agenga umugore we , nk’uko Kristu agenga Kiliziya akanayibera umutwe ukiza umubiri wose .
49005024	Nk’uko rero Kiliziya yumvira Kristu , bityo n’abagore nibajye bumvira abagabo babo muri byose .
49005025	Namwe bagabo , nimukunde abagore banyu , nk’uko Kristu yakunze Kiliziya , maze akayitangira .
49005026	Yarayitagatifuje , ayisukuza amazi n’ijambo ribiherekeza ,
49005027	kugira ngo ayihingutse imbere ye , ibengerana , nta bwandu n’iminkanyari , cyangwa indi nenge , ahubwo ari Kiliziya ntagatifu kandi itagira amakemwa .
49005028	Nguko uko abagabo bagomba gukunda abagore babo , mbese nk’imibiri yabo bwite . Ukunda umugore we aba yikunze ubwe .
49005029	Koko rero nta wigeze yanga umubiri we , ahubwo arawugaburira , akawitaho cyane , mbese nk’uko na Kristu agenzereza Kiliziya .
49005030	Muyobewe se ko turi ingingo z’umubiri we , ( nk’uko Ibyanditswe bivuga ngo )
49005031	« Ni cyo gituma umugabo azasiga se na nyina , akifatanya n’umugore we , bakaba umubiri umwe » .
49005032	Iryo yobera rirakomeye , cyakora ibyo mbivuze nzirikana Kristu na Kiliziya .
49005033	Nuko rero namwe , buri mugabo nakunde umugore we uko yikunda , n’umugore yubahe umugabo we .
49006001	Bana , nimwumvire ababyeyi muri Nyagasani , kuko ari byo bikwiye .
49006002	« Wubahe so na nyoko » ; mu mategeko yose ni ryo rya mbere rijyana n’isezerano :
49006003	« kugira ngo uzagire ihirwe , kandi urambe ku isi » .
49006004	Namwe babyeyi , ntimugakure umutima abana banyu , ahubwo mubarere neza , mubakosore kandi mubagire inama zikomoka kuri Nyagasani .
49006005	Bacakara namwe , nimwumvire ba shobuja ba hano ku isi ; mujye mububaha kandi mubatinye , nta buryarya ku mutima , nk’aho mwakumviye Kristu ubwe .
49006006	Ntimugakorere ijisho nk’abashaka gushimisha abantu , ahubwo mugenze nk’abagaragu ba Kristu , baharanira gukora icyo Imana ishaka .
49006007	Mushishikarire kurangiza ibyo mutegetswe , nk’aho mwaba mukorera Nyagasani , atari abantu mubigirira .
49006008	Umuntu wese , yaba umucakara , yaba uwigenga , muzi ko icyiza azaba yakoze , azakiturwa na Nyagasani .
49006009	Namwe ba shebuja , mujye mubagenzereza mutyo , mureke kubakangisha ibihano ; muzi neza ko Shebuja wabo n’uwanyu ari mu ijuru , We utarobanura abantu .
49006010	Ahasigaye rero , nimugire ubutwari muri Nyagasani , mugire imbaraga ze zibashoboza byose .
49006011	Nimwambare intwaro zikomoka ku Mana , kugira ngo mubashe guhangara imitego ya Sekibi .
49006012	Erega abanzi turwana si abantu , ahubwo abo turwana ni Ibikomangoma , n’Ibihangange , n’Abagenga b’iyi si y’umwijima , n’izindi roho mbi zo mu kirere .
49006013	Nuko rero nimwitwaze intwaro z’Imana , kugira ngo muzashobore gukomera ku munsi mubi , muzatsinde mudacogoye .
49006014	Ngaho rero , nimuhagarare gitwari ! Ukuri mukugire nk’umukandara mukenyeje , ubutungane mubwambare nk’ikoti ry’icyuma ,
49006015	umwete wo kogeza Inkuru Nziza y’amahoro ubabere nk’inkweto mu birenge .
49006016	Ariko cyane cyane muhorane ukwemera , kubabere nk’ingabo izazimya imyambi igurumana ya Nyakibi .
49006017	Nimwakire ingofero y’Umukiro , n’inkota muhawe na Roho , ari yo Jambo ry’Imana .
49006018	Igihe cyose muhore musenga kandi mwambaza ku buryo bwose mubwirijwe na Roho ; mubyitondere kandi musabire ubutitsa abatagatifujwe bose .
49006019	Nanjye munsabire kugira ngo mpabwe imbaraga zo kuvuga nshize amanga , namamaza iyobera ry’Inkuru Nziza
49006020	mbereye intumwa n’ubwo ndi mu munyururu bwose . Icyampa ngo nshobore kuvuga ibyayo nshize amanga , uko mbigomba .
49006021	Kugira ngo mumenye uko meze n’icyo nkora , mbatumyeho Tushiko , umuvandimwe nkunda , akaba n’umufasha wanjye w’indahemuka muri Nyagasani .
49006022	Mubatumyeho rero , kugira ngo abamenyeshe ibinyerekeyeho byose , kandi ngo ahumurize imitima yanyu .
49006023	Abavandimwe nibagire amahoro , n’urukundo hamwe n’ukwemera biva ku Mana Data no kuri Nyagasani Yezu Kristu .
49006024	Abakunda Umwami wacu Yezu Kristu bose baragahorana ineza ye mu rukundo rudatezuka .
50001001	Twebwe Pawulo na Timote , abagaragu ba Yezu Kristu , ku batagatifujwe bose muri Yezu Kristu bari i Filipi , hamwe n’abayobozi babo n’abadiyakoni babo :
50001002	tubifurije ineza n’amahoro biva ku Mana Umubyeyi wacu , no kuri Nyagasani Yezu Kristu .
50001003	Nshimira Imana yanjye igihe cyose mbibutse , no mu masengesho yanjye yose
50001004	buri gihe mbasabira mwese nishimye ,
50001005	kubera uruhare mwagize mu kwamamaza Inkuru Nziza kuva ku munsi wa mbere kugeza ubu .
50001006	Sinshidikanya rero ko Imana yabatangiyemo uwo murimo mwiza , izanawukomeza kugeza ku munsi Yezu Kristu azaziraho .
50001007	Ngibyo ibitekerezo mbafitiye mwese , kandi koko birakwiye , kuko mbahoza ku mutima , mwebwe muhora mwifatanyije nanjye mu neza yose Imana yangiriye , haba ubu ndi mu buroko , haba n’igihe twarwaniraga Inkuru Nziza , ngo ikomere .
50001008	Koko ndabakunda n’umutima wanjye wose , wuzuye urukundo rwa Yezu Kristu : Imana ubwayo nyitanzeho umugabo !
50001009	Icyo mbasabira rero ni uko urukundo rwanyu rwakomeza kwiyongera , mu bwenge no mu bumenyi bwose ,
50001010	kugira ngo mushobore guhitamo ibitunganye . Bityo muzabe abaziranenge n’indahemuka kugera ku munsi wa Kristu ,
50001011	maze muzere imbuto z’ubutungane zituruka kuri Kristu , zigahesha Imana ikuzo n’ishimwe .
50001012	Bavandimwe , ndashaka kubamenyesha ko ibyangwiririye byatumye ndetse Inkuru Nziza ijya mbere ,
50001013	ku buryo byagaragaye imbere y’urukiko rukuru n’imbere ya rubanda rwose , ko ndi mu buroko kubera Kristu ,
50001014	kandi ingoyi ndiho yatumye abavandimwe benshi barushaho kwizera Nyagasani , batinyuka kwamamaza ijambo ry’Imana nta mususu .
50001015	N’ubwo bamwe bagenza batyo babitewe n’ishyari no gushaka kurushanwa , abandi bamamaje Kristu babitewe n’umutima mwiza koko .
50001016	Bamwe babikorana urukundo , kuko bazi neza ko mbereyeho kurengera Inkuru Nziza .
50001017	Naho abandi bakamamaza Kristu bahimana kandi baryarya , bibwira ko bongera ububabare nterwa n’ingoyi ndiho .
50001018	Ariko se bitwaye iki ? Uko biri kose , baryarya cyangwa se babikora babikuye ku mutima , mpfa ko Kristu yamamazwa , ngicyo ikinshimisha . Ndetse bizakomeza kunshimisha iteka ,
50001019	kuko nzi neza ko ari byo bizangeza ku mukiro mbikesha amasengesho yanyu n’inkunga ya Roho wa Yezu Kristu .
50001020	Icyo ntegereje kandi nizeye ndashidikanya , ni uko ntazakorwa n’isoni ahubwo ubu n’iteka ryose nzahesha Kristu ikuzo nta mususu , haba mu bugingo bwanjye , haba mu rupfu rwanjye .
50001021	Koko rero , Kristu ni we bugingo bwanjye ndetse gupfa byambera urwunguko .
50001022	Niba ariko gukomeza kubaho muri uyu mubiri byatuma nkora umurimo w’ingirakamaro , simbona icyo nahitamo . . .
50001023	Ndagirijwe impande zombi : nifuzaga kwigendera ngo mbane na Kristu , kuko ari byo birushijeho kuba byiza ;
50001024	ariko gukomeza kubaho mu mubiri ni cyo mukeneye .
50001025	Mu by’ukuri , nzi neza ko nzakomeza kubaho , kandi nkagumana namwe , kugira ngo mujye mbere kandi mushimishwe n’ukwemera kwanyu ;
50001026	bityo , nimbagarukamo , bizababere impamvu yo kwishimana kurushaho muri Kristu Yezu .
50001027	Nyamara rero , nimukore ibikwiranye n’Inkuru Nziza ya Kristu . Bityo , nindamuka nje maze nkababona , cyangwa se nintahaba , nzumve ko mukomeye mufite ubumwe , kandi ko muhuje umutima mugafatanyiriza hamwe kurwanira ukwemera mukesha Inkuru Nziza .
50001028	Ababarwanya rero ntibakabatere ubwoba na busa ; maze ibyo bizabumvishe ko bazorekwa , naho mwebwe mukazarokorwa mubikesha Imana .
50001029	Kuko mutahawe gusa kwemera Kristu , mwahawe no kubabara ari We mugirira ,
50001030	ubwo mumurwanira intambara imwe n’iyanjye , nk’uko mwabimbonanye , kandi mukaba mubinyumvaho ubu .
50002001	Niba rero inkunga yanyu iri muri Kristu , niba koko mutera imbere mu rukundo , niba koko muhuriye kuri Roho Mutagatifu , niba kandi mufite umutima w’impuhwe ,
50002002	ngaho nimunsenderezemo ibyishimo , mutekereza kimwe , muhuje urukundo , muhuje n’umutima , murangamiye bimwe .
50002003	Ntimukagire icyo mukora mubitewe n’ishyari cyangwa ukwikuza , ahubwo mwicishe bugufi , buri muntu yibwire ko abandi bamuruta .
50002004	Mwoye guharanira ibyanyu gusa , ahubwo mwite no ku by’abandi .
50002005	Nimugire mu mitima yanyu amatwara ahuje n’aya Kristu Yezu ubwe :
50002006	N’ubwo we yari afite imimerere imwe n’iy’Imana , ntiyagundiriye kureshya na Yo .
50002007	Ahubwo yihinduye ubusabusa , yigira nk’umugaragu , maze mu migirire ye agaragaza ko ari umuntu . Nuko aho amariye kwishushanya n’abantu ,
50002008	yicisha bugufi kurushaho , yemera kumvira , ageza aho gupfa , apfiriye ndetse ku musaraba .
50002009	Ni cyo cyatumye Imana imukuza , imuha Izina risumbye ayandi yose ,
50002010	kugira ngo nibamara kumva izina rya Yezu , bose bamupfukamire , mu ijuru , ku isi n’ikuzimu ,
50002011	kandi indimi zose zamamaze ko Yezu Kristu ari We Nyagasani , biheshe Imana Se ikuzo .
50002012	None rero nkoramutima zanjye , ubwo mutahwemye kumvira igihe nari mpari , n’ubu ngubu ndahari mubikomeze ndetse murusheho ; ngaho nimushishikarire uburokorwe bwanyu mufite ubwoba kandi mudagadwa ,
50002013	kuko Imana ari yo ibatera gushaka no gukora ikiyishimisha .
50002014	Mukore byose mutinuba kandi mutagingimiranya ,
50002015	kugira ngo mube indakemwa n’indahinyuka , mube n’abana b’Imana bazira inenge rwagati mu bantu b’indyarya kandi bararutse , mukamurika muri bo nk’inyenyeri mu kirere ,
50002016	kubera iryo jambo ry’ubugingo mwifitemo . Bityo ku munsi wa Kristu , bizambere ikuzo kuba ntarirukiye ubusa kandi ntaravunikiye ubusa .
50002017	Kandi n’aho byaba ngombwa ko mena amaraso yanjye , akamishwa ku gitambo no ku ituro ry’ukwemera kwanyu , byanshimisha , kandi nasangira namwe mwese ibyo byishimo .
50002018	Bityo , namwe nimwishime , kandi muhimbarwe hamwe nanjye .
50002019	Icyakora nizeye muri Nyagasani Yezu kuboherereza bidatinze Timote , kugira ngo nanjye nimenya amakuru yanyu , nshyire umutima hamwe .
50002020	Mu by’ukuri nta wundi mfite duhuje umutima , wakwita ku byanyu koko :
50002021	kuko abandi bose bakurikira ibiri ibyabo , aho gukurikira ibya Yezu Kristu .
50002022	Naho we , muzi agaciro ke , n’ukuntu yagokeye Inkuru Nziza hamwe nanjye nk’uko umwana agokana na se .
50002023	Nizeye kumuboherereza , nkimara kubona aho ibyanjye byerekeye .
50002024	Byongeye nizeye rwose muri Nyagasani ko nanjye nzaza iwanyu bidatinze .
50002025	Ariko nasanze ari ngombwa kuboherereza Epaforoditi , umuvandimwe wanjye dusangiye umurimo n’intambara , mwari mwanyoherereje ngo anyunganire mu byo nkeneye ,
50002026	kuko yari abakumbuye mwese , akanashavuzwa n’uko mwumvise ko yarwaye .
50002027	Ni koko , yararwaye yenda gupfa , ariko Imana iramubabarira ; nyamara si we yababariye gusa , emwe nanjye , kugira ngo noye guhora nicwa n’agahinda .
50002028	Nihutiye rero kumuboherereza , kugira ngo nimumubona mwongere kwishima , nanjye kandi ako gahinda ngakire .
50002029	Nimumwakirane rero ibyishimo muri Nyagasani , kandi mugirire icyubahiro umuntu nk’uwo .
50002030	Yari agiye gupfa azize umurimo wa Kristu , yitanga atizigamye kugira ngo abasimbure mu byo mutari mubashije kumfasha .
50003001	Ahasigaye , bavandimwe banjye , nimwishimire muri Nyagasani . Ntibinduhije kongera kubibandikira , kandi bibafitiye akamaro .
50003002	Mwirinde izo mbwa ! Mwirinde abo bagiranabi ! Mwirinde abirata ko bagenywe !
50003003	Burya ni twe twagenywe by’ukuri , twe dusenga Imana ku bwa Roho wayo , twe dufite ikuzo ryacu muri Yezu Kristu , aho kwiringira umubiri .
50003004	Icyakora jyewe ubwanjye simbuze impamvu zo kwiringira iby’umubiri , ndetse nzirusha uwo ari we wese wabyiringira :
50003005	Jyewe , wagenywe ku munsi wa munani , nkaba uwo mu muryango wa Israheli no mu nzu ya Benyamini , Umuhebureyi ukomoka ku Bahebureyi , n’Umufarizayi mu byerekeye Amategeko !
50003006	Ku byerekeye umwete , natoteje Kiliziya ; naho ku byerekeye ubutungane bukeshwa amategeko , simpinyuka .
50003007	Ariko ibyo byose byampeshaga agaciro , nasanze ari igihombo , kubera Kristu .
50003008	Ndetse nsanga ko ibintu byose ari igihombo ubigereranije n’icyiza gisumba byose ari cyo kumenya Umwami wanjye Yezu Kristu . Kubera We nemeye guhara byose no kubyita umwanda , kugira ngo nunguke Kristu ,
50003009	maze nzamusange ntishingikirije ubutungane bwanjye bukomoka ku Mategeko , ahubwo mfite ubutungane bukomoka ku kwemera Kristu , buva ku Mana , bukaba bushingiye ku kwemera .
50003010	Igisigaye ni ukumumenya , We wazukanye ububasha , no kwifatanya na We mu bubabare bwe , ndetse no kwishushanya na We mu rupfu rwe ,
50003011	kugira ngo nibishoboka , nanjye nzagere ku izuka mu bapfuye .
50003012	Si ukuvuga ko ubu ibyo nabigezeho , cyangwa ko naba narabaye intungane , ahubwo ndatwaza ngo nsingire Yezu Kristu , mbese nk’uko We ubwe yansingiriye .
50003013	Koko , bavandimwe , sinemeza ko nabigezeho ; icyo mparanira ni kimwe gusa : ibyashize ndabyihorera nkihatira ibizaza .
50003014	Ntwaza rero ngana intego , ya ngororano Imana iduhamagarira mu ijuru muri Kristu Yezu .
50003015	Twese abagamije ubutungane , tugenze dutyo ; niba kandi mubyumva ukundi , na byo Imana izabibamurikira .
50003016	Aho tugereje rero , dufatanye gukomeza inzira imwe .
50003017	Mwese , bavandimwe , mugenze nkanjye , kandi mwitegereze abakurikira urugero tubahaye .
50003018	Koko rero nabibabwiye kenshi , kandi n’ubu ndabivugana amarira : hariho benshi bagenza nk’abanzi b’umusaraba wa Kristu .
50003019	Amaherezo yabo ni ukorama ; kuko inda yabo bayigize Imana yabo , maze bakikuriza mu byagombaga kubatera isoni , bo baharanira iby’isi gusa .
50003020	Twebweho , iwacu ni mu ijuru ; ni ho hazaturuka Umukiza dutegereje , Umwami wacu Yezu Kristu ,
50003021	We uzahindura ukundi umubiri wacu wa gitindi , ugasa n’umubiri we wakirana ikuzo , akoresheje ububasha afite bwo kwigarurira byose .
50004001	Nuko rero , bavandimwe banjye nkunda kandi nkumbuye cyane , mwebwe byishimo byanjye n’ingororano yanjye , nimukomere mutyo muri Nyagasani , nkoramutima zanjye !
50004002	Ndasaba Evodiya kandi ndinginga Sintike ngo bashyire hamwe muri Nyagasani .
50004003	Nawe rero , Sizugo , mugenzi wanjye w’indahinyuka , ndakwinginga ngo ubafashe , kuko bantabaye mu kogeza Inkuru Nziza , hamwe na Kilimenti n’abandi bangobotse ; none amazina yabo akaba yanditse mu Gitabo cy’ubugingo .
50004004	Muhore mwishima muri Nyagasani ; mbisubiyemo , nimwishime .
50004005	Ubugwaneza bwanyu nibumenyekane ku bantu bose . Nyagasani ari hafi .
50004006	Ntimugire ikibahagarika umutima , ahubwo nimumenyeshe Imana icyo mukeneye cyose , muyisenga , muyinginga , munayishimira .
50004007	Maze amahoro y’Imana arenze icyitwa ubwenge cyose , ahore mu mitima no mu bitekerezo byanyu , muri Kristu Yezu .
50004008	Ahasigaye , bavandimwe , icyitwa icy’ukuri cyose kimwe n’igikwiye kubahwa , igitunganye , ikitagira inenge , igikwiye gukundwa no kuratwa , mbese icyitwa ingeso nziza cyose kandi gikwiriye ishimwe , abe ari cyo muharanira .
50004009	Ibyo nabigishije kandi mwemeye , ibyo mwanyumvanye kandi mwambonanye , mujye mubikora , maze Imana y’amahoro izahorane namwe .
50004010	Narishimye cyane muri Nyagasani mbitewe n’uko ishyaka mumfitiye ryiyongereye ; icyakora , murarisanganywe , uretse ko mwari mwarabuze uko muringaragariza .
50004011	Ibyo simbivuga kubera ubukene ndimo , kuko nimenyereje kunyurwa n’ibyo mfite .
50004012	Nzi kubaho ntunzwe na bike , nzi no kubaho muri byinshi . Muri byose , buri gihe , nitoje guhaga no gusonza , gukira no gukena .
50004013	Nshobora byose muri Kristu untera imbaraga .
50004014	Icyakora mwagize neza muntabara mu kaga .
50004015	Mwebwe kandi , Banyafilipi , murabizi : Inkuru Nziza ikimenyekana iwanyu , ubwo nari nturutse i Masedoniya , nta Kiliziya n’imwe yangobotse ngo imfashe mu byo nari nkeneye , keretse mwebwe mwenyine .
50004016	N’ubwo nari ndi i Tesaloniki , mwanyoherereje imfashanyo , ndetse ubugira kabiri .
50004017	Mumenye ariko ko nta maturo mparanira ; icyo nkurikiranye ni uko inyungu yanyu yiyongera .
50004018	Ubu mfite ibya ngombwa byose , ndetse birarenze , byasendereye igihe Epaforoditi anshyikirije amaturo yanyu , yo mubavu mwiza n’igitambo kinyura Imana .
50004019	Kandi Imana yanjye , mu bukungahare n’ikuzo byayo , izabasenderezaho ingabire zayo mu byo mukeneye byose , muri Kristu Yezu .
50004020	Nihakuzwe Imana Umubyeyi wacu iteka ryose . Amen .
50004021	Mutashye uwatagatifujwe wese muri Yezu Kristu . Abavandimwe turi kumwe barabatashya .
50004022	Abatagatifujwe bose barabatashya , ariko cyane cyane abo mu ngoro ya Kayizari .
50004023	Muhorane ineza y’Umwami wacu Yezu Kristu .
51001001	Jyewe Pawulo , intumwa ya Yezu Kristu , uko Imana yabishatse , n’umuvandimwe wacu Timote ,
51001002	ku batagatifujwe b’i Kolosi , kuri mwebwe , bavandimwe b’indahemuka muri Kristu : tubifurije ineza n’amahoro biva ku Mana Umubyeyi wacu .
51001003	Turashimira Imana , Se w’Umwami wacu Yezu Kristu , kandi tukanabasabira ubudahwema ,
51001004	kuva aho twumviye ukwemera mufitiye Yezu Kristu , n’urukundo mugirira abatagatifujwe bose ,
51001005	mubitewe no kwizera ibyiza bibagenewe mu ijuru . Ayo mizero mwayamenyeshejwe n’ijambo ry’ukuri , ari yo Nkuru Nziza yageze iwanyu .
51001006	Nk’uko irumbuka kandi igakwira ku isi yose , no muri mwe ni ko bimeze , kuva aho mwumviye kandi mukamenya by’ukuri ingabire y’Imana .
51001007	Mugenzi wacu Epafurasi dufatanyije umurimo , ni we wayibigishije .
51001008	Uwo mugaragu w’indahemuka wa Yezu Kristu ubakorera mu kigwi cyacu , yanatumenyesheje urukundo mwasenderejwe na Roho Mutagatifu .
51001009	Ni cyo gituma natwe , kuva aho tubyumviye , tudahwema kwambaza tubasabira ku Mana , kugira ngo mugire ubumenyi bushyitse bw’icyo ishaka , muhore murangwa n’umutima wuzuye ubuhanga n’ubushishozi ku bwa Roho Mutagatifu .
51001010	Nguko uko muzizihiza Nyagasani mu mibereho yanyu imunyuze muri byose , munakore ibyiza byinshi kandi mugende murushaho kumenya Imana .
51001011	Bityo muzakomezwa n’imbaraga zayo zitagereranywa , mubashe kuba indacogora no kwihangana muri byose .
51001012	Nimunezerwe kandi mushimire Imana Data watumye mugira umugabane ku murage w’abatagatifujwe bari mu mucyo .
51001013	Koko rero , yatugobotoye ku ngoyi y’umwijima , atujyana mu Ngoma y’Umwana we akunda byimazeyo ,
51001014	ari na We dukesha gucungurwa no kubabarirwa ibyaha .
51001015	Ni We shusho ry’Imana itagaragara , Umuvukambere mu byitwa ikiremwa cyose ,
51001016	kuko byose byaremewe muri We , ari ibiri mu ijuru , ari n’ibiri ku isi . Ibigaragara n’ibitagaragara , Ibinyabubasha n’Inganji , Ibikomangoma n’Ibihangange : byose byaremwe na We , kandi ni We byaremewe ;
51001017	yariho mbere ya byose , kandi byose bibeshwaho na We .
51001018	Ni We kandi Mutwe w’umubiri , ari wo Kiliziya , akaba n’Ishingiro , n’Umuvukambere mu bapfuye , kugira ngo ahorane muri byose umwanya w’ibanze ;
51001019	kuko Imana yizihijwe no kumusenderezamo ibyiza byose ,
51001020	kandi muri We yiyunga n’ibiriho byose , ndetse ari We ibigirira , ari ibiri ku isi , ari n’ibiri mu ijuru , byose ibisakazaho amahoro aturutse ku maraso ye yameneye ku musaraba .
51001021	Namwe ubwanyu , kera mwari mwaraciye ukubiri n’Imana , mwari n’abanzi bayo kubera ibitekerezo n’ibikorwa byanyu bibi ,
51001022	none ubu ngubu yabahaye kwigorora na Yo , mubikesha Umwana wayo watanze umubiri we akabapfira , kugira ngo mube abatagatifu , nta mwanda kandi nta makemwa , imbere yayo .
51001023	Cyakora mukomere mu kwemera , ntimugahungabane , ngo muteshuke ku mizero mwasezeranyijwe n’Inkuru Nziza mwumvise , ari yo yamamarijwe ikiremwa cyose kiri mu nsi y’ijuru , akaba ari na yo jyewe Pawulo ndahwema kuruhira .
51001024	Ubu rero nshimishijwe n’uko mbabara ari mwe ngirira , maze ibyari bibuze ku mibabaro ya Kristu , nkabyuzuriza mu mubiri wanjye , mbigirira umubiri we , ari wo Kiliziya .
51001025	Koko rero , nabaye umugaragu wa Kiliziya , biturutse ku murimo Imana yanshinze muri mwe : ni uwo kubagezaho byuzuye ijambo ry’Imana ,
51001026	mbamenyesha ibanga ryari ryarahishwe kuva kera kose no mu bisekuruza byose , none rikaba rimaze guhishurirwa abatagatifujwe bayo .
51001027	Ni bo Imana yishakiye kumenyesha ikuzo n’ibyiza bitagereranywa iryo banga rizanira abanyamahanga : Kristu ari muri mwe , We uzaduhesha ikuzo twizeye !
51001028	Kristu uwo nyine ni We twamamaza , tuburira buri muntu kandi tumwigisha ubwenge bwose , kugira ngo buri wese tumuhindure intungane muri Kristu .
51001029	Ngicyo icyo nduhira nkakirwanirira nkoresheje imbaraga zose mpora nterwa na We .
51002001	Nifuza rero ko mumenya intambara ikomeye mbarwanira , mwebwe n’abo muri Lawodiseya , ndetse n’abandi batigeze bambona n’amaso yabo .
51002002	Icyo mparanira ni uko imitima yabo ihumurizwa , bakibumbira mu rukundo , kandi bakagera ku bumenyi bwuzuye bw’ibanga ry’Imana , ari ryo Kristu ,
51002003	We nganzo iganjemo icyitwa ubuhanga n’ubumenyi cyose .
51002004	Ibyo mbibabwiriye kugira ngo hatagira ubashukisha amagambo y’amaryohereza .
51002005	N’ubwo tutari kumwe bwose , mbahozaho umutima nejerejwe n’uko iwanyu ibintu byose biri mu buryo , n’uko kandi mukomeza kwemera Kristu mutadohoka .
51002006	Bityo rero , nimukomeze mujye mbere muri Kristu Yezu Umwami wacu , mbese nk’uko mwamubwiwe ;
51002007	mushore imizi muri We , kandi mube ari We mwishingikirizaho , mukomejwe n’ukwemera babatoje , mushimira Imana ubudahwema .
51002008	Muramenye ntihazagire ubashukisha bene za nyigisho z’ubuhendanyi bita ubuhanga bwahebuje , zihuje n’ibitekerezo by’ubuyobe bw’abantu , zigashingira ku by’isi , ariko zinyuranye na Kristu .
51002009	Koko rero ni We ubusendere bwose bwa kamere‐Mana butuyemo mu buryo bw’umubiri ,
51002010	kandi namwe ubwanyu abasenderezamo ibyiza byose , We mutware w’Ibikomangoma n’Ibihangange byose .
51002011	Mwagenywe muri We ; ariko iryo genywa si rya rindi rikorwa n’abantu , ahubwo ni igenywa mwakorewe na Kristu , ari ryo ribakiza irari ry’imibiri yanyu .
51002012	Igihe mubatijwe , mwahambanywe na Kristu , kandi muzukana na we , kuko mwemeye ububasha bw’Imana yamuzuye mu bapfuye .
51002013	Mwebwe mwari mwarapfuye muzize ibyaha byanyu n’umubiri wanyu wandavuye , none Imana yabashubije ubugingo hamwe na We , itubabarira ibicumuro byacu byose .
51002014	Yasibanganyije urwandiko rwadushinjaga imyenda twarimo kubera amategeko tutakurikije , irarushwanyaguza irubamba ku musaraba .
51002015	Yanyaze Ibikomangoma n’Ibihangange , ibakoza isoni ku mugaragaro , ibakurubana nk'ingaruzwamuheto inyuma ya Kristu utahanye intsinzi ku bw'umusaraba we .
51002016	Nuko rero ntihakagire ubacira urubanza mu byerekeye ibiribwa cyangwa ibinyobwa , cyangwa se kubera iminsi mikuru , imboneko z’ukwezi n’amasabato .
51002017	Ibyo byose ni amarenga y’ibyagombaga kuzaza , ariko ukuri nyako ni Kristu .
51002018	Ntihakagire kandi ababavutsa amahoro bakurikiza utugenzo tudafite akamaro , bagasenga abamalayika , bakirata ko babonekewe , bakurikije ibitekerezo byabo by’amanjwe .
51002019	Bene abo bitandukanyije n’Umutwe uhuza kandi ukagaburira umubiri wose , ukawukuza ubigirishije imitsi n’ingingo , nk’uko Imana ibishaka .
51002020	Ubwo mwapfanye na Kristu , mukagobotorwa ku by’isi , ni iki cyatuma mugenza nk’aho mukiri ab’isi ,
51002021	mugakurikiza bene iyi miziro , ngo « Wifata iki ! » , cyangwa « Ntusomeho ! » , cyangwa « Ntukoreho ! »
51002022	Kandi ibyo byose bizashira mukibikoresha ! Ngayo amategeko n’inyigisho z’abantu !
51002023	Koko , ibyo byose wagira ngo birimo ubwenge , cyangwa ngo bigamije gushimisha Imana mu kwicisha bugufi no kwigomwa , nyamara nta kamaro bifite na gato ko gucubya irari ry’umubiri .
51003001	Ubwo mwazukanye na Kristu , nimuharanire ibyo mu ijuru , aho Kristu ari , yicaye iburyo bw’Imana ;
51003002	nimurangamire iby’ijuru , aho kurarikira iby’isi .
51003003	Koko mwapfanye na Kristu , none ubugingo bwanyu bwihishe hamwe na We mu Mana .
51003004	Aho Kristu azigaragariza , We bugingo bwanyu , icyo gihe namwe muzagaragara muri kumwe na We , mu ikuzo ryisesuye .
51003005	Nimucike rero ku bibarimo byose bibatera gutwarwa n’iby’isi , nk’ubwiyandarike n’ubusambanyi , ingeso mbi n’irari ribi , ibyifuzo bibi n’ubugugu butuma musenga ibintu nk’ibigirwamana !
51003006	Ngibyo ibirakaza Imana .
51003007	Nguko uko namwe mwagenzaga kera , mugikora ibyo .
51003008	Noneho ubu , namwe ibyo byose nimubizinukwe : uburakari , umwaga , ubugome , ibitutsi , n’ibigambo bibi bibava mu kanwa .
51003009	Nimuherukire aho kubeshyana , kuko mwasezereye muntu w’igisazira hamwe n’imigenzereze ye ,
51003010	mugahinduka muntu mushya , uwo Umuremyi ahora avugurura amwishushanya , agira ngo amugeze ku bumenyi nyakuri .
51003011	Icyo gihe rero ntihaba hakivugwa Umugereki cyangwa Umuyahudi , uwagenywe cyangwa utagenywe , umunyeshyanga cyangwa Umushiti , umucakara cyangwa uwigenga ; ahubwo haba havugwa gusa Kristu , uba byose muri bose .
51003012	Naho mwebwe , ntore z’Imana , mukaba abatagatifu bayo ikunda byimazeyo , nimugire umutima wuje impuhwe , ubugiraneza , ubwiyoroshye , ituze , n’ukwiyumanganya .
51003013	Nimwihanganirane kandi , niba umwe agize icyo apfa n’undi mubabarirane . Nk’uko Nyagasani yabababariye , namwe nimugenze mutyo .
51003014	Ariko ikiruta ibyo byose , nimugire urukundo ruzabahuriza mwese mu butungane .
51003015	Kandi amahoro ya Kristu naganze mu mitima yanyu , kuko ari yo mwahamagariwe ngo mube umubiri umwe . Kandi mujye muhora mushimira .
51003016	Ijambo rya Kristu niribaturemo , risagambe rwose . Mujye mwigishanya kandi muhanane , mubigiranye ubwitonzi . Mujye mushimira Imana mu mitima yanyu , muyiririmbira zaburi , ibisingizo n’izindi ndirimbo mubwirijwe na Roho Mutagatifu .
51003017	Ari ibyo muvuze , ari n’ibyo mukoze , byose mujye mubigira mu izina rya Nyagasani Yezu , abe ari we mwisunga mushimira Imana Data .
51003018	Bagore , mujye mworohera abagabo banyu nk’uko bikwiye , mubigirira Nyagasani .
51003019	Bagabo , namwe nimukunde abagore banyu , mwoye kubabera abanyamwaga .
51003020	Bana , nimwumvire ababyeyi banyu muri byose , kuko ari byo binyura Nyagasani .
51003021	Babyeyi , namwe ntimugatonganye abana banyu ubutitsa , mutazabakura umutima .
51003022	Bagaragu , nimwumvire muri byose ba shobuja bo kuri iyi si , mudakorera ijisho , nk’aho ari abantu mushaka gushimisha , ahubwo mubigirane umutima utaryarya , mwubaha Nyagasani .
51003023	Icyo mukoze cyose , mujye mugikora mwimazeyo nk’abakorera Nyagasani , atari ugukorera abantu ,
51003024	muzirikana ko muzahembwa na Nyagasani umurage yageneye abe . Nyagasani Kristu ni We mukorera .
51003025	Ugira inabi wese azayiturwa , kandi bose bazagenzerezwa kimwe .
51004001	Namwe ba shebuja , mujye muha abagaragu banyu ibitunganye n’ibibakwiye , mwibuka ko namwe mufite Shobuja uri mu ijuru .
51004002	Nimukomere ku isengesho , muhugukire gushimira .
51004003	Mudusabire natwe , kugira ngo Imana idutegurire uburyo bwo kwamamaza ibanga rya Kristu , ari na ryo ritumye mba imfungwa ,
51004004	maze mbone kuritangaza uko mbishinzwe .
51004005	Abo mudasangiye ukwemera , mubagenderere mu bwitonzi , mubibonere umwanya n’uburyo .
51004006	Amagambo muvuze ahore arangwa n’ineza , amere nk’asize umunyu ; uwo muvuganye wese mumenye kumusubiza uko bikwiye .
51004007	Ibinyerekeyeho byose muzabibwirwa na Tushiko , uwo muvandimwe nkunda wandwanyeho kandi twafatanyije umurimo wa Nyagasani .
51004008	Ndamuboherereje kugira ngo ababwire amakuru yacu kandi abahumurize .
51004009	Mboherereje na Onezimi , uwo muvandimwe nkunda kandi w’inyangamugayo , ngo bazane maze babamenyeshe ibyabaye ino byose .
51004010	Arisitariko mugenzi wanjye dufunganywe arabatashya , na Mariko mwene sewabo wa Barinaba ; naza iwanyu , muzamwakire neza , mukurikije amabwiriza mwahawe .
51004011	Yezu , uwo bahimbye irya Yusito , na we arabatashya . Ni bo bonyine mu Bayahudi bamfashije kogeza Ingoma y’Imana , bambereye igihozo .
51004012	Epafurasi uvuka iwanyu arabatashya ; uwo mugaragu wa Yezu Kristu ntahwema kubasabira , kugira ngo mukomere mube intungane , kandi mukurikize muri byose ugushaka kw’Imana .
51004013	Rwose ndahamya ko abaruhira cyane , mwebwe n’abo muri Lawodiseya , n’abo kuri Hiyerapoli .
51004014	Arabatashya Luka , umuganga dukunda , na Demasi .
51004015	Mutashye abavandimwe bari i Lawodiseya , na Nimifa , n’abakoranira mu nzu ye bose .
51004016	Nimumara gusoma iyi baruwa , muzayoherereze na Kiliziya y’i Lawodiseya maze na bo bayisome ; namwe muzasome ivuye i Lawodiseya nibageraho .
51004017	Mubwire Arikipo muti « Witondere umurimo wahawe muri Nyagasani , kandi wihatire kuwutunganya ! »
51004018	Ngiyo intashyo yanjye mbandikiye ubwanjye , jyewe Pawulo . Mwibuke kandi ingoyi ndiho . Muhorane ineza ya Nyagasani !
52001001	Jyewe Pawulo , na Silivani , na Timote kuri Kiliziya y’Abanyatesaloniki , yibumbiye ku Mana Data no kuri Nyagasani Yezu Kristu : tubifurije ineza n’amahoro .
52001002	Iyo tubibutse mu masengesho yacu , ntiduhwema gushimira Imana kubera mwebwe mwese .
52001003	Duhora twibuka ibikorwa byiza n’ukwemera kwanyu , n’imiruho muterwa n’urukundo rwanyu , n’ukuntu mwiringiye Umwami wacu Yezu Kristu mudatezuka imbere y’Imana Umubyeyi wacu .
52001004	Bavandimwe , nkoramutima z’Imana , tuzi neza ko muri mu bo yatoye .
52001005	Koko rero , Inkuru Nziza tubamenyesha , nta bwo yabagejejweho mu magambo gusa , ahubwo twayamamaje dushize amanga , twishingikirije ububasha butyaye bwa Roho Mutagatifu . Muzi neza ukuntu twabagenjereje tugamije kubagirira akamaro .
52001006	Namwe mwaratwiganye , mwigana na Nyagasani , maze mu bitotezo byinshi , mwakirana ijambo ry’Imana ibyishimo bikomoka kuri Roho Mutagatifu .
52001007	Byatumye mubera urugero abemera bose bo muri Masedoniya n’abo muri Akaya .
52001008	Koko rero , ijambo rya Nyagasani , rihereye iwanyu , ntiryasakaye muri Masedoniya no muri Akaya gusa , ahubwo inkuru y’ukuntu mwemeye Imana yamamaye hose , ku buryo nta cyo twakwirirwa tubivugaho .
52001009	Bose kandi bavuga uko twakiriwe iwanyu , n’ukuntu mwayobotse Imana , mugata ibigirwamana , kugira ngo mukorere Imana nzima kandi nyakuri ,
52001010	kandi mutegereze Umwana wayo Yezu yazuye mu bapfuye , We uzaza ava mu ijuru ngo adukize uburakari bugiye kuza .
52002001	Namwe ubwanyu , bavandimwe , muzi ukuntu twaje iwanyu , kandi ntibibapfire ubusa .
52002002	N’ubwo i Filipi twari tumaze kuhabonera imibabaro no kuhatukirwa cyane , nk’uko musanzwe mubizi , ntibyatubujije kubasanga namwe , twiringiye Imana yacu , ngo tubagezeho Inkuru Nziza yayo mu ngorane nyinshi .
52002003	Inyigisho zacu ntizishingiye ku buyobe cyangwa ku migambi idahwitse , cyangwa se ku mayeri .
52002004	Ariko kubera ko yabanje kutugerageza kugira ngo idushinge Inkuru Nziza yayo , bituma tuyamamaza kuri ubu buryo : ntituvugira gushimisha abantu , ahubwo gushimisha Imana , Yo igenzura imitima yacu .
52002005	Ntitwigeze na rimwe tubabwira amagambo yo kubaryoshya , ibyo murabizi ; nta n’ubwo twigeze dushaka kubungukiraho , Imana irabibere umuhamya ;
52002006	nta na rimwe twigeze duharanira icyubahiro mu bantu , haba muri mwe cyangwa se mu bandi ,
52002007	n’ubwo twashoboraga kwitwaza ko turi intumwa za Kristu , tukabagora . Ahubwo twicishije bugufi cyane hagati yanyu , mbese nk’uko umubyeyi ashyashyanira abana be .
52002008	Bityo , kubera ubwuzu twari tubafitiye , uretse kubagezaho Inkuru Nziza y’Imana , twari twiteguye no guhara amagara yacu , bitewe n’urukundo twabakundaga .
52002009	Muribuka , bavandimwe , imvune n’imiruho yacu : igihe twabamenyeshaga Inkuru Nziza y’Imana : ntitwaburaga gukora ijoro n’amanywa kugira ngo hatagira n’umwe muri mwe tugora .
52002010	Yemwe , uko twifashe hagati yanyu , tubabera intungane , intabera n’indahinyuka , mwebwe abemera mushobora kubihamya , ndetse n’Imana ubwayo .
52002011	Kandi muzi uko twahuguraga buri muntu , nk’umubyeyi mu bana be ,
52002012	tubashishikaza , tubatera inkunga , kandi tubingingira gutunganira Imana Yo ibahamagarira ingoma yayo n’ikuzo ryayo .
52002013	Ngicyo igituma tudahwema gushimira Imana , kuko mwakiriye ijambo ryayo twabigishije nk’uko riri by’ukuri . Koko ntimwaryakiriye nk’ijambo ry’abantu , ahubwo nk’ijambo ry’Imana rigaragariza akamaro karyo muri mwebwe abemera .
52002014	Koko rero , bavandimwe , mwiganye Kiliziya z’Imana zo muri Yudeya , zibumbiye muri Kristu Yezu ; kuko namwe mwaboneye amagorwa kuri bene wanyu nk’uko na bo bayaboneye ku Bayahudi .
52002015	Uko bishe Nyagasani Yezu n’abahanuzi , ni ko badutoteje natwe . Nta bwo bashimisha Imana , kandi babangamiye abantu bose .
52002016	Batubuza kwigisha abanyamahanga ngo bakizwe , bakagumya kugwiza batyo ibyaha byabo . Amaherezo ariko , uburakari bw’Imana bwarabagwiriye .
52002017	Naho twebwe , bavandimwe , tumaze igihe gito dutandukanye , ariko kure y’amaso si ho kure y’umutima ; byatumye twihatira kongera kubabona , kuko twari tubakumbuye cyane .
52002018	Ni yo mpamvu twashatse kuza iwanyu , — jyewe ubwanjye Pawulo nabigambiriye kenshi — ariko Sekibi aratuzitira .
52002019	Usibye mwebwe , ugira ngo hari ahandi twakura amizero , n’ibyishimo , n’ishema rizatubera ikamba imbere y’Umwami wacu Yezu igihe azazira ?
52002020	Koko ni mwe shema n’ibyishimo byacu .
52003001	Aho rero tunaniriwe kwihangana , twahisemo gusigara twenyine Atene ,
52003002	nuko twohereza Timote , umuvandimwe wacu akaba n’umufasha w’Imana mu byo kwamamaza Inkuru Nziza ya Kristu . Twamushinze kubakomeza no kubatera umwete mu kwemera kwanyu ,
52003003	kugira ngo hatagira uhungabanywa n’aya makuba turimo , kuko musanzwe muzi ko ari yo twagenewe .
52003004	Igihe twari iwanyu , twababuriye hakiri kare ko tuzahura n’amagorwa , kandi muzi ko ari ko byagenze .
52003005	Ni cyo gituma aho naniriwe kwihangana , naboherereje intumwa kugira ngo menyeshwe iby’ukwemera kwanyu , hato Umushukanyi ataba yarabashutse , maze ibyo twakoze bikaba imfabusa .
52003006	None ubu Timote atugezeho avuye iwanyu , atuzanira amakuru meza yerekeye ukwemera n’urukundo byanyu ; yanatubwiye ko muhora mutwibuka , mukifuza kutubona nk’uko natwe tubyifuza .
52003007	Bityo rero , bavandimwe , ukwemera kwanyu kwatumaze agahinda mu mpagarara no mu magorwa yacu yose .
52003008	Ubu turumva tuguwe neza , ubwo mugikomeye muri Nyagasani .
52003009	Mbese twashimira Imana dute kubera ibyishimo byose mudutera imbere yayo ?
52003010	Ijoro n’amanywa , dusaba Imana , tukayinginga dukomeje , ngo iduhe kwongera kubonana , maze tubongerere ibyo mukibuze mu kwemera kwanyu .
52003011	Imana Data ubwayo , hamwe n’Umwami wacu Yezu , nibadutegurire urugendo ruzatugeza iwanyu .
52003012	Namwe kandi , Nyagasani arabongeremo kandi yuzuze urukundo mufitanye , n’urwo mufitiye abantu bose , nk’uko natwe tubakunda .
52003013	Nyagasani nakomeze imitima yanyu , igume mu butungane budahinyuka imbere y’Imana Umubyeyi wacu , kugeza igihe Umwami wacu Yezu azaza ashagawe n’abatagatifu be bose .
52004001	Ikindi kandi , bavandimwe , turabasaba tubinginga muri Nyagasani Yezu ngo mwifate ku buryo bushimisha Imana , nk’uko twabibigishije ; ni ko musanzwe mubigenza , ariko noneho nimurusheho .
52004002	Muzi kandi amategeko twabahaye muri Nyagasani Yezu ayo ari yo .
52004003	Dore icyo Imana ibashakaho : ni uko mwaba intungane , mukirinda ubusambanyi .
52004004	Ahubwo buri wese muri mwe amenyere kwifata , agumane ubumanzi n’ubwiyubahe ,
52004005	yange gutwarwa n’irari nk’abanyamahanga batazi Imana .
52004006	Kandi ntihakagire ucumura ku uwo bava inda imwe , cyangwa ngo amurenganye muri ibyo , kuko Nyagasani azahana abagenza batyo , nk’uko twabibabwiye , tubihanangiriza .
52004007	Koko rero , Imana ntiyaduhamagariye kwandavura , ahubwo yaduhamagariye kuba intungane .
52004008	Ni na yo mpamvu usuzugura aya mategeko , atari umuntu aba asuzuguye , ahubwo aba asuzuguye Imana yabashyizemo Roho Mutagatifu wayo .
52004009	Ibyerekeye urukundo rwa kivandimwe , si ngombwa ko tubibandikira , kuko Imana ubwayo yabiyigishirije gukundana ,
52004010	kandi ni na ko mubikorera abavandimwe bose bo muri Masedoniya yose . Bavandimwe , turabasaba gukomeza kujya mbere ;
52004011	nimwihatire gutuza , mwibande ku bibareba , kandi mukoreshe amaboko yanyu , nk’uko twabibategetse .
52004012	Bityo muzihesha agaciro muri rubanda , kandi nta we muzakenera .
52004013	Bavandimwe , nta bwo dushaka ko muguma mu bujiji ku byerekeye abapfuye , kugira ngo mudaheranwa n’ishavu , nk’abandi batagira icyo bizera .
52004014	Nk’uko twemera ko Yezu yapfuye kandi yazutse , ni na ko abapfuye bamwizera , Imana izabazura maze ikabashyira hamwe na We .
52004015	Dore icyo tubabwira giturutse ku ijambo rya Nyagasani : twebwe abazima , abazaba bakiriho ku munsi w’amaza ya Nyagasani , nta bwo tuzabanziriza na gato abapfuye .
52004016	Koko rero , ku kimenyetso gitanzwe n’umumalayika mukuru mu ijwi riranguruye , no ku mworomo w’impanda y’Imana , Nyagasani ubwe azamanuka mu ijuru . Nuko abapfuye bizera Kristu babanze bazuke ,
52004017	hanyuma twebwe abazima , abazaba basigaye , duhite twererezwa hamwe na bo mu bicu , kugira ngo dusanganire Nyagasani mu kirere , bityo tuzabane na Nyagasani iteka ryose .
52004018	Murajye rero muhumurizanya muri bene ayo magambo .
52005001	Naho ku byerekeye igihe n’amagingo ibyo bizabera , bavandimwe , ntimukeneye ko tubibandikira .
52005002	Ubwanyu muzi neza ko Umunsi wa Nyagasani uza nk’umujura wa nijoro .
