52005003	Igihe rero bazaba bavuga ngo ’ Mbega amahoro n’umutekano ! » ni bwo icyorezo kizabatungura , nk’uko ibise bitungura umugore utwite , kandi nta mahungiro .
52005004	Ariko mwebwe , bavandimwe , ntimukiri mu mwijima ku buryo uwo munsi wabatungura nk’umujura ;
52005005	mwese muri abana b’urumuri n’ab’amanywa ; ntituri ab’ijoro n’ab’umwijima .
52005006	None rero , ntitugasinzire nk’abandi , ahubwo tube maso kandi twirinde gutwarwa n’irari .
52005007	Abashaka gusinzira , nijoro ni ho basinzira ; n’abasinda , nijoro ni ho basinda ;
52005008	naho twebwe , ubwo turi ab’amanywa , tujye twiramira , kandi twambare intwaro z’Imana , ukwemera n’urukundo bibe ikoti ry’intamenwa , amizero y’uko tuzakizwa abe nk’ingofero y’icyuma .
52005009	Erega Imana ntiyatugeneye kurimburwa n’uburakari bwayo , ahubwo yatugeneye kuronka umukiro dukesha Umwami Yezu Kristu
52005010	wadupfiriye kugira ngo , twaba bazima cyangwa twaba twarapfuye , duhore twunze ubumwe na we .
52005011	Kubera iyo mpamvu , nimujye muhumurizanya kandi muterane inkunga nk’uko musanzwe mubigenza .
52005012	Turabasaba kandi , bavandimwe , ngo mumenye abanyu babaruhira , bakaba bashinzwe kubayobora muri Nyagasani no kubagira inama ;
52005013	mujye mububahana urukundo rwinshi , kubera ibyo babakorera . Namwe ubwanyu mubane mu mahoro .
52005014	Turabinginga , bavandimwe , ngo muhane inkorabusa , mukomeze umutima abacika intege , mushyigikire abatishoboye , bose mubihanganire .
52005015	Mumenye ntihakagire uwitura undi inabi , ahubwo muharanire iteka kugirirana ineza , ndetse muyigirire bose .
52005016	Mujye muhora mwishimye ,
52005017	musenge ubudahwema ,
52005018	mushimire Imana muri byose , kuko ari byo ibashakaho muri Yezu Kristu .
52005019	Muramenye ntimuzimye Roho w’Imana ,
52005020	ntimugahinyure ibyahanuwe ;
52005021	ahubwo mujye mugenzura byose , ibyiza mubigumane ,
52005022	naho ikibi cyose mucyirinde .
52005023	Imana y’amahoro ubwayo nibatagatifuze binonosoye , kugira ngo izasange muri indahemuka mwese nta makemwa mufite ku mutima no ku mubiri , ku munsi Umwami wacu Yezu Kristu azaziraho .
52005024	Ubahamagara ni indahemuka ; azakora n’ibyo ngibyo .
52005025	Bavandimwe , natwe mudusabire .
52005026	Muramukanye n’abavandimwe bose mu muhoberano mutagatifu .
52005027	Mbasabye nkomeje ku bwa Nyagasani , gusomera abavandimwe bose iyi baruwa .
52005028	Muhorane iteka ineza y’Umwami wacu Yezu Kristu .
53001001	Jyewe Pawulo , na Silivani , na Timote kuri Kiliziya y’Abanyatesaloniki , yibumbiye ku Mana Data no kuri Nyagasani Yezu Kristu :
53001002	tubifurije ineza n’amahoro biva ku Mana Data no kuri Nyagasani Yezu Kristu .
53001003	Bavandimwe , tugomba guhora dushimira Imana kubera mwebwe . Ibyo birakwiye , kuko ukwemera kwanyu kugenda kwiyongera , n’urukundo mufitanye rukabasenderamo uko mungana ,
53001004	bigatuma natwe muduhesha ishema muri Kiliziya z’Imana , kubera ubudacogora n’ukwemera bibaranga muri ibyo bitotezo n’amagorwa yose mwihanganira .
53001005	Ibyo birerekana urubanza Imana izaca mu butabera , kuko nimumara kubabara ku mpamvu y’Ingoma y’Imana , nta washidikanya ko izasanga mukwiye kuyinjizwamo .
53001006	Koko rero , biratunganye ko Imana isubiza amagorwa ku bayateye ,
53001007	naho mwebwe abagowe , ikabaha kuruhukana natwe , igihe cy’ukwigaragaza kwa Nyagasani Yezu , uzava mu ijuru ashagawe n’abamalayika be mu bubasha bwinshi ,
53001008	kandi ari hagati y’umuriro ugurumana , kugira ngo ahane abatazi Imana bakanga kumvira Inkuru Nziza y’Umwami wacu Yezu Kristu
53001009	Abo ngabo bazabona igihano kizahoraho , bacirirwe kure y’uruhanga rwa Nyagasani Nyir’ikuzo ,
53001010	kuri wa munsi azaza kugira ngo aherwe ikuzo mu batagatifu be , kandi ashimagirizwe mu bazaba baramwemeye bose : mwebweho rero , muri mu bemeye ubuhamya bwacu .
53001011	Ni yo mpamvu ituma tubasabira iteka , kugira ngo Imana yacu ibahe gutunganya ibyo yabatoreye , kandi ngo ku bubasha bwayo , ibahe gukora ibyiza byose mwiyemeje , mugire n’ukwemera kwigaragaza mu bikorwa .
53001012	Bityo , izina rya Nyagasani Yezu rizakurizwe muri mwe , namwe muri We , mubikesha ubuntu bw’Imana yacu n’ubwa Nyagasani Yezu Kristu .
53002001	Bavandimwe , ku byerekeye amaza y’Umwami wacu Yezu Kristu no ku byerekeye uko tuzakoranira iruhande rwe , hari icyo twabasaba :
53002002	muramenye ntimugahagarike imitima vuba , ngo muce igikuba mubitewe na bamwe biha kubemeza ko umunsi wa Nyagasani waba wageze , bitwaje ubuhanuzi batugerekaho , n’andi magambo tutigeze tuvuga , cyangwa se amabaruwa ngo twaba twaranditse .
53002003	Rwose ntihazagire ubabeshya na busa , kuko ibyo bitazaba hatabanje kuza igihe cy’ubuhakanyi , kandi hatabanje kwigaragaza Umuntu w’Umugomeramana , Umwana woramye ,
53002004	wa Mwanzi uzishyira hejuru y’icyitwa Imana cyose , no hejuru y’ibindi byose bikwiye gusengwa , akageza n’aho ubwe yicara mu Ngoro y’Imana , maze agatangaza ko ubwe ari Imana .
53002005	Mbese ntimwibuka ko tukiri kumwe najyaga mbibabwira ?
53002006	Muzi kandi ikimuzitiye ubu ngubu , ku buryo atakwigaragaza igihe cye kitaragera .
53002007	Ni koko , Ubugomeramana bw’urujijo bwatangiye guca ibintu mu cyayenge ; igisigaye gusa ni ukwigizayo ubuzitiye ubu ngubu .
53002008	Uwo nguwo rero namara kwigizwayo , ni bwo Umugomeramana azigaragaza , maze Nyagasani Yezu amwicishe umwuka umuva mu kanwa , amurimbuze ububengerane buranga amaza ye .
53002009	Naho amaza y’Umugomeramana yo azarangwa n’imigirire ikomoka kuri Sekibi , agaragarire mu bushobozi buhambaye , no mu bimenyetso n’ibitangaza by’ibinyoma biteye kwinshi ,
53002010	kimwe no mu bishuko byose by’ubugizi bwa nabi , bizitabirwa n’abagenewe korama bazize ko batakunze ukuri kugenewe kubarokora .
53002011	Ni yo mpamvu Imana ibareka bagaterwa n’ubuyobe bubarindagiza , bakemera ibinyoma ,
53002012	kugira ngo abazaba baranze kwemera ukuri , ahubwo bagahimbazwa n’ubugiranabi , bose bazacirwe urubanza .
53002013	Twebweho rero , tugomba guhora dushimira Imana kubera mwebwe , bavandimwe mukunzwe na Nyagasani , kuko Imana yabatoye kuva mu ntangiriro , kugira ngo murokorwe mubikesha Roho ubatagatifuza , mubikesha kandi no kwemera ukuri .
53002014	Ngicyo icyo yabatoreye , ibigirishije Inkuru Nziza twamamaza , kugira ngo muronke ikuzo ry’Umwami wacu Yezu Kristu .
53002015	None rero , bavandimwe , nimukomere kandi mukomeze ubutagerura inyigisho z’uruhererekane twabagejejeho , ari mu magambo , ari no mu nyandiko .
53002016	Umwami wacu Yezu Kristu ubwe , hamwe n’Imana Umubyeyi wacu wadukunze , maze ku neza ye akaduha kwizera ihumure ritazashira ,
53002017	bo nyine nibabahumurize kandi babahe gukomera mu byiza byose mukora cyangwa muvuga .
53003001	Ahasigaye , bavandimwe , mudusabire kugira ngo ijambo rya Nyagasani rikomeze gukwira hose , ryamamare nk’uko bimeze iwanyu .
53003002	Musabe kandi kugira ngo turokoke abantu b’abagome n’abagiranabi : koko rero kwemera si ibya bose .
53003003	Nyagasani ni indahemuka : azabakomeza , abarinde Nyakibi .
53003004	Kandi ku bwa Nyagasani ntidushidikanya ko ibyo tubategeka , mubikora mukazanabikomeza .
53003005	Nyagasani nayobore imitima yanyu , ayitoze gukunda Imana no kwiyumanganya nka Kristu .
53003006	Bavandimwe , mu izina rya Nyagasani Yezu Kristu , tubategetse kwirinda umuvandimwe wese w’inyandagazi , udakurikiza inyigisho n’umuco mudukomoraho .
53003007	Muzi neza ukuntu mugomba kudukurikiza : nta bwo twigeze tuba inkorabusa iwanyu ,
53003008	nta n’umwe twigeze dusaba umugati wadutunze ; ahubwo ijoro n’amanywa , mu mvune n’imiruho , twarikoreraga ubwacu , kugira ngo hatagira n’umwe muri mwe tugora .
53003009	Si ukuvuga ko tutari tubifitiye uburenganzira , ahubwo twashakaga kubabera urugero mukurikiza .
53003010	Igihe twari iwanyu , twabahaye uyu mugambi , tuti « Niba hari udashaka gukora , ajye areka no kurya ! »
53003011	None dusigaye twumva ko muri mwe harimo abandaraye , ntibagire icyo bakora , ahubwo bakivanga muri byose .
53003012	Abameze batyo tubategetse kandi tubasabye ibi ngibi ; muri Nyagasani Yezu Kristu : nibajye bakora mu ituze , batungwe n’umugati baruhiye ubwabo .
53003013	Namwe , bavandimwe , ntimukadohoke mu gukora neza .
53003014	Niba kandi hari utumvira ibyo tuvuze muri iyi baruwa , muramumenye , mumugendere kure , kugira ngo akorwe n’isoni .
53003015	Icyakora ntimukamufate nk’umwanzi , ahubwo mumugire inama bya kivandimwe .
53003016	Nyagasani Nyir’amahoro ubwe nabagwirize amahoro , aho muri hose n’igihe cyose . Nyagasani abane namwe mwese .
53003017	Iyi ndamutso , ni jyewe ubwanjye Pawulo uyiyandikiye . Kandi mu mabaruwa yanjye yose ni cyo kizabemeza ko ari jyewe : ni uko nandika !
53003018	Muhorane iteka ineza y’Umwami wacu Yezu Kristu .
54001001	Jyewe Pawulo , intumwa ya Yezu Kristu , uko Imana Umukiza wacu na Kristu Yezu amizero yacu babishatse ,
54001002	kuri Timote , umwana wanjye nyakuri nabyaye mu kwemera : nkwifurije ineza , impuhwe n’amahoro biva ku Mana Data no kuri Kristu Yezu Umwami wacu .
54001003	Igihe nendaga kujya i Masedoniya , nagusabye kuguma Efezi , kugira ngo ubuze bamwe gukwiza inyigisho z’intarurano ,
54001004	no kwibanda ku migani y’amahomvu hamwe n’ibisokuruza by’urudaca , bigamije gusa gukurura impaka zidashobotse , aho gushyigikira umugambi w’Imana ushingiye ku kwemera .
54001005	Ibyo mbivugiye guteza imbere urukundo rukomoka ku mutima usukuye , ku mutimanama ukeye no ku kwemera kutaryarya .
54001006	Kubera ko bamwe bataye uwo murongo , byatumye barorongotana mu magambo atagira shinge na rugero .
54001007	Bibwira ko ari abahanga mu by’Amategeko , kandi baba batazi n’icyo bavuga cyangwa barwanira ishyaka .
54001008	Koko , birazwi , Amategeko ni meza , apfa gusa gukoreshwa mu rugero rukwiye ,
54001009	umuntu akamenya ko Itegeko ritabereyeho intungane , ahubwo ko ryashyiriweho abantu b’ibigande n’ibyigomeke , abananira Imana n’abanyabyaha , inkorashyano n’inkozi z’ibibi , abica ba se cyangwa ba nyina , n’abandi bicanyi ,
54001010	ibyomanzi , abiyandarika , abacuruza abantu , ababeshyi n’abarahirabinyoma , n’abandi bose bakora ibitambamiye inyigisho zitunganye ,
54001011	za zindi zihuje n’Inkuru Nziza naragijwe n’Imana , Yo Nyir’ikuzo n’ihirwe .
54001012	Ndashimira cyane Kristu Yezu Umwami wacu wampaye imbaraga , kuko yasanze nkwiye kwizerwa , maze akantorera kumukorera ,
54001013	jyewe wahoze ndi umuntu utuka Imana , ngatoteza abayo , nkaba umunyarugomo . Ariko nagiriwe imbabazi , kuko ibyo nakoraga nabiterwaga n’ubujiji , ntaragira ukwemera .
54001014	None ingabire y’Umwami wacu yambayemo igisagirane , nsenderezwa ukwemera n’urukundo ruri muri Kristu Yezu .
54001015	Dore ijambo rigomba kwizerwa , kandi rikwiye kwakiranwa ubwuzu na bose : ni uko Kristu Yezu yaje ku isi kugira ngo akize abanyabyaha , muri bo jye nkaba uwa mbere .
54001016	Kandi kuba naragiriwe imbabazi , ni ukugira ngo Kristu Yezu ahere kuri jye , maze yerekane ubuntu bwe bwose , bityo angire urugero rw’abagomba kuzamwemera bose bizeye ubugingo bw’iteka .
54001017	Umwami w’ibihe byose , ari na We Mana imwe rukumbi , ihoraho kandi itagaragara , naharirwe icyubahiro n’ikuzo , uko ibihe bigenda bisimburana iteka . Amen .
54001018	Timote , mwana wanjye , ngiyo inyigisho nkuragije , ikaba ihuje n’ubuhanuzi bukwerekeye bakuvugiyeho kera , kugira ngo numara kubucengeramo , ubashe kurwana intambara ikwiye ,
54001019	ufite ukwemera n’umutimanama mwiza . Hari ababiretse , maze ukwemera kwabo kurayoyoka .
54001020	Abo ni nka ba Himene na Alegisanderi nashumurije Sekibi , kugira ngo bamenyereho kutazongera gutuka Imana ukundi .
54002001	Ndasaba rero nkomeje ko mbere ya byose mwakwambaza Imana , mukavuga amasengesho , mugatakamba kandi mugashimira Imana , mubigirira abantu bose .
54002002	Dukwiye gusabira abami n’abandi bategetsi bose , kugira ngo tubone kubaho mu ituze n’amahoro , turangwa n’ubusabane ku Mana kandi dutunganiwe .
54002003	Ngicyo ikintu gikwiye kandi kinogeye Imana Umukiza wacu ,
54002004	Yo ishaka ko abantu bose bakira kandi bakamenya ukuri .
54002005	Koko rero , Imana ni imwe rukumbi , n’umuhuza w’abantu n’Imana akaba umwe : ni Kristu Yezu , umuntu nyirizina ,
54002006	witanze ngo abe incungu ya bose . Ngicyo icyemezo cy’ugukizwa kwacu cyatanzwe igihe cyabigenewe kigeze ,
54002007	kandi nanjye ubwanjye nkaba naratorewe kuba intumwa yo kubyamamaza no kubyogeza . Ndavuga ukuri simbeshya , ndi umwarimu w’amahanga mu byerekeye ukwemera n’ukuri .
54002008	None rero ndashaka ko abagabo bajya basenga , aho bari hose , bakerekeza ku ijuru ibiganza bizira inenge , nta mwaga cyangwa intonganya .
54002009	Abagore na bo bagomba kugira imyifatire ikwiriye bakarimbana ubwiyoroshye , nta kurata ubukire , nta kuboha imisatsi , nta mitako ya zahabu , nta masaro cyangwa imyambaro y’igiciro ,
54002010	ahubwo bakihunda ibikorwa byiza , bya bindi bibereye abagore biyemeje kuyoboka Imana .
54002011	Igihe hari inyigisho itangwa , umugore agomba guceceka , agacisha make rwose .
54002012	Sinemereye umugore kwigisha cyangwa guha itegeko umugabo : najye ahama hamwe , aceceke .
54002013	Koko rero , Adamu ni we waremwe bwa mbere , hanyuma hakurikiraho Eva .
54002014	Kandi Adamu si we wemeye gushukwa , ahubwo umugore ni we wemeye gushukwa , maze aracumura .
54002015	Nyamara ariko azakizwa no kuba umubyeyi , apfa gusa guhorana ubwiyoroshye kandi akaba indacogora mu kwemera , mu rukundo no mu butungane .
54003001	Dore ijambo rigomba kwizerwa : ni uko umuntu wumva ashaka kuba umwepiskopi , aba yifuje gushingwa umurimo mwiza cyane .
54003002	Ariko rero , umwepiskopi agomba kuba ari umuntu w’inyangamugayo , washyingiwe rimwe risa , ntagire inda nini , agacisha make , akagira ubupfura , akamenya kwakira neza abamugana , kandi akaba ashoboye ibyo kwigisha ,
54003003	ntabe umunywi cyangwa umunyamahane , ahubwo agahorana ineza , akazira gushotorana kandi ntabe umunyabugugu .
54003004	Akamenya kugenga urugo rwe no gutoza abana be kumvira ; ibyo byose bigakorwa mu bwiyubahe .
54003005	None se koko umuntu utazi gutegeka urugo rwe bwite , yashobora ate kwita kuri Kiliziya y’Imana ?
54003006	Byongeye , ntazabe ari umuntu ugarukiye Imana mu bya vuba , hato atazatwarwa n’ubwirasi , bigatuma acirwa urwa Sekibi .
54003007	Ubundi kandi , rubanda rwo hanze rugomba kuba rumuvuga neza kugira ngo atava aho yamaganwa , cyangwa akongera kugwa mu mitego ya Sekibi .
54003008	Abadiyakoni na bo , bagomba kuba ari abantu b’inyangamugayo , bazira uburyarya , ntibarenze urugero mu kunywa inzoga , cyangwa ngo bararikire inyungu zidaciye mu mucyo .
54003009	Bagomba kandi gukomera ku iyobera ry’ukwemera , barangwa n’umutimanama ukeye .
54003010	Na bo kandi , bazabanze babagerageze , hanyuma nibasanga ari indakemwa , bazabone kubashinga umurimo w’ubudiyakoni .
54003011	N’abagore ni uko : bagomba kuba ari inyangamugayo , ntibabe abanyamazimwe , ntibagire inda nini , kandi bakaba indahemuka muri byose .
54003012	Abadiyakoni bagomba kuba barashyingiwe rimwe risa , bakanamenya gutegeka neza abana babo n’ingo zabo bwite .
54003013	Koko rero , abatunganya neza imirimo bashinzwe , bibahesha umwanya w’icyubahiro , bakanabikesha gushira amanga mu kwemera bafitiye Kristu Yezu .
54003014	Ibyo mbikwandikiye nizera ko nzaza vuba nkagusanga .
54003015	Nyamara ariko ndamutse ntinze , ni ngombwa ko umenya uko wifata mu nzu y’Imana : ndashaka kuvuga Kiliziya y’Imana nzima , yo nkingi ishyigikiye ukuri .
54003016	Rwose , nta watinya kubivuga , iyobera ry’ubusabaniramana rirakomeye : Kristu yigaragarije muri kameremuntu , aba intungane ku bwa Roho , arangamirwa n’abamalayika , yamamazwa mu banyamahanga , yemerwa ku isi hose , ajyanwa mu ikuzo .
54004001	Roho Mutagatifu abivuga yeruye ko mu minsi y’imperuka , bamwe bazihakana ukwemera , bishinge ababashukisha ibinyoma , maze batwarwe n’inyigisho zikomoka kuri Sekibi ,
54004002	bahendwe ubwenge n’abanyabinyoma buje uburyarya kandi basabitswe n’iyo ngeso ku mutima .
54004003	Abo bantu babuza abandi gushyingirwa cyangwa kurya ibiribwa bimwe , nyamara Imana ari yo yabiremye kugira ngo abayoboke bayo n’abandi bazi ukuri , bajye babirya bayishimira .
54004004	Koko rero , ikintu cyose Imana yaremye ni cyiza , nta kiribwa gikwiye kuba umuziro niba cyakiranywe umutima ushimira :
54004005	ijambo ry’Imana n’isengesho biragitagatifuza .
54004006	Ibyo byose nubisobanurira abavandimwe , uzaba ubereye Kristu Yezu umugaragu mwiza , utunzwe n’amagambo y’ukwemera n’inyigisho ziboneye witabiranye ubudahemuka .
54004007	Naho imigani y’amanjwe hamwe n’uburondogozi bw’abakecuru , urabigendere kure . Ahubwo itoze gusabanira Imana .
54004008	Koko ni byo : imyitozo y’umubiri ifite akamaro gake , naho gusabanira Imana bimaze byose , kuko ari byo birimo amasezerano y’ubugingo , ari ubwo turimo ubu , ari n’ubuzaza .
54004009	Iryo jambo rigomba kwizerwa kandi rikwiye kwakiranwa ubwuzu na bose .
54004010	Koko rero , niba tugoka ndetse tugaharana , ni uko twiringiye Imana nzima , yo Mukiza w’abantu bose , cyane cyane abayemera .
54004011	Ngibyo ibyo ugomba kwibandaho mu mabwiriza n’inyigisho utanga .
54004012	Ntihazagire ugusuzugurira ko ukiri muto . Ahubwo uzabere abayoboke urugero , ari mu magambo , ari mu migenzereze , mu rukundo , mu kwemera , no mu budakemwa .
54004013	Mu gihe ugitegereje ko nza , ihatire gusoma Ibyanditswe bitagatifu , ushishikarize abandi kugenza neza kandi utange inyigisho .
54004014	Ntuzarangarane ingabire y’Imana ikurimo , ya yindi wahawe igihe ugaragaweho n’ubuhanuzi , maze urugaga rw’abakuru b’umuryango rukakuramburiraho ibiganza .
54004015	Ibyo ngibyo bishyireho umutima , ubyibandeho rwose , maze uko ujya mbere bigende bigaragara mu maso ya bose .
54004016	Ihugukire ubwawe , uhugukire n’umurimo wawe wo kwigisha ; ube indatezuka kuri izo nama nkugiriye . Nugenza utyo , uzikiza wowe ubwawe , ukize n’abandi bose bagutega amatwi .
54005001	Ntukabwire nabi umuntu usheshe akanguhe , ahubwo ujye umuhugura nk’umubyeyi . Abasore , ujye ubafata nka bene so ;
54005002	abakecuru ujye ubagenzereza nk’ababyeyi bawe ; inkumi na zo , uzifate nka bashiki bawe ; byose kandi ubikorane umutima ukeye .
54005003	Uzajye wubaha abapfakazi ; ndavuga ariko abari bo by’ukuri .
54005004	Niba rero umupfakazi afite abana cyangwa abuzukuru , mbere na mbere ni ngombwa kubigisha kwita ku muryango wabo bwite , no kwitura ababyeyi babo ibyiza babagiriye . Ibyo ni byo rwose bishimisha Imana .
54005005	Naho umupfakazi nyakujya , wa wundi wasigaye wenyine , we yishyira mu maboko y’Imana , akibanda ku byo gusenga no kuzirikana iby’Imana ijoro n’umunsi .
54005006	Naho rero uwikurikiraniye iby’amaraha , we abarirwa mu bapfuye n’ubwo aba agihagaze .
54005007	Ibyo na byo ujye ubyibutsa kugira ngo abapfakazi babe indakemwa .
54005008	Niba umuntu atita kuri bene wabo , cyane cyane ku bo babana mu rugo , uwo aba yarihakanye ukwemera ; arutwa n’utemera na gato .
54005009	Umugore ushobora kwandikwa mu rugaga rw’abapfakazi ni uzaba agejeje nibura ku myaka mirongo itandatu , kandi akaba yarashyingiwe rimwe risa .
54005010	Agomba kuba azwiho ibikorwa byiza : nko kuba yarareze abana be neza , agacumbikira abagenzi , akoza ibirenge by’abatagatifujwe , agatabara imbabare , mbese agashishikarira ibikorwa byose by’ubugiraneza .
54005011	Abapfakazi bakiri bato , bo uzabihorere ; iyo ibyifuzo bidakwiranye na Kristu bibatashyemo , bumva bashaka gushyingirwa na none ,
54005012	bityo bakikururira umugayo , kuko baba batatiye amasezerano yabo ya mbere .
54005013	Nuko rero , kubera ko baba ari imburamukoro , bagakurizaho kuzerera mu mihana ; usibye no kuba imburamukoro gusa , baba bagiye kurondogora no kwivanga mu bitabareba , no kurocangwa .
54005014	Ndashaka rero ko abapfakazi bakiri bato bakongera gushyingirwa , bakabyara abana , bakagenga ingo zabo , bityo ntibahe umwanzi urwaho ngo abambike urubwa .
54005015	Ni koko , hari bamwe muri bo barohamye bakurikiye Sekibi .
54005016	Niba hari umukristukazi ufite benewabo b’abapfakazi , najye abitaho , kugira ngo bitaba ngombwa ko Kiliziya ibishingira , ahubwo ishobore kurwana ku bari abapfakazi by’ukuri .
54005017	Abakuru b’ikoraniro bariyobora neza , bakwiye kubyubahirwa kabiri , cyane cyane abagokera ku murimo wo kwamamaza ijambo ry’Imana no kurisobanura .
54005018	Koko rero Ibyanditswe biravuga , ngo « Ntuzahambire umunwa w’ikimasa kivungagura ingano » , kandi ngo « Umukozi akwiye igihembo cye . » .
54005019	Ntuzakire ikirego gishinja umukuru w’ikoraniro nta gihamya cy’abagabo babiri cyangwa batatu
54005020	Abakoze icyaha , urajye ubihanangiriza ubigiriye mu ruhame rwa bose , kugira ngo n’abandi bagire ubwoba .
54005021	Mbigusabiye imbere y’Imana , n’imbere ya Kristu n’abamalayika b’intore , urakurikize aya mategeko nta ho ubogamiye , ntuzagire icyo ukora ugambiriye kugira uwo ubera .
54005022	Ntuzagire ubwira bwo kuramburira ibiganza ku muntu ubonetse wese , hato utagira uruhare ku cyaha cy’undi . Nawe kandi ubwawe , urakomeze kuba umuziranenge .
54005023	Uzareke kunywa amazi yonyine , ahubwo uzajye unywa na ka divayi gakeya kubera igifu cyawe n’intege nke uhorana .
54005024	Hariho abantu ibyaha bihama na mbere y’uko babacira urubanza ; ariko hariho n’abo bigaragaraho nyuma .
54005025	Ibikorwa byiza na byo ni uko , birigaragaza ; ndetse n’ibitari byiza ntibishobora kuguma mu bwihisho .
54006001	Abari ku ngoyi y’ubucakara bose bagomba kumva ko ba shebuja bakwiye icyubahiro cyose , kugira ngo Izina ry’Imana n’inyigisho y’ukuri bitazatukwa .
54006002	Abafite ba shebuja b’abakristu , baririnde kubasuzugura bitwaje ko ari abavandimwe . Ahubwo bazabakorere neza kurushaho , kuko nyine iyo mirimo iba igenewe abayoboke n’abavandimwe batoneshejwe n’Imana . Ngibyo ibyo ugomba kwigisha no gushishikariza abandi .
54006003	Nihagira umuntu wigisha ukundi , ntiyite ku magambo aboneye y’Umwami wacu Yezu Kristu no ku nyigisho itoza gusabanira Imana ,
54006004	azaba ari umuntu wahumishijwe n’ubwirasi ; aba ari injiji irwaye gukurura impaka no guterana amagambo . Aho ni ho hava ishyari , amakimbirane , gutukana , gukekana nabi ,
54006005	n’impaka z’urudaca ziterwa n’abantu bararutse umutima , batakimenya ukuri , kandi bakibwira ko ubusabaniramana ari uburyo bwo kwishakira inyungu .
54006006	Yego nanone gusabanira Imana birimo inyungu nyinshi cyane , ariko ku muntu wishimiye ibyo afite .
54006007	Koko rero , nta kintu twazanye kuri iyi si , kandi ni na ko nta cyo dushobora kuzayimukanaho .
54006008	Igihe rero dufite ibyo kurya n’icyo kwambara , tujye dushimishwa n’ibyo .
54006009	Naho abararikiye kurunda ubukire , bagwa mu mutego w’ibishuko no mu byifuzo byinshi by’ubucucu n’ubugiranabi , bya bindi biroha abantu mu butindi no mu cyorezo .
54006010	Ni koko , umuzi w’ibibi byose ni irari ry’imari . Kubera ko bamwe bayohotseho , byatumye bitandukanya n’ukwemera , maze umutima wabo ushengurwa n’imibabaro itabarika .
54006011	Naho wowe , muntu w’Imana , ibyo bintu ubihe akato ; ahubwo ujye uharanira ubutungane , ubusabaniramana , ukwemera , urukundo , ubwiyumanganye n’ubugwaneza .
54006012	Rwana intambara nyayo y’ukwemera , uronke ubugingo bw’iteka wahamagariwe , nk’uko wabyiyemeje igihe wahamyaga ukwemera kwawe ushize amanga , mu ruhame rwa benshi .
54006013	Mbigutegekeye imbere y’Imana ibeshaho byose , n’imbere ya Kristu Yezu wabaye umuhamya uhebuje w’Imana imbere ya Ponsiyo Pilato :
54006014	wite ku mategeko , ukomeze kuba umuziranenge n’indakemwa kugeza ku munsi w’Ukwigaragaza kw’Umwami wacu Yezu Kristu .
54006015	Koko rero igihe cyagenywe nikigera , azagaragazwa n’Imana Nyir’ihirwe na Mugengabyose umwe rukumbi , Umwami w’abami , n’Umutegetsi w’abategetsi ,
54006016	Yo yonyine yihariye ukudapfa , igahora ituye mu rumuri rudahangarwa , ntihagire umuntu n’umwe waba yarayibonye cyangwa ngo ashobore kuzayibona bibaho . Niharirwe icyubahiro n’ububasha ubuziraherezo ! Amen .
54006017	Abakire bo kuri iyi si , ubasabe ukomeje kutirata no kutiringira ubukungu buyoyoka , ahubwo bizere Imana , yo itugabira byose uko dushaka ngo tubitunge .
54006018	Nibajye bagenza neza , babe abakire ku bikorwa byiza , batange batitangiriye itama , bamenye gusangira n’abandi .
54006019	Bityo , bazaba bizigamiye ubwabo ubukungu nyabwo mu gihe kizaza , bazakesha kuronka ubugingo nyakuri .
54006020	Timote rero , wite ku byo waragijwe , wirinde abavuga amagambo y’amahomvu n’ubwigomeke ku Mana , bakabyutsa impaka zishingiye ku ngirwabuhanga .
54006021	Kubera ko ari bwo bashyize imbere , byatumye bamwe bitandukanya n’inzira y’ukwemera . Ineza y’Imana ihorane namwe !
55002001	Wowe rero , mwana wanjye , wikomezemo ingabire ukesha Kristu Yezu .
55002002	Kandi ibyo wanyumvanye mu ruhame rwa benshi , nawe ubihererekanye mu bantu b’indahemuka , kandi bazashobora na bo kubyigisha abandi .
55002003	Emera ufatanye nanjye imibabaro , nk’uko bikwiriye umusirikare mwiza wa Kristu Yezu .
55002004	Nta n’umwe mu bajya ku rugamba ukomeza kwizirika ku mirimo yari asanganywe , ngo abe agishimishije uwamuhuruje .
55002005	Kandi n’urushanwa ku kibuga cy’imikino wese , ntahabwa ikamba atabanje kurushanwa akurikije amategeko .
55002006	Umuhinzi wagotse ni we ukwiriye kubanza kuganura ku mbuto z’ibyo yahinze .
55002007	Ngira ngo urumva icyo nshaka kuvuga ; n’ubundi kandi , Nyagasani ubwe azaguha kubyumva byose .
55002008	Ujye wibuka Yezu Kristu wazutse mu bapfuye , kandi uvuka mu bwoko bwa Dawudi , nk’uko Inkuru Nziza namamaza ibihamya .
55002009	Ni na yo mporwa , ngatotezwa , nkabohwa , boshye umugome . Nyamara ariko ijambo ry’Imana ntiribohwa !
55002010	Ni cyo gituma nihanganira byose mbigirira abo Imana yatoye , kugira ngo na bo babone umukiro uba muri Kristu Yezu , babone n’ikuzo rizahoraho iteka .
55002011	Dore ijambo rikwiye kwizerwa : Nidupfana na We , tuzabaho hamwe na We ;
55002012	nituba intwari hamwe na We , tuzima ingoma hamwe na We ; nitumwihakana , na We azatwihakana ;
55002013	nituramuka tubaye abahemu , We azaguma kuba indahemuka , kuko adashobora kwivuguruza .
55002014	Jya wibutsa abandi ibyo ngibyo , kandi urahirire imbere y’Imana ko ari ngombwa kwirinda kujya mu mpaka z’amahomvu , zidafite icyo zimaze , uretse gusa kuyobya abazumva .
55002015	Ihatire guhagarara imbere y’Imana nk’umuntu w’inararibonye , nk’umukozi mwiza udakwiye kugira ipfunwe , nk’umugabuzi udahemuka w’ijambo ry’ukuri .
55002016	Naho amagambo y’amahomvu n’ubwigomeke ku Mana ujye uyagendera kure , kuko bene kuyavuga bazakomeza kurorongotana mu nzira y’ubugomeramana ,
55002017	maze ijambo ryabo rigende rimunga byose nk’igisebe cy’umufunzo . Muri bo navuga nka Himene na Fileto ,
55002018	baciye ukubiri n’ukuri , bakiha kuvuga ko izuka ryarangije kubaho , bityo bagahubanganya ukwemera kwa benshi .
55002019	Nyamara ishingiro rihamye Imana yashyizeho riracyakomeye kandi rizahoraho , rikarangwa n’aya magambo aryanditsweho ngo « Imana izi abayo » , kandi ngo « Abambaza izina ry’Uhoraho bose nibitarure ikibi . »
55002020	N’ubundi , mu nzu ngari ntihabamo gusa inkongoro zakozwe muri zahabu na feza , ahubwo habamo n’izakozwe mu biti no mu ibumba ; zimwe zikagenerwa iby’icyubahiro , naho izindi bakazikoresha imirimo isuzuguritse .
55002021	Umuntu wese rero niyirinda gukora ibibi navuze , azaba nk’inkongoro yubahiritse , yatagatifujwe kandi y’ingirakamaro kuri Nyirayo , mbese ibereye imirimo myiza yose .
55002022	Irinde rero imigenzo mibi y’abasore , ahubwo uharanire ubutungane , ukwemera , urukundo , n’amahoro , wunge ubumwe n’abiyambaza Nyagasani barangwa n’umutima ukeye .
55002023	Naho ibibazo n’ubushakashatsi bitagira shinge na rugero , ubyitarure : uzi ko bibyara impaka z’ubusa .
55002024	Umugaragu wa Nyagasani rero ntakwiriye kuba umunyamahane , ahubwo akwiye kuba umugwaneza kuri bose , akamenya kwigisha no kwiyumanganya ibyago .
55002025	Iyo hagize abamugisha impaka , abahugurana imico myiza , kuko aba yizeye ko wenda Imana izabaha kwisubiraho , bakamenya ukuri ,
55002026	bakongera gushyira mu gaciro bamaze kwigobotora mu mitego ya Sekibi wari warabagize imfungwa ze , akabakoresha icyo ashaka .
55003001	Umenye neza kandi ko mu minsi y’imperuka hazaza ibihe by’amakuba .
55003002	Koko hazagwira abantu bikunda ubwabo , n’abafite inyota nyinshi y’ibintu , n’abirasi , n’abikuza , n’abanyarubwa , n’ibyigomeke ku babyeyi , n’indashima , n’inkorashyano ,
55003003	n’abagome , n’abazirampuhwe , n’abanyamazimwe , n’abatihanganira abandi , n’indakoreka , n’abanzi b’ibyiza ,
55003004	n’abagambanyi , n’ibishihanyi , n’abahumwe amaso n’ubwirasi , n’abakunda ibyishimo by’umubiri aho gukunda Imana ,
55003005	n’abiha isura y’ubusabaniramana , ariko mu by’ukuri bahakana ishingiro ryabwo . N’abo ngabo rero urabirinde .
55003006	Ndetse n’ubu , bene abo babarimo ; navuga nk’abacengera mu ngo , bagashuka abagore b’abapfayongo baheranywe n’ibyaha , bagatwarwa n’ingeso mbi zose ,
55003007	maze n’ubwo bahora baharanira kwigishwa , ugasanga badashobora na busa kumenya ukuri .
55003008	Nk’uko kera Yanesi na Yambure barwanije Musa , ni na ko abo ngabo barwanya ukuri , kuko ari abantu bafite umutima ucuramye , ntibagire ukwemera guhamye .
55003009	Ariko ntibazashobora kubikomeza , kuko amaherezo ubusazi bwabo buzatahurwa na bose , nk’uko ubwa bariya bombi bwagaragaye .
55003010	Naho wowe , wakomeje kunkurikira muri byose : mu nyigisho zanjye , mu migenzereze yanjye , mu migambi yanjye , mu kwemera kwanjye , mu kwihangana kwanjye , mu rukundo n’ubudacogora byanjye ,
55003011	mu bitotezo n’ibyago naboneye Antiyokiya , n’Ikoniyo n’i Lisitiri . Mbega ibitotezo nabonye ! Ariko byose Nyagasani yabinkuyemo .
55003012	Ni koko , abashaka bose kubaho muri Kristu barangwa n’ubuyoboke , ntibazabura gutotezwa .
55003013	Naho abagiranabi n’abahendanyi , bo ntibazabura kugenda barushaho gukora nabi ubudahwema bataretse guhenda abandi no guhendwa ubwabo .
55003014	Ariko wowe , gumya kwibanda ku byo wigishijwe kandi wakiriye udashidikanya . Uzi neza uwo ubikomoraho ;
55003015	kandi kuva mu buto bwawe wamenye Ibyanditswe Bitagatifu ; ni byo bishobora kukubera isoko y’ubuhanga bukuganisha ku mukiro ubikesheje kwemera Kristu Yezu .
55003016	Icyitwa Igitabo gitagatifu cyose cyahumekewemo n’Imana kandi gifite akamaro mu byerekeye kwigisha , no kuvuguruza ubuyobe , gukosora no gutoza umuntu iby’ubutungane ;
55003017	bityo umuntu w’Imana wese akabasha kuba igihame kandi akabona intwaro zimufasha gukora icyiza cyose .
55004001	Nkurahirije imbere y’Imana n’imbere ya Kristu Yezu uzacira imanza abazima n’abapfuye , ku mpamvu y’ukwigaragaza kwe n’Ubwami bwe :
55004002	amamaza ijambo , uryigishe igihe n’imburagihe , wumvishe ingingo , utote , ushishikaze , mu bwihangane butarambirwa , uharanira kujijura .
55004003	Kuko hazaza igihe abantu batazihanganira inyigisho ziboneye , ahubwo bakurikije irari ryabo , n’ubukirigitwa bw’amatwi yabo , bakazikoranyirizaho umukumbi w’abigisha ,
55004004	maze ukuri bakakwima amatwi yabo , ngo bahugukire ibitagira shinge .
55004005	Wowe rero urabe maso muri byose , wiyumanganye ibitotezo , ushishikarire kogeza Inkuru Nziza , urangize neza ubutumwa bwawe .
55004006	Naho jyewe , dore maze kumera nk’igitambo giseswa , n’amagingo y’ukwigendera kwanjye aregereje .
55004007	Urugamba rwiza narurwanye inkundura , intera nagombaga kwiruka narayirangije , ukwemera nagukomeyeho .
55004008	None dore ikamba rigenewe intungane rirantegereje , iryo Nyagasani umucamanza utabera azangororera kuri wa Munsi we , ariko atari jyewe jyenyine , ahubwo n’abandi bose bazaba barakunze Ukwigaragaza kwe .
55004009	Banguka uze kundeba bidatinze ,
55004010	kuko Demasi yantaye , abitewe no gukunda iyi isi : yigiriye i Tesaloniki ; Kirisensi na we yagiye mu Bugalati , Tito ajya muri Dalimatiya ,
55004011	Luka ni we wenyine tukiri kumwe . Shaka Mariko , muzazane , kuko amfitiye akamaro cyane mu byo kumfasha ;
55004012	Tushiko , namwohereje Efezi .
55004013	Nuza , uzanzanire umwitero wanjye nasize i Torowadi kwa Karupo ; uzanzanire n’ibitabo byanjye , cyane cyane iby’impu .
55004014	Alegisanderi w’umucuzi yangiriye nabi cyane ; Nyagasani azamwitura ibihwanye n’ibikorwa bye .
55004015	Nawe umwirinde , kuko arwanya bikomeye ibyo twigisha .
55004016	Ubwo najyaga mu rukiko bwa mbere kugira ngo niregure , nta n’umwe wanshyigikiye ; bose barantereranye . Ntibazabihorwe !
55004017	Naho Nyagasani we yambaye hafi , maze antera imbaraga kugira ngo mbashe kuhamamariza ubutumwa nshize amanga , kandi ngo abanyamahanga bose babwumve . Nuko nkizwa urwasaya rw’intare .
55004018	Nyagasani azansimbukisha ikintu cyose kigamije kungirira nabi , maze ankize anjyana mu Ngoma ye y’ijuru . Naharirwe ikuzo uko ibihe bigenda bisimburana iteka ! Amen .
55004019	Utashye Purisika na Akwila , n’urugo rwa Onesifori .
55004020	Erasito yasigaye i Korinti ; naho Tirofimo namusize i Mileto arwaye .
55004021	Wihutire kuza mbere y’itumba . Ewubuli aragutashya , na Pudensi , na Lini , na Kalawudiya , n’abavandimwe bose .
55004022	Nyagasani nabane nawe . Ineza ye nihorane namwe !
56001001	Jyewe Pawulo , umugaragu w’Imana n’intumwa ya Yezu Kristu igenewe kugeza intore z’Imana ku kwemera no ku bumenyi bw’ukuri guhuje n’ubusabaniramana ,
56001002	mu bwizere bwo kuzabona ubugingo buhoraho , ubwo Imana itabasha kubeshya yasezeranye mbere y’ibihe bya kera na kare ,
56001003	maze amagingo yagennye yagera ikamenyekanya ijambo ryayo ibigirishije iyamamazabutumwa nashinzwe ku bushake bw’Imana Umukiza wacu :
56001004	kuri Tito , umwana wanjye nyakuri nabyaye mu byerekeye ukwemera duhuriyeho , nkwifurije ineza n’amahoro biva ku Mana Data no kuri Kristu Yezu Umukiza wacu .
56001005	Nagusize i Kireta ari ukugira ngo utunganye ibyo nasize bituzuye , kandi ngo ushyireho abakuru b’ikoraniro mu migi yose ukurikije amabwiriza naguhaye .
56001006	Buri wese uhawe ubwo bukuru agomba kuba ari indakemwa , yarashyingiwe rimwe risa , afite abana bemera batavugwaho ubwomanzi cyangwa kuba intumvira .
56001007	Koko rero , umwepiskopi , kubera ko ari umugabuzi w’ibintu by’Imana , agomba kuba indakemwa , ntabe umwirasi n’umunyamwaga , ntabe umunywi n’indwanyi , ntabe n’umuntu ukurikiranye inyungu itanyuze mu mucyo ,
56001008	ahubwo akamenya kwakira abamugana , agakunda ibiboneye , akitonda , akaba intabera n’umuyoboke ku Mana , akamenya kwitsinda ,
56001009	kandi akihatira gutanga inyigisho zitagoragora , zihuje n’idini , kugira ngo abone uko ashishikariza abandi inyigisho ziboneye , n’uko kandi amwaza abamugisha impaka .
56001010	Koko rero hariho benshi b’ibyigomeke , n’abavuga ibitagira shinge , n’abashukanyi , cyane cyane mu bagenywe .
56001011	Abo ngabo ni ngombwa kubaziba akanwa , kuko bahubanganya ingo nyinshi , igihe baba bigisha ibidakwiye kugira ngo bibonere inyungu mbi .
56001012	Umwe muri bo , umuhanuzi wabo bwite , yaravuze ati « Abanyakireta ! Ni abanyabinyoma iteka , ni inyamaswa mbi , ni abanyenda mbi b’abanebwe . »
56001013	Icyo cyemezo gihuje n’ukuri . Kubera ibyo rero , ujye ubacyaha cyane , kugira ngo bagumane ukwemera nyako ,
56001014	boye kwita ku migani y’amahomvu y’Abayahudi , no ku mategeko y’abantu bihunza ukuri .
56001015	Ikintu cyose kiba cyiza ku bere . Naho ku bandavuye kandi badafite ukwemera , nta na kimwe kiba cyiza ; ahubwo ubwenge n’umutimanama byabo byarandavuye .
56001016	Biratana ko bazi Imana , nyamara bakayihakana mu migirire yabo . Bateye isesemi , bakaba ibyigomeke ; no ku cyitwa igikorwa cyiza cyose , nta cyo bamaze .
56002001	Wowe rero , jya uvuga ibikwiranye n’inyigisho ziboneye .
56002002	Abasaza nibajye birinda isindwe , biyubahe , bashyire mu gaciro , bakomere mu kwemera , mu rukundo , n’ubudacogora .
56002003	N’abakecuru ni uko , na bo bagomba kwifata nk’uko bikwiriye abatagatifujwe : nibirinde amazimwe no gutwarwa n’akayoga , ahubwo bajye batoza abandi ingeso nziza ;
56002004	bityo bigishe abagore bakiri bato gukunda abagabo babo n’abana babo ,
56002005	banabatoze kwitonda , kwirinda ingeso mbi , kwita ku by’ingo zabo , kugwa neza , no kumvira abagabo babo , kugira ngo ijambo ry’Imana bataritukisha .
56002006	Jya ushishikaza n’abasore ngo bashyire mu gaciro .
56002007	Nawe ubwawe kandi jya ubabera urugero rwiza mu byo ukora byose : haba mu nyigisho ziboneye , haba se mu kwiyubaha ,
56002008	cyangwa mu magambo aboneye kandi adahinyuka ; bityo umubisha azabure ikibi yatuvugaho , maze amware .
56002009	Wigishe n’abacakara kumvira ba shebuja no kubashimisha muri byose , batabagisha impaka ,
56002010	birinde kwiba , ahubwo bahore barangwa n’ubudahemuka budakemangwa ; bityo bazubahisha muri byose inyigisho z’Imana Umukiza wacu .
56002011	Koko rero ineza y’Imana , soko y’umukiro ku bantu bose , yarigaragaje ,
56002012	itwigisha kureka kugomera Imana no gutwarwa n’irari ry’iby’iyi si , kugira ngo guhera ubu ngubu tubeho turangwa n’ubwitonzi , ubutungane , n’ubusabaniramana ,
56002013	mu gihe tugitegereje ya mizero mahire hamwe n’Ukwigaragaza kwa Yezu Kristu yisesuyeho ikuzo , We Mana yacu y’igihangange , akaba n’Umukiza wacu ,
56002014	witanze kubera twebwe , kugira ngo aturokore ubugome bwose kandi yuhagire umuryango ugenewe kuba ubukonde bwe no kugira ishyaka ryo gukora icyiza cyose .
56002015	Ujye uvuga ibyo ngibyo , ubibashishikarize , ndetse ubacyahe ubigiranye igitsure cy’umutware . Ntihakagire ugusuzugura .
56003001	Jya wibutsa bose ko bagomba kuyoboka abatware n’abategetsi , bakabumvira , bagahora bakereye gukora umurimo mwiza wose ,
56003002	ntibagire uwo batuka , bakirinda kurwana , bakaba abantu bagira neza , bakagaragariza abandi bose ubugwaneza budakemwa .
56003003	Koko rero natwe kera twari ibicucu , n’intumvira , n’ibirara ; twari twaratwawe n’irari ry’ibibi bitagira ingano , tukibera mu bugizi bwa nabi n’ishyari , dufite n’icyangiro , kandi natwe ubwacu tuzirana .
56003004	Ariko igihe higaragaje ubuntu bw’Imana Umukiza wacu n’urukundo ifitiye abantu ,
56003005	yaradukijije , itabitewe n’ibyiza twaba twarakoze , ahubwo ibitewe n’impuhwe igira , idukirisha icyuhagiro dukesha kuvuka bwa kabiri no guhinduka abantu bashya muri Roho Mutagatifu .
56003006	Kandi uwo Roho , yamudusakajemo ku bwa Yezu Kristu Umukiza wacu ,
56003007	kugira ngo tube intungane , kandi twiringire kuzahabwa umurage w’ubugingo bw’iteka , tubikesha ubuntu bwayo .
56003008	Iryo jambo rikwiye kwizerwa , kandi ndashaka ko kuri izo ngingo wajya uvuga wihanukiriye , kugira ngo abemeye Imana barushanwe kugira umwete wo kugenza neza . Ibyo ni byo byiza bifitiye abantu akamaro .
56003009	Naho ibibazo bidafite ishingiro , n’ibyerekeye amasekuruza , intonganya n’impaka za ngo turwane zerekeye Amategeko , jya ubigendera kure , kuko ari nta cyo bimaze kandi bikaba iby’ubusa .
56003010	Nihagira umuntu uca ukubiri n’ukwemera , maze wamuburira ubwa mbere n’ubwa kabiri ntiyumve , uzatane na we ;
56003011	uzi yuko bene uwo muntu aba yarataye inzira , akaba n’umunyabyaha wicira ubwe urubanza rubi .
56003012	Ninkoherereza Aritemasi na Tushiko , uzihutire kunsanga i Nikopoli , kuko ari ho nageneye kuzamara itumba .
56003013	Ugire umwete wo gutegura urugendo rwa Zenasi , impuguke mu by’amategeko , n’urwa Apolo , kugira ngo batazagira icyo babura .
56003014	Kandi n’abacu bitoze kurushanwa kugira umwete wo kugenza neza , bakenure ababikwiriye , kugira ngo batabura icyo bamarira abandi .
56003015	Abo turi kumwe bose baragutashya . Nawe utashye abadukunda dusangiye ukwemera . Ineza y’Imana ihorane namwe mwese .
57001001	Jyewe Pawulo , infungwa kubera Kristu Yezu , n’umuvandimwe Timote , kuri Filemoni umufasha wacu dukunda , no kuri Afiya mushiki wacu ,
57001002	no kuri Arikipo twatabaranye ku rugamba , no kuri Kiliziya iteranira mu nzu yawe :
57001003	tubifurije ineza n’amahoro bituruka ku Mana Umubyeyi wacu no kuri Nyagasani Yezu Kristu .
57001004	Mpora nkwibuka mu masengesho , ngashimira Imana yanjye ,
57001005	kuko numva barata urukundo n’ukwemera ufitiye Nyagasani Yezu n’abatagatifujwe bose .
57001006	Ndagusabira kugira ngo uko kwemera kube gushingiye ku bikorwa , maze ugaragarize mu ruhame ibyiza byose twashobora kugirira Kristu .
57001007	Koko , muvandimwe , nagize ibyishimo bikomeye , kandi ndahozwa ku mpamvu y’urukundo rwawe , numvise ukuntu wahumurije imitima y’abatagatifujwe .
57001008	Kubera ibyo , n’ubwo mfite uburenganzira bwose muri Kristu bwo kugutegeka ibyo ugomba gukora ,
57001009	mpisemo kwiyambaza urukundo , jyewe Pawulo w’umusaza , nkubitiyeho no kuba ndi infungwa kubera Yezu Kristu ubu ngubu .
57001010	Ndagutakambira kubera umwana wanjye nabyariye mu buroko , Onezimi uwo nguwo ,
57001011	wakubereye imburamumaro , ariko noneho azatubera twembi ingirakamaro .
57001012	Ubu ndamukugaruriye , we nkoramutima yanjye .
57001013	Nashakaga kumugumana hafi yanjye , kugira ngo ajye amfasha mu kigwi cyawe , muri ubu buroko nafungiwemo mporwa Inkuru Nziza .
57001014	Ariko nta cyo nashatse gukora utabyemeye , kugira ngo icyo gikorwa cyiza kitakubera agahato , ahubwo gituruke ku bwende bwawe .
57001015	Kandi wenda wamubuze igihe gito none arakugarukiye , kugira ngo uzamuhorane iteka .
57001016	Uzasanga atakiri umucakara , ahubwo atambutse umucakara , usange ari umuvandimwe wawe ukunda : jyeweho ni ko amereye rwose , nawe ni ko azakumerera ndetse arusheho , ari mu maso y’abantu , ari no mu maso ya Nyagasani .
57001017	Niba rero wemera ko ndi incuti yawe , uramwakire nk’uko wanyakira .
57001018	Kandi niba hari icyawe yatwaye cyangwa akaba akurimo umwenda , uzabimbaze .
57001019	Jyewe Pawulo ndabyiyandikiye ubwanjye : nzabyishyura . . . siniriwe mvuga ko nawe undimo umwenda , kandi uwo mwenda ni wowe ubwawe .
57001020	Ngaho , muvandimwe , ungirire ubwo buntu muri Nyagasani , ushimishe umutima wanjye muri Kristu !
57001021	Nkwandikiye niringiye rwose ko uzanyumva ; ndetse nzi neza ko uzakora ibitambutse ibyo ngusabye .
57001022	Byongeye kandi , untegurire n’icumbi , kuko nizeye ko bazandekura nkabagarukira mbikesheje amasengesho yanyu .
57001023	Aragutashya Epafurasi dufunganywe kubera Kristu Yezu .
57001024	Na Mariko aragutashya , na Arisitariko , na Demasi , na Luka , abafasha banjye .
57001025	Nimuhorane ineza ya Nyagasani Yezu Kristu !
58001001	Imana imaze kubwira abasokuruza bacu kenshi no ku buryo bwinshi , ikoresheje abahanuzi ,
58001002	natwe muri iyi minsi turimo , ari na yo y’imperuka , yatubwirishije Umwana wayo , ari We yageneye kwegurirwa byose , akaba ari na We yabiremesheje byose iyo biva bikagera .
58001003	Mwana uwo , ni We buranga bw’ikuzo ry’Imana n’ishusho rya kamere yayo , ni na We kandi uhagaritse byose ku bubasha bw’ijambo rye . Amaze rero kuhagira abantu ibyaha byabo , yicaye iburyo bwa Nyirikuzo mu ijuru .
58001004	Asumba atyo abamalayika kuko n’izina yahawe ritambutse kure ayabo .
58001005	Koko rero , ni nde wo mu bamalayika Imana yigeze ibwira iti « Uri Umwana wanjye ; ni Jye wakwibyariye uyu munsi » ? Cyangwa se iti , « Nzamubera umubyeyi , na we ambere umwana » ?
58001006	Kandi igihe yohereje imfura yayo ku isi , yaravuze iti « Abamalayika bose b’Imana bazamupfukamire . »
58001007	Abamalayika bo , ibavugaho iti « Abamalayika bayo yabagize nk’imiyaga , maze abagaragu bayo ibagira nk’imirabyo . »
58001008	Naho Umwana wayo iramubwira iti « Mana , intebe yawe y’ubwami ihoraho iteka ; umuryango wawe , uwuyoborana ubutabera .
58001009	Ukunda ibiboneye ukazirana n’ubukozi bw’ibibi . Ni yo mpamvu Imana , Imana yawe , yishimiye kugusiga amavuta y’ubutore , ikurobanuye muri bagenzi bawe . »
58001010	Irongera iti « Nyagasani , ni wowe wahanze isi kuva mu ntangiriro , n’ijuru rikaba igikorwa cy’ibiganza byawe .
58001011	Ibyo byose bizayoyoka , ariko wowe uhoraho iteka . Isi n’ijuru bizashira ak’imyenda ishaje ,
58001012	uzabizingazinga nk’igishura , maze bizasimburwe nk’uko umwenda ukura undi . Naho wowe uhora uri wa wundi , n’imibereho yawe ntigira iherezo » .
58001013	Ni nde wo mu bamalayika bayo Imana yigeze ibwira iti « Icara iburyo bwanjye , kugeza ko abanzi bawe mbahinduramo akabaho ushyira mu nsi y’ibirenge byawe » ?
58001014	Abamalayika rero bagenewe iki ? Si ibiremwa se bigaragira Imana kandi yohereza gufasha abazahabwa umurage w’uburokorwe ?
58002001	Ni yo mpamvu tugomba guhugukira cyane ibyo twumvise , niba tudashaka kugenda tuyobagurika .
58002002	Tuzirikane ukuntu ijambo ryavuzwe kera n’abamalayika ryabaye impamo , n’ukuntu abarirenzeho bakarisuzugura bikururiye igihano kibakwiye .
58002003	Twebwe rero twazarokoka dute niba turangaranye umukiro wa bene ako kageni , wabanje kwamamazwa na Nyagasani ubwe , nyuma natwe abawumvise tukawuhamya ,
58002004	kandi Imana ubwayo iwukomeresha ibimenyetso , ibitangaza n’ibikorwa by’impangare by’amoko yose , n’ingabire Roho Mutagatifu atanga nk’uko abishaka .
58002005	Abamalayika si bo bahawe kugenga isi izaza tuvuga . Umwanditsi wa zaburi abihamya agira ati
58002006	« Umuntu ni iki kugira ngo wirirwe umwibuka ? Mwene Muntu ni iki kugira ngo wirirwe umwitaho ?
58002007	Wamucishije bugufi y’abamalayika ho gato ; umutamiriza ikamba ry’ikuzo n’icyubahiro ;
58002008	ibintu byose ubishyira mu nsi ye . » Ubwo byose yamuhaye kubigenga , nta kintu na kimwe rero kitamweguriwe . Icyakora kuri ubu ntibiragaragara ko byose byamuyobotse ,
58002009	nyamara dore icyo tubona : Yezu uwo , wagizwe muto ku bamalayika mu gihe kigufi , ubu kubera ko yababaye agapfa , tumubona atamirije ikamba ry’ikuzo n’icyubahiro . Bityo , ku bw’ineza y’Imana , urupfu yigabije rwagiriye buri muntu akamaro .
58002010	Mu by’ukuri , byari bikwiye ko Imana , Yo irema byose ikabibeshaho , igira ikirenga Umwana wayo — ari we uburokorwe bwose buturukaho — , imunyujije mu bubabare , ngo ibonereho kwigarurira abana batabarika basangira ikuzo ryayo .
58002011	Koko rero utagatifuza n’abatagatifujwe basangiye inkomoko , bigatuma adashidikanya kubita abavandimwe ,
58002012	avuga ati « Nzogeza izina ryawe mu bavandimwe banjye ; nzagusingirize rwagati mu ikoraniro . »
58002013	Akongera ati « Ni we nzashyiramo amizero yanjye . » Kandi ati « Dore ndi hano , jyewe n’abana Imana yampaye . »
58002014	None rero , ubwo abana bafitanye ubumwe bw’amaraso n’umubiri , Yezu na We yasangiye na bo ubwo bumwe kugira ngo mu rupfu rwe atsiratsize umugenga warwo , ari we Sekibi ,
58002015	maze abohore abatinyaga urupfu rubahoza mu bucakara igihe cy’ubuzima bwabo bwose .
58002016	Koko ntiyaje atabaye abamalayika , ahubwo yaje atabaye inkomoko y'Abrahamu .
58002017	Kubera iyo mpamvu yagombaga kwishushanya n’abavandimwe be muri byose , akaba Umuherezagitambo Mukuru w’umunyampuhwe , kandi wishyikira ku Mana ngo ahanagure ibyaha by’imbaga .
58002018	Ubwo We yababaye kandi akageragezwa , ashobora no gutabara abageragezwa .
58003001	Nuko rero , bavandimwe mwatagatifujwe mukaba musangiye ubutorwe bw’ijuru , nimuhugukire Uwo twohererejweho Umuherezagitambo Mukuru ari na We ukwemera kwacu gushingiyeho .
58003002	Yabereye indahemuka Uwamushinze inzu ye yose , nk’uko byabaye kuri Musa .
58003003	Mu by’ukuri ikuzo rye risumbye kure irya Musa , mu rugero rw’uko uwubatse inzu arusha icyubahiro iyo nzu yubatse .
58003004	Buri nzu yose igira umwubatsi , ariko umwubatsi wa byose ni Imana .
58003005	Musa yashinzwe inzu yayo yose , ari umugaragu wo guhamya ibyo Imana yari igiye kuvuga .
58003006	Naho Kristu We yashinzwe inzu yayo , ari Umwana bwite . Iyo nzu yayo ni twebwe , niba twikomejemo ubwiringire buhamye , kandi tugaterwa ishema n’ukwizera dufite .
58003007	Ni nk’uko Roho Mutagatifu abihamya , ati « Uyu munsi , nimwumva ijwi rye ,
58003008	ntimunangire imitima yanyu nk’igihe cy’amananiza , nk’uko byabaye ku munsi w’igeragezwa , mu butayu ;
58003009	aho abasekuruza banyu bangeragereje , bashaka kunyinja , n’ubwo bari barabonye ibikorwa byanjye , mu myaka mirongo ine .
58003010	Ni cyo cyatumye ndakarira iyo nyoko , maze ndavuga nti ’ Iteka ryose umutima wabo urararuka ; ntibamenye inzira zanjye ! ’
58003011	None narahije uburakari bwanjye ko batazinjira mu buruhukiro bwanjye ! »
58003012	Muramenye rero , bavandimwe , ntihakabe n’umwe muri mwe wigiramo umutima mubi , ngo yitandukanye n’Imana Nzima abitewe no kubura ukwemera .
58003013	Ahubwo buri munsi nimuterane inkunga , igihe cyose hakiri « Uyu munsi » Ibyanditswe bivuga , maze ntihagire n’umwe muri mwe unangira umutima , ayobejwe n’icyaha .
58003014	Twabaye koko umwe na Kristu , niba ariko dukomeje kudahinyuka ku mimerere yacu yo mu ntangiriro ,
58003015	nk’uko byanditswe ngo « Uyu munsi , nimwumva ijwi rye , ntimunangire imitima yanyu nk’igihe cy’amananiza . »
58003016	Ni bande se koko « bumvise » maze bagatera « amananiza » ? Si abimutse mu Misiri bose , bayobowe na Musa ?
58003017	Kandi ni bande yarakariye « imyaka mirongo ine » yose ? Si abaguye mu cyaha , imirambo yabo ikararikwa mu butayu ?
58003018	Ni bande kandi « yarahiriye ko batazinjira mu buruhukiro bwe » , atari izo ntumvira nyine ?
58003019	Kandi tuzi ko batabwinjiyemo , ku mpamvu y’ukutemera kwabo .
58004001	Bityo rero , ubwo isezerano ryo kwinjira mu buruhukiro bwayo rikiri ryose , turamenye ntihazagire uwibwira ko we arihejweho .
58004002	Kuko natwe twashyikirijwe iyo nkuru nziza kimwe na bo , ariko ijambo bumvise ryabapfiriye ubusa , kuko bataryakiranye ukwemera .
58004003	Naho twebwe abemeye tuzinjira koko muri ubwo buruhukiro , ari bwo Imana yabatangarijeho iti « Narahije uburakari bwanjye ko batazinjira mu buruhukiro bwanjye ! » Nta we ushidikanya ko Imana yujuje ibikorwa byayo byose kuva isi ikiremwa ,
58004004	nk’uko hari aho bavuga iby’umunsi wa karindwi , ngo « Nuko kuri uwo munsi wa karindwi Imana iruhuka umurimo yari imaze gukora . »
58004005	Hanyuma kandi nk’uko bimaze kuvugwa ngo « Ntibazinjira mu buruhukiro bwanjye . »
58004006	Ubwo rero hakiri abagenewe kubwinjiramo , kandi abumvise bwa mbere iyo Nkuru Nziza batabwinjiyemo ku mpamvu y’ukutemera kwabo ,
58004007	Imana yongeye gushyiraho undi munsi mushya , uwa none , ibisobanurisha Dawudi , hashize igihe kirekire , muri aya magambo , iti « Uyu munsi , nimwumva ijwi rye , ntimunangire imitima yanyu . »
58004008	Kandi koko , iyo Yozuwe aza kuba ari we wabagejeje mu buruhukiro , Imana ntiba yaravuze iby’umunsi wundi .
58004009	Hakaba rero hari ikindi kiruhuko cy’umunsi wa karindwi kizigamiwe umuryango w’Imana .
58004010	Kuko uwinjiye muri icyo kiruhuko , na we aruhuka imirimo ye , nk’uko Imana yaruhutse iyayo .
58004011	Nitwihutire rero kwinjira muri icyo kiruhuko , ngo hato urugero rw’ukutemera kwacu rutagira uwo rugusha .
58004012	Koko Ijambo ry’Imana ni irinyabuzima , ni irinyabushobozi , kandi riratyaye kurusha inkota y’amugi abiri . Riracengera kugeza aho umutima n’ubwenge bitandukanira , hagati y’ingingo n’imisokoro ; rigasobanura ibyifuzo n’ibitekerezo byihishe muri muntu .
58004013	Nta kiremwa na kimwe kiribera intaboneka , ahubwo byose biratamuruye kandi biritaragaje mu maso y’Uwo tuzagomba kumurikira ibyacu .
58004014	Ubwo dufite Umuherezagitambo mukuru uhebuje , watashye mu ijuru , Yezu , Umwana w’Imana , nitwikomezemo ukwemera .
58004015	Koko rero ntidufite Umuherezagitambo mukuru wananirwa kudutabara mu ntege nke zacu ; yageragejwe muri byose , ku buryo bumwe natwe , ariko ntiyatsindwa n’icyaha .
58004016	Nitwegerane rero ubwizere intebe ya Nyirineza , kugira ngo tugirirwe impuhwe , kandi duhabwe imbaraga zizadufasha igihe kigeze .
58005001	Umuherezabitambo mukuru wese atorwa mu bantu kandi agashyirirwaho gufasha abantu mu mubano wabo n’Imana ; ashinzwe guhereza amaturo n’ibitambo bihongerera ibyaha .
58005002	Ubwo na we ari umunyantege nke muri byinshi , ashobora kumva abatarasobanukirwa , bagihuzagurika ;
58005003	kandi nk’uko atambirira ibyaha by’imbaga , na we aboneraho guhongerera ibye bwite .
58005004	Nta wiha ubwe bwite icyo cyubahiro , ahubwo gihabwa uwo Imana ibihamagariye , kimwe na Aroni .
58005005	Mbese nk’uko Kristu atihaye ubwe iryo kuzo ryo kuba Umuherezagitambo mukuru , ahubwo akaba yararihawe n’Uwamubwiye ati « Uri umwana wanjye , ni jye wakwibyariye uyu munsi » ;
58005006	kimwe n’uko avuga ahandi ati « Uri umuherezagitambo iteka ryose , wo mu cyiciro cya Malekisedeki . »
58005007	Mu gihe cy’imibereho ye yo ku isi , ni We wasengaga atakamba mu miborogo n’amarira , abitura Uwashoboraga kumurokora urupfu , maze arumvirwa kuko yagororokeye Imana .
58005008	Nubwo yari Mwana bwose , ibyo yababaye byamwigishije kumvira ;
58005009	maze aho amariye kuba intagereranywa , abamwumvira bose abaviramo isoko y’ubucungurwe bw’iteka .
58005010	Imana yamugize Umuherezagitambo mukuru wo mu cyiciro cya Malekisedeki .
58005011	Turacyafite byinshi byo kubabwira kuri izo ngingo , ariko biraruhije kubibasobanurira kuko muri abantu batumva vuba .
58005012	Mwagombye kuba mwarabaye abahanga kuva kera , nyamara muracyakeneye ko babigisha ingingo z’ibanze z’amagambo y’Imana . Muracyakeneye gutungwa n’amata mu mwanya w’ibiryo bikomeye .
58005013	Unywa amata gusa aba akiri umwana , ntashobore kugira igitekerezo gihamye ku byaba bitunganye .
58005014	Abaciye akenge bo , batungwa n’ibiryo bikomeye , kuko bafite akamenyero ko gusobanura mu bitekerezo byabo icyiza n’ikibi .
58006001	Nuko rero , tube turetse inyigisho z’ibanze zerekeye Kristu , maze tujye mu byisumbuye bikwiriye abakuze . Ntitugaruka ku mahame y’ishingiro ariyo y’aya : gutandukana n’ibikorwa bikurura urupfu , kwemera Imana ,
58006002	inyigisho zerekeye za batisimu , kuramburirwaho ibiganza , izuka ry’abapfuye , n’urubanza rw’iteka .
58006003	Ndetse ni uko tugiye kubigenza , niba Imana ibitwemereye .
58006004	Abigeze gushyikirizwa urumuri , bagasogongera ku ngabire z’Imana , bagahabwa Roho Mutagatifu ,
58006005	bakaryoherwa n’Ijambo ryiza ry’Imana , bakibonera ububasha bw’igihe kizaza , bazamera bate niba bararenze kuri ibyo bakagwa ?
58006006	Ntibishoboka ko bivugurura bundi bushya bicuza , kandi ku bwabo bakomeza kubamba ku musaraba Umwana w’Imana bamusuzuguza ku mugaragaro .
58006007	Iyo ubutaka bunywa amazi abugwaho maze bukabyarira ababuhinga imbuto z’ingirakamaro , buba buhawe umugisha w’Imana .
58006008	Naho iyo bumezeho amahwa n’ibitovu , buba butaye agaciro , bukwiye kuvumwa , amaherezo bukagabizwa umuriro .
58006009	Mwebweho rero , nkoramutima , nubwo tumaze kuvuga dutyo , ntidushidikanya ko muri mu nzira nziza , ari yo y’uburokorwe .
58006010	Imana rwose ntirenganya , ntishobora kwibagirwa umwete wanyu n’urukundo mwagaragarije izina ryayo , mufasha abatagatifujwe nk’uko n’ubu mukibikomeje .
58006011	Cyakora , icyo twifuza ni uko buri wese yakomeza iryo shyaka rizamugeza ku ndunduro y’ibyo yizeye .
58006012	Bityo rero , umurego wanyu ntugacogore , ahubwo mukurikize urugero rw’abahawe umurage wabasezeranijwe , babikesheje ukwemera n’ukwiyumanganya .
58006013	Igihe Imana isezeranyije Abrahamu , kuko nta wundi wari uyisumbye ngo imurahirire , yarirahiriye ubwayo iti
58006014	« Rwose nzaguhundazaho imigisha , kandi nzaguha inkomoko nyamwinshi . »
58006015	Abrahamu akomeza kwihangana bigeza aho yuzurizwa amasezerano .
58006016	Ubusanzwe abantu barahirira imbere y’ubaruta , maze kugira ngo bakemure impaka bakishingikiriza iyo ndahiro .
58006017	Ni cyo cyatumye Imana ubwayo ikoresha indahiro ngo igaragarize abo yageneye isezerano ko umugambi wayo udakuka .
58006018	Iryo sezerano n’iyo ndahiro bidakuka kandi bitarangwamo ubuhendanyi bw’Imana , ni byo shingiro ridahungabana ry’amizero yacu , twe abemeye guhara byose ngo tugere ku mizero twasezeranijwe .
58006019	Ayo mizero ni nk’inkingi umutima wacu wegamiye , kandi akaba ari yo atugeza hirya y’umubambiko ,
58006020	ha handi Yezu yatubanjirije kwinjira , ari Umuherezagitambo mukuru kandi w’iteka ryose , wo mu cyiciro cya Malekisedeki .
58007001	Uwo Malekisedeki , Umwami w’i Salemu , umuherezabitambo w’Imana Isumba byose , ni we wasanganiye Abrahamu wari umaze gutsinda Abami , nuko amuvugiraho amagambo y’umugisha .
58007002	Ni we kandi Abrahamu yeguriye igice cya cumi cy’iminyago . Izina rye risobanura mbere na mbere « umwami w’ubutabera » , hanyuma kandi kuba umwami w’i Salemu bivuga « Umwami w’amahoro » .
58007003	Byongeye Malekisedeki , nta se uzwi , nta nyina , nta bisekuruza , nta we uzi igihe yavukiye n’igihe yapfiriye , maze agashushanya atyo Umwana w’Imana , akaba kandi n’Umuherezabitambo w’iteka ryose .
58007004	Nimwirebere ubukuru bw’uwo muntu , Abrahamu , umukurambere wacu , yeguriye igice cya cumi cy’iminyago myiza !
58007005	Abakomoka kuri Levi batorewe kuba abaherezabitambo , ni bo bonyine Amategeko ashinga kwakirira rubanda kimwe cya cumi cy’umusaruro wabo ugenewe Ingoro ; abo bawutanga kandi ni abavandimwe babo bakomoka kuri Abrahamu .
58007006	Ariko Malekisedeki we , utari uwo mu bisekuruza byabo , yegukanye igice cya cumi cy’umutungo wa Abrahamu , kandi aha umugisha uwaragijwe amasezerano y’Imana .
58007007	Nta we ushidikanya ko umuto ari we uhabwa umugisha n’umukuru .
58007008	Bisubiye kandi bene Levi basoresha ni abagenewe kuzapfa , naho Malekisedeki we bahamya ko ariho .
58007009	Twavuga ndetse ko Levi , wakiraga kimwe cya cumi , na we ubwe yagitangiye muri Abrahamu ,
58007010	kuko yari akiri mu nda ya sekuruza igihe asanganiwe na Malekisedeki .
58007011	Iyaba ubuherezabitambo bwa Levi bwari bwuzuye — kandi mu by’ukuri ari bwo shingiro ry’amategeko yahawe Israheli — ntibiba byarabaye ngombwa ko haduka undi muherezabitambo , wo mu cyiciro cya Malekisedeki , aho kuba uwo mu cyiciro cya Aroni .
58007012	Igihe rero ubuherezabitambo buhindutse , ni ngombwa ko n’amategeko ahinduka .
58007013	Uwo ibi bivugwaho — Nyagasani Umwami wacu — avuka mu bundi bwoko butigeze gushingwa imirimo y’urutambiro .
58007014	Nta we uyobewe ko Umwami wacu akomoka kuri Yuda , ubwoko Musa atigeze ahingutsa mu bagenewe ubuherezabitambo .
58007015	Bikarushaho kumvikana , iyo tuzirikana ko umuherezabitambo uje ari uwo mu cyiciro cya Malekisedeki ;
58007016	akaba atabugejejweho n’amategeko y’abantu , ahubwo n’ububasha bw’ubugingo buhoraho .
58007017	Dore koko ibyamwemejweho : « Uri umuherezabitambo iteka ryose , wo mu cyiciro cya Malekisedeki . »
58007018	Bityo amahame ya mbere akaba avuyeho , kuko yari adafashe kandi nta kamaro .
58007019	Amategeko koko nta cyo yigeze ageza ku ndunduro ; ni yo mpamvu twahawe amizero yisumbuye ari yo dukesha kwegera Imana .
58007020	Uretse ibyo kandi habaye n’indahiro y’Imana : ubwo abaherezabitambo ba mbere bashyirwagaho nta ndahiro ,
58007021	Uwacu we yashyirishijweho indahiro y’Uwamubwiye ati « Uhoraho yarabirahiriye , kandi ntazisubiraho : Uri Umuherezagitambo iteka ryose . »
58007022	Ni kuri ubwo buryo Yezu ahagarariye Isezerano ryisumbuye .
58007023	Byongeye kandi , abaherezabitambo ba mbere bakurikiranye ari benshi , kuko urupfu rwabatwaraga ;
58007024	ariko We , kuko ari uw’iteka ryose , ubuherezagitambo bwe ntibusimburanwaho .
58007025	Ni cyo gituma ashobora kurokora burundu abamunyuraho bagana Imana , kuko abereyeho kubingingira iteka ryose .
58007026	Uwo ni we koko muherezagitambo mukuru twari dukeneye , w’intungane , w’umuziranenge , w’umuzirabwandu , utabarirwa mu banyabyaha , wakiriwe ahasumbye ijuru .
58007027	Ntameze nk’abandi baherezabitambo bakuru bagomba gutamba buri munsi , bakabanza guhongerera ibyaha byabo bwite , bakabona guhongerera iby’imbaga ; ibyo We yabigize rimwe rizima yitangaho igitambo ubwe .
58007028	Abo Amategeko ashyiriraho kuba abaherezabitambo bakuru ni abanyantege nke , ariko Uwashyirishijweho indahiro yakuye Amategeko , ni Umwana w’Imana wuje ubutungane iteka ryose .
58008001	Ingingo y’ingenzi y’ibyo tuvuga ni uko dufite Umuherezagitambo mukuru wa bene ako kageni , wicaye mu ijuru iburyo bwa Nyirikuzo ,
58008002	akaba ashinzwe ingoro n’ihema nyaryo , ritubatswe n’abantu , ahubwo Imana yiyubakiye ubwayo .
58008003	Umuherezabitambo mukuru wese ashyirirwaho guhereza amaturo n’ibitambo , bikamubera ngombwa ko na we agira icyo atura .
58008004	Mu by’ukuri , iyaba Yezu yari ari ku isi , ntiyaba umuherezabitambo , kuko hatabuze abahereza amaturo bakurikije Amategeko .
58008005	Ibyo abo ngabo bakora ku isi ni ibishushanyo bica amarenga y’ibiriho mu ijuru , nk’uko Musa agiye kubaka Ihema yabwirijwe n’Imana ngo « Itegereze , uzakore byose ukurikije urugero rw’ibyo werekewe hejuru y’umusozi . »
58008006	Ariko ubu ngubu Umuherezagitambo wacu mukuru yeguriwe umurimo uruta cyane uwabo , kuko ari umuhuza w’Isezerano rishingiye ku byiza bihebuje , biruse ibyari byarasezeranywe mbere .
58008007	Iyaba Isezerano rya mbere ryarabaye indakemwa , ntiriba ryaragombye gusimburwa n’irya kabiri .
58008008	Kuko Imana yabatonganyije , igira iti « Ngaha iminsi igiye kuza , uwo ari Nyagasani ubivuga , maze nzagirane Isezerano rishya n’inzu ya Israheli , n’inzu ya Yuda ;
58008009	atari nk’isezerano nagiranye n’abasekuruza babo umunsi mbafata ikiganza ngo mbakure mu gihugu cya Misiri . Kubera ko batakomeje isezerano ryanjye , nanjye narabitaruye , uwo ari Nyagasani ubivuga .
58008010	None ngiri Isezerano nzagirana n’inzu ya Israheli nyuma y’iyo minsi , uwo ari Nyagasani ubivuga : ’ Nzashyira amategeko yanjye mu bwenge bwabo , maze nyandike mu mutima wabo ; nzababera Imana , na bo bazambere umuryango . ’
58008011	Maze hekuzagira uwongera kwigisha mugenzi we cyangwa ubwiriza umuvandimwe we , ati ’ Umenye Nyagasani ’ , kuko bose bazaba banzi , kuva ku muto kugeza ku mukuru .
58008012	Kuko nzabababarira ubuhemu bwabo bwose , maze ibicumuro byabo sinongere kubyibuka . »
58008013	Kuvuga rero « isezerano rishya » , ni uko irya mbere Imana iba irigize impitagihe ; ikibaye kandi icya kera n’igisazira kiba kigiye gushiraho
58009001	Isezerano rya mbere ryari rifite imihango irigenga , n’ingoro Imana isingirizwamo hano ku isi .
58009002	Bari barashinze ihema , rigizwe n’ibyumba bibiri . Icya mbere cyabagamo ikinyarumuri , n’imigati y’umumuriko , kikitwa ahatagatifu .
58009003	Hirya y’umubambiko wa kabiri hakaba icyumba cyitwa ahatagatifu rwose ,
58009004	cyabagamo urutambiro rwa zahabu rutwikirwaho imibavu , hakabamo kandi Ubushyinguro bw’Isezerano busizwe hose zahabu ; muri bwo harimo agaherezo ka zahabu kuzuyemo manu , harimo kandi inkoni ya Aroni yari yarashibutseho indabo , n’ibimanyu by’amabuye byanditsweho Isezerano .
58009005	Hejuru y’Ubushyinguro hakaba Abakerubimu b’ikuzo batwikiriye urwicurizo . Ariko si igihe cyo kuvuga umwirondoro w’ibyo byose .
58009006	Ibikoresho iyo bimaze gutunganywa mu myanya yabyo , abaherezabitambo binjira igihe cyose mu cyumba cya mbere , bakahakorera imihango yo gusenga .
58009007	Mu cyumba cya kabiri ho , umuherezabitambo mukuru ahinjira gusa rimwe mu mwaka , kandi yitwaje amaraso yo guhongerera ibyaha by’ubujiji bwe bwite , kimwe n’iby’imbaga .
58009008	Roho Mutagatifu agaragaza atyo ko inzira y’ahatagatifu rwose itarugururwa mu gihe ingoro ya mbere ikiriho .
58009009	Ni amarenga y’iki gihe turimo , atwumvisha ko amaturo n’ibitambo bihaturirwa bidashobora kugeza ku butungane umutima w’ukora iyo mihango .
58009010	Ubwo ishingiye ku biribwa , ku binyobwa no kwisukurisha amazi , ni imihango iringaniye n’intege nke z’abantu , yemewe kuzageza igihe Imana izavugururira byose .
58009011	Igihe Kristu ahingukiye , yaje ari Umuherezagitambo mukuru , w’ibyiza bizaza . Yambukiranyije ingoro isumbije iya mbere agaciro n’ubutungane , itubatswe n’ikiganza cy’abantu , ari byo kuvuga ko itari iyo muri ibi byaremwe .
58009012	Yinjiye rimwe rizima ahatagatifu rwose , atahinjiranye amaraso ya za ruhaya n’ay’ibimasa , ahubwo aye bwite , aturonkera atyo ubucungurwe bw’iteka .
58009013	Niba koko amaraso ya za ruhaya n’ay’ibimasa , kimwe n’umuyonga w’inyana yatwitswe , bishobora gusukura no gutagatifuza umubiri w’abo byuhagijwe ,
58009014	nk’amaraso ya Kristu wituye Imana ho igitambo kitagira inenge ku bwa Roho Uhoraho , yo azarushaho ate gusukura umutima wacu , awukiza ibikorwa bitera urupfu , ngo dushobore gusingiza Imana Nzima ?
58009015	Ni cyo gituma Kristu yabaye ishingiro ry’Isezerano rishya , kuko yapfiriye gukiza ibicumuro by’abari bakigengwa n’Isezerano rya mbere , kandi ngo abatowe bazahabwe umurage w’iteka wabasezeranijwe .
58009016	Koko rero iyo hari uburage , ni ngombwa ko urupfu rw’uraga rubanza kugaragara .
58009017	Uburage bugira agaciro iyo uraga yapfuye ; naho iyo akiriho , nta gaciro buba bufite .
58009018	Ni cyo cyatumye n’Isezerano rya mbere ritashoboye kubaho hatabanje kumenwa amaraso .
58009019	Koko rero , igihe Musa yari amaze gutangariza imbaga amabwiriza yose uko yanditswe mu Mategeko , yafashe amaraso y’ibimasa n’aya za ruhaya , hamwe n’amazi , abimisha ku gitabo no ku mbaga yose akoresheje ubwoya bw’intama butukura n’icyuhagiro ,
58009020	avuga ati « Aya ni amaraso y’Isezerano Imana yabageneye . »
58009021	Hanyuma kandi ayo maraso ayuhagiza Ihema n’ibikoresho byose by’imihango mitagatifu .
58009022	Bityo , nk’uko Amategeko abivuga , hafi ya byose bisukurishwa amaraso , maze ntihabe ibabarirwa ry’ibyaha , hatabanje kumenwa amaraso .
58009023	Niba ibishushanya iby’ijuru bisukurwa kuri ubwo buryo , ni ngombwa ko iby’ijuru nyirizina bisukurwa n’ibitambo byisumbuyeho .
58009024	Koko , Kristu ntiyinjiye mu ngoro yubatswe n’abantu yacaga amarenga y’Ingoro y’ukuri , ahubwo yatashye mu ijuru ubwaryo , kugira ngo aduhagararire ubu ngubu imbere y’Imana .
58009025	Kandi ntiyagombaga kwitamba ubwe incuro nyinshi , nk’uko umuherezabitambo mukuru yinjiranaga buri mwaka ahatagatifu rwose amaraso atari aye .
58009026	Iyo biba ibyo , Kristu aba yaragombye kubabara incuro nyinshi kuva isi ikiremwa . Mu by’ukuri , yahingutse rimwe rizima , ibihe byuzurijwe , kugira ngo icyaha agihanagurishe igitambo cye .
58009027	Nk’uko kandi umuntu wese yagenewe gupfa rimwe rizima , nyuma agacirwa urubanza ,
58009028	ni na ko Kristu yatuweho igitambo rimwe rizima kugira ngo avaneho ibyaha by’abantu batabarika , nyuma akazaza ubwa kabiri , bitagifite amahuriro n’icyaha , azaniye uburokorwe abamutegereje bose .
58010001	Amategeko ya kera ntiyarangaga bihagije amahame y’ukuri , ahubwo yari amarenga y’ibyiza bizaza . Ntiyashoboraga na gato kugeza ku butungane abaturaga ubudahwema ibyo bitambo bidahinduka , basubiragamo buri mwaka .
58010002	Iyo bitaba ibyo , baba bararetse kubitura , kuko iyo baza gusukurwa burundu , ntibari gukomeza kwigiramo inkeke y’icyaha .
58010003	Nyamara ahubwo ibyo bitambo byari bigamije buri mwaka kwibutsa imbaga ibyaha byayo .
58010004	Koko rero nta kuntu amaraso y’ibimasa n’aya za ruhaya ashobora kuvanaho ibyaha .
58010005	Ni cyo cyatumye igihe Kristu aje ku isi , yavuze ati « Ntiwanyuzwe n’ibitambo n’amaturo , ahubwo wampangiye umubiri .
58010006	Ntiwashimishijwe n’ibitambo bitwikwa bihongerera ibyaha ;
58010007	nuko ndavuga nti ’ Dore ndaje , kuko ari jye uvugwa mu muzingo w’igitabo , ngo nkore ugushaka kwawe , Dawe ’ . »
58010008	Umva ko abanje kuvuga ati « Ntiwanyuzwe cyangwa ngo ushimishwe n’amaturo n’ibitambo bitwikwa » , bihongerera ibyaha » , nyamara biturwa uko biteganywa n’Amategeko !
58010009	Hanyuma akongeraho ati « Dore ndaje ngo nkore ugushaka kwawe . » Ni uko yakuyeho uburyo bwa mbere bwo gutura , ashinga ubwa kabiri .
58010010	Ni ku bw’uko gushaka kandi twatagatifujwe n’ituro ry’umubiri wa Kristu ryabaye rimwe rizima .
58010011	Mu gihe umuherezabitambo wese ahora ahagaze ngo akore buri munsi imihango , atura kenshi ibitambo bihora ari bimwe kandi bidashobora kuvanaho ibyaha ,
58010012	Kristu We , aho amariye guhereza igitambo rukumbi gihongerera ibyaha , « yicaye iburyo bw’Imana ubuziraherezo » ,
58010013	akaba kuva ubwo ategereje ko « abanzi be bahindurwamo akabaho ko mu nsi y’ibirenge bye . »
58010014	Ku bw’iryo turo rimwe rukumbi yagejeje ku butungane abo yiyemeje gutagatifuza .
58010015	Ni na byo kandi Roho Mutagatifu ubwe atwemeza . Kuko amaze kuvuga ati
58010016	« Ngiri Isezerano nzagirana na bo nyuma y’iyo minsi » . Nyagasani yaratangaje ati « Nzashyira amategeko yanjye mu mutima wabo , maze nzayandike no mu bwenge bwabo .
58010017	Sinzongera kwibuka ibyaha byabo . »
58010018	Bityo rero ahari ibabarirwa , ntihaba hagikeneye ibitambo byo guhongerera ibyaha .
58010019	Kuri ubwo buryo , bavandimwe , dufite ubwizere buhagije bwo kuzataha mu ngoro ntagatifu , tubikesheje amaraso ya Kristu .
58010020	Yaduhangiye inzira nshya kandi nyabuzima , ihinguranya umubambiko , ari byo kuvuga umubiri we .
58010021	Tukaba ubu dufite umuherezagitambo uhebuje uyobora inzu y’Imana .
58010022	Nitumwegerane rero umutima ugororotse n’ukwemera guhamye , dufite umutima wakijijwe inkeke yose y’icyaha n’umubiri wuhagijwe amazi asukuye .
58010023	Nitwikomezemo amizero yacu tudacogora , kuko Uwatugiriye amasezerano ari indahemuka .
58010024	Bamwe bajye bita ku bandi , duterana umwete mu rukundo no mu bikorwa byiza .
58010025	Ntitukihunze amakoraniro yacu , nk’uko bamwe babigizemo akamenyero ; ahubwo niturusheho guterana inkunga , cyane cyane ndetse ubwo mubona ko umunsi wa Nyagasani wegereje .
58010026	Tumenye ko , niba dukomeje gucumura tubishaka , kandi twaramenyeshejwe ukuri kose , nta gitambo kindi gisigaye cyo guhongerera ibyaha byacu ;
58010027	ahasigaye ni ugutegereza urubanza rukaze n’inkongi y’umuriro uzatsemba ibyigomeke .
58010028	Uwagira atya akarenga ku mategeko ya Musa , nta shiti azicwa nta mbabazi , niba byemejwe n’abagabo babiri cyangwa batatu .
58010029	Bizagendekera bite rero uzaba asuzuguye Umwana w’Imana , akandavuza amaraso y’Isezerano ry’Imana yamutagatifuje , kandi agatuka Roho Nyir’ingabire ? Nimwiyumvishe ukuntu igihano azaba akwiye kizarushaho kuba gikaze .
58010030	Ntituyobewe , Uwavuze ati « Uguhora ni ukwanjye ; ni jye kandi utanga ibihembo » , akongera ati « Nyagasani azacira urubanza umuryango we . »
58010031	Ni akaga gakomeye kwibasirwa n’ikiganza cy’Imana Nzima .
58010032	Nimwibuke uko mwatangiye mukimara kubona urumuri , ukuntu mwarwanye intambara ikomeye kandi ibabaje :
58010033	rimwe mushungerwa mu bitutsi no mu bitotezo , ubundi mwifatanya n’abagirirwaga ayo marorerwa .
58010034	Kandi koko mwasangiye ububabare n’abafunzwe , mwakirana ibyishimo isahurwa ry’ibintu byanyu , kuko mwari muzi ko mufite ubukungu bwisumbuyeho kandi buzahoraho .
58010035	Amizero yanyu ntagacogore , azabahesha ingororano ikomeye .
58010036	Ubu icyo mukeneye ni ubutwari buzabafasha kuzuza ugushaka kw’Imana no kuronka ibyiza mwasezeranijwe .
58010037	Kuko « hasigaye akanya gato , ndetse gatoya cyane , maze Ugomba kuza akaza bidatinze .
58010038	Intungane yanjye izabeshwaho n’ukwemera ; nyamara niba inyuze ukwayo , ntizongera guhimbaza umutima wanjye . »
58010039	Twebweho ntituri abantu bo gutezuka ngo bitume tworama , ahubwo turi abantu bafite ukwemera kuzaduhesha uburokorwe .
58011001	Ukwemera ni ishingiro ry’ibyo twizeye , kukatubera n’icyemezo cy’ibitagaragara .
58011002	Ukwemera ni ko kwahesheje abakera gushimwa n’Imana .
58011003	Ukwemera kutwumvisha ko ibyaremwe byatunganijwe n’Ijambo ry’Imana , bityo rero ko ibigaragara bikomoka ku bitagaragara .
58011004	Ukwemera kwatumye Abeli ahereza Imana igitambo gitambutse icya Kayini . Kwamugaragajeho rero kuba intungane kuko Imana yashimye amaturo ye . Ku bw’uko kwemera , n’ubwo yapfuye bwose , aracyavuga na n’ubu .
58011005	Ukwemera kwatumye Henoki ajyanwa , maze ahonoka urupfu , akaba rero nta wongeye kumubona , kuko Imana yamwijyaniye ; koko mbere y’uko ajyanwa yari yaragaragaweho ko yanogeye Imana .
58011006	Nuko rero nta we ushobora kunyura Imana adafite ukwemera , kuko uwegera Imana wese agomba kwemera ko ibaho kandi igahemba abayishakashaka .
58011007	Aho Nowa amariye kumenyeshwa ibyari bitaraba , ukwemera kwatumye adashidikanya maze aremekanya ubwato bwo kurokoreramo umuryango we . Ubwo ahamya isi icyaha , maze asigara ari ingenerwamurage y’ubutungane buturuka ku kwemera .
58011008	Ukwemera kwatumye Abrahamu yumvira Imana , agenda agana igihugu yari agiye guhabwa ho umurage , kandi agenda atazi iyo ajya .
58011009	Ukwemera kwatumye atura nk’umushyitsi mu gihugu yasezeranijwe , acumbika mu ihema , hamwe na Izaki na Yakobo , ari bo basangiye amasezerano .
58011010	Abrahamu uwo yari ategereje umurwa wubatse ku kibanza gikomeye , watekerejwe kandi ukubakwa n’Imana ubwayo .
58011011	Ukwemera kwatumye na Sara , wari ugeze mu zabukuru , ahabwa ubushobozi bwo gusama inda , kuko yari yizeye ubudahemuka bw’Uwabagiriye amasezerano .
58011012	Ni na yo mpamvu umuntu umwe , ndetse wari wegereje urupfu yakomotsweho n’imbaga ingana n’inyenyeri zo mu kirere kandi itabarika nk’umusenyi wo ku nkombe y’inyanja .
58011013	Abo bose bapfanye ukwemera , na none bataragera ku byiza basezeranijwe , ariko basa n’ababirabukwa , babiramukiriza kure , bahamya ko ari abagenzi n’abashyitsi kuri iyi si .
58011014	Abavuga batyo baragaragaza rwose ko bari mu gushakashaka igihugu cy’iwabo nyakuri ;
58011015	kuko iyo baza kuba bakumbuye icyo baturutsemo , bari bagifite umwanya uhagije wo gusubirayo .
58011016	Mu by’ukuri bari barangamiye ikindi gihugu cyiza , ari cyo iwabo ho mu ijuru . Ni na yo mpamvu Imana itagira ipfunwe ryo kwitwa Imana yabo , kuko ari Yo yabateguriye umurwa .
58011017	Ukwemera kwatumye , mu gihe cy’igeragezwa , Abrahamu atura Izaki ho igitambo ; atura umwana we w’ikinege , kandi yari yarahawe amasezerano ,
58011018	abwirwa ati « Izaki ni we uzaguhesha urubyaro ruzakwitirirwa . »
58011019	Yiyemezaga ko Imana ishobora no kuzura uwapfuye , bituma asubizwa umwana we , biba n’amarenga y’ibizaza .
58011020	Ukwemera kwatumye Izaki aha Yakobo na Ezawu umugisha uzabafasha mu gihe kizaza .
58011021	Ukwemera kwatumye Yakobo , igihe yari agiye gupfa , aha umugisha buri muhungu wa Yozefu , nuko apfukama yishingikirije inkoni ye .
58011022	Ukwemera kwatumye Yozefu wendaga gupfa atangaza imitahukire y’abana ba Israheli , kandi agena n’uko bazagenzereza amagufa ye .
58011023	Ukwemera kwatumye Musa , amaze kuvuka , ahishwa n’ababyeyi be amezi atatu yose , kuko bari banyuzwe n’uburanga bwe , ntibatinya guca ku itegeko ry’umwami .
58011024	Ukwemera kwatumye Musa , aho amariye gukura , yigurutsa kwitwa umwana w’umukobwa wa Farawo ,
58011025	ahitamo kuburagizwa hamwe n’umuryango w’Imana aho kwishimishiriza mu byaha by’igihe gito .
58011026	Yiyumvisha ko kwifatanya n’ugusuzugurwa k’umuryango watowe bitambukije kure agaciro ubukire bwose bwo mu Misiri , kuko amaso ye yari arangamiye indi ngororano .
58011027	Ukwemera kwatumye yimuka mu Misiri ntiyakangwa n’uburakari bw’umwami , nuko ntiyahindagana amera nk’umuntu wizigiye Utaboneshwa amaso .
58011028	Ukwemera kwatumye ahimbaza Pasika , maze asiga amaraso ku nzu z’Abayisraheli , kugira ngo Umunyacyorezo atarimbura abana b’imfura .
58011029	Ukwemera kwabambukije Inyanja Itukura nko ku butaka bwumutse , mu gihe Abanyamisiri babiganye , bo bararohama .
58011030	Ukwemera kwatumye inkuta zizitiye Yeriko zihirika , bamaze kuzizenguruka iminsi irindwi yose .
58011031	Ukwemera kwatumye Rahabu w’ihabara atarimburwa hamwe n’ibyigomeke , kuko yakiranye amahoro intasi za Israheli .
58011032	Mbese mvuge nte kandi ? Nta gihe nabona cyo kuvuga bihagije ibya Gideyoni , Baraki , Samusoni , Yefute , Dawudi , Samweli , n’Abahanuzi .
58011033	Ukwemera kwabo kwatumye batsinda amahanga , bategekana ubutabera , buzurizwa amasezerano , bazibiranya urwasaya rw’intare ,
58011034	bazimya ubukana bw’umuriro , bahonoka ubugi bw’inkota , bashinga intege bakirutse indwara , bagira ubutwari igihe cy’intambara , bakumira ingabo z’abanyamahanga .
58011035	Hari n’abagore bazuriwe abana babo bari bapfuye . Hari n’abahisemo gutanyaguzwa , banga kubabarirwa , kugira ngo bazashyikire ubugingo bwisumbuye bw’abazutse .
58011036	Abandi bemeye agashinyaguro n’ibiboko , ndetse n’ingoyi n’uburoko .
58011037	Hari abatewe amabuye , basatuzwa urukero , batemaguzwa inkota ; hari abatorongeye , bagenda bambaye impu z’intama n’iz’ihene , ari abatindahare , bapfukiranwa kandi batotezwa ,
58011038	— abatari bagenewe kuba ab’isi — babuyeraga ku gasi no mu misozi , bahungira mu bigugu no mu masenga y’isi .
58011039	Abo bose , n’ubwo Imana yashimye ukwemera kwabo , ntibashoboye gushyikira iyuzuzwa ry’amasezerano ;
58011040	kuko Imana yari iduteganyirije ibyiza biruseho , ntiyashatse kubageza ku ndunduro yabyo , tutari kumwe .
58012001	Natwe rero , ubwo duhagarikiwe n’inteko ingana ityo y’ababaye intwari mu kwemera , nitwigobotore imizigo idushikamiye n’icyaha gihora kiducogoza , maze tuboneze inzira ubutagerura mu ntambara twahamagariwe ,
58012002	duhanze amaso Yezu , We ntangiriro n’iherezo ry’ukwemera kwacu , We wemeye guhara ibyishimo byari bimukwiye , akiyumanganya umusaraba adatinya ko byamuviramo ikimwaro , nuko kuva ubwo akicara iburyo bw’intebe y’Imana .
58012003	Koko nimutekereze uwababajwe cyane n’abanyabyaha bari bamwibasiye , agira ngo imitima yanyu itazacogozwa n’ukwiheba .
58012004	Ntimurarwana bigeze aho kuvushwa amaraso mu ntambara y’icyaha murimo ,
58012005	kandi mwiyibagije inama yabagiriwe kimwe n’abana ngo « Mwana wanjye , ntukange ko Nyagasani aguhana , cyangwa ngo ucogozwe n’uko agucyashye ;
58012006	kuko Nyagasani ahana abo akunda , agacyaha uwo yemereye kuba umwana we bwite . »
58012007	Ububabare bwanyu bugenewe kubagorora , kandi Imana ibafata nk’abana bayo . Ni uwuhe mwana rero udakosorwa na se ?
58012008	Niba muri abarindwabihano kandi abandi bose babihuriyeho , ubwo muri ibibyarirano , ntimuri abana b’ukuri .
58012009	Twarezwe n’ababyeyi bacu b’umubiri kandi bitugwa neza ; tuzarushaho dute rero kuyoboka Umubyeyi w’imitima yacu , ngo aduhaze ubugingo ?
58012010	Bo baducyahaga by’igihe gito , uko babyumvaga ; Imana Yo ibigirira ikidufitiye akamaro , igamije kutugeza ku butungane bwayo .
58012011	Nanone nta we uhita ashimishwa n’igihano , ahubwo kiramubabaza ; nyuma y’aho ariko , abo cyagoroye kibabyarira imbuto y’amahoro n’ubutungane .
58012012	« Nimukomeze rero ibiganza bidandabirana n’amavi ajegajega ;
58012013	kandi mutegurire ibirenge byanyu amayira agororotse » , kugira ngo ucumbagurika adahinyagara , ahubwo akurizeho gukira .
58012014	Nimuharanire kugirana amahoro n’abantu bose , no gutunga ubutungane kuko utabufite atazigera abona Imana .
58012015	Muramenye ntihazagire n’umwe usaguka ku ngabire y’Imana , ntihazamere kandi muri mwe ingemwe isharira yabatera imidugararo maze ikanduza imbaga yose .
58012016	Muramenye ntimukabemo inkozi y’ibibi n’imwe cyangwa umusebyamana , nka Ezawu waguranye imbehe icyubahiro cye cyo kuba imfura ya se .
58012017	Muzi kandi ko , hanyuma yashatse kuragwa umugisha , akabihakanirwa , akabura n’uburyo yabihindura , n’ubwo yatakambaga kandi asuka amarira !
58012018	Ntimwaje mugana ibintu bigaragara , nk’umuriro uhinda cyangwa igicu kibuditse , umwijima cyangwa inkubi y’umuyaga ,
58012019	umworomo w’impanda cyangwa ijwi risakabaka , ku buryo abaryumvise basabye ngo bekongera kuryumva .
58012020	« Ntibashoboye kwihanganira iri tegeko ryababwiraga ngo ’ Nihagira uwegera uyu musozi , ndetse n’ubwo ryaba ari itungo rizicishwe amabuye . »
58012021	Ibyo babonye byari biteye ubwoba kugeza aho Musa avuga ati « Nakutse umutima , none ndadagadwa ! »
58012022	Mwebweho mwaje mugana umusozi wa Siyoni n’umurwa w’Imana Nzima , ari wo Yeruzalemu yo mu ijuru , n’inteko itabarika y’abamalayika bakereye ibirori ;
58012023	mwasanze ikoraniro ry’abavukambere banditswe mu ijuru , mwegera n’Imana Umucamanza wa bose , n’intungane zageze ku ndunduro ,
58012024	mwegera kandi Yezu , We muhuza w’Isezerano rishya ku bw’amaraso yamishwe , aruta kure ay’Abeli .
58012025	Muririnde rero kwima amatwi Nyir’ukubabwira ! Abanze kumva uwabahanuriraga hano ku isi ntibashoboye kuzibukira igihano ; twebwe se tuzakitaza dute niba twirengagije Utubwirira mu ijuru ?
58012026	Ijwi rye ryahungabanyije isi kandi n’ubu aravuga ati « Hasigaye indi ncuro maze nekuzahungabanya isi yonyine , ahubwo ndetse n’ijuru . »
58012027	Ayo magambo ngo « hasigaye indi ncuro » aratwumvisha ko ibyo bihindagurika ari ibintu byaremwe bizavanwaho , kugira ngo ibidahindagurika bihoreho iteka .
58012028	Ubwo rero duhawe Ubwami budahindagurika , nidukomere kuri iyo ngabire , dukorere Imana ku buryo buyinogeye , mu cyubahiro n’igitinyiro ,
58012029	kuko Imana yacu ari umuriro ugurumana .
58013001	Nimwikomezemo urukundo rwa kivandimwe .
58013002	Ntimukibagirwe kwakira abashyitsi , kuko hariho ababikesheje kwakira abamalayika batabizi .
58013003	Muzirikane abari mu buroko nk’aho mwabaye imbohe hamwe na bo ; muzirikane kandi abababazwa kuko namwe mufite umubiri .
58013004	Ugushyingirwa nikubahwe na bose , n’uburiri bw’abashakanye buzire inenge , kuko Imana izacira urubanza abasambanyi n’inkozi z’ibibi .
58013005	Imibereho yanyu izire ubugugu , munyurwe n’ibyo mufite , kuko Nyagasani ubwe yavuze ati « Sinzaguhara , kandi sinzagutererana ! »
58013006	ku buryo dushobora kuvuga nta shiti tuti « Nyagasani arampagarikiye , ntakizantera ubwoba ; mbese ni nde wagira icyo antwara ? »
58013007	Nimuzirikane abayobozi banyu , ababamenyesheje Ijambo ry’Imana ; mwitegereze uko barangije ubutumwa bwabo , maze mukurikize ukwemera kwabo .
58013008	Yezu Kristu ntahinduka , ari ejo , ari none , no mu bihe byose .
